Wuh pi-maat-kur kushel wuh ac'ruth sa-te'kru had wuh vaksurik bah-ker, heh svi' wuh bah-ker lam-tor wuh lap if spitau pi-maat-kur savas. Aifa savas vesh' kwon-hau-ov tum-tor, heh pa' wuh wak lu au began tor tor'ovau piyah ish-veh vesh' afer-tor ik kanok mu-yor veh t' au vesh' hal-tor. Wuh sa-te'kru became maut reshnek na' nash, heh ordered wuh bahsu tor potau glantau ek' mu-yor ne' wuh lap. Wuh bahsu eku ish-veh eldest sa-fu tor glantau; tonk'peh pa' leh-dah o'wak-vel au tevan-tor asleep, heh svi' wuh asal wuh'ashiv t' wuh savas vesh' missing. Yi wuh dahr sa-fu vesh' ordered tor glantau; heh na' midnight au nuh' tevan-tor asleep, heh svi' wuh asal wuh'ashiv savas vesh' hal-tor. Yi wuh wuh sa-fu nufau tor potau glantau; tonk'peh wuh bahsu palikauk would ri kal-tor ish-veh, na' pthak ein klau dang sarlah tor ish-veh: however, na' kim-shah au consented, heh wuh nu'ri sasu laid himself ne' wuh lap tor glantau. U' wuh wak-vel kwul-tor leh-dah au puzhu-tor wuh rustling ralash svi' wuh sov, heh wuh kushel sarlah hashan ik vesh' t' pure pi-maat-tukh; heh u' ish-veh vesh' snapping na' veh t' wuh savas k' its beak, wuh bahsu's sa-fu spen-tor abru heh pohshaya wuh kliton na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh kliton did wuh kushel rai klau; goh ish-veh eku-tor wuh pi-maat-kur kan s' its harr, heh yi flew maf. Wuh pi-maat-kur kan vesh' katau tor wuh sa-te'kru svi' wuh asal, heh ek' wuh shikh-orna vesh' puvutau teretuhr. Kanok-veh sep-wafikh ik ish-veh vesh' don weht do ek' wuh don-tak t' wuh kingdom: tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'veh kan nam-tor t' rai nam-tor-tor tor me, i bolau ma wuh bosh kushel.' yi wuh bahsu's eldest sa-fu eku si' heh nahp tor talal wuh pi-maat-kur kushel maut easily; heh lu au had hal-tor tonk'peh wuh pi' yut, sarlah ish-veh tor wuh lapan, heh k' wuh vla t' wuh lapan gla-tor ish-veh wuh fox sitting; ni au nem-tor ish-veh kes-wun heh tor pok tor pohshau na' ish-veh. Yi wuh fox leralmin-tor, 'ri tor pohshau me, na' i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du rom counsel; i fai-tor ra ish-veh business nam-tor, heh ik du aitlun tor talal wuh pi-maat-kur kushel. Du dungi pulau wuh pi'kahr svi' wuh khru; heh lu du prah tra', du dungi gla-tor dahkuh ha-shal mesyutik tor tik vath, veh t' if nam-tor maut vaksurik heh vaksurik tor glazhau na': hal-tor ri svi' tra', tonk'peh shom na' wuh mu-yor svi' wuh vath, hi ish-veh lau saudau tor du tor nam-tor maut ri donku-tor heh tvai.' tonk'peh wuh sa-fu nahp tor himself, 'ra mokuhlek such wuh beast u' nash fai-tor pa' wuh tukh?' ni au pohshaya ish-veh kliton na' wuh fox; tonk'peh au din-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh eku abru its harr abru' its pla' heh sahr-tor vi' wuh lapan. Yi au went ish-veh yut, heh svi' wuh khru sarlah tor wuh pi'kahr wilat wuh dahkuh ha-shal vesh'; heh svi' veh t' aifa vesh' sutra uralaun, heh taman, heh feasting; tonk'peh wuh vath glazhau maut kitork, heh ri donku-tor. 'i dang nam-tor maut silly, ' leralmin-tor au, 'kuv i went tor ik shabby kelek, heh losrak nash sem-rik-tor shi'; ni au went vi' wuh klon kelek, heh ate heh drank na' ish-veh ease, heh forgot wuh kushel, heh ish-veh shasol nuh'. Wak be' dvun-tor fi'; heh u' wuh eldest sa-fu did ri sarlah pla', heh rai tidings vesh' puzhu-tor t' ish-veh, wuh dahr sa-fu eku si', heh wuh ka vel pavesh-tor tor ish-veh. Au ragel-tor wuh fox, vi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh rom na'shikh: tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh dahkuh ha-shal, ish-veh eldest sa-kai vesh' standing na' wuh krani wilat wuh merrymaking vesh', heh puvutau tor ish-veh tor sarlah svi'; heh au kupi ri withstand wuh temptation, tonk'peh went svi', heh forgot wuh pi-maat-kur kushel heh ish-veh shasol svi' wuh ka manner. Wak be' dvun-tor fi' va'ashiv, heh wuh youngest sa-fu nuh' istau tor eku si' vi' wuh eik panu tor seek na' wuh pi-maat-kur kushel; tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh would ri shroi tor ish-veh na' wuh wu du', na' au vesh' maut tishau t' ish-veh sa-fu, heh vesh' kwes ik ein has-bosh kunli lau pavesh-tor tor ish-veh isha, heh prevent ish-veh coming pla'. However, na' kim-shah ish-veh vesh' sep-wafikh au dang hal-tor, na' au would ri shom na' ha-kel; heh u' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh lapan, au ragel-tor wuh fox, heh puzhu-tor wuh ka rom counsel. Tonk'peh au vesh' itar-bosh tor wuh fox, heh did ri attempt ish-veh ha'kiv u' ish-veh sa-kai had ovsoh; ni wuh fox leralmin-tor, 'hayal-tor fi-tor t'nash-veh harr, heh du dungi haolvaya faster.' ni au hayal-tor ne', heh wuh fox began tor sahr-tor, heh maf au went abru' fek heh kov ni sahris ik ish-veh isachya whistled svi' wuh salan. Lu sarlah au tor wuh pi'kahr, wuh sa-fu zahal-tor wuh fox's counsel, heh rik' looking pa' ish-veh went tor wuh shabby ha-shal heh shom-tor tra' ek' mu-yor na' ish-veh ease. Svi' wuh asal sarlah wuh fox va'ashiv heh ragel-tor ish-veh u' au vesh' palikaya ish-veh halovaya, heh leralmin-tor, 'hal-tor zehik fa'rak, till sarlah du tor wuh castle, fa' if ti wuh bosh vus t' ask'ersu sahris asleep heh snoring: nem-tor rai beglanau t' au, tonk'peh hal-tor vi' wuh castle heh be' dvun fi' heh fi' till sarlah du tor wuh tvi-shal, wilat wuh pi-maat-kur kushel hayal-tor svi' wuh wooden kraisek; beyik ish-veh lam-tor wuh vaksurik pi-maat-kur kraisek; tonk'peh ri tor ar'kadan tor nem-tor wuh kushel s' wuh shabby kraisek heh shitau ish-veh vi' wuh handsome veh, vathru du dungi repent ish-veh.' yi wuh fox sakadau si' ish-veh harr va'ashiv, heh wuh nu'ri sasu hayal-tor himself ne', heh maf au went abru' fek heh kov till ish-veh isachya whistled svi' wuh salan. Fa' wuh castle temep ek' vesh' u' wuh fox had leralmin-tor: ni wuh sa-fu went svi' heh afer-tor wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh pi-maat-kur kushel geldau svi' wuh wooden kraisek, heh ne' lam-tor wuh pi-maat-kur kraisek, heh wuh rehkuh pi-maat-kur savas ik had vesh' pakik vesh' lying beyik ish-veh. Yi nahp au tor himself, 'ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh maut droll vel tor katau maf such wuh tok-ti kushel svi' nash shabby kraisek'; ni au tu'ash wuh svep heh nem-tor meskaraya t' ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh vi' wuh pi-maat-kur kraisek. Tonk'peh wuh kushel eku abru such wuh ral shei ik ek' wuh ask'ersu awoke, heh au nem-tor ish-veh prisoner heh lesh ish-veh fa' wuh sa-te'kru. Wuh thurai asal wuh kelek hayal-tor tor judge ish-veh; heh lu ek' vesh' puzhu-tor, ish-veh sentenced ish-veh tor tev-tor, vita au dang katau wuh sa-te'kru wuh pi-maat-kur jarel if kupi sahr-tor u' swiftly u' wuh salan; heh kuv au did nash, au vesh' ki' wuh pi-maat-kur kushel putan-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh sha'. Ni au eku si' wuh'wak weht fi' ish-veh halovaya, sighing, heh svi' lo'uk despair, lu fi' wuh sudden ish-veh t'hy'la wuh fox ragel-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'gla-tor du i' ra has pavesh-tor fi' khrosahp t' ish-veh ri listening tor t'nash-veh counsel. I dungi fam dvun, however, var-tor du uf tor talal wuh pi-maat-kur jarel, kuv du dungi tor u' i nufai du. Du bolau hal-tor zehik fi' till sarlah du tor wuh castle wilat wuh jarel lam-tor svi' ish-veh stall: k' ish-veh vla dungi ti wuh groom sahris asleep heh snoring: nem-tor maf wuh jarel quietly, tonk'peh nam-tor sure tor shitau wuh hinek leathern saddle fi-tor ish-veh, heh ri wuh pi-maat-kur veh ik nam-tor beyik ish-veh.' yi wuh sa-fu hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh fox's harr, heh maf au went abru' fek heh kov till ish-veh isachya whistled svi' wuh salan. Ek' went gas'rak, heh wuh groom ti snoring k' ish-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh pi-maat-kur saddle. Tonk'peh lu wuh sa-fu glazhau na' wuh jarel, au nahp ish-veh wuh lo'uk pity tor shitau wuh leathern saddle fi-tor ish-veh. 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh rom veh, ' leralmin-tor au; 'i am sure au nazh-tor ish-veh.' u' au nem-tor abru wuh pi-maat-kur saddle wuh groom awoke heh lit'dhae ni ral, ik ek' wuh klashau sahr-tor svi' heh nem-tor ish-veh prisoner, heh svi' wuh asal au vesh' va'ashiv katau fa' wuh kelek tor nam-tor judged, heh vesh' sentenced tor tev-tor. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' sep-wafikh, ik, kuv au kupi katau thither wuh vaksurik princess, au dang ha-tor, heh ma wuh kushel heh wuh jarel putan-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh sha'. Yi au went ish-veh yut maut sorrowful; tonk'peh wuh hinek fox sarlah heh leralmin-tor, 'po did ri du shroi tor me? Kuv du had, du would ma lesh maf fi' wuh kushel heh wuh jarel; wi dungi i wuh'wak weht mazhiv-kur-tor du counsel. Hal-tor zehik fi', heh svi' wuh khru du dungi lasha na' wuh castle. Na' leh-dah o'wak-vel na' mu-yor wuh princess hal-tor tor wuh bathing-kelek: hal-tor abru tor ish-veh heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shok, heh she dungi kal-tor du ras-tukh ish-veh maf; tonk'peh nem-tor tun du ri tor dash ish-veh tor hal-tor heh nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh.' yi wuh fox sakadau si' ish-veh harr, heh ni maf au went abru' fek heh kov till ish-veh isachya whistled va'ashiv. U' sarlah au tor wuh castle, ek' vesh' u' wuh fox had leralmin-tor, heh na' leh-dah o'wak-vel wuh nu'ri sasu ragel-tor wuh princess going tor wuh wu'sibav heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shok, heh she sep-wafikh tor sahr-tor maf k' ish-veh, tonk'peh eit'jae k' wehk bezhun-masu ik au would kal-tor ish-veh nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh sa-mekh. Palikauk au klee'fah, tonk'peh she wept fam dvun weht heh weht, heh tevan-tor na' ish-veh ash'ya, till na' kim-shah au consented; tonk'peh wuh moment sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek wuh klashau awoke heh au vesh' taken prisoner va'ashiv. Yi au vesh' katau fa' wuh sa-te'kru, heh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'du dungau worla ma t'nash-veh ko-fu vita svi' ohkuh gad du hil-tor maf wuh kunel ik pehkau wuh zan-tor s' t'nash-veh krani.' i' nash kunel vesh' ni suk' ik wuh bosh panu kupi ri nem-tor ish-veh maf: heh lu au had ar'kada na' stehkuh gad, heh had ovsoh maut pi', wuh fox sarlah heh leralmin-tor. 'ti ne' heh hal-tor tor yuk; i dungi ar'kadan na' du.' heh svi' wuh asal au awoke heh wuh kunel vesh' hal-tor; ni au went merrily tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh var-tor ish-veh ik i' ik ish-veh vesh' snem-tor au bolau mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh princess. Yi wuh sa-te'kru vesh' obliged tor potau ish-veh zhit, heh maf went wuh nu'ri sasu heh wuh princess; heh wuh fox sarlah heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'etek dungi ma ek' rehkuh, wuh princess, wuh jarel, heh wuh kushel.' 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri sasu, 'ik would nam-tor wuh lo'uk vel, tonk'peh uf mokuhlek du contrive ish-veh?' 'kuv du dungi goh shroi, ' leralmin-tor wuh fox, 'ish-veh mokuhlek nam-tor ovsoh. Lu sarlah du tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh au ya'akash na' wuh vaksurik princess, du bolau leralmin, "la' she nam-tor!" yi au dungi nam-tor maut joyful; heh du dungi mount wuh pi-maat-kur jarel ik au nam-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor du, heh shitau si' ish-veh el'ru tor nem-tor trasha t' au; tonk'peh hutau el'ru k' wuh princess kim-shah. Yi abertau ish-veh sahris fi' tor wuh jarel za' du; clap ish-veh spurs tor ish-veh vla, heh ausahr maf u' sahris u' du mokuhlek.' ek' went gas'rak: yi wuh fox leralmin-tor, 'lu sarlah du tor wuh castle wilat wuh kushel nam-tor, i dungi stay k' wuh princess na' wuh svep, heh du dungi fau svi' heh stariben tor wuh sa-te'kru; heh lu gla-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh gas'rak jarel, au dungi katau si' wuh kushel; tonk'peh du bolau hayal-tor fam dvun, heh leralmin ik du aitlun tor glazhau na' ish-veh, tor gla-tor whether ish-veh nam-tor wuh yeht pi-maat-kur kushel; heh lu du prah ish-veh vi' ish-veh el'ru, fau maf.' nash, nuh', pavesh-tor u' wuh fox leralmin-tor; au lesh ska' wuh kushel, wuh princess mounted va'ashiv, heh au fau-tor fi' tor wuh lo'uk lapan. Yi wuh fox sarlah, heh leralmin-tor, 'pray stau me, heh tresahk ska' t'nash-veh patam heh t'nash-veh ash'ya.' tonk'peh wuh nu'ri sasu klee'fah tor tor ish-veh: ni wuh fox leralmin-tor, 'i dungi na' sovek tav mazhiv-kur-tor du rom counsel: beware t' dahkuh vel; ransom kling s' wuh geld-stau-nentu, heh hayal-tor ne' k' wuh vla t' rai pilash.' yi maf au went. 'muhl, ' nahp wuh nu'ri sasu, 'ish-veh nam-tor rai lerash tukh tor potau ik na'shikh.' au fau-tor fi' k' wuh princess, till na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor wuh pi'kahr wilat au had losrak ish-veh dahkuh sa-kai. Heh tra' au puzhu-tor wuh lo'uk ralash heh uproar; heh lu au ya'akash ra vesh' wuh tukh, wuh sutra leralmin-tor, 'dahkuh sasu nam-tor going tor nam-tor geldau.' u' sarlah ish-veh nearer, gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh dahkuh sasu vesh' ish-veh sa-kai, vi had da-tor robbers; ni au leralmin-tor, 'fam yehat au svi' sovek yut nam-tor korsau?' tonk'peh wuh sutra leralmin-tor 'rai, ' vita au would bestow ek' ish-veh donku fi-tor wuh rascals heh mahr-tor ish-veh liberty. Yi au did ri stay tor nah-tor pa' wuh tukh, tonk'peh vlitau ra vesh' ya'akash, heh ish-veh sa-kai vesh' putan-tor abru, heh went fi' k' ish-veh na' ish-veh ha-kel. Heh u' sarlah au tor wuh lapan wilat wuh fox wuh'rak ragel-tor au, ish-veh vesh' ni samuyau heh vaksurik ik wuh dahkuh sa-kai leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne' k' wuh vla t' wuh pilash, heh shom wuh du', tor yokul heh mon.' ni au leralmin-tor, 'ha, ' heh forgot wuh fox's counsel, heh hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh vla t' wuh pilash; heh du' au suspected nothing, sarlah au za', heh threw ish-veh ne' wuh kutra, heh nem-tor wuh princess, wuh jarel, heh wuh kushel, heh went ha-kel tor wuh sa-te'kru ish-veh trensu, heh leralmin-tor. 'ek' nash ma etek skil-tor k' etwel zup.' yi tra' vesh' lo'uk rejoicing tor; tonk'peh wuh jarel would ri yokul, wuh kushel would ri uralau, heh wuh princess wept. Wuh youngest sa-fu tevan-tor tor wuh lanet t' wuh pilash's sar-tak: luckily ish-veh vesh' nearly pseth, tonk'peh ish-veh hinek vesh' siyah pushau, heh wuh kutra vesh' ni menal ik au kupi talal rai yut tor prah si'. Yi wuh hinek fox sarlah wuh'wak weht, heh scolded ish-veh na' ri zahalik ish-veh na'shikh; vathru rai ek'rasah would ma befallen ish-veh: 'wi, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i fam yehat trasha du la', ni ti meskaraya t' t'nash-veh harr heh meskaraya sahris.' yi au seshau ish-veh s' wuh pilash, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, u' au prah fi-tor wuh kutra, 'ish-veh sa-kai ma eku glantau tor stau du, kuv au talal du svi' wuh kingdom.' ni au sai-vel-tor himself u' wuh ri donku-tor sasu, heh sarlah secretly tor wuh sa-te'kru's kelek, heh vesh' scarcely k'svi wuh svep lu wuh jarel began tor yokul, heh wuh kushel tor uralau, heh wuh princess losrak ska' weeping. Yi au went tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh var-tor ish-veh ek' ish-veh sa-kai' roguery; heh au vesh' seized heh taflau, heh au had wuh princess putan-tor tor ish-veh va'ashiv; heh po' wuh sa-te'kru's tevakh au vesh' heir tor ish-veh kingdom. Wuh wu du' po', au went tor lates veh gad svi' wuh lapan, heh wuh hinek fox ragel-tor ish-veh, heh besought ish-veh k' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun tor stau ish-veh, heh tresahk ska' ish-veh patam heh ash'ya. Heh na' kim-shah au did ni, heh svi' wuh moment wuh fox vesh' rubai vi' wuh sasu, heh da-tor si' tor nam-tor wuh sa-kai t' wuh princess, vi had vesh' pakik wuh lo'uk wehk wehk tevun. Hans svi' kunli ein sasu nam-tor pukeshta tor rom kunli: ek' au tor il ar'kadan tor tor sarlah gas'rak--ek' ik tevan-tor tor au nam-tor ni mau nazh-kap--ek' ish-veh kushel nam-tor kushel--ek' ish-veh nop nam-tor trumps--toss au if yut du dungi, au dungi kwon-hau-ov, spo' ri donku-tor puss, alight fi-tor ish-veh mal, heh goh dvun fi' ni mau wuh faster. Wuh panu lau maut kesik ri kwon-hau-ov nah-tor t' au u' au nah-tor t' themselves, tonk'peh ra tun au na' wuh panu? Ra mokuhlek ish-veh fai-tor pa' wuh tukh? Veh t' aifa kunli beings vesh' behsu hans. Stehkuh wu tevun au had ar'kada lerash na' ish-veh trensu. Na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor, 'trensu, t'nash-veh wak nam-tor abru; i bolau hal-tor ha-kel heh gla-tor t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-mekh wuh'wak weht: ni pray vlitau me t'nash-veh wages heh ti'amah.' heh wuh trensu leralmin-tor, 'du ma vesh' wuh faithful heh rom dvinsu, hans, ni ish-veh vlitau dungau nam-tor handsome.' yi au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh vihk t' haul-tukh u' suk' u' ish-veh patam. Hans nem-tor si' ish-veh abru'lik-handkerchief, shitau wuh krus t' haul-tukh vi' ish-veh, threw ish-veh abru' ish-veh tipan, heh jogged ska' fi' ish-veh fau-yut homewards. U' au went lazily fi', dragging veh ash'ya po' wuh'ashiv, wuh sasu sarlah svi' glan, sahr-tor gaily bi' fi' wuh capital jarel. 'ah!' leralmin-tor hans aloud, 'ra wuh tok-ti vel ish-veh nam-tor tor fau fi' horseback! Tra' au hayal-tor u' hagik heh kunli u' kuv au vesh' na' ha-kel, svi' wuh ku-san k' ish-veh yon-shal; au hal-tor tehnat rai kov, korsau ash'el-duf, heh prah fi' au hardly fai-tor uf.' hans did ri stariben ni softly tonk'peh wuh horseman puzhu-tor ish-veh ek', heh leralmin-tor, 'muhl, t'hy'la, po tor du hal-tor fi' ash'ya yi?' 'ah!' leralmin-tor au, 'i ma nash tus tor lesh: tor nam-tor sure ish-veh nam-tor haul-tukh, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ni ras ik i mokuhlek't meskaraya abru t'nash-veh patam, heh du bolau fai-tor ish-veh dash-tor t'nash-veh tipan sadly.' 'ra tor du leralmin t' tor wuh di'kizh?' leralmin-tor wuh horseman. 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du t'nash-veh jarel, heh du dungau mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh haul-tukh; if dungi korsau du wuh lo'uk deal t' trouble svi' carrying such wuh ras tus pa' k' du.' 'k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ' leralmin-tor hans: 'tonk'peh u' du nam-tor ni ves tor me, i bolau var-tor du veh vel--du dungi ma wuh weary task tor bes-tor ik haul-tukh pa' k' du.' however, wuh horseman prah ska', nem-tor wuh haul-tukh, gol-tor hans abru, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh bridle vi' veh el'ru heh wuh wonil-zehl vi' wuh vath, heh leralmin-tor, 'lu du aitlun tor hal-tor maut sahris, smack ish-veh bru-lar loudly teretuhr, heh maf "jip!"' hans vesh' delighted u' au hayal-tor fi' wuh jarel, drew himself abru, shai-wehkovau ish-veh kar-nef, da-tor si' ish-veh gof, treshau ish-veh wonil-zehl, heh fau-tor merrily ska', veh minute whistling wuh merry tvelkau, heh wuh'ashiv uralaun, 'rai tun heh rai sorrow, wuh savas na' wuh morrow! Etek'll abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh nam-tor merry, uralau neigh ne' derry!' po' wuh wak au nahp au dang spo' tor hal-tor wuh pi' faster, ni au smacked ish-veh bru-lar heh maf-tor 'jip!' maf went wuh jarel bosh ausahr; heh fa' hans fai-tor ra au vesh' pa', au vesh' lehm-tor ska', heh ti fi' ish-veh pla' k' wuh fau-yut-vla. Ish-veh jarel would ma sahr-tor ska', kuv wuh shepherd vi vesh' coming k', driving wuh aushfa, had ri pehkau ish-veh. Hans ak sarlah tor himself, heh prah fi-tor ish-veh mal va'ashiv, sadly smertau, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh shepherd, 'nash riding nam-tor rai kha'wal, lu wuh sasu has wuh kunli tor prah fi-tor wuh beast spo' nash ik stumbles heh flings ish-veh ska' u' kuv ish-veh would shaya ish-veh talu. However, i'm ska' i' wuh'wak na' ek': i spo' ish-veh aushfa i' wuh lo'uk deal weh-rom do nash klon beast ik mavau me nash trick, heh has spoiled t'nash-veh buhfik tor-pal, gla-tor du, svi' nash pi'muzh; if, k' wuh k', fnish-tor ri maut spo' wuh nosegay. Veh mokuhlek lates bi' na' veh's el-wak za' ik aushfa--potau rom apc'koik, heh ma thas, butter, heh thuhk, kanok gad, vi' wuh bargain. Ra would i mazhiv-kur-tor ki' such wuh prize!' 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh shepherd, 'kuv du nam-tor ni tishau t' ish-veh, i dungi rubah t'nash-veh aushfa na' ish-veh jarel; i spo' tor tor rom tor t'nash-veh behsu, kauk hi i pak-tor k' ish-veh myself.' 'ovsoh!' leralmin-tor hans, merrily. 'ra wuh thol khaf-spol ik rom sasu has!' nahp au. Yi wuh shepherd spen-tor fi-tor wuh jarel, istau hans heh wuh aushfa rom asal, heh maf au fau-tor. Hans brushed ish-veh tor-pal, psethau ish-veh limuk heh el'ru, shom-tor wuh du', heh yi drove ska' ish-veh aushfa quietly, heh nahp ish-veh bargain wuh maut kunli veh. 'kuv i ma goh wuh krus t' kap (heh i certainly dungau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor kup tor prah ik), i mokuhlek, whenever i spo', yokul t'nash-veh butter heh thuhk k' ish-veh; heh lu i am thirsty i mokuhlek thas t'nash-veh aushfa heh mon wuh thas: heh ra mokuhlek i istaya na' weht?' lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh ha-shal, au halted, ate abru ek' ish-veh kap, heh mazhiv-kur-tor maf ish-veh kim-shah qsu'lit na' wuh makh t' naliveh. Lu au had shom-tor himself au eku ska' va'ashiv, driving ish-veh aushfa na' ish-veh ko-mekh's pi'kahr. Tonk'peh wuh falek grew greater u' ak u' aru sarlah fi', till na' kim-shah, u' au afer-tor himself fi' wuh eik heath ik would nem-tor ish-veh weht do wuh wadan tor tuhs, au began tor nam-tor ni fal heh parched ik ish-veh lahv clave tor wuh kamu t' ish-veh ru'lut. 'i mokuhlek talal wuh bohrau na' nash, ' nahp au; 'i' i dungi thas t'nash-veh aushfa heh quench t'nash-veh mag': ni au tied ish-veh tor wuh stump t' wuh lap, heh meskarau ish-veh leathern taik tor thas vi'; tonk'peh ri wuh eku vesh' tor nam-tor had. Vi would ma nahp ik nash aushfa, if vesh' tor katau ish-veh thas heh butter heh thuhk, vesh' ek' ik wak utterly pseth? Hans had ri nahp t' looking tor ik. Du' au vesh' trying ish-veh kunli svi' milking, heh managing wuh tukh maut clumsily, wuh uneasy beast began tor nah-tor ish-veh maut troublesome; heh na' kim-shah mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh such wuh kick fi' wuh patam u' knocked ish-veh ne'; heh tra' au ti wuh wu du' senseless. Luckily wuh butcher ak sarlah k', driving wuh pig svi' wuh wheelbarrow. 'ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' du, t'nash-veh sasu?' leralmin-tor wuh butcher, u' au gol-tor ish-veh abru. Hans var-tor ish-veh ra had pavesh-tor, uf au vesh' pseth, heh aitlu tor thas ish-veh aushfa, tonk'peh afer-tor wuh aushfa vesh' pseth nuh'. Yi wuh butcher mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh mashek t' ale, taran, 'tra', mon heh uzhau yourself; ish-veh aushfa dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du rai thas: ri tor gla-tor du she nam-tor wuh hinek beast, rom na' nothing tonk'peh wuh slaughter-kelek?' 'alas, alas!' leralmin-tor hans, 'vi would ma nahp ish-veh? Ra wuh mesh tor nem-tor t'nash-veh jarel, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me goh wuh pseth aushfa! Kuv i stau ish-veh, ra dungi she nam-tor rom na'? I fnu-ven aushfa-kahm; ish-veh nam-tor ri sival hiyet na' me. Kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh pig i'--spo' ik thelik gentleman du nam-tor driving bi' na' ish-veh ease--veh kupi tor vel k' ish-veh; ish-veh would na' sovek tav tor kahm.' 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh butcher, 'i ri tor spo' tor leralmin rai, lu veh nam-tor ya'akash tor tor wuh ves, neighbourly vel. Tor sanoi du i dungi rubah, heh mazhiv-kur-tor du t'nash-veh tok-ti thelik pig na' wuh aushfa.' 'sha-ka-ri reward du na' ish-veh kindness heh shal-wafaya!' leralmin-tor hans, u' au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh butcher wuh aushfa; heh taking wuh pig ska' wuh halek-barrow, drove ish-veh maf, holding ish-veh k' wuh string ik vesh' tied tor its mal. Ni fi' au jogged, heh ek' seemed i' tor hal-tor gas'rak k' ish-veh: au had ragel-tor k' ein misfortunes, tor nam-tor sure; tonk'peh au vesh' i' muhl repaid na' ek'. Uf kupi ish-veh nam-tor vathru k' such wuh travelling besu u' au had na' kim-shah prah? Wuh thurai sasu au ragel-tor vesh' wuh countryman carrying wuh tok-ti wan-kur kushel. Wuh countryman pehkau tor ya'akash ra vesh' o'wak-vel; nash pufulag-tor tor further chat; heh hans var-tor ish-veh ek' ish-veh kunli, uf au had ni wehk rom bargains, heh uf ek' wuh panu went sa-ka-ashausu heh smiling k' ish-veh. Wuh countryman yi began tor var-tor ish-veh var, heh leralmin-tor au vesh' going tor nem-tor wuh kushel tor wuh christening. 'olau, ' leralmin-tor au, 'uf ras ish-veh nam-tor, heh wi ish-veh nam-tor goh ohkuh wehk gad hinek. Whoever roasts heh yokul ish-veh dungi talal plenty t' thelik fi-tor ish-veh, ish-veh has ha-tor ni muhl!' 'du're gas'rak, ' leralmin-tor hans, u' au rasathau ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru; 'tonk'peh kuv du variben t' thelik, t'nash-veh pig nam-tor rai trifle.' meantime wuh countryman began tor glazhau shi'vukhut, heh hutau ish-veh patam. 'hark ye!' leralmin-tor au, 't'nash-veh worthy t'hy'la, du seem wuh rom wihfelau t' katravahsu, ni i mokuhlek't gol'nev doing du wuh ves da-tor. Ish-veh pig lau prah du vi' wuh theshau. Svi' wuh pi'kahr i aishan sarlah s', wuh squire has had wuh pig stolen s' ish-veh sty. I vesh' dreadfully kwes lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh du ik du had prah wuh squire's pig. Kuv du ma, heh au kum du, ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh rasahkos job na' du. Wuh least au dungi tor dungi nam-tor tor lehm du vi' wuh jarel-muzh. Mokuhlek du mahal-tor?' ri donku-tor hans vesh' sadly koltha. 'rom sasu, ' maf-tor au, 'pray prah me si' t' nash theshau. I fai-tor nothing t' wilat wuh pig vesh' either bred il pukeshta; tonk'peh au lau ma vesh' wuh squire's na' aught i mokuhlek var-tor: du fai-tor nash shasol weh-rom do i tor, nem-tor t'nash-veh pig heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh kushel.' 'i ought ki' vel vi' wuh bargain, ' leralmin-tor wuh countryman; 'mazhiv-kur-tor wuh thelik kushel na' wuh pig, indeed! 'tis ri kanok-veh would tor ni mau na' du u' ik. However, i dungi ri nam-tor lerash fi-tor du, u' du nam-tor svi' trouble.' yi au nem-tor wuh string svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh drove ska' wuh pig k' wuh vla yut; du' hans went fi' wuh yut homewards elik s' tun. 'po' ek', ' nahp au, 'ik chap nam-tor takov muhl taken svi'. I ri tor tun t'vi pig ish-veh nam-tor, tonk'peh wherever sarlah ish-veh s' ish-veh has vesh' wuh maut rom t'hy'la tor me. I ma mau wuh buhfik t' wuh bargain. Wuh'rak tra' dungi nam-tor wuh capital roast; yi wuh thelik dungi talal me svi' kushel-elmin na' shehkuh tevun-krus; heh yi tra' nam-tor ek' wuh vaksurik wan-kur kan. I dungi shitau au vi' t'nash-veh trak, heh yi i am sure i dungau yuk soundly rik' rocking. Uf kunli t'nash-veh ko-mekh dungi nam-tor! Variben t' wuh pig, indeed! Mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh tok-ti thelik kushel.' u' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh thurai pi'kahr, gla-tor ish-veh wuh scissor-grazhayek k' ish-veh halek, working heh uralaun, 'o'er kunel heh o'er dale ni kunli i roam, ar'kadan ta'hal heh ha-tor muhl, ek' wuh panu nam-tor t'nash-veh ha-kel; yi vi ni blythe, ni merry u' i?' hans lam-tor looking fi' na' wuh du', heh na' kim-shah leralmin-tor, 'du bolau nam-tor muhl ska', trensu grazhayek! Du seem ni kunli na' ish-veh ar'kadan.' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath, 't'nash-veh nam-tor wuh pi-maat-kur trade; wuh rom grazhayek worla shitau ish-veh el'ru vi' ish-veh abru'lik rik' finding donku svi' ish-veh--tonk'peh wilat did du prah ik vaksurik kushel?' 'i did ri mahr-tor ish-veh, i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh pig na' ish-veh.' 'heh wilat did du prah wuh pig?' 'i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh aushfa na' ish-veh.' 'heh wuh aushfa?' 'i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh jarel na' ish-veh.' 'heh wuh jarel?' 'i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh vihk t' haul-tukh u' suk' u' t'nash-veh patam na' ish-veh.' 'heh wuh haul-tukh?' 'oh! I ar'kada lerash na' ik stehkuh wu tevun.' 'du ma thriven muhl svi' wuh panu hitherto, ' leralmin-tor wuh grazhayek, 'i' kuv du kupi talal donku svi' ish-veh abru'lik whenever du shitau ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh, ish-veh fortune would nam-tor tor.' 'maut yeht: tonk'peh uf nam-tor ik tor nam-tor khartau?' 'uf? Po, du bolau da-tor grazhayek spo' myself, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath; 'du goh aitlun wuh grindstone; wuh shom dungi sarlah t' itself. La' nam-tor veh ik nam-tor tonk'peh pi' wuh weh-rasahkos na' sai-vel-tor: i would ri ya'akash weht do wuh tala t' ish-veh kushel na' ish-veh--dungi du mahr-tor?' 'uf mokuhlek du ya'akash?' leralmin-tor hans; 'i dang nam-tor wuh happiest sasu svi' wuh panu, kuv i kupi ma donku whenever i shitau t'nash-veh el'ru svi' t'nash-veh abru'lik: ra sos aitlun weht? Tra''s wuh kushel.' 'i', ' leralmin-tor wuh grazhayek, u' au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh tsuri rough kov ik ti k' ish-veh vla, 'nash nam-tor wuh danik capital kov; tor tonk'peh ar'kadan ish-veh muhl hiyet, heh du mokuhlek tor wuh hinek felu tresahk k' ish-veh.' hans nem-tor wuh kov, heh went ish-veh yut k' wuh ta'hal khaf-spol: ish-veh bezhun sparkled na' mak, heh au leralmin-tor tor himself, 'surely i bolau ma vesh' pukeshta svi' wuh kunli wadan; kanok-vei i kupi aitlun il istaya na' sarlah t' itself. Sutra nam-tor ni ves; au seem really tor nah-tor i tor au wuh favour svi' letting au tor me don-ka, heh giving me rom bargains.' meantime au began tor nam-tor zungor, heh k'avon nuh', na' au had putan-tor maf ish-veh kim-shah qsu'lit svi' ish-veh mak na' getting wuh aushfa. Na' kim-shah au kupi hal-tor rai weh-irak, na' wuh kov zungor ish-veh sadly: heh au zaseshau himself tor wuh vla t' wuh pilash, ik au lau nem-tor wuh mon t' masu, heh shom wuh du'. Ni au laid wuh kov carefully k' ish-veh vla fi' wuh kutra: tonk'peh, u' au stooped ne' tor mon, au forgot ish-veh, kwitau ish-veh wuh pi', heh ne' ish-veh padukau, plump vi' wuh pilash. Na' wuh du' au glantau ish-veh sinking svi' wuh glu pa'shik masu; yi sprang abru heh tam-tor na' mak, heh va'ashiv tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef heh itaren sha-ka-ri, k' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun, na' its kindness svi' taking maf ish-veh goh plague, wuh watosh ras kov. 'uf kunli am i!' maf-tor au; 'kling vesh' ek'wak ni kunli u' i.' yi abru au prah k' wuh ta'hal khaf-spol, elik s' ek' ish-veh troubles, heh lates-tor fi' till au pulau ish-veh ko-mekh's kelek, heh var-tor ish-veh uf maut hagik wuh fau-yut tor rom kunli vesh'. Jorinda heh jorindel tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh hinek castle, ik lam-tor svi' wuh svitan t' wuh glu gloomy lapan, heh svi' wuh castle ha-tor wuh hinek pu'a. I' nash pu'a kupi nem-tor sovek shid she sanoi. Ek' wuh gad wu she flew pa' svi' wuh shid t' wuh owl, il crept pa' wuh shasol spo' wuh aushfa; tonk'peh na' mu-yor she kwon-hau-ov became wuh hinek kosu va'ashiv. Lu sovek nu'ri sasu sarlah k'svi wuh hundred sahr-tor t' ish-veh castle, au became ved teslau, heh kupi ri dvun wuh ash till sarlah ish-veh heh eku ish-veh elik; if she would ri tor till au had putan-tor ish-veh ish-veh zhit worla tor sarlah tra' va'ashiv: tonk'peh lu sovek takov maiden sarlah k'svi ik ret she vesh' rubai vi' wuh kushel, heh wuh pu'a shitau ish-veh vi' wuh kraisek, heh geldau ish-veh abru svi' wuh tvi-shal svi' wuh castle. Tra' vesh' stehkuh hundred t' aifa kraisek hanging svi' wuh castle, heh ek' k' vaksurik kushel svi' au. I' tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh maiden t'vi ahm vesh' jorinda. She vesh' prettier do ek' wuh takov ko-kan ik ek'wak vesh' gla-tor fa', heh wuh shepherd lad, t'vi ahm vesh' jorindel, vesh' maut tishau t' ish-veh, heh au vesh' ak tor nam-tor telik. Veh gad au went tor lates svi' wuh lapan, ik au lau nam-tor sa'awek; heh jorindel leralmin-tor, 'etek bolau nem-tor tun ik etek ri tor hal-tor nuh' be' tor wuh pu'a's castle.' ish-veh vesh' wuh vaksurik khru; wuh kim-shah ha'zehl t' wuh setting yel min-tor ugelik k'fai wuh wu kas-fek t' wuh lap fi-tor wuh yar-kur underwood ne'rak, heh wuh turtle-doves sang s' wuh ha-vol birches. Jorinda hayal-tor ne' tor gaze fi-tor wuh yel; jorindel hayal-tor k' ish-veh vla; heh fi' olau maf, au fai-tor ri po; tonk'peh ish-veh seemed u' kuv au vesh' tor nam-tor parted s' veh wuh'ashiv na' ek'wak. Au had czar-tor wuh wu yut; heh lu au glazhau tor gla-tor if yut au dang hal-tor ha-kel, au afer-tor themselves na' wuh pak tor fai-tor ra yut tor nem-tor. Wuh yel vesh' setting sahris, heh already ulef t' its da-kuv had ne'hal-tor za' wuh kunel: jorindel fi' wuh sudden glazhau za' ish-veh, heh gla-tor k'fai wuh bushes ik au had, rik' fai-tor ish-veh, hayal-tor ne' ikap-tor ne' wuh hinek temok t' wuh castle. Yi au shrank na' pthak, da-tor spoh, heh trembled. Jorinda vesh' aishan uralaun, 'wuh mokov-dove sang s' wuh willow spray, muhl-wuh-gad! Muhl-wuh-gad! Au la'tusa'd na' wuh buk t' ish-veh ashal-veh katelau, muhl-wuh-gad!' lu ish-veh song pehkau suddenly. Jorindel da-tor tor gla-tor wuh utvau, heh beheld ish-veh jorinda rubai vi' wuh nightingale, ni ik ish-veh song shahtau k' wuh mournful mashek, mashek. Wuh owl k' yonalik bezhun flew rehkuh wak pauk au, heh rehkuh wak shei: 'tu whu! Tu whu! Tu whu!' jorindel kupi ri dvun; au lam-tor teslau u' wuh kov, heh kupi neither tusa, il stariben, il stir el'ru il ash'ya. Heh i' wuh yel went ved ne'; wuh gloomy mu-yor sarlah; wuh owl flew vi' wuh bush; heh wuh moment po' wuh hinek pu'a sarlah forth spoh heh meagre, k' staring bezhun, heh wuh han heh chin ik siyah ragel-tor veh wuh'ashiv. She mumbled vel tor herself, seized wuh nightingale, heh went maf k' ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru. Ri donku-tor jorindel gla-tor wuh nightingale vesh' hal-tor--tonk'peh ra kupi au tor? Au kupi ri stariben, au kupi ri dvun s' wuh gla-tor wilat au lam-tor. Na' kim-shah wuh pu'a sarlah pla' heh sang k' wuh hoarse spes: 'till wuh prisoner nam-tor sahris, heh ish-veh doom nam-tor vishizhau, tra' stay! Oh, stay! Lu wuh sem-rik nam-tor pa' ish-veh, heh wuh spell has bound ish-veh, hie maf! Maf!' fi' wuh sudden jorindel afer-tor himself elik. Yi au tevan-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef fa' wuh pu'a, heh prayed ish-veh tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh pla' ish-veh tal-kam jorinda: tonk'peh she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor au dang worla gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv; yi she went ish-veh yut. Au prayed, au wept, au sorrowed, tonk'peh ek' svi' vain. 'alas!' au leralmin-tor, 'ra dungi shetau t' me?' au kupi ri hal-tor pla' tor ish-veh sha' ha-kel, ni au went tor wuh flekh pi'kahr, heh employed himself svi' keeping sheep. Wehk wuh wak did au lates pauk heh pauk u' be' tor wuh fnu-ven castle u' au dared hal-tor, tonk'peh ek' svi' vain; au puzhu-tor il gla-tor nothing t' jorinda. Na' kim-shah au dreamt veh mu-yor ik au afer-tor wuh vaksurik gahv-kur svai, heh ik svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh ti wuh ost'syn pearl; heh au dreamt ik au plucked wuh svai, heh went k' ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru vi' wuh castle, heh ik kanok-vei au estuhl k' ish-veh vesh' disenchanted, heh ik tra' au afer-tor ish-veh jorinda va'ashiv. Svi' wuh asal lu au awoke, au began tor psthan abru' kunel heh dale na' nash takov svai; heh ohkuh wu gad au sought na' ish-veh svi' vain: tonk'peh fi' wuh ninth gad, lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, au afer-tor wuh vaksurik gahv-kur svai; heh svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh vesh' wuh suk asal-masu-thek, u' suk' u' wuh ost'syn pearl. Yi au plucked wuh svai, heh eku si' heh travelled gad heh mu-yor, till sarlah ish-veh va'ashiv tor wuh castle. Au lates-tor nearer do wuh hundred sahr-tor tor ish-veh, heh wi au did ri shetau teslau u' fa', tonk'peh afer-tor ik au kupi hal-tor ved ikap-tor abru tor wuh svep. Jorindel vesh' maut glad indeed tor gla-tor nash. Yi au estuhl wuh svep k' wuh svai, heh ish-veh sprang tu'ash; ni ik au went svi' k'fai wuh kelek, heh shroi lu au puzhu-tor ni wehk kushel uralaun. Na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh pu'a hayal-tor, k' wuh stehkuh hundred kushel uralaun svi' wuh stehkuh hundred kraisek. Lu gla-tor ish-veh jorindel she vesh' maut reshnek, heh shei k' reshan; tonk'peh she kupi ri sarlah k'svi dahkuh ker t' ish-veh, na' wuh svai au meskarau svi' ish-veh el'ru vesh' ish-veh safeguard. Au glazhau pa' na' wuh kushel, tonk'peh alas! Tra' vesh' wehk, wehk nightingales, heh uf yi dang au talal si' if vesh' ish-veh jorinda? Du' au vesh' thinking ra tor tor, gla-tor ish-veh wuh pu'a had taken ne' veh t' wuh kraisek, heh vesh' tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh yut ska' k'fai wuh svep. Au sahr-tor il flew po' ish-veh, estuhl wuh kraisek k' wuh svai, heh jorinda lam-tor fa' ish-veh, heh threw ish-veh kar pauk ish-veh talu looking u' vaksurik u' ek'wak, u' vaksurik u' lu au lates-tor teretuhr svi' wuh lapan. Yi au estuhl ek' wuh vath kushel k' wuh svai, ni ik au ek' nem-tor ish-veh hinek shidau va'ashiv; heh au nem-tor jorinda ha-kel, wilat au vesh' telik, heh ha-tor kunling teretuhr wehk tevun: heh ni did wuh rom wehk vath lads, t'vi maidens had vesh' punekwitau tor uralau svi' wuh hinek pu'a's kraisek k' themselves, mau longer do au tishau. Wuh travelling ralash-tanafsu wuh trau uroshitausu had wuh'wak wuh ass ik had vesh' wuh faithful dvinsu tor ish-veh wuh lo'uk wehk tevun, tonk'peh vesh' i' growing hinek heh kanok gad weht heh weht unfit na' ar'kadan. Ish-veh trensu therefore vesh' zungor t' keeping ish-veh heh began tor nah-tor t' putting wuh shaht tor ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh ass, vi gla-tor ik ein mischief vesh' svi' wuh salan, nem-tor himself slyly ska', heh began ish-veh halovaya na' wuh lo'uk kahr, 'na' tra', ' nahp au, 'i lau da-tor ralash-tanafsu.' po' au had travelled wuh pi' yut, au zama-tor wuh dog lying k' wuh roadside heh panting u' kuv au vesh' zungor. 'ra tor du pant ni, t'nash-veh t'hy'la?' leralmin-tor wuh ass. 'alas!' leralmin-tor wuh dog, 't'nash-veh trensu vesh' going tor knock me fi' wuh patam, fai'ei i am hinek heh kobat, heh mokuhlek rai longer tor myself useful tor ish-veh svi' hunting; ni i sahr-tor maf; tonk'peh ra mokuhlek i tor tor pinkau t'nash-veh livelihood?' 'hark ye!' leralmin-tor wuh ass, 'i am going tor wuh lo'uk kahr tor da-tor ralash-tanafsu: suppose du hal-tor k' me, heh ar'kadan ra du mokuhlek tor svi' wuh ka yut?' wuh dog leralmin-tor au vesh' willing, heh au jogged fi' teretuhr. Au had ri hal-tor irak fa' gla-tor au wuh aushfa sitting svi' wuh svitan t' wuh fau-yut heh tor wuh danik rueful limuk. 'pray, t'nash-veh rom t'sai, ' leralmin-tor wuh ass, 'ra's wuh tukh k' du? Du glazhau ved s' tam'a!' 'ah, me!' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa, 'uf mokuhlek veh nam-tor svi' rom tam'a lu veh's ha'kiv nam-tor svi' tehvar? Fai'ei i am palikaya tor tor'ovau hinek, heh had rather ti na' t'nash-veh ease k' wuh yon do sahr-tor pa' wuh kelek po' wuh aushfa, t'nash-veh mistress laid meskaraya t' me, heh vesh' going tor mastevau me; heh hi i ma vesh' kunli hiyet tor prah maf s' ish-veh, i ri tor fai-tor ra i am tor ha-tor fi-tor.' 'oh, ' leralmin-tor wuh ass, 'k' ek' tvai hal-tor k' etek tor wuh lo'uk kahr; du nam-tor wuh rom mu-yor uralausu, heh lau tor ish-veh fortune u' wuh ralash-tanafsu.' wuh aushfa vesh' sanoi k' wuh nahp, heh hau wuh party. Ak afterwards, u' au vesh' be' dvun-tor k' wuh farmyard, gla-tor au wuh cock perched fi-tor wuh temep, heh screaming si' k' ek' ish-veh lau heh nen. 'bravo!' leralmin-tor wuh ass; 'fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, du tor wuh khinik ralash; pray ra nam-tor ek' nash pa'?' 'po, ' leralmin-tor wuh cock, 'i vesh' aishan i' taran ik etek dang ma tok-ti igen-va na' etwel washing-gad, heh wi t'nash-veh mistress heh wuh fas-tor ri tor itaren me na' t'nash-veh kusut-tor, tonk'peh nan-tor tor tresahk ska' t'nash-veh patam fa-gad, heh tor broth t' me na' wuh be'hai'la ik nam-tor coming fi' gad!' 'sha-ka-ri zadau!' leralmin-tor wuh ass, 'sarlah k' etek trensu chanticleer; ish-veh dungi nam-tor weh-rom, na' sovek tav, do staying la' ki' ish-veh patam tresahk ska'! Isha, vi fai-tor? Kuv etek tun tor uralau svi' tvelkau, etek lau prah abru ein ves t' wuh concert; ni sarlah bi' k' etek.' 'k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ' leralmin-tor wuh cock: ni au ek' kehkuh went fi' jollily teretuhr. Au kupi ri, however, pulau wuh lo'uk kahr wuh wuh'rak gad; ni lu mu-yor sarlah fi', au went vi' wuh lapan tor yuk. Wuh ass heh wuh dog laid themselves ne' ne' wuh lo'uk lap, heh wuh aushfa sasu-tor abru vi' wuh khlup; du' wuh cock, thinking ik wuh higher au hayal-tor wuh safer au dang nam-tor, flew abru tor wuh maut fik t' wuh lap, heh yi, fupa s' ish-veh custom, fa' au went tor yuk, glazhau si' fi' ek' vla t' ish-veh tor gla-tor ik kanok-vei vesh' muhl. Svi' doing nash, gla-tor ish-veh afar ska' vel ugelik heh shining heh calling tor ish-veh besu leralmin-tor, 'tra' bolau nam-tor wuh kelek rai lo'uk yut ska', na' gla-tor nash-veh wuh ta'hal.' 'kuv ik nam-tor wuh nuf, ' leralmin-tor wuh ass, 'etek had weh-rom rubah etwel ha-shal, na' etwel lodging nam-tor ri wuh buhfik svi' wuh panu!' 'isha, ' hau wuh dog, 'i dang ri nam-tor wuh weh-rasahkos na' wuh hinek il dahkuh, il wuh zeshau t' kahm.' ni au lates-tor ska' teretuhr na' wuh gla-tor wilat chanticleer had gla-tor wuh ta'hal, heh u' au drew be' ish-veh became larger heh brighter, till au na' kim-shah sarlah beyik wuh kelek svi' if wuh gang t' robbers ha-tor. Wuh ass, hasu wuh tallest t' wuh apc'koik, marched abru tor wuh krani heh peeped svi'. 'muhl, donkey, ' leralmin-tor chanticleer, 'ra tor gla-tor du?' 'ra tor gla-tor nash-veh?' kilko-tor wuh ass. 'po, gla-tor nash-veh wuh pasu sak-tor k' ek' ves t' rom vel, heh robbers sitting pauk ish-veh tor merry.' 'ik would nam-tor wuh thol lodging na' etek, ' leralmin-tor wuh cock. 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh ass, 'kuv etek kupi goh prah svi''; ni au consulted teretuhr uf au dang contrive tor prah wuh robbers si'; heh na' kim-shah au kwul fi-tor wuh dotor. Wuh ass shitau himself abruvenik fi' ish-veh hind mal, k' ish-veh forefeet resting tehnat wuh krani; wuh dog prah fi-tor ish-veh pla'; wuh aushfa parish-tor abru tor wuh dog's tipan, heh wuh cock flew abru heh hayal-tor fi-tor wuh aushfa's patam. Lu ek' vesh' pok wuh glantokaya vesh' putan-tor, heh au began ish-veh ralash-tanaf. Wuh ass brayed, wuh dog barked, wuh aushfa mewed, heh wuh cock shei; heh yi au ek' shau k'fai wuh krani na' wuh'wak, heh sarlah tumbling vi' wuh tvi-shal, svi' wuh pushau makh, k' wuh danik hideous clatter! Wuh robbers, vi had vesh' ri wuh pi' koltha k' wuh sharu concert, had i' rai vet ik ein frightful hobgoblin had pushau svi' fi-tor au, heh scampered maf u' sahris u' au kupi. Wuh gef wuh'wak pa'shik, etwel travellers ak hayal-tor ne' heh dispatched ra wuh robbers had losrak, k' u' mau eagerness u' kuv au had ri gishu tor yokul va'ashiv na' wuh tevun-krus. U' ak u' au had satisfied themselves, au shitau si' wuh ha'ge, heh tik wuh'wak weht sought si' wuh resting-shi tor ish-veh sha' liking. Wuh donkey laid himself ne' fi-tor wuh tuh t' terp svi' wuh ker, wuh dog sakadau himself fi-tor wuh pev za' wuh svep, wuh aushfa padukau herself abru fi' wuh hearth fa' wuh lamekh vitush, heh wuh cock perched fi-tor wuh ha-zehl fi' wuh fik t' wuh kelek; heh, u' au vesh' ek' rather zungor k' ish-veh halovaya, au ak tevan-tor asleep. Tonk'peh pa' midnight, lu wuh robbers gla-tor s' afar ik wuh ha'ge vesh' si' heh ik ek' seemed hizhuk, au began tor nah-tor ik au had vesh' svi' nuh' lo'uk wuh brax tor sahr-tor maf; heh veh t' au, vi vesh' bolder do wuh shom, went tor gla-tor ra vesh' going fi'. Finding kanok-vei fam dvun, au marched vi' wuh af'tum, heh groped pa' till au afer-tor wuh match svi' zek tor ta'hal wuh ha'fek; heh yi, espying wuh glittering yonalik bezhun t' wuh aushfa, au mistook au na' ha-tor kastik-kov, heh meskarau wuh match tor au tor ta'hal ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh aushfa, ri understanding nash kha'wal, sprang na' ish-veh limuk, heh spat, heh scratched na' ish-veh. Nash koltha ish-veh dreadfully, heh maf au sahr-tor tor wuh pla' svep; tonk'peh tra' wuh dog spen-tor abru heh zeshau ish-veh svi' wuh mal; heh u' au vesh' mes abru' wuh ker wuh ass kicked ish-veh; heh wuh cock, vi had vesh' awakened k' wuh ralash, crowed k' ek' ish-veh lau. Na' nash wuh robber sahr-tor pla' u' sahris u' au kupi tor ish-veh comrades, heh var-tor wuh khart-lan uf wuh horrid witch had prah vi' wuh kelek, heh had spat na' ish-veh heh scratched ish-veh limuk k' ish-veh wu bony ozh; uf wuh sasu k' wuh lipau svi' ish-veh el'ru had ipik himself za' wuh svep, heh stabbed ish-veh svi' wuh mal; uf wuh nesh-kur stislak lam-tor svi' wuh ker heh kwul-tor ish-veh k' wuh muhd, heh uf wuh e'shua had hayal-tor fi-tor wuh fik t' wuh kelek heh lit'dhae, 'lehm wuh rascal abru la'!' po' nash wuh robbers worla dared tor hal-tor pla' tor wuh kelek; tonk'peh wuh ralash-tanafsu vesh' ni sanoi k' ish-veh ha-shal ik au nem-tor abru ish-veh abode tra'; heh tra' au nam-tor, i dare leralmin, na' nash maut gad. Hinek sultan wuh shepherd had wuh faithful dog, puvutau sultan, vi vesh' grown maut hinek, heh had pakik ek' ish-veh zud. Heh veh gad lu wuh shepherd heh ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' standing teretuhr fa' wuh kelek wuh shepherd leralmin-tor, 'i dungi pohshau hinek sultan fa-gad asal, na' au nam-tor t' rai nam-tor-tor i'.' tonk'peh ish-veh ko-telsu leralmin-tor, 'pray kal-tor wuh ri donku-tor faithful creature ha-tor; au has dvin-tor etek muhl wuh lo'uk wehk tevun, heh etek ought tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh livelihood na' wuh shom t' ish-veh gad.' 'tonk'peh ra mokuhlek etek tor k' ish-veh?' leralmin-tor wuh shepherd, 'au has ri wuh zud svi' ish-veh patam, heh wuh pi'tak ri tor palutunau ish-veh na' ek'; tor nam-tor sure au has dvin-tor etek, tonk'peh yi au did ish-veh tor pinkau ish-veh livelihood; fa-gad dungau nam-tor ish-veh kim-shah gad, nerau fi-tor ish-veh.' ri donku-tor sultan, vi vesh' lying beyik au, puzhu-tor ek' ik wuh shepherd heh ish-veh ko-telsu leralmin-tor tor veh wuh'ashiv, heh vesh' maut mau koltha tor nah-tor fa-gad would nam-tor ish-veh kim-shah gad; ni svi' wuh khru au went tor ish-veh rom t'hy'la wuh wolf, vi ha-tor svi' wuh lapan, heh var-tor ish-veh ek' ish-veh sorrows, heh uf ish-veh trensu tvai tor stau ish-veh svi' wuh asal. 'tor yourself hagik, ' leralmin-tor wuh wolf, 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du ein rom na'shikh. Ish-veh trensu, du fai-tor, hal-tor si' kanok asal maut lehkuh-mal k' ish-veh ko-telsu vi' wuh vunai; heh au nem-tor ish-veh pi' kan k' au, heh ti ish-veh ne' za' wuh labah svi' wuh duvek du' au nam-tor na' ar'kadan. I' tor du ti ne' beyik wuh kan, heh pretend tor nam-tor watching ish-veh, heh dungi-sarlah nash-veh s' wuh lapan heh sahr-tor maf k' ish-veh; du bolau sahr-tor po' me u' sahris u' du mokuhlek, heh i dungi kal-tor ish-veh eku; yi du lau lesh ish-veh pla', heh au dungi nah-tor du ma korsau ish-veh kan, heh dungi nam-tor ni itar-bosh tor du ik au dungi nem-tor tun t' du u' wu u' du ha-tor.' wuh dog tishau nash dotor maut muhl; heh accordingly ni ish-veh vesh' khartau. Wuh wolf sahr-tor k' wuh kan wuh pi' yut; wuh shepherd heh ish-veh ko-telsu shei si'; tonk'peh sultan ak overtook ish-veh, heh lesh wuh ri donku-tor pi' vel pla' tor ish-veh trensu heh mistress. Yi wuh shepherd patted ish-veh fi' wuh patam, heh leralmin-tor, 'hinek sultan has korsau etwel kan s' wuh wolf, heh therefore au dungau ha-tor heh nam-tor muhl taken tun t', heh ma plenty tor yokul. Ko-telsu, hal-tor ha-kel, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh rom aru-yem, heh kal-tor ish-veh ma t'nash-veh hinek an'kar tor yuk fi' u' wu u' au ha-tor.' ni s' nash wak fa'rak sultan had ek' ik au kupi istaya na'. Ak afterwards wuh wolf sarlah heh istau ish-veh mak, heh leralmin-tor, 'i', t'nash-veh rom katravahsu, du bolau var-tor rai var, tonk'peh da-tor ish-veh patam wuh vath yut lu i aitlun tor zahvan veh t' wuh hinek shepherd's tok-ti thelik sheep.' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh sultan; 'i dungi nam-tor yeht tor t'nash-veh trensu.' however, wuh wolf nahp au vesh' svi' kha'wal, heh sarlah veh mu-yor tor prah wuh dainty morsel. Tonk'peh sultan had var-tor ish-veh trensu ra wuh wolf tvai tor tor; ni au laid bek-tor na' ish-veh za' wuh aushfa-kel svep, heh lu wuh wolf vesh' toranik looking si' na' wuh rom thelik sheep, au had wuh stout cudgel laid pa' ish-veh pla', ik dref-tor ish-veh klachek na' ish-veh finely. Yi wuh wolf vesh' maut reshnek, heh puvutau sultan 'wuh hinek rogue, ' heh swore au would ma ish-veh revenge. Ni wuh thurai asal wuh wolf satau wuh boar tor kali-fi sultan tor sarlah vi' wuh lapan tor puk wuh tukh. I' sultan had kling au kupi ya'akash tor nam-tor ish-veh dahr tonk'peh wuh shepherd's hinek rehkuh-legged aushfa; ni au nem-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh, heh u' wuh ri donku-tor vel limped bi' k' ein trouble, she terpau abru ish-veh harr zehik svi' wuh sov. Wuh wolf heh wuh kwai boar vesh' wuh'rak fi' wuh solektra; heh lu au espied ish-veh nemut coming, heh gla-tor wuh aushfa's wu-harr standing zehik svi' wuh sov, au nahp she vesh' carrying wuh shek na' sultan tor puk k'; heh kanok wak she limped, au nahp she vesh' picking abru wuh kov tor lehm na' au; ni au leralmin-tor au dang ri spo' nash yut t' fighting, heh wuh boar ti ne' za' wuh bush, heh wuh wolf spen-tor abru vi' wuh lap. Sultan heh wuh aushfa ak sarlah abru, heh glazhau pa' heh wondered ik kling vesh' tra'. Wuh boar, however, had ri ved ipik himself, na' ish-veh kaluk terpau s' wuh bush; heh lu au hutau veh t' au wuh pi', wuh aushfa, seeing vel dvun, heh thinking ish-veh vesh' wuh aushfa, sprang fi-tor ish-veh, heh zeshau heh scratched ish-veh, ni ik wuh boar spen-tor abru heh grunted, heh sahr-tor maf, roaring si', 'glazhau abru svi' wuh lap, tra' hayal-tor wuh veh vi nam-tor tor tenai.' ni au glazhau abru, heh espied wuh wolf sitting svi' wuh khlup; heh au puvutau ish-veh wuh cowardly rascal, heh would ri dash ish-veh tor sarlah ne' till au vesh' heartily kafusik t' himself, heh had ugau tor nam-tor rom t'hylara va'ashiv k' hinek sultan. Wuh terp, wuh kastik-kov, heh wuh bean svi' wuh pi'kahr dwelt wuh ri donku-tor hinek kosu, vi had hoknau teretuhr wuh dish t' beans heh aitlu tor fas-tor au. Ni she tor wuh yon fi' ish-veh hearth, heh ik ish-veh lau yontau wuh quicker, she lighted ish-veh k' wuh handful t' terp. Lu she vesh' emptying wuh beans vi' wuh sunil, veh eku-tor rik' ish-veh observing ish-veh, heh ti fi' wuh solektra be' wuh terp, heh ak afterwards wuh yontau kastik-kov s' wuh yon leapt ne' tor wuh dahkuh. Yi wuh terp began heh leralmin-tor: 'tal-kam t'hylara, s' whence tor sarlah du la'?' wuh kastik-kov kilko-tor: 'i fortunately sprang s' wuh yon, heh kuv i had ri stron-tor k' sheer nekwitaya, t'nash-veh tevakh would ma vesh' ac'ruth, --i dang ma vesh' yontau tor vitush.' wuh bean leralmin-tor: 'i nuh' ma stron-tor k' wuh bosh wadi, tonk'peh kuv wuh hinek kosu had prah me vi' wuh sunil, i dang ma vesh' tor vi' broth rik' sovek mercy, spo' t'nash-veh comrades.' 'heh would wuh weh-rom buk ma tevan-tor tor t'nash-veh lot?' leralmin-tor wuh terp. 'wuh hinek kosu has vashau ek' t'nash-veh brethren svi' yon heh vuzh; she seized sheh-leh t' au na' wuh'wak, heh nem-tor ish-veh ha-tor. I luckily trel-tor k'fai ish-veh ozh.' 'tonk'peh ra nam-tor etek tor tor i'?' leralmin-tor wuh kastik-kov. 'i nah-tor, ' kilko-tor wuh bean, 'ik u' etek ma ni fortunately stron-tor tevakh, etek dang potau teretuhr spo' rom besu, heh lest wuh uzh mischance dang overtake etek la', etek dang hal-tor maf teretuhr, heh teslau tor wuh k'shatri shasol.' wuh proposition sanoi wuh dahkuh vath, heh au eku si' fi' ish-veh yut teretuhr. Ak, however, sarlah au tor wuh pi' brook, heh u' tra' vesh' rai mesut il ash'ya-plank, au did ri fai-tor uf au vesh' tor prah abru' ish-veh. Wuh terp kwul fi' wuh rom idea, heh leralmin-tor: 'i dungi ti myself zehik mes', heh yi du mokuhlek lates abru' fi' me u' fi' wuh mesut.' wuh terp therefore sakadau itself s' veh kutra tor wuh vath, heh wuh kastik-kov, vi vesh' t' wuh impetuous disposition, hal-tor ved boldly fi' tor wuh newly-torvau mesut. Tonk'peh lu she had pulau wuh svitan, heh puzhu-tor wuh masu rushing ne'rak ish-veh, she vesh' po' ek', kwes, heh lam-tor fam dvun, heh ventured rai weh-irak. Wuh terp, however, began tor yontau, shau svi' dahkuh krus, heh tevan-tor vi' wuh pilash. Wuh kastik-kov trel-tor po' ish-veh, shisau lu she prah vi' wuh masu, heh breathed ish-veh kim-shah. Wuh bean, vi had prudently hafau fi' wuh gef, kupi ri tonk'peh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh pavek, vesh' unable tor pehkaya, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor ni heartily ik she thorau. Ish-veh would ma vesh' ek' abru' k' ish-veh, likewise, kuv, k' rom fortune, wuh ogsu vi vesh' travelling svi' psthan t' ar'kadan, had ri hayal-tor ne' tor shom k' wuh brook. U' au had wuh compassionate khaf-spol au seshau si' ish-veh og-lum heh og-elakh, heh og-tor ish-veh teretuhr. Wuh bean itaren ish-veh danik prettily, tonk'peh u' wuh ogsu nam-tor-tor nesh-kur og-elakh, ek' beans opi' yi ma wuh nesh-kur fenul. Briar she-tor wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak reigned svi' wuh shasol wuh lo'uk yut ska', wilat tra' vesh' svi' eifa gad pu'a. I' nash sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru had plenty t' donku, heh plenty t' tok-ti sai-vel sai-vel-tor, heh plenty t' rom vel tor yokul heh mon, heh wuh coach tor fau si' svi' kanok gad: tonk'peh hi au had vesh' telik wehk tevun au had rai kanu, heh nash grieved au maut mau indeed. Tonk'peh veh gad u' wuh ko-te'kru vesh' walking k' wuh vla t' wuh pilash, na' wuh lanet t' wuh bah-ker, gla-tor ish-veh wuh ri donku-tor pi' aluk, ik had lehm-tor itself s' wuh masu, heh ti gasping heh nearly tevik fi' wuh kutra. Yi wuh ko-te'kru nem-tor pity fi' wuh pi' aluk, heh threw ish-veh pla' va'ashiv vi' wuh pilash; heh fa' ish-veh swam maf ish-veh abertau its patam s' wuh masu heh leralmin-tor, 'i fai-tor ra ish-veh istaya nam-tor, heh ish-veh dungau nam-tor fulfilled, svi' fun na' ish-veh kindness tor me--du dungi ak ma wuh ko-fu.' ra wuh pi' aluk had fa-ariben ak sarlah tor be' dvun; heh wuh ko-te'kru had wuh pi' ko-kan, ni maut vaksurik ik wuh sa-te'kru kupi ri cease looking fi' ish-veh na' mak, heh leralmin-tor au would meskaraya wuh lo'uk gadzhak heh tor merry, heh gluvaya wuh kan tor ek' wuh solektra. Ni au ya'akash ish-veh kinsmen, heh thol, heh t'hylara, heh behsu. Tonk'peh wuh ko-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'i dungi ma wuh pu'a isha, ik au lau nam-tor ves heh rom tor etwel pi' ko-fu.' i' tra' vesh' leh-reh pu'a svi' wuh kingdom; tonk'peh u' wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru had goh leh-dah pi-maat-kur dishes na' au tor yokul s', au vesh' punekwitau tor trasha veh t' wuh pu'a rik' asking ish-veh. Ni leh-dah pu'a sarlah, tik k' wuh pid yon-kur taik fi' ish-veh patam, heh yon-kur ash'el k' pid timut fi' ish-veh ash'ya, heh wuh wu wan-kur wand svi' ish-veh el'ru: heh po' wuh gadzhak vesh' abru' au hoknau pauk svi' wuh mokov heh mazhiv-kur-tor ek' ish-veh buhfik mazhiv-kur tor wuh pi' princess. Veh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh goodness, wuh'ashiv vaksur, wuh'ashiv don-tak, heh ni fi' till she had ek' ik vesh' rom svi' wuh panu. Aishan u' leh-wun t' au had ovsoh kudaya ish-veh, wuh lo'uk ralash vesh' puzhu-tor svi' wuh courtyard, heh zhit vesh' katau ik wuh thirteenth pu'a vesh' sarlah, k' wuh nesh-kur taik fi' ish-veh patam, heh nesh-kur ash'el fi' ish-veh ash'ya, heh wuh broomstick svi' ish-veh el'ru: heh presently abru sarlah ish-veh vi' wuh dining-tvur. I', u' she had ri vesh' ya'akash tor wuh gadzhak she vesh' maut reshnek, heh scolded wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru maut mau, heh eku tor ar'kadan tor nem-tor ish-veh revenge. Ni she lit'dhae, 'wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu dungau, svi' ish-veh fifteenth tevun, nam-tor wounded k' wuh magu, heh tevan ne' tevik.' yi wuh twelfth t' wuh friendly pu'a, vi had ri wi putan-tor ish-veh mazhiv-kur, sarlah fa'rak, heh leralmin-tor ik wuh ek'rasah istaya bolau nam-tor fulfilled, tonk'peh ik she kupi soften its mischief; ni ish-veh mazhiv-kur vesh', ik wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, lu wuh magu wounded ish-veh, dang ri really tev-tor, tonk'peh dang goh tevan asleep na' wuh hundred tevun. However, wuh sa-te'kru rok-tor fam dvun tor korsau ish-veh tal-kam kan altogether s' wuh threatened ek'rasah; ni au ordered ik ek' wuh magu svi' wuh kingdom dang nam-tor bought abru heh yontau. Tonk'peh ek' wuh mazhiv-kur t' wuh wuh'rak leh-wun pu'a vesh' svi' wuh meantime fulfilled; na' wuh princess vesh' ni vaksurik, heh muhl behaved, heh rom, heh kau-bosh, ik kanok-veh vi fai-tor ish-veh ashau ish-veh. Ish-veh pavesh-tor ik, fi' wuh maut gad she vesh' leh-kau tevun hinek, wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru vesh' ri na' ha-kel, heh she vesh' losrak sa'awek svi' wuh palace. Ni she roved pa' k' herself, heh glazhau na' ek' wuh tvi-shal heh tvi-shal, till na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor wuh hinek kispek, tor if tra' vesh' wuh wonil staircase shahtan k' wuh pi' svep. Svi' wuh svep tra' vesh' wuh pi-maat-kur tal-muv, heh lu she da-tor ish-veh wuh svep sprang tu'ash, heh tra' hayal-tor wuh hinek t'sai spinning maf maut busily. 'po, uf i', rom ko-mekh, ' leralmin-tor wuh princess; 'ra nam-tor du doing tra'?' 'spinning, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek t'sai, heh nodded ish-veh patam, humming wuh tvelkau, du' buzz! Went wuh halek. 'uf prettily ik pi' vel da-tor pauk!' leralmin-tor wuh princess, heh nem-tor wuh magu heh began tor ar'kadan heh padan. Tonk'peh scarcely had she estuhl ish-veh, fa' wuh pu'a's prophecy vesh' fulfilled; wuh magu wounded ish-veh, heh she tevan-tor ne' lifeless fi' wuh solektra. However, she vesh' ri tevik, tonk'peh had goh tevan-tor vi' wuh glu yuk; heh wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh ko-te'kru, vi had aishan sarlah ha-kel, heh ek' ish-veh kelek, tevan-tor asleep nuh'; heh wuh jarel yuk-tor svi' wuh stables, heh wuh dogs svi' wuh kelek, wuh pigeons fi' wuh kelek-fik, heh wuh maut hash-tor yuk-tor fi-tor wuh temok. Kauk wuh yon fi' wuh hearth losrak ska' blazing, heh went tor yuk; wuh jack pehkau, heh wuh spit ik vesh' turning pa' k' wuh kushel fi-tor ish-veh na' wuh sa-te'kru's aru-yem lam-tor fam dvun; heh wuh fas-tor, vi vesh' na' ik moment pulling wuh af'tum-sa-kan k' wuh isachya tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh natuhn fi' wuh kaluk na' vel au had ovsoh amiss, kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, heh fi' tevan-tor asleep; wuh butler, vi vesh' slyly tasting wuh ale, tevan-tor asleep k' wuh mashek na' ish-veh bru-lar: heh thus kanok-vei lam-tor fam dvun, heh yuk-tor soundly. Wuh suk labah t' thorns ak grew pauk wuh palace, heh kanok tevun ish-veh became higher heh thicker; till na' kim-shah wuh hinek palace vesh' vikuvau heh ipik, ni ik ri kauk wuh kamu il wuh vuzh-mev kupi nam-tor gla-tor. Tonk'peh tra' went wuh report k'fai ek' wuh solektra t' wuh vaksurik sleeping briar she-tor (na' ni wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu vesh' puvutau): ni ik, s' wak tor wak, several sa-te'kru' sa-fu sarlah, heh ar'kada tor shaya k'fai wuh pi'laptra vi' wuh palace. Nash, however, rim t' au kupi ek'wak tor; na' wuh thorns heh bushes laid meskaraya t' au, u' ish-veh vesh' k' el'ru; heh tra' au terpau sahris, heh tev-tor wretchedly. Po' wehk, wehk tevun tra' sarlah wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu vi' ik solektra: heh wuh hinek sasu var-tor ish-veh wuh var t' wuh pi'laptra t' thorns; heh uf wuh vaksurik palace lam-tor za' ish-veh, heh uf wuh wonderful princess, puvutau briar she-tor, ti svi' ish-veh asleep, k' ek' ish-veh kelek. Au var-tor, nuh', uf au had puzhu-tor s' ish-veh sa'mekh'al ik wehk, wehk princes had sarlah, heh had ar'kada tor shaya k'fai wuh pi'laptra, tonk'peh ik au had ek' terpau sahris svi' ish-veh, heh tev-tor. Yi wuh nu'ri prince leralmin-tor, 'ek' nash dungau ri koltha me; i dungi hal-tor heh gla-tor nash briar she-tor.' wuh hinek sasu ar'kada tor hinder ish-veh, tonk'peh au vesh' keh'sei fi-tor going. I' ik maut gad wuh hundred tevun vesh' shahtau; heh u' wuh prince sarlah tor wuh pi'laptra gla-tor ish-veh nothing tonk'peh vaksurik flowering labah, k'fai if au went k' ease, heh au ikap-tor svi' po' ish-veh u' bali u' ek'wak. Yi sarlah ish-veh na' kim-shah tor wuh palace, heh tra' svi' wuh kelek ti wuh dogs asleep; heh wuh jarel vesh' standing svi' wuh stables; heh fi' wuh kamu hayal-tor wuh pigeons sahris asleep, k' ish-veh patam ne' ish-veh rala. Heh lu au sarlah vi' wuh palace, wuh hash-tor vesh' sleeping fi' wuh temok; wuh spit vesh' standing fam dvun; wuh butler had wuh mashek t' ale na' ish-veh bru-lar, going tor mon wuh draught; wuh maid hayal-tor k' wuh kushel svi' ish-veh lap pok tor nam-tor plucked; heh wuh fas-tor svi' wuh af'tum vesh' fam dvun holding abru ish-veh el'ru, u' kuv she vesh' going tor kuhsh-tor wuh sa-kan. Yi au went fi' fam dvun weh-irak, heh ek' vesh' ni fam dvun ik au kupi zhu-tor kanok esh au drew; till na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor wuh hinek kispek, heh tu'ash wuh svep t' wuh pi' tvi-shal svi' if briar she-tor vesh'; heh tra' she ti, sahris asleep fi' wuh ku-san k' wuh krani. She glazhau ni vaksurik ik au kupi ri nem-tor ish-veh bezhun ska' ish-veh, ni au stooped ne' heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shok. Tonk'peh wuh moment au shok-tor ish-veh she tu'ash ish-veh bezhun heh awoke, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi-tor ish-veh; heh au went si' teretuhr; heh ak wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru isha awoke, heh ek' wuh kelek, heh gazed fi' tik vath k' lo'uk wonder. Heh wuh jarel hutau themselves, heh wuh dogs spen-tor abru heh barked; wuh pigeons nem-tor ish-veh patam s' ne' ish-veh rala, heh glazhau pa' heh flew vi' wuh vunai; wuh hash-tor fi' wuh temok buzzed va'ashiv; wuh yon svi' wuh af'tum blazed abru; pauk went wuh jack, heh pauk went wuh spit, k' wuh kushel na' wuh sa-te'kru's aru-yem fi-tor ish-veh; wuh butler shahtau ish-veh draught t' ale; wuh maid went fi' plucking wuh kushel; heh wuh fas-tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sa-kan wuh natuhn fi' ish-veh kaluk. Heh yi wuh prince heh briar she-tor vesh' telik, heh wuh wedding gadzhak vesh' putan-tor; heh au ha-tor kunling teretuhr ek' ish-veh ha-tor wu. Wuh dog heh wuh sparrow wuh shepherd's dog had wuh trensu vi nem-tor rai tun t' ish-veh, tonk'peh k'ashiv kal-tor ish-veh dash wuh greatest avon. Na' kim-shah au kupi lesh ish-veh rai longer; ni au nem-tor tor ish-veh timut, heh ska' au sahr-tor svi' wuh maut maf heh sorrowful mood. Fi' wuh fau-yut au ragel-tor wuh sparrow ik leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'po nam-tor du ni maf, t'nash-veh t'hy'la?' 'fai'ei, ' leralmin-tor wuh dog, 'i am maut maut k'avon, heh ma nothing tor yokul.' 'kuv ik nam-tor ek', ' kilko-tor wuh sparrow, 'sarlah k' me vi' wuh thurai kahr, heh i dungi ak talal du plenty t' yem-tukh.' ni fi' au went teretuhr vi' wuh kahr: heh u' au be' dvun-tor k' wuh butcher's mahr-kel, wuh sparrow leralmin-tor tor wuh dog, 'lamok tra' wuh pi' du' till i peck du ne' wuh krus t' kahm.' ni wuh sparrow perched fi-tor wuh nef: heh having wuh'rak glazhau carefully pa' ish-veh tor gla-tor kuv sovek-veh vesh' watching ish-veh, she pecked heh scratched na' wuh steak ik ti fi-tor wuh rihk t' wuh nef, till na' kim-shah ne' ish-veh tevan-tor. Yi wuh dog snapped ish-veh abru, heh parish-tor maf k' ish-veh vi' wuh teruk, wilat au ak ate ish-veh ek' abru. 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh sparrow, 'du dungau ma ein weht kuv du dungi; ni sarlah k' me tor wuh thurai mahr-kel, heh i dungi peck du ne' wuh'ashiv steak.' lu wuh dog had yokul nash nuh', wuh sparrow leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'muhl, t'nash-veh rom t'hy'la, ma du had hiyet i'?' 'i ma had plenty t' kahm, ' kilko-tor au, 'tonk'peh i dang spo' ki' wuh krus t' kap tor yokul po' ish-veh.' 'sarlah k' me yi, ' leralmin-tor wuh sparrow, 'heh du dungau ak ma ik nuh'.' ni she nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh leipausu's mahr-kel, heh pecked na' dahkuh padukau ik ti svi' wuh krani, till au tevan-tor ne': heh u' wuh dog fam dvun istau na' weht, she nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh'ashiv mahr-kel heh pecked ne' ein weht na' ish-veh. Lu ik vesh' yokul, wuh sparrow ya'akash ish-veh whether au had had hiyet i'. 'ha, ' leralmin-tor au; 'heh i' kal-tor etek nem-tor wuh lates wuh pi' yut s' wuh kahr.' ni au fi' went si' fi-tor wuh pid fau-yut; tonk'peh u' wuh igen-va vesh' lamekh, au had ri hal-tor irak fa' wuh dog leralmin-tor, 'i am maut mau zungor--i dang spo' tor nem-tor wuh nap.' 'maut muhl, ' kilko-tor wuh sparrow, 'tor ni, heh svi' wuh meantime i dungi perch fi-tor ik bush.' ni wuh dog sakadau himself si' fi' wuh fau-yut, heh tevan-tor sahris asleep. Whilst au yuk-tor, tra' sarlah k' wuh carter k' wuh hal drawn k' rehkuh jarel, heh putush-tor k' dahkuh casks t' wine. Wuh sparrow, seeing ik wuh carter did ri da-tor s' wuh yut, tonk'peh would hal-tor fi' svi' wuh yut svi' if wuh dog ti, ni u' tor yetur abru' ish-veh, puvutau si', 'pehkaya! Pehkaya! Mr carter, il ish-veh dungau nam-tor wuh weh-rasahkos na' du.' tonk'peh wuh carter, grumbling tor himself, 'du tor ish-veh wuh weh-rasahkos na' me, indeed! Ra mokuhlek du tor?' treshau ish-veh wonil-zehl, heh drove ish-veh hal abru' wuh ri donku-tor dog, ni ik wuh halek plesh-tor ish-veh tor tevakh. 'tra', ' maf-tor wuh sparrow, 'thou pi-maat'rer villain, thou hast pustau t'nash-veh t'hy'la wuh dog. I' kashek ra i leralmin. Nash deed t' thine dungau kodona thee ek' thou tanaf don.' 'tor ish-veh rasahkos, heh welcome, ' leralmin-tor wuh brute, 'ra klau mokuhlek du tor me?' heh be' dvun-tor fi'. Tonk'peh wuh sparrow crept ne' wuh ayaya t' wuh hal, heh pecked na' wuh bung t' veh t' wuh casks till she loosened ish-veh; heh yi ek' wuh wine sahr-tor si', rik' wuh carter seeing ish-veh. Na' kim-shah au glazhau pauk, heh gla-tor ik wuh hal vesh' dripping, heh wuh cask ved herbosh. 'ra wuh unlucky wretch i am!' maf-tor au. 'ri wretch hiyet wi!' leralmin-tor wuh sparrow, u' she alighted fi-tor wuh patam t' veh t' wuh jarel, heh pecked na' ish-veh till au reared abru heh kicked. Lu wuh carter gla-tor nash, au drew si' ish-veh hatchet heh mokh-tor wuh salur na' wuh sparrow, meaning tor stau ish-veh; tonk'peh she flew maf, heh wuh salur tevan-tor fi-tor wuh ri donku-tor jarel's patam k' such nekwitaya, ik au tevan-tor ne' tevik. 'unlucky wretch ik i am!' maf-tor au. 'ri wretch hiyet wi!' leralmin-tor wuh sparrow. Heh u' wuh carter went fi' k' wuh vath dahkuh jarel, she va'ashiv crept ne' wuh ayaya t' wuh hal, heh pecked si' wuh bung t' wuh dahr cask, ni ik ek' wuh wine sahr-tor si'. Lu wuh carter gla-tor nash, au va'ashiv lit'dhae, 'miserable wretch ik i am!' tonk'peh wuh sparrow kilko-tor, 'ri wretch hiyet wi!' heh perched fi' wuh patam t' wuh dahr jarel, heh pecked na' ish-veh nuh'. Wuh carter sahr-tor abru heh kwul-tor na' ish-veh va'ashiv k' ish-veh hatchet; tonk'peh maf she flew, heh wuh salur tevan-tor fi-tor wuh dahr jarel heh pustau ish-veh fi' wuh gla-tor. 'unlucky wretch ik i am!' leralmin-tor au. 'ri wretch hiyet wi!' leralmin-tor wuh sparrow; heh perching fi-tor wuh wuh jarel, she began tor peck ish-veh nuh'. Wuh carter vesh' mad k' fury; heh rik' looking pa' ish-veh, il caring ra au vesh' pa', kwul-tor va'ashiv na' wuh sparrow; tonk'peh pustau ish-veh wuh jarel u' au ovsoh wuh vath dahkuh. 'alas! Miserable wretch ik i am!' maf-tor au. 'ri wretch hiyet wi!' kilko-tor wuh sparrow u' she flew maf; 'i' dungi i plague heh taflau thee na' thy sha' kelek.' wuh carter vesh' punekwitau na' kim-shah tor trasha ish-veh hal za' ish-veh, heh tor hal-tor ha-kel overflowing k' reshan heh vexation. 'alas!' leralmin-tor au tor ish-veh ko-telsu, 'ra has-bosh kunli has befallen me!--t'nash-veh wine nam-tor ek' spilt, heh t'nash-veh jarel ek' rehkuh tevik.' 'alas! Sa-telsu, ' kilko-tor she, 'heh wuh wicked kushel has sarlah vi' wuh kelek, heh has katau k' ish-veh ek' wuh kushel svi' wuh panu, i am sure, heh au ma tevan-tor fi-tor etwel corn svi' wuh loft, heh nam-tor eating ish-veh abru na' such wuh tav!' maf sahr-tor wuh sa-telsu upstairs, heh gla-tor thousands t' kushel sitting fi-tor wuh lan-tol eating abru ish-veh corn, k' wuh sparrow svi' wuh midst t' au. 'unlucky wretch ik i am!' maf-tor wuh carter; na' gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh corn vesh' siyah ek' hal-tor. 'ri wretch hiyet wi!' leralmin-tor wuh sparrow; 'thy cruelty dungau kodona thee thy ha'kiv wi!' heh maf she flew. Wuh carter seeing ik au had thus pakik ek' ik au had, went ne' vi' ish-veh af'tum; heh vesh' fam dvun ri sorry na' ra au had ovsoh, tonk'peh hayal-tor himself angrily heh sulkily svi' wuh vuzh-mev teruk. Tonk'peh wuh sparrow hayal-tor fi' wuh si' wuh krani, heh maf-tor 'carter! Thy cruelty dungau kodona thee thy ha'kiv!' k' ik au spen-tor abru svi' wuh reshan, seized ish-veh hatchet, heh threw ish-veh na' wuh sparrow; tonk'peh ish-veh din-tor ish-veh, heh goh shau wuh krani. Wuh sparrow i' spen-tor svi', perched fi-tor wuh krani-ku-san, heh maf-tor, 'carter! Ish-veh dungau kodona thee thy ha'kiv!' yi au became mad heh glan-fam k' reshan, heh kwul-tor wuh krani-ku-san k' such nekwitaya ik au thresh ish-veh svi' dahkuh: heh u' wuh sparrow flew s' shi tor shi, wuh carter heh ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' ni furious, ik au shau ek' ish-veh furniture, bezhun-zaneshu, ku-san, wu-ku-san, wuh pasu, heh na' kim-shah wuh temok, rik' touching wuh kushel na' ek'. Svi' wuh shaht, however, au kum-tor ish-veh: heh wuh ko-telsu leralmin-tor, 'dungau i stau ish-veh na' wuh'wak?' 'rai, ' maf-tor au, 'ik nam-tor letting ish-veh ska' nuh' easily: she dungau tev-tor wuh mau weht pi-maat'rer tevakh; i dungi yokul ish-veh.' tonk'peh wuh sparrow began tor nuv pa', heh sakadaya si' ish-veh talu heh maf-tor, 'carter! Ish-veh dungau kodona thee thy ha'kiv wi!' k' ik au kupi bek-tor rai longer: ni au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ko-telsu wuh hatchet, heh maf-tor, 'ko-telsu, kwul na' wuh kushel heh stau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh el'ru.' heh wuh ko-telsu kwul-tor; tonk'peh she din-tor ish-veh mokh, heh kwul ish-veh sa-telsu fi' wuh patam ni ik au tevan-tor ne' tevik, heh wuh sparrow flew quietly ha-kel tor ish-veh ha-kel. Wuh leh-dah taman princesses tra' vesh' wuh sa-te'kru vi had leh-dah vaksurik daughters. Au yuk-tor svi' leh-dah sar-tak ek' svi' veh tvi-shal; heh lu au went tor sar-tak, wuh svep vesh' ikap-tor heh klacha abru; tonk'peh kanok asal ish-veh ash'el vesh' afer-tor tor nam-tor ved worn k'fai u' kuv au had vesh' tam-tor svi' ek' mu-yor; heh wi kling kupi talal si' uf ish-veh pavesh-tor, il wilat au had vesh'. Yi wuh sa-te'kru tor ish-veh fainu tor ek' wuh solektra, ik kuv sovek person kupi discover wuh tsat, heh talal si' wilat ish-veh vesh' ik wuh princesses tam-tor svi' wuh mu-yor, au dang ma wuh veh au tishau buhfik na' ish-veh ko-telsu, heh dang nam-tor sa-te'kru po' ish-veh tevakh; tonk'peh whoever ar'kada heh did ri navau, po' rehkuh gad heh mu-yor, dang nam-tor tostau. Wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu ak sarlah. Au vesh' muhl entertained, heh svi' wuh khru vesh' taken tor wuh tvi-shal nam-tor' wuh veh wilat wuh princesses ti svi' ish-veh leh-dah sar-tak. Tra' au vesh' tor hayal-tor heh glantau wilat au went tor tam; heh, svi' zek ik nothing lau be' dvun rik' ish-veh khaf-spol ish-veh, wuh svep t' ish-veh tvi-shal vesh' losrak tu'ash. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu ak tevan-tor asleep; heh lu au awoke svi' wuh asal au afer-tor ik wuh princesses had ek' vesh' taman, na' wuh lad t' ish-veh ash'el vesh' bosh t' razh. Wuh ka vel pavesh-tor wuh dahr heh wuh mu-yor: ni wuh sa-te'kru ordered ish-veh patam tor nam-tor tresahk ska'. Po' ish-veh sarlah several vath; tonk'peh au had ek' wuh ka kunli, heh ek' pakik ish-veh ha-tor svi' wuh ka manner. I' ish-veh chanced ik wuh hinek ask'ersu, vi had vesh' wounded svi' puk heh kupi puk rai longer, be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh shasol wilat nash sa-te'kru reigned: heh u' au vesh' travelling k'fai wuh lapan, au ragel-tor wuh hinek kosu, vi ya'akash ish-veh wilat au vesh' going. 'i hardly fai-tor wilat i am going, il ra i had weh-rom tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh ask'ersu; 'tonk'peh i nah-tor i dang spo' maut muhl tor talal si' wilat ish-veh nam-tor ik wuh princesses tam, heh yi svi' wak i lau nam-tor wuh sa-te'kru.' 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek dame, 'ik nam-tor rai maut lerash task: goh nem-tor tun ri tor mon sovek t' wuh wine if veh t' wuh princesses dungi katau tor du svi' wuh khru; heh u' ak u' she mor du pretend tor nam-tor sahris asleep.' yi she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh tor-sai, heh leralmin-tor, 'u' ak u' du shitau ik fi' du dungi shetau invisible, heh du dungi yi nam-tor kup tor zahal-tor wuh princesses wherever au hal-tor.' lu wuh ask'ersu puzhu-tor ek' nash rom counsel, au satalau tor ar'kadan ish-veh kunli: ni au went tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh leralmin-tor au vesh' willing tor undertake wuh task. Au vesh' u' muhl poprah u' wuh vath had vesh', heh wuh sa-te'kru ordered tok-ti royal pelal tor nam-tor putan-tor ish-veh; heh lu wuh khru sarlah au vesh' pufulag-tor tor wuh sik tvi-shal. Aishan u' au vesh' going tor ti ne', wuh eldest t' wuh princesses katau ish-veh wuh cup t' wine; tonk'peh wuh ask'ersu threw ish-veh ek' maf secretly, taking tun ri tor mon wuh eku. Yi au laid himself ne' fi' ish-veh sar-tak, heh svi' wuh pi' du' began tor snore maut ral u' kuv au vesh' sahris asleep. Lu wuh leh-dah princesses puzhu-tor nash au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heartily; heh wuh eldest leralmin-tor, 'nash katravahsu nuh' lau ma ovsoh wuh wiser vel do pak-tor ish-veh ha'kiv svi' nash yut!' yi au she-tor abru heh tu'ash ish-veh zish-nef heh natuhn, heh nem-tor si' ek' ish-veh tok-ti sai-vel, heh sai-vel-tor themselves na' wuh makh, heh skipped pa' u' kuv au vesh' nayik tor palikau taman. Tonk'peh wuh youngest leralmin-tor, 'i ri tor fai-tor uf ish-veh nam-tor, du' du nam-tor ni kunli i olau maut uneasy; i am sure ein mischance dungi befall etek.' 'du simpleton, ' leralmin-tor wuh eldest, 'du nam-tor kwon-hau-ov kwes; ma du yen-tor uf wehk sa-te'kru' sa-fu ma already glantau svi' vain? Heh u' na' nash ask'ersu, kauk kuv i had ri putan-tor ish-veh ish-veh sleeping draught, au would ma yuk-tor soundly hiyet.' lu au vesh' ek' pok, au went heh glazhau na' wuh ask'ersu; tonk'peh au snored fi', heh did ri stir el'ru il ash'ya: ni au nahp au vesh' ved safe; heh wuh eldest went abru tor ish-veh sha' sar-tak heh clapped ish-veh el'ru, heh wuh sar-tak sank vi' wuh lan-tol heh wuh pash-svep flew tu'ash. Wuh ask'ersu gla-tor au going ne' k'fai wuh pash-svep veh po' wuh'ashiv, wuh eldest leading wuh yut; heh thinking au had rai wak tor pak-tor, au spen-tor abru, shitau fi' wuh tor-sai if wuh hinek kosu had putan-tor ish-veh, heh zahal-tor au; tonk'peh svi' wuh svitan t' wuh kaiden au sahr-tor fi' wuh gown t' wuh youngest princess, heh she lit'dhae tor ish-veh ko-kai, 'ek' nam-tor ri gas'rak; ein-veh nem-tor meskaraya t' t'nash-veh gown.' 'du silly creature!' leralmin-tor wuh eldest, 'ish-veh nam-tor nothing tonk'peh wuh felu svi' wuh temok.' yi ne' au ek' went, heh na' wuh lanet au afer-tor themselves svi' wuh danik delightful pi'laptra t' lap; heh wuh mor vesh' ek' t' haul-tukh, heh glittered heh sparkled beautifully. Wuh ask'ersu istau tor nem-tor maf ein token t' wuh shi; ni au shau ska' wuh pi' khlup, heh tra' sarlah wuh ral ralash s' wuh lap. Yi wuh youngest ko-fu leralmin-tor va'ashiv, 'i am sure ek' nam-tor ri gas'rak--did ri du zhu-tor ik ralash? Ik worla pavesh-tor fa'.' tonk'peh wuh eldest leralmin-tor, 'ish-veh nam-tor goh etwel princes, vi nam-tor shouting na' mak na' etwel betaya.' yi sarlah au tor wuh'ashiv pi'laptra t' lap, wilat ek' wuh mor vesh' t' pi-maat-tukh; heh afterwards tor wuh wuh, wilat wuh mor vesh' ek' glittering lerash-khush. Heh wuh ask'ersu shau wuh khlup s' tik; heh kanok wak tra' vesh' wuh ral ralash, if tor wuh youngest ko-kai tremble k' pthak; tonk'peh wuh eldest fam dvun leralmin-tor, ish-veh vesh' goh wuh princes, vi vesh' maf-tor na' mak. Ni au went fi' till sarlah au tor wuh lo'uk suk'muzh; heh na' wuh vla t' wuh suk'muzh tra' ti leh-dah pi' masu-hali k' leh-dah handsome princes svi' au, vi seemed tor nam-tor waiting tra' na' wuh princesses. Veh t' wuh princesses went vi' tik masu-hali, heh wuh ask'ersu ash-tor vi' wuh ka masu-hali k' wuh youngest. U' au vesh' rowing abru' wuh suk'muzh, wuh prince vi vesh' svi' wuh masu-hali k' wuh youngest princess heh wuh ask'ersu leralmin-tor, 'i ri tor fai-tor po ish-veh nam-tor, tonk'peh hi i am rowing k' ek' t'nash-veh lau etek ri tor prah fi' ni sahris u' tsuri, heh i am ved zungor: wuh masu-hali seems maut ras nash-gad.' 'ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh falek t' wuh igen-va, ' leralmin-tor wuh princess: 'i olau ish-veh maut lamekh nuh'.' fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh suk'muzh lam-tor wuh tok-ti illuminated castle, s' if sarlah wuh merry ralash-tanaf t' stonn heh trumpets. Tra' au ek' landed, heh went vi' wuh castle, heh tik prince tam-tor k' ish-veh princess; heh wuh ask'ersu, vi vesh' ek' wuh wak invisible, tam-tor k' au nuh'; heh lu sovek t' wuh princesses had wuh cup t' wine eku k' ish-veh, au drank ish-veh ek' abru, ni ik lu she shitau wuh cup tor ish-veh ru'lut ish-veh vesh' herbosh. Na' nash, nuh', wuh youngest ko-kai vesh' terribly koltha, tonk'peh wuh eldest kwon-hau-ov silenced ish-veh. Au tam-tor fi' till rehkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh asal, heh yi ek' ish-veh ash'el vesh' worn si', ni ik au vesh' obliged tor trasha ska'. Wuh princes fel-tor au pla' va'ashiv abru' wuh suk'muzh (tonk'peh nash wak wuh ask'ersu shitau himself svi' wuh masu-hali k' wuh eldest princess); heh fi' wuh mesyutik gef au nem-tor trasha t' tik vath, wuh princesses promising tor sarlah va'ashiv wuh thurai mu-yor. Lu sarlah au tor wuh kaiden, wuh ask'ersu sahr-tor fi' fa' wuh princesses, heh laid himself ne'; heh u' wuh leh-dah ko-kai slowly sarlah abru maut mau zungor, au puzhu-tor ish-veh snoring svi' ish-veh sar-tak; ni au leralmin-tor, 'i' ek' nam-tor ved safe'; yi au undressed themselves, shitau maf ish-veh tok-ti sai-vel, seshau ska' ish-veh ash'el, heh went tor sar-tak. Svi' wuh asal wuh ask'ersu leralmin-tor nothing pa' ra had pavesh-tor, tonk'peh satalau tor gla-tor weht t' nash flekh adventure, heh went va'ashiv wuh dahr heh wuh mu-yor; heh kanok vel pavesh-tor aishan u' fa'; wuh princesses tam-tor tik wak till ish-veh ash'el vesh' worn tor krus, heh yi fun-tor ha-kel. However, fi' wuh wuh mu-yor wuh ask'ersu lesh maf veh t' wuh pi-maat-kur cups u' wuh token t' wilat au had vesh'. U' ak u' wuh wak sarlah lu au vesh' tor afsakau wuh tsat, au vesh' taken fa' wuh sa-te'kru k' wuh rehkuh khlup heh wuh pi-maat-kur cup; heh wuh leh-dah princesses lam-tor listening za' wuh svep tor zhu-tor ra au would leralmin. Heh lu wuh sa-te'kru ya'akash ish-veh. 'wilat tor t'nash-veh leh-dah daughters tam na' mu-yor?' au kilko-tor, 'k' leh-dah princes svi' wuh castle ne' solektra.' heh yi au var-tor wuh sa-te'kru ek' ik had pavesh-tor, heh gluvau ish-veh wuh rehkuh khlup heh wuh pi-maat-kur cup if au had katau k' ish-veh. Yi wuh sa-te'kru puvutau na' wuh princesses, heh ya'akash au whether ra wuh ask'ersu leralmin-tor vesh' yeht: heh lu gla-tor au ik au vesh' discovered, heh ik ish-veh vesh' t' rai nam-tor-tor tor wafu ra had pavesh-tor, au confessed ish-veh ek'. Heh wuh sa-te'kru ya'akash wuh ask'ersu if t' au au would dvel-tor na' ish-veh ko-telsu; heh au kilko-tor, 'i am ri maut nu'ri, ni i dungi ma wuh eldest.'--heh au vesh' telik ik maut gad, heh wuh ask'ersu vesh' pudvel-tor tor nam-tor wuh sa-te'kru's heir. Wuh aluk-kumsu heh ish-veh ko-telsu tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh aluk-kumsu vi ha-tor k' ish-veh ko-telsu svi' wuh pigsty, ikap-tor k' wuh seaside. Wuh aluk-kumsu nam-tor-tor tor hal-tor si' ek' gad wu wuh-fishing; heh veh gad, u' au hayal-tor fi' wuh gef k' ish-veh fek, looking na' wuh sparkling pral heh watching ish-veh zehl, ek' fi' wuh sudden ish-veh marek vesh' zaseshau maf glu vi' wuh masu: heh svi' bestan ish-veh abru au seshau si' wuh lo'uk aluk. Tonk'peh wuh aluk leralmin-tor, 'pray kal-tor me ha-tor! I am ri wuh yeht aluk; i am wuh enchanted prince: shitau me svi' wuh masu va'ashiv, heh ti'amah!' 'oh, ho!' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'du bolaya ri tor ni wehk zhit pa' wuh tukh; i dungi ma nothing tor tor k' wuh aluk ik mokuhlek variben: ni mahal-tor maf, osu, u' ak u' du sanoi!' yi au shitau ish-veh pla' vi' wuh masu, heh wuh aluk darted zehik ne' tor wuh lanet, heh losrak wuh wu wesh t' khaf za' ish-veh fi' wuh pral. Lu wuh aluk-kumsu went ha-kel tor ish-veh ko-telsu svi' wuh pigsty, au var-tor ish-veh uf au had kum-tor wuh lo'uk aluk, heh uf ish-veh had var-tor ish-veh ish-veh vesh' wuh enchanted prince, heh uf, fi' khaf-spol ish-veh stariben, au had kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor va'ashiv. 'did ri du ya'akash ish-veh na' sovek-vel?' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu, 'etek ha-tor maut wretchedly la', svi' nash rasahkos kitork pigsty; tor hal-tor pla' heh var-tor wuh aluk etek aitlun wuh snug pi' cottage.' wuh aluk-kumsu did ri mau spo' wuh business: however, au went tor wuh seashore; heh lu sarlah ish-veh pla' tra' wuh masu glazhau ek' kin-kur heh yar-kur. Heh au lam-tor na' wuh masu's rihk, heh leralmin-tor: 'o sasu t' wuh masutra! Hearken tor me! T'nash-veh ko-telsu ilsabill dungi ma ish-veh sha' dungi, heh hath satau me tor eit'jae wuh boon t' thee!' yi wuh aluk sarlah mahalan tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'muhl, ra nam-tor ish-veh dungi? Ra tor ish-veh ko-telsu aitlun?' 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'she leralmin-tor ik lu i had kum-tor du, i ought ki' ya'akash du na' vel fa' i kal-tor du hal-tor; she tor ri spo' living sovek longer svi' wuh pigsty, heh aitlu wuh snug pi' cottage.' 'hal-tor ha-kel, yi, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk; 'she nam-tor svi' wuh cottage already!' ni wuh sasu went ha-kel, heh gla-tor ish-veh ko-telsu standing na' wuh svep t' wuh nice trim pi' cottage. 'sarlah svi', sarlah svi'!' leralmin-tor she; 'nam-tor ri nash mau weh-rom do wuh filthy pigsty etek had?' heh tra' vesh' wuh parlour, heh wuh bedchamber, heh wuh af'tum; heh za' wuh cottage tra' vesh' wuh pi' bah-ker, kastkau k' ek' wihfelau t' svai heh savas; heh tra' vesh' wuh courtyard za', bosh t' ducks heh kahm. 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'uf kunling etek dungau ha-tor i'!' 'etek dungi ar'kadan tor tor ni, na' least, ' leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-telsu.
