Kanok-vei went gas'rak na' wuh wehk gad il dahkuh, heh yi dame ilsabill leralmin-tor, 'sa-telsu, tra' nam-tor ri be' tvi-shal hiyet na' etek svi' nash cottage; wuh courtyard heh wuh bah-ker nam-tor wuh lo'uk deal nuh' pi'; i dang spo' tor ma wuh suk kov castle tor ha-tor svi': hal-tor tor wuh aluk va'ashiv heh var-tor ish-veh tor mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh castle.' 'ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'i ri tor spo' tor hal-tor tor ish-veh va'ashiv, na' sos'eh au dungi nam-tor reshnek; etek ought tor nam-tor hagik k' nash takov cottage tor ha-tor svi'.' 'nonsense!' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu; 'au dungi tor ish-veh maut willingly, i fai-tor; hal-tor bi' heh ar'kadan!' wuh aluk-kumsu went, tonk'peh ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' maut ras: heh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh masutra, ish-veh glazhau pla-kur heh gloomy, hi ish-veh vesh' maut hayal; heh au went beyik wuh rihk t' wuh pral, heh leralmin-tor: 'o sasu t' wuh masutra! Hearken tor me! T'nash-veh ko-telsu ilsabill dungi ma ish-veh sha' dungi, heh hath satau me tor eit'jae wuh boon t' thee!' 'muhl, ra tor she aitlun i'?' leralmin-tor wuh aluk. 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, dolefully, 't'nash-veh ko-telsu aitlu tor ha-tor svi' wuh kov castle.' 'hal-tor ha-kel, yi, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk; 'she nam-tor standing na' wuh temep t' ish-veh already.' ni maf went wuh aluk-kumsu, heh afer-tor ish-veh ko-telsu standing fa' wuh temep t' wuh lo'uk castle. 'gla-tor, ' leralmin-tor she, 'nam-tor ri nash grand?' k' ik au went vi' wuh castle teretuhr, heh afer-tor wuh lo'uk wehk dvinsu tra', heh wuh tvi-shal ek' richly furnished, heh bosh t' pi-maat-kur ku-san heh pasu; heh za' wuh castle vesh' wuh bah-ker, heh pa' ish-veh vesh' wuh shi'sochya ulef wuh mile wu, bosh t' sheep, heh vralt, heh hares, heh deer; heh svi' wuh courtyard vesh' stables heh aushfa-kelek. 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'i' etek dungi ha-tor cheerful heh kunli svi' nash vaksurik castle na' wuh shom t' etwel ha-tor.' 'sos'eh etek lau, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu; 'tonk'peh kal-tor etek yuk fi-tor ish-veh, fa' etek tor abru etwel kashkau tor ik.' ni au went tor sar-tak. Wuh thurai asal lu dame ilsabill awoke ish-veh vesh' sax'ksei gad-ha'khlup, heh she jogged wuh aluk-kumsu k' ish-veh kar-nef, heh leralmin-tor, 'prah abru, sa-telsu, heh bestir yourself, na' etek bolau nam-tor sa-te'kru t' ek' wuh solektra.' 'ko-telsu, ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'po dang etek istaya tor nam-tor wuh sa-te'kru? I dungi ri nam-tor sa-te'kru.' 'yi i dungi, ' leralmin-tor she. 'tonk'peh, ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'uf mokuhlek du nam-tor sa-te'kru--wuh aluk fam yehat tor du wuh sa-te'kru?' 'sa-telsu, ' leralmin-tor she, 'leralmin rai weht pa' ish-veh, tonk'peh hal-tor heh ar'kadan! I dungi nam-tor sa-te'kru.' ni wuh sasu went maf ved sorrowful tor nah-tor ik ish-veh ko-telsu dang aitlun tor nam-tor sa-te'kru. Nash wak wuh masutra glazhau wuh ras-kur kur, heh vesh' overspread k' tcha-tor pral heh wuh tauf t' puhsh u' au lit'dhae: 'o sasu t' wuh masutra! Hearken tor me! T'nash-veh ko-telsu ilsabill dungi ma ish-veh sha' dungi, heh hath satau me tor eit'jae wuh boon t' thee!' 'muhl, ra would she ma i'?' leralmin-tor wuh aluk. 'alas!' leralmin-tor wuh ri donku-tor sasu, 't'nash-veh ko-telsu aitlu tor nam-tor sa-te'kru.' 'hal-tor ha-kel, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk; 'she nam-tor sa-te'kru already.' yi wuh aluk-kumsu went ha-kel; heh u' sarlah ish-veh beyik wuh palace gla-tor ish-veh wuh vus t' ask'ersu, heh puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' vluhn heh trumpets. Heh lu au went svi' gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh ko-telsu sitting fi' wuh throne t' pi-maat-tukh heh lerash-khush, k' wuh pi-maat-kur tarkiv fi-tor ish-veh patam; heh fi' tik vla t' ish-veh lam-tor shehkuh rom maidens, tik wuh patam taller do wuh vath. 'muhl, ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'nam-tor du sa-te'kru?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i am sa-te'kru.' heh lu au had glazhau na' ish-veh na' wuh akarshif, au leralmin-tor, 'ah, ko-telsu! Ra wuh tok-ti vel ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor sa-te'kru! I' etek dungau worla ma sovek-vel weht tor istaya na' u' wu u' etek ha-tor.' 'i ri tor fai-tor uf ik lau nam-tor, ' leralmin-tor she; 'worla nam-tor wuh wu wak. I am sa-te'kru, ish-veh nam-tor yeht; tonk'peh i palikau tor nam-tor zungor t' ik, heh i nah-tor i dang spo' tor nam-tor sa-eik-te'krusu.' 'alas, ko-telsu! Po dang du istaya tor nam-tor sa-eik-te'krusu?' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu. 'sa-telsu, ' leralmin-tor she, 'hal-tor tor wuh aluk! I leralmin i dungi nam-tor sa-eik-te'krusu.' 'ah, ko-telsu!' kilko-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'wuh aluk fam yehat tor wuh sa-eik-te'krusu, i am sure, heh i dang ri spo' tor ya'akash ish-veh na' such wuh vel.' 'i am sa-te'kru, ' leralmin-tor ilsabill, 'heh du nam-tor t'nash-veh kafeh; ni hal-tor na' wuh'wak!' ni wuh aluk-kumsu vesh' punekwitau tor hal-tor; heh au muttered u' au went bi', 'nash dungi sarlah tor rai rom, ish-veh nam-tor nuh' mau tor ya'akash; wuh aluk dungi nam-tor zungor na' kim-shah, heh yi etek dungau nam-tor sorry na' ra etek ma ovsoh.' au ak sarlah tor wuh seashore; heh wuh masu vesh' ved nesh-kur heh muddy, heh wuh mighty whirlwind blew abru' wuh pral heh padukau au pa', tonk'peh au went u' be' u' au kupi tor wuh masu's rihk, heh leralmin-tor: 'o sasu t' wuh masutra! Hearken tor me! T'nash-veh ko-telsu ilsabill dungi ma ish-veh sha' dungi, heh hath satau me tor eit'jae wuh boon t' thee!' 'ra would she ma i'?' leralmin-tor wuh aluk. 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 'she aitlu tor nam-tor sa-eik-te'krusu.' 'hal-tor ha-kel, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk; 'she nam-tor sa-eik-te'krusu already.' ni au went ha-kel va'ashiv; heh u' sarlah ish-veh be' gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh ko-telsu ilsabill sitting fi' wuh maut lofty throne tor t' huhtik pi-maat-tukh, k' wuh lo'uk tarkiv fi' ish-veh patam bosh dahkuh ker pid; heh fi' tik vla t' ish-veh lam-tor ish-veh klashau heh attendants svi' wuh zehl, tik veh smaller do wuh vath, s' wuh tallest masuk'veh ne' tor wuh pi' kobsu rai bigger do t'nash-veh ozh. Heh fa' ish-veh lam-tor princes, heh dukes, heh earls: heh wuh aluk-kumsu went abru tor ish-veh heh leralmin-tor, 'ko-telsu, nam-tor du sa-eik-te'krusu?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i am sa-eik-te'krusu.' 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, u' au gazed fi-tor ish-veh, 'ra wuh tok-ti vel ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor sa-eik-te'krusu!' 'sa-telsu, ' leralmin-tor she, 'po dang etek pehkaya na' hasu sa-eik-te'krusu? I dungi nam-tor pope thurai.' 'o ko-telsu, ko-telsu!' leralmin-tor au, 'uf mokuhlek du nam-tor pope? Tra' nam-tor tonk'peh veh pope na' wuh wak svi' christendom.' 'sa-telsu, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i dungi nam-tor pope nash maut gad.' 'tonk'peh, ' kilko-tor wuh sa-telsu, 'wuh aluk fam yehat tor du pope.' 'ra nonsense!' leralmin-tor she; 'kuv au mokuhlek tor wuh sa-eik-te'krusu, au mokuhlek tor wuh pope: hal-tor heh ar'kadan ish-veh.' ni wuh aluk-kumsu went. Tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh gef wuh salan vesh' raging heh wuh masutra vesh' tossed abru heh ne' svi' boiling pral, heh wuh ships vesh' svi' trouble, heh padukau fearfully fi-tor wuh fik t' wuh billows. Svi' wuh svitan t' wuh heavens tra' vesh' wuh pi' krus t' pla-kur igen, tonk'peh na' wuh khu'rak ek' vesh' yon-kur, u' kuv wuh dreadful sahriv vesh' rising. Na' nash glan wuh aluk-kumsu vesh' dreadfully koltha, heh au trembled ni ik ish-veh mal-nef knocked teretuhr: tonk'peh fam dvun au went ne' be' tor wuh gef, heh leralmin-tor: 'o sasu t' wuh masutra! Hearken tor me! T'nash-veh ko-telsu ilsabill dungi ma ish-veh sha' dungi, heh hath satau me tor eit'jae wuh boon t' thee!' 'ra tor she aitlun i'?' leralmin-tor wuh aluk. 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, 't'nash-veh ko-telsu aitlu tor nam-tor pope.' 'hal-tor ha-kel, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk; 'she nam-tor pope already.' yi wuh aluk-kumsu went ha-kel, heh afer-tor ilsabill sitting fi' wuh throne ik vesh' dahkuh miles pid. Heh she had rehkuh lo'uk tarkiv fi' ish-veh patam, heh pa' ish-veh lam-tor ek' wuh pomp heh tepul t' wuh church. Heh fi' tik vla t' ish-veh vesh' dahkuh fel-tor t' yontau ha'ge, t' ek' suk'es, wuh greatest u' suk u' wuh k'lek heh biggest kispek svi' wuh panu, heh wuh least rai larger do wuh pi' rushlight. 'ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk-kumsu, u' au glazhau na' ek' nash greatness, 'nam-tor du pope?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i am pope.' 'muhl, ko-telsu, ' kilko-tor au, 'ish-veh nam-tor wuh grand vel tor nam-tor pope; heh i' du bolau nam-tor hagik, na' du mokuhlek nam-tor nothing greater.' 'i dungi nah-tor pa' ik, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu. Yi au went tor sar-tak: tonk'peh dame ilsabill kupi ri yuk ek' mu-yor na' thinking ra she dang nam-tor thurai. Na' kim-shah, u' she vesh' dropping asleep, asal shau, heh wuh yel she-tor. 'ha!' nahp she, u' she woke abru heh glazhau na' ish-veh k'fai wuh krani, 'po' ek' i fam yehat prevent wuh yel rising.' na' nash nahp she vesh' maut reshnek, heh wakened ish-veh sa-telsu, heh leralmin-tor, 'sa-telsu, hal-tor tor wuh aluk heh var-tor ish-veh i bolau nam-tor s'haile t' wuh yel heh aikum.' wuh aluk-kumsu vesh' ulef asleep, tonk'peh wuh nahp koltha ish-veh ni mau ik au palikau heh tevan-tor s' sar-tak. 'alas, ko-telsu!' leralmin-tor au, 'fam yehat du nam-tor hagik k' hasu pope?' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i am maut uneasy u' wu u' wuh yel heh aikum shen rik' t'nash-veh trasha. Hal-tor tor wuh aluk na' wuh'wak!' yi wuh sasu went shivering k' pthak; heh u' au vesh' going ne' tor wuh gef wuh dreadful sahriv arose, ni ik wuh lap heh wuh maut kov hutau. Heh ek' wuh heavens became nesh-kur k' stormy wan, heh wuh lightnings mavau, heh wuh thunders padukau; heh du lau ma gla-tor svi' wuh masutra lo'uk nesh-kur pral, puv abru spo' suk'kunel k' tarkiv t' wan-kur puhsh fi-tor ish-veh patam. Heh wuh aluk-kumsu crept na' wuh masutra, heh lit'dhae, u' muhl u' au kupi: 'o sasu t' wuh masutra! Hearken tor me! T'nash-veh ko-telsu ilsabill dungi ma ish-veh sha' dungi, heh hath satau me tor eit'jae wuh boon t' thee!' 'ra tor she aitlun i'?' leralmin-tor wuh aluk. 'ah!' leralmin-tor au, 'she aitlu tor nam-tor s'haile t' wuh yel heh aikum.' 'hal-tor ha-kel, ' leralmin-tor wuh aluk, 'tor ish-veh pigsty va'ashiv.' heh tra' au ha-tor tor nash maut gad. Wuh willow-wren heh wuh lesh wuh'wak svi' belaar-wak wuh lesh heh wuh wolf vesh' walking svi' wuh laptra, heh wuh lesh puzhu-tor wuh kushel uralaun ni beautifully ik au leralmin-tor: 'sa-kai wolf, ra kushel nam-tor ish-veh ik uralau ni muhl?' 'ik nam-tor wuh sa-te'kru t' kushel, ' leralmin-tor wuh wolf, 'fa' ik etek bolau kes-wun ne'.' svi' reality wuh kushel vesh' wuh willow-wren. 'kuv ik's wuh nuf, ' leralmin-tor wuh lesh, 'i dang maut mau spo' tor gla-tor ish-veh royal palace; sarlah, nem-tor me thither.' 'ik nam-tor ri ovsoh ved u' du seem tor nah-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh wolf; 'du bolau bek-tor abi' wuh ko-te'kru sarlah, ' ak afterwards, wuh ko-te'kru lasha k' ein yem-tukh svi' ish-veh beak, heh wuh s'haile sa-te'kru sarlah nuh', heh au began tor yem-tor ish-veh nu'ri ones. Wuh lesh would ma tishau tor hal-tor na' wuh'wak, tonk'peh wuh wolf meskarau ish-veh pla' k' wuh sleeve, heh leralmin-tor: 'rai, du bolau bek-tor abi' wuh s'haile heh t'sai ko-te'kru ma hal-tor maf va'ashiv.' ni au nem-tor fek t' wuh razh wilat wuh ha-kel ti, heh sahr-tor maf. Wuh lesh, however, kupi ri shom abi' au had gla-tor wuh royal palace, heh lu wuh pen wak had be' dvun-tor, went tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru had aishan flown si', ni au peeped svi' heh gla-tor kaukuh il shehkuh nu'ri ones lying tra'. 'nam-tor ik wuh royal palace?' maf-tor wuh lesh; 'ish-veh nam-tor wuh wretched palace, heh du nam-tor ri sa-te'kru's kanu, du nam-tor disreputable kanu!' lu wuh nu'ri wrens puzhu-tor ik, au vesh' frightfully reshnek, heh shei: 'rai, ik etek nam-tor ri! Etwel mekhlar nam-tor trau sutra! Lesh, du dungi ma tor vlitau na' ik!' wuh lesh heh wuh wolf grew uneasy, heh da-tor pla' heh went vi' ish-veh razh. Wuh nu'ri willow-wrens, however, fator tor maf heh shei, heh lu ish-veh mekhlar va'ashiv katau yem-tukh au leralmin-tor: 'etek dungi ri ni mau u' esta veh hash-tor's mal, rai, ri kuv etek vesh' dying t' avon, abi' du ma settled whether etek nam-tor respectable kanu il ri; wuh lesh has vesh' la' heh has insulted etek!' yi wuh hinek sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: 'nam-tor hagik, au dungau nam-tor taflau, ' heh au na' wuh'wak flew k' wuh ko-te'kru tor wuh lesh's tauk, heh puvutau svi': 'hinek growler, po ma du insulted t'nash-veh kanu? Du dungau dash na' ish-veh--etek dungi taflau du k' wuh bloody t'naehm.' thus t'naehm vesh' tor'pra tor wuh lesh, heh ek' kehkuh-footed animals vesh' summoned tor nem-tor krus svi' ish-veh, oxen, asses, aushfa, deer, heh kanok vath aushfa wuh terra tuhlau. Heh wuh willow-wren summoned kanok-vei if flew svi' wuh sov, ri goh kushel, suk heh pi', tonk'peh midges, heh hornets, bees heh hash-tor had tor sarlah. Lu wuh wak sarlah na' wuh t'naehm tor palikau, wuh willow-wren satau si' zamasu tor discover vi vesh' wuh nemut's commander-svi'-chief. Wuh gnat, vi vesh' wuh danik crafty, flew vi' wuh laptra wilat wuh nemut vesh' assembled, heh ip-sut herself ne'rak wuh mor t' wuh lap wilat wuh password vesh' tor nam-tor tor'pra. Tra' lam-tor wuh lesh, heh au puvutau wuh fox fa' ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'fox, du nam-tor wuh danik cunning t' ek' animals, du dungau nam-tor paik heh ras-tukh etek.' 'rom, ' leralmin-tor wuh fox, 'tonk'peh ra glantokaya dungau etek sep-wafikh fi-tor?' kling fai-tor ik, ni wuh fox leralmin-tor: 'i ma wuh tok-ti wu bushy harr, if siyah glazhau spo' wuh plume t' yon-kur kan. Lu i abertau t'nash-veh harr abru ved pid, ek' nam-tor going muhl, heh du bolau falun; tonk'peh kuv i kal-tor ish-veh geldau ne', sahr-tor maf u' sahris u' du mokuhlek.' lu wuh gnat had puzhu-tor ik, she flew maf va'ashiv, heh revealed kanok-vei, ne' tor wuh minutest detail, tor wuh willow-wren. Lu gad shau, heh wuh puk vesh' tor palikau, ek' wuh kehkuh-footed animals sarlah sahran abru k' such wuh ralash ik wuh terra trembled. Wuh willow-wren k' ish-veh ya'akash'er isha sarlah hashan k'fai wuh sov k' such wuh humming, heh whirring, heh swarming ik kanok veh vesh' uneasy heh kwes, heh fi' fi' vla au storilau tehnat tik vath. Tonk'peh wuh willow-wren satau ne' wuh hornet, k' zek tor settle ne'rak wuh fox's harr, heh rakus k' ek' ish-veh lau. Lu wuh fox olau wuh wuh'rak string, au palikau ni ik au abertau veh mal, s' kusut, tonk'peh au spitau ish-veh, heh fam dvun potau ish-veh harr pid svi' wuh sov; na' wuh dahr rakus, au vesh' punekwitau tor shitau ish-veh ne' na' wuh moment; na' wuh wuh, au kupi meskaraya si' rai longer, shei, heh shitau ish-veh harr svi' ish-veh mal. Lu wuh animals gla-tor ik, au nahp ek' vesh' pakik, heh began tor sasahr-tor, tik vi' ish-veh razh, heh wuh kushel had skil-tor wuh puk. Yi wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru flew ha-kel tor ish-veh kanu heh maf-tor: 'kanu, rejoice, yokul heh mon tor ish-veh khaf-spol's content, etek ma skil-tor wuh puk!' tonk'peh wuh nu'ri wrens leralmin-tor: 'etek dungi ri yokul wi, wuh lesh bolau sarlah tor wuh ha-kel, heh eit'jae na' pardon heh leralmin ik etek nam-tor dorli kanu, fa' etek dungi tor ik.' yi wuh willow-wren flew tor wuh lesh's razh heh maf-tor: 'growler, du nam-tor tor sarlah tor wuh ha-kel tor t'nash-veh kanu, heh eit'jae ish-veh pardon, il else kanok bak t' ish-veh ak'shem dungau nam-tor pushau.' ni wuh lesh crept thither svi' wuh greatest pthak, heh eit'jae ish-veh pardon. Heh i' na' kim-shah wuh nu'ri wrens vesh' satisfied, heh hayal-tor ne' teretuhr heh ate heh drank, heh tor merry till ved tab-ma vi' wuh mu-yor. Wuh git'woa-prince veh tok-ti khru wuh nu'ri princess shitau fi' ish-veh bonnet heh clogs, heh went si' tor nem-tor wuh lates k' herself svi' wuh lapan; heh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh samuyau sikar t' masu, ik she-tor svi' wuh midst t' ish-veh, she hayal-tor herself ne' tor shom wuh du'. I' she had wuh pi-maat-kur rin'k'n svi' ish-veh el'ru, if vesh' ish-veh favourite plaything; heh she vesh' kwon-hau-ov tossing ish-veh abru vi' wuh sov, heh catching ish-veh va'ashiv u' ish-veh tevan-tor. Po' wuh wak she threw ish-veh abru ni pid ik she din-tor catching ish-veh u' ish-veh tevan-tor; heh wuh rin'k'n bounded maf, heh padukau bi' fi-tor wuh solektra, till na' kim-shah ish-veh tevan-tor ne' vi' wuh sikar. Wuh princess glazhau vi' wuh sikar po' ish-veh rin'k'n, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' maut glu, ni glu ik she kupi ri gla-tor wuh lanet t' ish-veh. Yi she began tor bewail ish-veh pak, heh leralmin-tor, 'alas! Kuv i kupi goh prah t'nash-veh rin'k'n va'ashiv, i would mazhiv-kur-tor ek' t'nash-veh tok-ti sai-vel heh ek'zer, heh kanok-vei ik i ma svi' wuh panu.' whilst she vesh' speaking, wuh git'woa shitau its patam s' wuh masu, heh leralmin-tor, 'princess, po tor du tusa ni bitterly?' 'alas!' leralmin-tor she, 'ra mokuhlek du tor na' me, du rasahkos git'woa? T'nash-veh pi-maat-kur rin'k'n has tevan-tor vi' wuh sikar.' wuh git'woa leralmin-tor, 'i aitlun ri ish-veh pearls, heh ek'zer, heh tok-ti sai-vel; tonk'peh kuv du dungi ashaya me, heh kal-tor me ha-tor k' du heh yokul s' ska' ish-veh pi-maat-kur math, heh yuk fi-tor ish-veh sar-tak, i dungi katau du ish-veh rin'k'n va'ashiv.' 'ra nonsense, ' nahp wuh princess, 'nash silly git'woa nam-tor talking! Au mokuhlek worla kauk prah s' wuh sikar tor yaret me, hi au lau nam-tor kup tor prah t'nash-veh rin'k'n na' me, heh therefore i dungi var-tor ish-veh au dungau ma ra au ya'akash.' ni she leralmin-tor tor wuh git'woa, 'muhl, kuv du dungi katau me t'nash-veh rin'k'n, i dungi tor ek' du ya'akash.' yi wuh git'woa shitau ish-veh patam ne', heh taul-tor glu ne' wuh masu; heh po' wuh pi' du' sarlah ish-veh abru va'ashiv, k' wuh rin'k'n svi' ish-veh ru'lut, heh threw ish-veh fi' wuh rihk t' wuh sikar. U' ak u' wuh nu'ri princess gla-tor ish-veh rin'k'n, she sahr-tor tor pick ish-veh abru; heh she vesh' ni overjoyed ki' ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru va'ashiv, ik she worla nahp t' wuh git'woa, tonk'peh sahr-tor ha-kel k' ish-veh u' sahris u' she kupi. Wuh git'woa puvutau po' ish-veh, 'stay, princess, heh nem-tor me k' du u' du leralmin-tor, ' tonk'peh she did ri pehkaya tor zhu-tor wuh zhit. Wuh thurai gad, aishan u' wuh princess had hayal-tor ne' tor aru-yem, she puzhu-tor wuh flekh ralash--sayumak, sayumak--plash, plash--u' kuv vel vesh' coming abru wuh marble staircase: heh ak afterwards tra' vesh' wuh gentle knock na' wuh svep, heh wuh pi' spes lit'dhae heh leralmin-tor: 'tu'ash wuh svep, t'nash-veh princess tal-kam, tu'ash wuh svep tor thy yeht ashaya la'! Heh kashek wuh zhit ik thou heh i leralmin-tor k' wuh mashulek samuyau, svi' wuh greenwood duvek.' yi wuh princess sahr-tor tor wuh svep heh tu'ash ish-veh, heh tra' gla-tor ish-veh wuh git'woa, ik she had ved yen-tor. Na' nash glan she vesh' sadly koltha, heh shutting wuh svep u' sahris u' she kupi sarlah pla' tor ish-veh ku-san. Wuh sa-te'kru, ish-veh sa-mekh, seeing ik vel had koltha ish-veh, ya'akash ish-veh ra vesh' wuh tukh. 'tra' nam-tor wuh rasahkos git'woa, ' leralmin-tor she, 'na' wuh svep, ik abertau t'nash-veh rin'k'n na' me s' wuh sikar nash asal: i var-tor ish-veh ik au dang ha-tor k' me la', thinking ik au kupi worla prah s' wuh sikar; tonk'peh tra' au nam-tor na' wuh svep, heh au aitlu tor sarlah svi'.' du' she vesh' speaking wuh git'woa knocked va'ashiv na' wuh svep, heh leralmin-tor: 'tu'ash wuh svep, t'nash-veh princess tal-kam, tu'ash wuh svep tor thy yeht ashaya la'! Heh kashek wuh zhit ik thou heh i leralmin-tor k' wuh mashulek samuyau, svi' wuh greenwood duvek.' yi wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor tor wuh nu'ri princess, 'u' du ma putan-tor ish-veh zhit du bolau potau ish-veh; ni hal-tor heh kal-tor ish-veh svi'.' she did ni, heh wuh git'woa spen-tor vi' wuh tvi-shal, heh yi zehik fi'--sayumak, sayumak--plash, plash--s' wuh lanet t' wuh tvi-shal tor wuh fik, till sarlah ish-veh abru beyik wuh pasu wilat wuh princess hayal-tor. 'pray abertau me fi-tor ku-san, ' leralmin-tor au tor wuh princess, 'heh kal-tor me hayal-tor nam-tor' du.' u' ak u' she had ovsoh nash, wuh git'woa leralmin-tor, 'shitau ish-veh math nearer tor me, ik i lau yokul s' ish-veh.' nash she did, heh lu au had yokul u' mau u' au kupi, au leralmin-tor, 'i' i am zungor; lesh me upstairs, heh shitau me vi' ish-veh sar-tak.' heh wuh princess, hi maut unwilling, nem-tor ish-veh abru svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh shitau ish-veh fi-tor wuh trak t' ish-veh sha' sar-tak, wilat au yuk-tor ek' mu-yor wu. U' ak u' ish-veh vesh' ta'hal au spen-tor abru, spen-tor downstairs, heh went s' wuh kelek. 'i', yi, ' nahp wuh princess, 'na' kim-shah au nam-tor hal-tor, heh i dungau nam-tor troubled k' ish-veh rai weht.' tonk'peh she vesh' mistaken; na' lu mu-yor sarlah va'ashiv she puzhu-tor wuh ka tapping na' wuh svep; heh wuh git'woa sarlah wuh'wak weht, heh leralmin-tor: 'tu'ash wuh svep, t'nash-veh princess tal-kam, tu'ash wuh svep tor thy yeht ashaya la'! Heh kashek wuh zhit ik thou heh i leralmin-tor k' wuh mashulek samuyau, svi' wuh greenwood duvek.' heh lu wuh princess tu'ash wuh svep wuh git'woa sarlah svi', heh yuk-tor fi-tor ish-veh trak u' fa', till wuh asal shau. Heh wuh wuh mu-yor au did wuh ka. Tonk'peh lu wuh princess awoke fi' wuh zahalik asal she vesh' astonished tor gla-tor, instead t' wuh git'woa, wuh handsome prince, gazing fi' ish-veh k' wuh danik vaksurik bezhun she had ek'wak gla-tor, heh standing na' wuh patam t' ish-veh sar-tak. Au var-tor ish-veh ik au had vesh' enchanted k' wuh spiteful pu'a, vi had rubai ish-veh vi' wuh git'woa; heh ik au had vesh' fated ni tor abide till ein princess dang nem-tor ish-veh s' wuh sikar, heh kal-tor ish-veh yokul s' ish-veh math, heh yuk fi-tor ish-veh sar-tak na' rehkuh mu-yor. 'du, ' leralmin-tor wuh prince, 'ma pushau ish-veh pi-maat'rer sem-rik, heh i' i ma nothing tor istaya na' tonk'peh ik du dang hal-tor k' me vi' t'nash-veh sa-mekh's kingdom, wilat i dungi marry du, heh ashaya du u' wu u' du ha-tor.' wuh nu'ri princess, du lau nam-tor sure, vesh' ri wu svi' taran 'ha' tor ek' nash; heh u' au stariben wuh sa-ka-ashausu coach drove abru, k' ohkuh vaksurik jarel, decked k' plumes t' kan heh wuh pi-maat-kur harness; heh za' wuh coach fau-tor wuh prince's dvinsu, faithful heinrich, vi had bewailed wuh misfortunes t' ish-veh tal-kam trensu du' ish-veh enchantment ni wu heh ni bitterly, ik ish-veh khaf-spol had muhl-nigh thorau. Au yi nem-tor trasha t' wuh sa-te'kru, heh prah vi' wuh coach k' ohkuh jarel, heh ek' eku si', bosh t' mak heh merriment, na' wuh prince's kingdom, if au pulau safely; heh tra' au ha-tor kunling wuh lo'uk wehk tevun. Aushfa heh aushfa svi' partnership wuh ac'ruth aushfa had tor wuh acquaintance t' wuh aushfa, heh had leralmin-tor ni mau tor ish-veh pa' wuh lo'uk ashaya heh friendship she olau na' ish-veh, ik na' wu-vath wuh aushfa sep-wafikh ik au dang ha-tor heh potau kelek teretuhr. 'tonk'peh etek bolau tor wuh provision na' karil, il else etek dungau dash s' avon, ' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa; 'heh du, pi' aushfa, fam yehat venture kanok-wilat, il du dungi nam-tor kum-tor svi' wuh pash ein gad.' wuh rom na'shikh vesh' zahal-tor, heh wuh sunil t' thelik vesh' bought, tonk'peh au did ri fai-tor wilat tor shitau ish-veh. Na' wu-vath, po' mau consideration, wuh aushfa leralmin-tor: 'i fai-tor rai shi wilat ish-veh dungi nam-tor weh-rom tsorau abru do svi' wuh church, na' kling dares nem-tor sovek-vel maf s' tra'. Etek dungi eku ish-veh ne'rak wuh altar, heh ri esta ish-veh abi' etek nam-tor really svi' bolaya t' ish-veh.' ni wuh sunil vesh' shitau svi' ek'manek, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' wuh aushfa had wuh lo'uk yearning na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh aushfa: 'i aitlun tor var-tor du vel, pi' aushfa; t'nash-veh krei has katau wuh pi' sa-fu vi' wuh panu, heh has ya'akash me tor nam-tor godmother; au nam-tor wan-kur k' khav-kur gla-tor, heh i am tor meskaraya ish-veh abru' wuh lef' na' wuh christening. Ti'amah si' nash-gad, heh du glazhau po' wuh kelek k' yourself.' 'ha, ha, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa, 'k' ek' tvai hal-tor, heh kuv du prah sovek-vel maut rom tor yokul, nah-tor t' me. I dang spo' wuh eku t' slor yon-kur christening wine myself.' ek' nash, however, vesh' untrue; wuh aushfa had rai krei, heh had ri vesh' ya'akash tor nam-tor godmother. She went zehik tor wuh church, vazgau tor wuh sunil t' thelik, began tor lick na' ish-veh, heh licked wuh fik t' wuh thelik ska'. Yi she nem-tor wuh lates fi-tor wuh kamu t' wuh kahr, glazhau si' na' opportunities, heh yi sakadau herself svi' wuh yel, heh licked ish-veh bru-lar whenever she nahp t' wuh sunil t' thelik, heh ri abi' ish-veh vesh' khru did she fun ha-kel. 'muhl, la' du nam-tor va'ashiv, ' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa, 'rai vet du ma had wuh merry gad.' 'ek' went ska' muhl, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa. 'ra ahm did au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kan?' 'fik ska'!' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa ved coolly. 'fik ska'!' maf-tor wuh aushfa, 'ik nam-tor wuh maut shaik heh uncommon ahm, nam-tor ish-veh wuh tsuri veh svi' ish-veh skan?' 'ra tor ik tukh, ' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa, 'ish-veh nam-tor rai weh-rasahkos do crumb-stealer, u' ish-veh godchildren nam-tor puvutau.' fa' wu wuh aushfa vesh' seized k' wuh'ashiv nunau t' yearning. She leralmin-tor tor wuh aushfa: 'du bolau tor me wuh favour, heh wuh'wak weht khartau wuh kelek na' wuh gad sa'awek. I am va'ashiv ya'akash tor nam-tor godmother, heh, u' wuh kan has wuh wan-kur mokov pauk its talu, i fam yehat klee'fah.' wuh rom aushfa consented, tonk'peh wuh aushfa crept za' wuh kahr temok tor wuh church, heh katau ulef wuh sunil t' thelik. 'nothing ek'wak seems ni rom u' ra veh potau tor oneself, ' leralmin-tor she, heh vesh' ved satisfied k' ish-veh gad's ar'kadan. Lu she went ha-kel wuh aushfa inquired: 'heh ra vesh' wuh kan christened?' 'ulef-ovsoh, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa. 'ulef-ovsoh! Ra nam-tor du taran? I worla puzhu-tor wuh ahm svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, i'll wager sovek-vel ish-veh nam-tor ri svi' wuh gad-besan!' wuh aushfa's ru'lut ak began tor masu na' ein weht licking. 'ek' rom vel hal-tor svi' threes, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i am ya'akash tor lamok godmother va'ashiv. Wuh kan nam-tor ved nesh-kur, goh ish-veh has wan-kur paws, tonk'peh k' ik kaulauf, ish-veh has ri wuh single wan-kur isachya fi' its bosh ak'shem; nash goh pavesh-tor wuh'wak kanok zamu tevun, du dungi ti'amah, skil-tor't du?' 'fik-ska'! Ulef-ovsoh!' kilko-tor wuh aushfa, 'au nam-tor such shaik ahm, au tor me maut thoughtful.' 'du hayal-tor na' ha-kel, ' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa, 'svi' ish-veh gu'gelik-zhai-kur ausachya tor-pal heh wu-harr, heh nam-tor boshau k' fancies, ik's fai'ei du ri tor hal-tor si' svi' wuh gad-wakik.' du' wuh aushfa's absence wuh aushfa pu-tor wuh kelek, heh shitau ish-veh svi' zek, tonk'peh wuh greedy aushfa entirely emptied wuh sunil t' thelik. 'lu kanok-vei nam-tor yokul abru veh has ein sochya, ' leralmin-tor she tor herself, heh muhl boshau heh thelik she did ri fun ha-kel till mu-yor. Wuh aushfa na' wuh'wak ya'akash ra ahm had vesh' putan-tor tor wuh wuh kan. 'ish-veh dungi ri sanoi du weht do wuh vath, ' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa. 'au nam-tor puvutau ek'-hal-tor.' 'ek'-hal-tor, ' maf-tor wuh aushfa 'ik nam-tor wuh danik suspicious ahm t' ek'! I ma worla gla-tor ish-veh svi' hish. Ek'-hal-tor; ra mokuhlek ik tvai?' heh she hutau ish-veh patam, tcha-tor herself abru, heh ti ne' tor yuk. S' nash wak forth kling invited wuh aushfa tor nam-tor godmother, tonk'peh lu wuh karil had sarlah heh tra' vesh' rai longer sovek-vel tor nam-tor afer-tor s'udish, wuh aushfa nahp t' ish-veh provision, heh leralmin-tor: 'sarlah, aushfa, etek dungi hal-tor tor etwel sunil t' thelik if etek ma tsorau abru na' ourselves--etek dungau tizh-tor ik.' 'ha, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa, 'du dungi tizh-tor ish-veh u' mau u' du would tizh-tor sticking ik dainty lahv t' ish-veh s' wuh krani.' au eku si' fi' ish-veh yut, tonk'peh lu au lasha, wuh sunil t' thelik certainly vesh' fam dvun svi' its shi, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' herbosh. 'alas!' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa, 'i' gla-tor nash-veh ra has pavesh-tor, i' sarlah ish-veh tor ta'hal! Du nam-tor wuh yeht t'hy'la! Du ma katau ek' lu du vesh' standing godmother. Wuh'rak fik ska', yi ulef-ovsoh, yi--' 'dungi du meskaraya ish-veh lahv, ' maf-tor wuh aushfa, 'veh zhit weht, heh i dungi yokul du nuh'.' 'ek'-hal-tor' vesh' already fi' wuh ri donku-tor aushfa's bru-lar; scarcely had she spoken ish-veh fa' wuh aushfa sprang fi' ish-veh, seized ish-veh, heh vitem-tor ish-veh ne'. Verily, ik nam-tor wuh yut t' wuh panu. Wuh kushel-ko-kan wuh sa-te'kru t' wuh lo'uk solektra tev-tor, heh losrak ish-veh ko-te'kru tor nem-tor tun t' ish-veh goh kan. Nash kan vesh' wuh ko-fu, vi vesh' maut vaksurik; heh ish-veh ko-mekh ashau ish-veh dearly, heh vesh' maut ves tor ish-veh. Heh tra' vesh' wuh rom pu'a nuh', vi vesh' tishau t' wuh princess, heh gol-tor ish-veh ko-mekh tor glantau abru' ish-veh. Lu she grew abru, she vesh' betrothed tor wuh prince vi ha-tor wuh lo'uk yut ska'; heh u' wuh wak drew be' na' ish-veh tor nam-tor telik, she prah pok tor eku ska' fi' ish-veh halovaya tor ish-veh shasol. Yi wuh ko-te'kru ish-veh ko-mekh, sa'haf-tor abru wuh lo'uk wehk ost'syn vel; ek'zer, heh pi-maat-tukh, heh haul-tukh; trinkets, tok-ti sai-vel, heh svi' pen kanok-vei ik became wuh royal bride. Heh she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh waiting-maid tor fau k' ish-veh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh vi' wuh bridegroom's el'ru; heh tik had wuh jarel na' wuh halovaya. I' wuh princess's jarel vesh' wuh pu'a's mazhiv-kur, heh ish-veh vesh' puvutau falada, heh kupi stariben. Lu wuh wak sarlah na' au tor eku si', wuh pu'a went vi' ish-veh sar-tak-tvi-shal, heh nem-tor wuh pi' lipau, heh tresahk ska' wuh klachek t' ish-veh isachya, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor wuh princess, heh leralmin-tor, 'nem-tor tun t' ish-veh, tal-kam kan; na' ish-veh nam-tor wuh sem-rik ik lau nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor tor du fi' wuh fau-yut.' yi au ek' nem-tor wuh sorrowful trasha t' wuh princess; heh she shitau wuh klachek t' isachya vi' ish-veh bosom, prah fi-tor ish-veh jarel, heh eku ska' fi' ish-veh halovaya tor ish-veh bridegroom's kingdom. Veh gad, u' au vesh' riding bi' k' wuh brook, wuh princess began tor olau maut thirsty: heh she leralmin-tor tor ish-veh maid, 'pray prah ne', heh zaprah me ein masu svi' t'nash-veh pi-maat-kur cup s' yonder brook, na' i aitlun tor mon.' 'nay, ' leralmin-tor wuh maid, 'kuv du nam-tor thirsty, prah ska' yourself, heh stoop ne' k' wuh masu heh mon; i dungau ri nam-tor ish-veh waiting-maid sovek longer.' yi she vesh' ni thirsty ik she prah ne', heh knelt abru' wuh pi' brook, heh drank; na' she vesh' koltha, heh dared ri katau si' ish-veh pi-maat-kur cup; heh she wept heh leralmin-tor, 'alas! Ra dungi shetau t' me?' heh wuh klachek kilko-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 'alas! Alas! Kuv thy ko-mekh fai-tor ish-veh, sadly, sadly, would she rue ish-veh.' tonk'peh wuh princess vesh' maut gentle heh meek, ni she leralmin-tor nothing tor ish-veh maid's has-bosh kloshai, tonk'peh prah fi-tor ish-veh jarel va'ashiv. Yi ek' fau-tor weh-irak fi' ish-veh halovaya, till wuh gad grew ni lamekh, heh wuh yel ni scorching, ik wuh bride began tor olau maut thirsty va'ashiv; heh na' kim-shah, lu sarlah au tor wuh pilash, she forgot ish-veh maid's snertau starun, heh leralmin-tor, 'pray prah ne', heh zaprah me ein masu tor mon svi' t'nash-veh pi-maat-kur cup.' tonk'peh wuh maid kilko-tor ish-veh, heh kauk stariben weht haughtily do fa': 'mon kuv du dungi, tonk'peh i dungau ri nam-tor ish-veh waiting-maid.' yi wuh princess vesh' ni thirsty ik she prah ska' ish-veh jarel, heh ti ne', heh meskarau ish-veh patam abru' wuh sahran pilash, heh maf-tor heh leralmin-tor, 'ra dungi shetau t' me?' heh wuh klachek t' isachya kilko-tor ish-veh va'ashiv: 'alas! Alas! Kuv thy ko-mekh fai-tor ish-veh, sadly, sadly, would she rue ish-veh.' heh u' she gal-tor ne' tor mon, wuh klachek t' isachya tevan-tor s' ish-veh bosom, heh markau maf k' wuh masu. I' she vesh' ni koltha ik she did ri gla-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh ish-veh maid gla-tor ish-veh, heh vesh' maut glad, na' she fai-tor wuh sem-rik; heh gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh ri donku-tor bride would nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul, i' ik she had pakik wuh isachya. Ni lu wuh bride had ovsoh drinking, heh would ma prah fi-tor falada va'ashiv, wuh maid leralmin-tor, 'i dungau fau fi-tor falada, heh du lau ma t'nash-veh jarel instead'; ni she vesh' punekwitau tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru ish-veh jarel, heh ak afterwards tor nem-tor ska' ish-veh royal sai-vel heh shitau fi' ish-veh maid's shabby ones. Na' kim-shah, u' au drew be' wuh shaht t' ish-veh halovaya, nash treacherous dvinsu threatened tor stau ish-veh mistress kuv she ek'wak var-tor sovek-veh ra had pavesh-tor. Tonk'peh falada gla-tor ish-veh ek', heh pu'ulidau ish-veh muhl. Yi wuh waiting-maid prah fi-tor falada, heh wuh yeht bride fau-tor fi-tor wuh vath jarel, heh au went fi' svi' nash yut till na' kim-shah sarlah au tor wuh royal kelek. Tra' vesh' lo'uk mak na' ish-veh coming, heh wuh prince flew tor ragel-tor au, heh abertau wuh maid s' ish-veh jarel, thinking she vesh' wuh veh vi vesh' tor nam-tor ish-veh ko-telsu; heh she vesh' pufulag-tor upstairs tor wuh royal tvi-shal; tonk'peh wuh yeht princess vesh' var-tor tor stay svi' wuh kelek ne'. I' wuh hinek sa-te'kru pavesh-tor aishan yi ki' nothing else tor tor; ni au amused himself k' sitting na' ish-veh af'tum krani, looking na' ra vesh' going fi'; heh gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh svi' wuh courtyard. U' she glazhau maut takov, heh nuh' delicate na' wuh waiting-maid, au went abru vi' wuh royal tvi-shal tor ya'akash wuh bride vi ish-veh vesh' she had katau k' ish-veh, ik vesh' thus losrak standing svi' wuh kelek ne'. 'i katau ish-veh k' me na' wuh sake t' ish-veh apc'koik fi' wuh fau-yut, ' leralmin-tor she; 'pray mazhiv-kur-tor wuh ko-kan ein ar'kadan tor tor, ik she lau ri nam-tor idle.' wuh hinek sa-te'kru kupi ri na' ein wak nah-tor t' sovek ar'kadan na' ish-veh tor tor; tonk'peh na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor, 'i ma wuh lad vi nem-tor tun t' t'nash-veh kushel; she lau hal-tor heh gol'nev ish-veh.' i' wuh ahm t' nash lad, ik wuh yeht bride vesh' tor gol'nev svi' watching wuh sa-te'kru's kushel, vesh' curdken. Tonk'peh wuh riyeht bride leralmin-tor tor wuh prince, 'tal-kam sa-telsu, pray tor me veh krus t' kindness.' 'ik i dungi, ' leralmin-tor wuh prince. 'yi var-tor veh t' ish-veh slaughterers tor tresahk ska' wuh patam t' wuh jarel i fau-tor fi-tor, na' ish-veh vesh' maut unruly, heh plagued me sadly fi' wuh fau-yut'; tonk'peh wuh yeht'es vesh', she vesh' maut mau kwes lest falada dang ein gad il vath stariben, heh var-tor ek' she had ovsoh tor wuh princess. She lesh ish-veh sfek, heh wuh faithful falada vesh' pustau; tonk'peh lu wuh yeht princess puzhu-tor t' ish-veh, she wept, heh eit'jae wuh sasu tor felu abru falada's patam tehnat wuh suk gu'gelik temep t' wuh kahr, k'fai'ei she had tor be' dvun kanok asal heh khru, ik tra' she lau fam dvun gla-tor ish-veh sometimes. Yi wuh slaughterer leralmin-tor au would tor u' she istau; heh tresahk ska' wuh patam, heh nailed ish-veh abru ne' wuh gu'gelik temep. Lehkuh-mal wuh thurai asal, u' she heh curdken went si' k'fai wuh temep, she leralmin-tor sorrowfully: 'falada, falada, tra' thou hangest!' heh wuh patam kilko-tor: 'bride, bride, tra' thou gangest! Alas! Alas! Kuv thy ko-mekh fai-tor ish-veh, sadly, sadly, would she rue ish-veh.' yi au went s' wuh kahr, heh drove wuh kushel fi'. Heh lu she sarlah tor wuh ne-yartra, she hayal-tor ne' fi-tor wuh kutra tra', heh kal-tor ne' ish-veh pral-tor klachek t' isachya, if vesh' ek' t' pure haul-tukh; heh lu curdken gla-tor ish-veh glitter svi' wuh yel, au sahr-tor abru, heh would ma seshau ein t' wuh klachek si', tonk'peh she maf-tor: 'salur, pi'salan, salur! Kal-tor curdken's taik hal-tor! Salur, pi'salan, salur! Kal-tor ish-veh po' ish-veh hal-tor! O'er kunel, dales, heh kov, maf nam-tor ish-veh whirl'd till wuh silvery klachek nam-tor ek' dref'd heh tcha'd! Yi tra' sarlah wuh salan, ni karik ik ish-veh blew ska' curdken's taik; heh maf ish-veh flew abru' wuh kunel: heh au vesh' punekwitau tor da-tor heh sahr-tor po' ish-veh; till, k' wuh wak sarlah ish-veh pla', she had ovsoh combing heh tcha-tor ish-veh isachya, heh had shitau ish-veh abru va'ashiv safe. Yi au vesh' maut reshnek heh sulky, heh would ri stariben tor ish-veh na' ek'; tonk'peh au glantau wuh kushel abi' ish-veh grew gu'gelik svi' wuh khru, heh yi drove au homewards. Wuh thurai asal, u' au vesh' going k'fai wuh gu'gelik temep, wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan glazhau abru na' falada's patam, heh maf-tor: 'falada, falada, tra' thou hangest!' heh wuh patam kilko-tor: 'bride, bride, tra' thou gangest! Alas! Alas! Kuv thy ko-mekh fai-tor ish-veh, sadly, sadly, would she rue ish-veh.' yi she drove fi' wuh kushel, heh hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv svi' wuh ne-yartra, heh began tor dref si' ish-veh isachya u' fa'; heh curdken sahr-tor abru tor ish-veh, heh aitlu tor nem-tor meskaraya t' ish-veh; tonk'peh she lit'dhae sahris: 'salur, pi'salan, salur! Kal-tor curdken's taik hal-tor! Salur, pi'salan, salur! Kal-tor ish-veh po' ish-veh hal-tor! O'er kunel, dales, heh kov, maf nam-tor ish-veh whirl'd till wuh silvery klachek nam-tor ek' dref'd heh tcha'd! Yi wuh salan sarlah heh blew maf ish-veh taik; heh ska' ish-veh flew wuh lo'uk yut, abru' wuh kunel heh irak maf, ni ik au had tor sahr-tor po' ish-veh; heh lu sarlah ish-veh pla' she had bound abru ish-veh isachya va'ashiv, heh ek' vesh' safe. Ni au glantau wuh kushel till ish-veh grew gu'gelik. Svi' wuh khru, po' sarlah au ha-kel, curdken went tor wuh hinek sa-te'kru, heh leralmin-tor, 'i fam yehat ma ik flekh ko-kan tor gol'nev me tor potau wuh kushel sovek longer.' 'po?' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. 'fai'ei, instead t' doing sovek rom, she tor nothing tonk'peh tease me ek' gad wu.' yi wuh sa-te'kru tor ish-veh var-tor ish-veh ra had pavesh-tor. Heh curdken leralmin-tor, 'lu etek hal-tor svi' wuh asal k'fai wuh gu'gelik temep k' etwel treit t' kushel, she maf-tor heh variben k' wuh patam t' wuh jarel ik geldau fi-tor wuh temok, heh leralmin-tor: 'falada, falada, tra' thou hangest!' heh wuh patam kilko-srashiv: 'bride, bride, tra' thou gangest! Alas! Alas! Kuv thy ko-mekh fai-tor ish-veh, sadly, sadly, would she rue ish-veh.' heh curdken went fi' telling wuh sa-te'kru ra had pavesh-tor fi-tor wuh ne-yartra wilat wuh kushel puyem-tot; uf ish-veh taik vesh' blown maf; heh uf au vesh' punekwitau tor sahr-tor po' ish-veh, heh tor trasha ish-veh treit t' kushel tor themselves. Tonk'peh wuh hinek sa-te'kru var-tor wuh sa-kan tor hal-tor si' va'ashiv wuh thurai gad: heh lu asal sarlah, au shitau himself za' wuh gu'gelik temep, heh puzhu-tor uf she stariben tor falada, heh uf falada kilko-tor. Yi au went vi' wuh vunai, heh ip-sut himself svi' wuh bush k' wuh ne-yartra's vla; heh au ak gla-tor k' ish-veh sha' bezhun uf au drove wuh treit t' kushel; heh uf, po' wuh pi' wak, she kal-tor ne' ish-veh isachya ik glittered svi' wuh yel. Heh yi au puzhu-tor ish-veh leralmin: 'salur, pi'salan, salur! Kal-tor curdken's taik hal-tor! Salur, pi'salan, salur! Kal-tor ish-veh po' ish-veh hal-tor! O'er kunel, dales, heh kov, maf nam-tor ish-veh whirl'd till wuh silvery klachek nam-tor ek' dref'd heh tcha'd! Heh ak sarlah wuh karik salan t' salan, heh lesh maf curdken's taik, heh maf went curdken po' ish-veh, du' wuh ko-kan went fi' combing heh tcha-tor ish-veh isachya. Ek' nash wuh hinek sa-te'kru gla-tor: ni au went ha-kel rik' hasu gla-tor; heh lu wuh pi' kushel-ko-kan sarlah pla' svi' wuh khru au puvutau ish-veh aside, heh ya'akash ish-veh po she did ni: tonk'peh she thorau vi' bezhun-masu, heh leralmin-tor, 'ik i bolau ri var-tor du il sovek sasu, il i dungau pak-tor t'nash-veh ha'kiv.' tonk'peh wuh hinek sa-te'kru eit'jae ni lerash, ik she had rai sochya till she had var-tor ish-veh ek' wuh var, s' palikaya tor shaht, zhit na' zhit. Heh ish-veh vesh' maut kunli na' ish-veh ik she did ni, na' lu she had ovsoh wuh sa-te'kru ordered royal sai-vel tor nam-tor shitau fi-tor ish-veh, heh gazed fi' ish-veh k' wonder, she vesh' ni vaksurik. Yi au puvutau ish-veh sa-fu heh var-tor ish-veh ik au had goh wuh riyeht bride; na' ik she vesh' goh wuh waiting-maid, du' wuh yeht bride lam-tor k'. Heh wuh nu'ri sa-te'kru rejoiced lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh vaksur, heh puzhu-tor uf meek heh hasausu she had vesh'; heh rik' taran sovek-vel tor wuh riyeht bride, wuh sa-te'kru ordered wuh lo'uk gadzhak tor nam-tor prah pok na' ek' ish-veh kelek. Wuh bridegroom hayal-tor na' wuh fik, k' wuh riyeht princess fi' veh vla, heh wuh yeht veh fi' wuh vath; tonk'peh kling fai-tor ish-veh va'ashiv, na' ish-veh vaksur vesh' ved dazzling tor ish-veh bezhun; heh she did ri seem na' ek' spo' wuh pi' kushel-ko-kan, i' ik she had ish-veh maut-ugelik sai-vel fi'. Lu au had yokul heh drank, heh vesh' maut merry, wuh hinek sa-te'kru leralmin-tor au would var-tor au wuh var. Ni au began, heh var-tor ek' wuh var t' wuh princess, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' veh ik au had wuh'wak puzhu-tor; heh au ya'akash wuh yeht waiting-maid ra she nahp ought tor nam-tor ovsoh tor sovek-veh vi would kloshah thus. 'nothing weh-rom, ' leralmin-tor nash riyeht bride, 'do ik she dang nam-tor lehm-tor vi' wuh cask terpau pauk k' nasik felu, heh ik dahkuh wan-kur jarel dang nam-tor shitau tor ish-veh, heh dang zaseshau ish-veh s' yut tor yut till she vesh' tevik.' 'thou tanaf she!' leralmin-tor wuh hinek sa-te'kru; 'heh u' thou has judged thyself, ni dungau ish-veh nam-tor ovsoh tor thee.' heh wuh nu'ri sa-te'kru vesh' yi telik tor ish-veh yeht ko-telsu, heh au reigned abru' wuh kingdom svi' sochya heh happiness ek' ish-veh ha-tor; heh wuh rom pu'a sarlah tor gla-tor au, heh restored wuh faithful falada tor ha'kiv va'ashiv. Wuh adventures t' chanticleer heh partlet 1. Uf au went tor wuh suk'kunel tor yokul kov-sayas 'wuh kov-sayas nam-tor ved piyah i', ' leralmin-tor chanticleer tor ish-veh ko-telsu partlet, 'suppose etek hal-tor teretuhr tor wuh suk'kunel, heh yokul u' wehk u' etek mokuhlek, fa' wuh squirrel nem-tor au ek' maf.' 'k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ' leralmin-tor partlet, 'kal-tor etek hal-tor heh tor wuh holiday t' ish-veh teretuhr.' ni au went tor wuh suk'kunel; heh u' ish-veh vesh' wuh lovely gad, au stayed tra' till wuh khru. I', whether ish-veh vesh' ik au had yokul ni wehk kov-sayas ik au kupi ri lates, il whether au vesh' kas'el heh would ri, i ri tor fai-tor: however, au nem-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh patam ik ish-veh did ri shetau au tor hal-tor ha-kel fi' ash'ya. Ni chanticleer began tor torvau wuh pi' carriage t' nutshells: heh lu ish-veh vesh' shahtau, partlet spen-tor vi' ish-veh heh hayal-tor ne', heh nufai chanticleer harness himself tor ish-veh heh bes-tor ish-veh ha-kel. 'ik's wuh rom kha'wal!' leralmin-tor chanticleer; 'rai, ik dungi worla tor; i had rather k' ulef lates ha-kel; i'll hayal-tor fi' wuh natuhn heh nam-tor coachman, kuv du spo', tonk'peh i'll ri bes-tor.' du' nash vesh' be' dvun-tor, wuh duck sarlah quacking abru heh lit'dhae, 'du thieving vagabonds, ra business ma du svi' t'nash-veh solektra? I'll mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh du muhl na' ish-veh insolence!' heh fi-tor ik she tevan-tor fi-tor chanticleer danik lustily. Tonk'peh chanticleer vesh' rai coward, heh fun-tor wuh duck's salur k' ish-veh nasik spurs ni fiercely ik she ak began tor lit'dhae na' mercy; if vesh' goh vahl ish-veh fi-tor nosh ik she would bes-tor wuh carriage ha-kel na' au. Nash she sep-wafikh tor tor; heh chanticleer prah fi-tor wuh natuhn, heh drove, maf-tor, 'i', duck, prah fi' u' sahris u' du mokuhlek.' heh maf au went na' wuh takov rom sahr. Po' au had travelled bi' wuh pi' yut, au ragel-tor wuh og-lum heh wuh pin walking teretuhr bi' wuh fau-yut: heh wuh og-lum lit'dhae, 'pehkaya, pehkaya!' heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ni gu'gelik ik au kupi hardly talal ish-veh yut, heh such kitork walking au kupi ri prah fi' na' ek': au var-tor au ik au heh ish-veh t'hy'la, wuh pin, had vesh' na' wuh tsuri-kelek wuh zamu miles ska', heh had hayal-tor drinking till au had yen-tor uf tab-ma ish-veh vesh'; au eit'jae therefore ik wuh travellers would nam-tor ni ves u' tor mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh abertau svi' ish-veh carriage. Chanticleer observing ik au vesh' tonk'peh wonil katravahsu, heh ri kesik tor nem-tor abru mau tvi-shal, var-tor au au lau fau, tonk'peh tor au ugaya ri tor kitork wuh halek t' wuh carriage svi' getting svi', il tor tread fi' partlet's gof. Tab-ma na' mu-yor au lasha na' wuh ha-shal; heh u' ish-veh vesh' rasahkos travelling svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh wuh duck seemed mau zungor, heh waddled pa' wuh rom deal s' veh vla tor wuh vath, au tor abru ish-veh kashkau tor teslau ish-veh ha-shal tra': tonk'peh wuh landlord palikauk vesh' unwilling, heh leralmin-tor ish-veh kelek vesh' bosh, thinking au lau ri nam-tor maut respectable apc'koik: however, au stariben civilly tor ish-veh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh yu-mur if partlet had laid k' wuh yut, heh leralmin-tor au would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh duck, vi vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' laying veh kanok gad: ni na' kim-shah au kal-tor au sarlah svi', heh au bespoke wuh handsome mu'yor-yem, heh spent wuh khru maut jollily. Lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, fa' ish-veh vesh' ved ta'hal, heh lu kling vesh' stirring svi' wuh ha-shal, chanticleer awakened ish-veh ko-telsu, heh, fetching wuh yu-mur, au pecked wuh razh svi' ish-veh, ate ish-veh abru, heh threw wuh fo vi' wuh yon-sha'ti: au yi went tor wuh pin heh og-lum, vi vesh' sahris asleep, heh seizing au k' wuh patam, terpau veh vi' wuh landlord's hagik ku-san heh wuh vath vi' ish-veh handkerchief; heh, having ovsoh nash, au crept maf u' softly u' tor-yehat. However, wuh duck, vi yuk-tor svi' wuh tu'ash sov svi' wuh ker, puzhu-tor au coming, heh jumping vi' wuh brook if sahr-tor beyik wuh ha-shal, ak swam s' ish-veh pulau. Wuh wadan il dahkuh afterwards wuh landlord prah abru, heh nem-tor ish-veh handkerchief tor psethau ish-veh limuk, tonk'peh wuh pin sahr-tor vi' ish-veh heh pricked ish-veh: yi au lates-tor vi' wuh af'tum tor ta'hal ish-veh mev na' wuh yon, tonk'peh lu au stirred ish-veh abru wuh yu-mur-fo flew vi' ish-veh bezhun, heh siyah blinded ish-veh. 'kudau me!' leralmin-tor au, 'ek' wuh panu seems ki' wuh design tehnat t'nash-veh patam nash asal': heh ni taran, au threw himself sulkily vi' ish-veh hagik ku-san; tonk'peh, oh tal-kam! Wuh og-lum sahr-tor vi' ish-veh; heh nash wak wuh kusut vesh' ri svi' ish-veh patam. Au i' flew vi' wuh maut lo'uk shaukaush, heh, suspecting wuh apc'koik vi had sarlah svi' wuh mu-yor fa', au went tor glazhau po' au, tonk'peh au vesh' ek' ska'; ni au swore ik au worla va'ashiv would nem-tor svi' such wuh vus t' vagabonds, vi ate wuh lo'uk deal, vlitau rai reckoning, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh nothing na' ish-veh trouble tonk'peh ish-veh apish tricks. 2. Uf chanticleer heh partlet went tor yaret mr korbes wuh'ashiv gad, chanticleer heh partlet istau tor fau si' teretuhr; ni chanticleer torvau wuh handsome carriage k' kehkuh yon-kur halek, heh harnessed shehkuh aushfa tor ish-veh; heh yi au heh partlet prah vi' wuh carriage, heh maf au drove. Ak afterwards wuh aushfa ragel-tor au, heh leralmin-tor, 'wilat nam-tor du going?' heh chanticleer kilko-tor, 'ek' fi' etwel yut wuh yaret tor vlitau tor mr korbes, wuh fox, nash-gad.' yi wuh aushfa leralmin-tor, 'nem-tor me k' du, ' chanticleer leralmin-tor, 'k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol: prah abru za', heh nam-tor sure du ri tor tevan ska'.' 'nem-tor tun t' nash handsome coach t' t'nash-veh, il kitork t'nash-veh takov yon-kur halek ni tok-ti! I', aushfa, nam-tor pok, heh, halek, sahr-tor br'xan! Na' etek nam-tor going wuh yaret tor vlitau tor mr korbes, wuh fox, nash-gad.' ak po' sarlah abru wuh millstone, wuh yu-mur, wuh duck, heh wuh pin; heh chanticleer mazhiv-kur-tor au ek' trasha tor prah vi' wuh carriage heh hal-tor k' au. Lu au lasha na' mr korbes's kelek, au vesh' ri na' ha-kel; ni wuh aushfa drew wuh carriage vi' wuh coach-kelek, chanticleer heh partlet flew fi-tor wuh ha-zehl, wuh aushfa hayal-tor ne' svi' wuh yon-sha'ti, wuh duck prah vi' wuh washing cistern, wuh pin terpau himself vi' wuh sar-tak trak, wuh millstone laid himself abru' wuh kelek svep, heh wuh yu-mur padukau himself abru svi' wuh towel. Lu mr korbes sarlah ha-kel, au went tor wuh yon-sha'ti tor tor wuh yon; tonk'peh wuh aushfa threw ek' wuh vitush svi' ish-veh bezhun: ni au sahr-tor tor wuh af'tum tor pu-tor himself; tonk'peh tra' wuh duck splashed ek' wuh masu svi' ish-veh limuk; heh lu au ar'kada tor psethau himself, wuh yu-mur shau tor krus svi' wuh towel ek' abru' ish-veh limuk heh bezhun. Yi au vesh' maut reshnek, heh went rik' ish-veh mu'yor-yem tor sar-tak; tonk'peh lu au laid ish-veh patam fi' wuh trak, wuh pin sahr-tor vi' ish-veh nak: na' nash au became ved furious, heh, jumping abru, would ma sahr-tor s' wuh kelek; tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh svep, wuh millstone tevan-tor ne' fi' ish-veh patam, heh pustau ish-veh fi' wuh gla-tor. 3. Uf partlet tev-tor heh vesh' visolektau, heh uf chanticleer tev-tor t' tushat wuh'ashiv gad chanticleer heh partlet sep-wafikh tor hal-tor va'ashiv tor wuh suk'kunel tor yokul kov-sayas; heh ish-veh vesh' settled ik ek' wuh kov-sayas if au afer-tor dang nam-tor thresh-tor kaing svi' au. I' partlet afer-tor wuh maut suk kov-sayas; tonk'peh she leralmin-tor nothing pa' ish-veh tor chanticleer, heh potau ish-veh ek' tor herself: however, ish-veh vesh' ni suk' ik she kupi ri vitem-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh terpau svi' ish-veh drahk. Yi she vesh' svi' wuh lo'uk kolthak, heh lit'dhae tor chanticleer, 'pray sahr-tor u' sahris u' du mokuhlek, heh zaprah me ein masu, il i dungau nam-tor khluhkau.' chanticleer sahr-tor u' sahris u' au kupi tor wuh pilash, heh leralmin-tor, 'pilash, mazhiv-kur-tor me ein masu, na' partlet ti svi' wuh suk'kunel, heh dungi nam-tor khluhkau k' wuh lo'uk kov-sayas.' wuh pilash leralmin-tor, 'sahr-tor wuh'rak tor wuh bride, heh ya'akash ish-veh na' wuh silken elakh tor bes-tor abru wuh masu.' chanticleer sahr-tor tor wuh bride, heh leralmin-tor, 'bride, du bolau mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh silken elakh, na' yi wuh pilash dungi mazhiv-kur-tor me masu, heh wuh masu i dungi lesh tor partlet, vi ti fi' wuh suk'kunel, heh dungi nam-tor khluhkau k' wuh lo'uk kov-sayas.' tonk'peh wuh bride leralmin-tor, 'sahr-tor wuh'rak, heh katau me t'nash-veh garland ik nam-tor hanging fi' wuh willow svi' wuh bah-ker.' yi chanticleer sahr-tor tor wuh bah-ker, heh nem-tor wuh garland s' wuh bough wilat ish-veh geldau, heh katau ish-veh tor wuh bride; heh yi wuh bride mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh silken elakh, heh au nem-tor wuh silken elakh tor wuh pilash, heh wuh pilash mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh masu, heh au lesh wuh masu tor partlet; tonk'peh svi' wuh meantime she vesh' khluhkau k' wuh lo'uk kov-sayas, heh ti ved tevik, heh worla dvun-tor sovek weht. Yi chanticleer vesh' maut sorry, heh maf-tor bitterly; heh ek' wuh beasts sarlah heh wept k' ish-veh abru' ri donku-tor partlet. Heh shehkuh aushfa torvau wuh pi' hearse tor lesh ish-veh tor ish-veh shi'vukhut; heh lu ish-veh vesh' pok au harnessed themselves fa' ish-veh, heh chanticleer drove au. Fi' wuh yut au ragel-tor wuh fox. 'wilat nam-tor du going, chanticleer?' leralmin-tor au. 'tor visolektau t'nash-veh partlet, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath. 'sos hal-tor k' du?' leralmin-tor wuh fox. 'ha; tonk'peh du bolau prah abru za', il t'nash-veh jarel dungi ri nam-tor kup tor bes-tor du.' yi wuh fox prah abru za'; heh presently wuh wolf, wuh lesh, wuh vralt, heh ek' wuh beasts t' wuh lapan, sarlah heh sasu-tor fi-tor wuh hearse. Ni fi' au went till sarlah au tor wuh rapid pilash. 'uf dungau etek prah abru'?' leralmin-tor chanticleer. Yi leralmin-tor wuh terp, 'i dungi ti myself mes', heh du lau be' dvun abru' fi-tor me.' tonk'peh u' wuh aushfa vesh' going abru', wuh terp trel-tor maf heh tevan-tor vi' wuh masu, heh wuh shehkuh aushfa ek' tevan-tor svi' heh vesh' mastevau. Ra vesh' tor nam-tor ovsoh? Yi wuh suk lap-fek t' lapan sarlah heh leralmin-tor, 'i am suk' hiyet; i dungi ti myself mes' wuh pilash, heh du dungau be' dvun abru' fi-tor me.' ni au laid himself ne'; tonk'peh au khartau ni clumsily, ik wuh lap-fek t' lapan tevan-tor svi' heh vesh' lesh maf k' wuh pilash. Yi wuh kov, vi gla-tor ra had pavesh-tor, sarlah abru heh kindly nufau tor gol'nev ri donku-tor chanticleer k' laying himself mes' wuh pilash; heh nash wak au prah safely tor wuh vath vla k' wuh hearse, heh khartau tor prah partlet s' ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh fox heh wuh vath mourners, vi vesh' sitting za', vesh' nuh' ras, heh tevan-tor pla' vi' wuh masu heh vesh' ek' lesh maf k' wuh pilash heh mastevau. Thus chanticleer vesh' losrak sa'awek k' ish-veh tevik partlet; heh having hil-tor wuh shi'vukhut na' ish-veh, au laid ish-veh svi' ish-veh, heh tor wuh pi' hillock abru' ish-veh. Yi au hayal-tor ne' k' wuh shi'vukhut, heh wept heh pula'tusa, till na' kim-shah au tev-tor nuh'; heh ni ek' vesh' tevik. Rapunzel tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh sasu heh wuh kosu vi had wu svi' vain istau na' wuh kan. Na' wu-vath wuh kosu rok-tor ik oekon vesh' pa' tor vahl ish-veh aitlun. Aifa sutra had wuh pi' krani na' wuh pla' t' ish-veh kelek s' if wuh splendid bah-ker kupi nam-tor gla-tor, if vesh' bosh t' wuh danik vaksurik svai heh bar-got. Ish-veh vesh', however, vikuvau k' wuh pid temok, heh rai veh dared tor hal-tor vi' ish-veh fai'ei ish-veh belonged tor wuh enchantress, vi had lo'uk tepul heh vesh' dreaded k' ek' wuh panu. Veh gad wuh kosu vesh' standing k' nash krani heh looking ne' vi' wuh bah-ker, lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh sar-tak if vesh' kastkau k' wuh danik vaksurik rampion (rapunzel), heh ish-veh glazhau ni sluk heh yar-kur ik she longed na' ish-veh, she ved pined maf, heh began tor glazhau spoh heh miserable. Yi ish-veh sa-telsu vesh' alarmed, heh ya'akash: 'ra ails du, tal-kam ko-telsu?' 'ah, ' she kilko-tor, 'kuv i mokuhlek't yokul ein t' wuh rampion, if nam-tor svi' wuh bah-ker za' etwel kelek, i dungau tev-tor.' wuh sasu, vi ashau ish-veh, nahp: 'sooner do kal-tor ish-veh ko-telsu tev-tor, katau ish-veh ein t' wuh rampion yourself, kal-tor ish-veh kodona ra ish-veh dungi.' na' twilight, au clambered ne' abru' wuh temok vi' wuh bah-ker t' wuh enchantress, hastily clutched wuh handful t' rampion, heh nem-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh ko-telsu. She na' wuh'wak tor herself wuh yarmok t' ish-veh, heh ate ish-veh greedily. Ish-veh zahv-tor ni rom tor ish-veh--ni maut rom, ik wuh thurai gad she longed na' ish-veh rehkuh wak u' mau u' fa'. Kuv au vesh' ki' sovek shom, ish-veh sa-telsu bolau wuh'wak weht tev-tor vi' wuh bah-ker. Svi' wuh gloom t' khru therefore, au kal-tor himself ne' va'ashiv; tonk'peh lu au had clambered ne' wuh temok au vesh' terribly kwes, na' gla-tor ish-veh wuh enchantress standing fa' ish-veh. 'uf mokuhlek du dare, ' leralmin-tor she k' reshnek glazhau, 'tev-tor vi' t'nash-veh bah-ker heh vazgau t'nash-veh rampion spo' wuh pi'tak? Du dungau dash na' ish-veh!' 'ah, ' kilko-tor au, 'kal-tor mercy nem-tor wuh shi' yeht-gav, i goh tor abru t'nash-veh kashek tor tor ish-veh s' bolayek. T'nash-veh ko-telsu gla-tor ish-veh rampion s' wuh krani, heh olau such wuh longing na' ish-veh ik she would ma tev-tor kuv she had ri prah ein tor yokul.' yi wuh enchantress kal-tor ish-veh reshan tor nam-tor softened, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'kuv wuh nuf nam-tor u' du leralmin, i dungi kal-tor du tor nem-tor maf k' du u' mau rampion u' du dungi, goh i tor veh nosh, du bolau mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh kan if ish-veh ko-telsu dungi katau vi' wuh panu; ish-veh dungau nam-tor muhl skasau, heh i dungi palutunau ish-veh spo' wuh ko-mekh.' wuh sasu svi' ish-veh vash consented tor kanok-vei, heh lu wuh kosu vesh' katau tor sar-tak, wuh enchantress saudau na' wuh'wak, mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kan wuh ahm t' rapunzel, heh nem-tor ish-veh maf k' ish-veh. Rapunzel grew vi' wuh danik vaksurik kan ne' wuh yel. Lu she vesh' leh-dah tevun hinek, wuh enchantress ikap-tor ish-veh vi' wuh kispek, if ti svi' wuh laptra, heh had neither kaiden il svep, tonk'peh ved na' wuh fik vesh' wuh pi' krani. Lu wuh enchantress aitlu tor hal-tor svi', she shitau herself ne'rak ish-veh heh maf-tor: 'rapunzel, rapunzel, kal-tor ne' ish-veh isachya tor me.' rapunzel had magnificent wu isachya, tok-ti u' pada-tor pi-maat-tukh, heh lu she puzhu-tor wuh spes t' wuh enchantress she unfastened ish-veh pris-tor tresses, skek au pauk veh t' wuh kik t' wuh krani abru', heh yi wuh isachya tevan-tor dah-leh ells ne', heh wuh enchantress sasu-tor abru k' ish-veh. Po' wuh tevun il dahkuh, sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun ik wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu fau-tor k'fai wuh laptra heh be' dvun-tor k' wuh kispek. Yi au puzhu-tor wuh song, if vesh' ni sem-rik-tor ik au lam-tor fam dvun heh shroi. Nash vesh' rapunzel, vi svi' ish-veh awek'es be' dvun-tor ish-veh wak svi' letting ish-veh slor spes resound. Wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu aitlu tor qots'noi abru tor ish-veh, heh glazhau na' wuh svep t' wuh kispek, tonk'peh rim vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor. Au fau-tor ha-kel, tonk'peh wuh uralaun had ni deeply estuhl ish-veh khaf-spol, ik kanok gad au went si' vi' wuh laptra heh shroi tor ish-veh. Wuh'wak lu au vesh' thus standing za' wuh lap, gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh enchantress sarlah tra', heh au puzhu-tor uf she maf-tor: 'rapunzel, rapunzel, kal-tor ne' ish-veh isachya tor me.' yi rapunzel kal-tor ne' wuh pris-tor t' ish-veh isachya, heh wuh enchantress sasu-tor abru tor ish-veh. 'kuv ik nam-tor wuh pu'uth k' if veh mounts, i nuh' dungi ar'kadan t'nash-veh fortune, ' leralmin-tor au, heh wuh thurai gad lu ish-veh began tor tor'ovau gu'gelik, au went tor wuh kispek heh maf-tor: 'rapunzel, rapunzel, kal-tor ne' ish-veh isachya tor me.' iyi wuh isachya tevan-tor ne' heh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu sasu-tor abru. Palikauk rapunzel vesh' terribly koltha lu wuh sasu, such u' ish-veh bezhun had worla wi beheld, sarlah tor ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu began tor variben tor ish-veh ved spo' wuh t'hy'la, heh var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh khaf-spol had vesh' ni stirred ik ish-veh had kal-tor ish-veh ma rai shom, heh au had vesh' punekwitau tor gla-tor ish-veh. Yi rapunzel pakik ish-veh pthak, heh lu au ya'akash ish-veh kuv she would nem-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh sa-telsu, heh gla-tor ish-veh ik au vesh' nu'ri heh handsome, she nahp: 'au dungi ashaya me weht do hinek dame gothel tor'; heh she leralmin-tor ha, heh laid ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh. She leralmin-tor: 'i dungi willingly hal-tor maf k' du, tonk'peh i ri tor fai-tor uf tor prah ne'. Katau k' du wuh skein t' silk kanok wak ik sarlah du, heh i dungi pris-tor wuh pu'uth k' ish-veh, heh lu ik nam-tor pok i dungi tev-tor, heh du dungi nem-tor me fi' ish-veh jarel.' au sep-wafikh ik abi' ik wak au dang sarlah tor ish-veh kanok khru, na' wuh hinek kosu sarlah k' gad. Wuh enchantress remarked nothing t' nash, abi' wuh'wak rapunzel leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'var-tor me, dame gothel, uf ish-veh pavesh-tor ik du nam-tor ni mau heavier na' me tor bes-tor abru do wuh nu'ri sa-te'kru's sa-fu--au nam-tor k' me svi' wuh moment.' 'ah! Du wicked kan, ' maf-tor wuh enchantress. 'ra tor i zhu-tor du leralmin! I nahp i had dahshau du s' ek' wuh panu, heh wi du ma tehs-tor me!' svi' ish-veh reshan she clutched rapunzel's vaksurik tresses, wrapped au dah'wak pauk ish-veh losrak el'ru, seized wuh shif t' scissors k' wuh gas'rak, heh snip, snap, au vesh' tresahk ska', heh wuh lovely pris-tor ti fi' wuh solektra. Heh she vesh' ni pitiless ik she nem-tor ri donku-tor rapunzel vi' wuh eshikh wilat she had tor ha-tor svi' lo'uk tushat heh misery. Fi' wuh ka gad ik she dakh rapunzel, however, wuh enchantress terau wuh pris-tor t' isachya, if she had tresahk ska', tor wuh kik t' wuh krani, heh lu wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu sarlah heh maf-tor: 'rapunzel, rapunzel, kal-tor ne' ish-veh isachya tor me.' she kal-tor wuh isachya ne'. Wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu she-tor, tonk'peh instead t' finding ish-veh dearest rapunzel, au afer-tor wuh enchantress, vi gazed na' ish-veh k' wicked heh venomous glazhau. 'aha!' she maf-tor mockingly, 'du would zaprah ish-veh dearest, tonk'peh wuh vaksurik kushel hayal-tor rai longer uralaun svi' wuh ha-kel; wuh aushfa has prah ish-veh, heh dungi scratch si' ish-veh bezhun u' muhl. Rapunzel nam-tor pakik tor du; du dungi worla gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv.' wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu vesh' be' himself k' kusut, heh svi' ish-veh despair au leapt ne' s' wuh kispek. Au stron-tor k' ish-veh ha'kiv, tonk'peh wuh thorns vi' if au tevan-tor tilau ish-veh bezhun. Yi au czar-tor ved glan-fam pa' wuh laptra, ate nothing tonk'peh gir heh nei-savas, heh did naught tonk'peh lament heh tusa abru' wuh pak t' ish-veh dearest ko-telsu. Thus au roamed pa' svi' misery na' ein tevun, heh na' wu-vath sarlah tor wuh eshikh wilat rapunzel, k' wuh t'dahsu tor if she had putan-tor keshtan, wuh sa-kan heh wuh ko-kan, ha-tor svi' wretchedness. Au puzhu-tor wuh spes, heh ish-veh seemed ni familiar tor ish-veh ik au went na' ish-veh, heh lu au betau, rapunzel fai-tor ish-veh heh tevan-tor fi' ish-veh talu heh wept. Dahkuh t' ish-veh bezhun-masu wetted ish-veh bezhun heh au grew pa'shik va'ashiv, heh au kupi gla-tor k' au u' fa'. Au pufulag-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh kingdom wilat au vesh' joyfully poprah, heh au ha-tor na' wuh akarshif afterwards, kunli heh contented. Fundevogel tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh forester vi went vi' wuh laptra tor shi'kar, heh u' au svi-tor ish-veh au puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' screaming u' kuv wuh pi' kan vesh' tra'. Au zahal-tor wuh ralash, heh na' kim-shah sarlah tor wuh pid lap, heh na' wuh fik t' nash wuh pi' kan vesh' sitting, na' wuh ko-mekh had tevan-tor asleep ne' wuh lap k' wuh kan, heh wuh kushel t' shi-kar-tor had gla-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar, had flown ne', snatched ish-veh maf, heh eku ish-veh fi' wuh pid lap. Wuh forester sasu-tor abru, katau wuh kan ne', heh nahp tor himself: 'du dungi nem-tor ish-veh ha-kel k' du, heh katau ish-veh abru k' ish-veh lina.' au nem-tor ish-veh ha-kel, therefore, heh wuh dahkuh kanu grew abru teretuhr. Heh wuh veh, if au had afer-tor fi' wuh lap vesh' puvutau fundevogel, fai'ei wuh kushel had lesh ish-veh maf. Fundevogel heh lina ashau tik vath ni dearly ik lu au did ri gla-tor tik vath au vesh' maf. I' wuh forester had wuh hinek fas-tor, vi veh khru nem-tor dahkuh pails heh began tor zaprah masu, heh did ri hal-tor wuh'wak goh, tonk'peh wehk wak, si' tor wuh sikar. Lina gla-tor nash heh leralmin-tor, 'shroi, hinek sanna, po nam-tor du fetching ni mau masu?' 'kuv du dungi worla ashiv-tor ish-veh tor sovek-veh, i dungi var-tor du po.' ni lina leralmin-tor, rai, she would worla ashiv-tor ish-veh tor sovek-veh, heh yi wuh fas-tor leralmin-tor: 'lehkuh-mal fa-gad asal, lu wuh forester nam-tor si' hunting, i dungi falek wuh masu, heh lu ish-veh nam-tor boiling svi' wuh kettle, i dungi lehm svi' fundevogel, heh dungi kan-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh.' lehkuh-mal thurai asal wuh forester prah abru heh went si' hunting, heh lu au vesh' hal-tor wuh kanu vesh' fam dvun svi' sar-tak. Yi lina leralmin-tor tor fundevogel: 'kuv du dungi worla trasha me, i nuh' dungi worla trasha du.' fundevogel leralmin-tor: 'neither i', il ek'wak dungi i trasha du.' yi leralmin-tor lina: 'yi dungi i var-tor du. Kim-shah mu-yor, hinek sanna lesh ni wehk mashuk t' masu vi' wuh kelek ik i ya'akash ish-veh po she vesh' doing ik, heh she leralmin-tor ik kuv i would ugaya ri tor var-tor sovek-veh, heh she leralmin-tor ik lehkuh-mal fa-gad asal lu sa-mekh vesh' si' hunting, she would eku wuh kettle bosh t' masu, lehm du vi' ish-veh heh kan-tor du; tonk'peh etek dungi prah abru sahris, sai-vel ourselves, heh hal-tor maf teretuhr.' wuh dahkuh kanu therefore prah abru, sai-vel-tor themselves sahris, heh went maf. Lu wuh masu svi' wuh kettle vesh' boiling, wuh fas-tor went vi' wuh shi'yuk tor zaprah fundevogel heh lehm ish-veh vi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh svi', heh went tor wuh sar-tak, fi' wuh kanu vesh' hal-tor. Yi she vesh' terribly alarmed, heh she leralmin-tor tor herself: 'ra dungau i leralmin i' lu wuh forester sarlah ha-kel heh gla-tor ik wuh kanu nam-tor hal-tor? Au bolau nam-tor zahal-tor instantly tor prah au pla' va'ashiv.' yi wuh fas-tor satau rehkuh dvinsu po' au, vi vesh' tor sahr-tor heh overtake wuh kanu. Wuh kanu, however, vesh' sitting s'udish wuh laptra, heh lu gla-tor au s' afar wuh rehkuh dvinsu sahran, lina leralmin-tor tor fundevogel: 'worla trasha me, heh i dungi worla trasha du.' fundevogel leralmin-tor: 'neither i', il ek'wak.' yi leralmin-tor lina: 'tor du shetau wuh she-tor-lap, heh i wuh she-tor fi-tor ish-veh.' lu wuh rehkuh dvinsu sarlah tor wuh laptra, nothing vesh' tra' tonk'peh wuh she-tor-lap heh veh she-tor fi' ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh kanu vesh' nowhere. Yi leralmin-tor au: 'tra' nam-tor nothing tor nam-tor ovsoh la', ' heh au went ha-kel heh var-tor wuh fas-tor ik au had gla-tor nothing svi' wuh laptra tonk'peh wuh pi' she-tor-bush k' veh she-tor fi' ish-veh. Yi wuh hinek fas-tor scolded heh leralmin-tor: 'du simpletons, du dang ma tresahk wuh she-tor-bush svi' dahkuh, heh ma pushau ska' wuh she-tor heh katau ish-veh ha-kel k' du; hal-tor, heh tor ish-veh na' wuh'wak.' au had therefore tor hal-tor si' heh glazhau na' wuh dahr wak. Wuh kanu, however, gla-tor au coming kwi'. Yi lina leralmin-tor: 'fundevogel, worla trasha me, heh i dungi worla trasha du.' fundevogel leralmin-tor: 'neither i'; il ek'wak.' leralmin-tor lina: 'yi tor du shetau wuh church, heh i'll nam-tor wuh chandelier svi' ish-veh.' ni lu wuh rehkuh dvinsu sarlah, nothing vesh' tra' tonk'peh wuh church, k' wuh chandelier svi' ish-veh. Au leralmin-tor therefore tor tik vath: 'ra mokuhlek etek tor la', kal-tor etek hal-tor ha-kel.' lu au prah ha-kel, wuh fas-tor ya'akash kuv au had ri afer-tor au; ni au leralmin-tor rai, au had afer-tor nothing tonk'peh wuh church, heh tra' vesh' wuh chandelier svi' ish-veh. Heh wuh fas-tor scolded au heh leralmin-tor: 'du duhsu! Po did du ri seshaya wuh church tor krus, heh katau wuh chandelier ha-kel k' du?' heh i' wuh hinek fas-tor herself prah fi' ish-veh mal, heh went k' wuh rehkuh dvinsu svi' pursuit t' wuh kanu. Wuh kanu, however, gla-tor s' afar ik wuh rehkuh dvinsu vesh' coming, heh wuh fas-tor waddling po' au. Yi leralmin-tor lina: 'fundevogel, worla trasha me, heh i dungi worla trasha du.' yi leralmin-tor fundevogel: 'neither i', il ek'wak.' leralmin-tor lina: 'nam-tor wuh fishpond, heh i dungi nam-tor wuh duck fi-tor ish-veh.' wuh fas-tor, however, sarlah abru tor au, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh muzh she ti ne' k' ish-veh, heh vesh' pa' tor mon ish-veh abru. Tonk'peh wuh duck swam sahris tor ish-veh, seized ish-veh patam svi' its beak heh drew ish-veh vi' wuh masu, heh tra' wuh hinek witch had tor mastevau. Yi wuh kanu went ha-kel teretuhr, heh vesh' heartily delighted, heh kuv au ma ri tev-tor, au nam-tor living fam dvun. Wuh valiant pi' ogsu veh belaar's asal wuh pi' ogsu vesh' sitting fi' ish-veh pasu k' wuh krani; au vesh' svi' rom tam'a, heh og-tor k' ek' ish-veh lau. Yi sarlah wuh peasant kosu ne' wuh yut maf-tor: 'rom jams, cheap! Rom jams, cheap!' nash rang pleasantly svi' wuh ogsu's kaluk; au sakadau ish-veh delicate patam s' wuh krani, heh puvutau: 'sarlah abru la', tal-kam kosu; la' du dungi prah rid t' ish-veh goods.' wuh kosu sarlah abru wuh rehkuh ash-tor tor wuh ogsu k' ish-veh ras ki'haf, heh au tor ish-veh unpack ek' wuh sunil na' ish-veh. Au inspected tik veh, abertau ish-veh abru, shitau ish-veh han tor ish-veh, heh na' wu-vath leralmin-tor: 'wuh khlup seems tor me tor nam-tor rom, ni rasathau me si' kehkuh ounces, tal-kam kosu, heh kuv ish-veh nam-tor wuh yonuk t' wuh plesh-tor ik nam-tor t' rai consequence.' wuh kosu vi had rok-tor tor talal wuh rom sale, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ra au aitlu, tonk'peh went maf ved reshnek heh grumbling. 'i', nash khlup dungau nam-tor blessed k' oekon, ' maf-tor wuh pi' ogsu, 'heh mazhiv-kur-tor me muhl'es heh karik'es'; ni au katau wuh kap s' wuh cupboard, tresahk himself wuh krus gas'rak mes' wuh loaf heh sak-tor wuh khlup abru' ish-veh. 'nash skil-tor't zahvan sfith(-), ' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh i dungi aishan shaht wuh jacket fa' i nem-tor wuh zeshaya.' au laid wuh kap be' ish-veh, og-tor fi', heh svi' ish-veh mak, tor bigger heh bigger og. Svi' wuh meantime wuh fnish-tor t' wuh slor khlup she-tor tor wilat wuh hash-tor vesh' sitting svi' lo'uk su'etek, heh au vesh' skamau heh tev-tor fi' ish-veh svi' kasu-tor. 'tonk'peh! Vi invited du?' leralmin-tor wuh pi' ogsu, heh drove wuh unbidden be'hai'la maf. Wuh hash-tor, however, vi ken-tor rai german, would ri nam-tor da-tor maf, tonk'peh sarlah pla' va'ashiv svi' ek'wak-increasing apc'koik. Wuh pi' ogsu na' kim-shah pakik ek' tranush, heh drew wuh krus t' sai s' wuh razh ne' ish-veh ar'kadan-pasu, heh taran: 'bek-tor, heh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor du, ' kwul-tor ish-veh mercilessly fi' au. Lu au drew ish-veh maf heh tum-tor, tra' ti fa' ish-veh rai fewer do stehkuh, tevik heh k' mal sakadau si'. 'nam-tor du wuh katravahsu t' ik wihfelau?' leralmin-tor au, heh kupi ri gol'nev krol-tor ish-veh sha' bravery. 'wuh bosh kahr dungau fai-tor t' nash!' heh wuh pi' ogsu hastened tor tresahk himself wuh girdle, og-tor ish-veh, heh embroidered fi' ish-veh svi' suk nuhm: 'stehkuh na' veh shad-kisheya!' 'ra, wuh kahr!' au fator, 'wuh bosh panu dungau zhu-tor t' ish-veh!' heh ish-veh khaf-spol wagged k' mak spo' wuh lamb's harr. Wuh ogsu shitau fi' wuh girdle, heh resolved tor hal-tor forth vi' wuh panu, fai'ei au nahp ish-veh zup-shal vesh' nuh' pi' na' ish-veh valour. Fa' au went maf, au sought pa' svi' wuh kelek tor gla-tor kuv tra' vesh' sovek-vel if au kupi nem-tor k' ish-veh; however, au afer-tor nothing tonk'peh wuh hinek thuhk, heh ik au shitau svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Svi' khom t' wuh svep au glantau wuh kushel if had kum-tor itself svi' wuh pi'laptra. Ish-veh had tor hal-tor vi' ish-veh abru'lik k' wuh thuhk. I' au nem-tor tor wuh fau-yut boldly, heh u' au vesh' ta'hal heh nimble, au olau rai zung. Wuh fau-yut pufulag-tor ish-veh abru wuh suk'kunel, heh lu au had pulau wuh k'lek sfek t' ish-veh, tra' hayal-tor wuh powerful masuk'veh looking peacefully pa' ish-veh. Wuh pi' ogsu went bravely abru, stariben tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 'rom gad, comrade, ni du nam-tor sitting tra' overlooking wuh eik-sak-tor panu! I am aishan fi' t'nash-veh yut thither, heh aitlun tor ar'kadan t'nash-veh kunli. Ma du sovek inclination tor hal-tor k' me?' wuh masuk'veh glazhau contemptuously na' wuh ogsu, heh leralmin-tor: 'du ragamuffin! Du miserable creature!' 'oh, indeed?' kilko-tor wuh pi' ogsu, heh unbuttoned ish-veh tor-pal, heh gluvau wuh masuk'veh wuh girdle, 'tra' lau du telv-tor ra ves t' wuh sasu i am!' wuh masuk'veh telv-tor: 'stehkuh na' veh shad-kisheya, ' heh nahp ik au had vesh' sasu ik wuh ogsu had pustau, heh began tor olau wuh pi' respect na' wuh tiny katravahsu. Nevertheless, au istau tor ar'kadan ish-veh wuh'rak, heh nem-tor wuh kov svi' ish-veh el'ru heh lerakhovau ish-veh teretuhr ni ik masu eku-tor si' t' ish-veh. 'tor ik likewise, ' leralmin-tor wuh masuk'veh, 'kuv du ma karik'es.' 'nam-tor ik ek'?' leralmin-tor wuh ogsu, 'ik nam-tor kan's mavau k' etek!' heh shitau ish-veh el'ru vi' ish-veh abru'lik, katau si' wuh mos thuhk, heh hish-tor ish-veh abi' wuh masu sahr-tor s' ish-veh. 'odva, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ik vesh' wuh pi' weh-rom, wasn't ish-veh?' wuh masuk'veh did ri fai-tor ra tor leralmin, heh kupi ri dva-tor ish-veh t' wuh pi' sasu. Yi wuh masuk'veh abrashau wuh kov heh threw ish-veh ni pid ik wuh bezhun kupi scarcely zahal-tor ish-veh. 'i', pi' mite t' wuh sasu, tor ik likewise, ' 'muhl lehm-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh ogsu, 'tonk'peh po' ek' wuh kov sarlah ne' tor terra va'ashiv; i dungi lehm du veh if dungau worla sarlah pla' na' ek', ' heh au shitau ish-veh el'ru vi' ish-veh abru'lik, nem-tor si' wuh kushel, heh threw ish-veh vi' wuh sov. Wuh kushel, delighted k' its liberty, she-tor, flew maf heh did ri sarlah pla'. 'uf tor ik pohshaya sanoi du, comrade?' ya'akash wuh ogsu. 'du mokuhlek certainly lehm, ' leralmin-tor wuh masuk'veh, 'tonk'peh i' etek dungi gla-tor kuv du nam-tor kup tor lesh sovek-vel properly.' au nem-tor wuh pi' ogsu tor wuh mighty oak lap if ti tra' felled fi' wuh solektra, heh leralmin-tor: 'kuv du nam-tor karik hiyet, gol'nev me tor lesh wuh lap s' wuh laptra.' 'readily, ' kilko-tor wuh pi' sasu; 'nem-tor du wuh lap-fek fi' ish-veh tipan, heh i dungi ashenau abru wuh khlup heh pi'gel; po' ek', au nam-tor wuh heaviest.' wuh masuk'veh nem-tor wuh lap-fek fi' ish-veh tipan, tonk'peh wuh ogsu hayal-tor himself fi' wuh khlup, heh wuh masuk'veh, vi kupi ri glazhau pauk, had tor lesh maf wuh bosh lap, heh wuh pi' ogsu vi' wuh bargain: au za', vesh' ved merry heh kunli, heh whistled wuh song: 'rehkuh ogsu fau-tor forth s' wuh temep, ' u' kuv carrying wuh lap vesh' kan's mavau. Wuh masuk'veh, po' au had zaseshau wuh ras burden krus t' wuh yut, kupi hal-tor rai further, heh maf-tor: 'hark du, i dungau ma tor kal-tor wuh lap tevan!' wuh ogsu sprang nimbly ne', seized wuh lap k' fi' kar u' kuv au had vesh' carrying ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh masuk'veh: 'du nam-tor such wuh lo'uk katravahsu, heh wi fam yehat kauk lesh wuh lap!' au went fi' teretuhr, heh u' au be' dvun-tor wuh cherry-lap, wuh masuk'veh laid meskaraya t' wuh fik t' wuh lap wilat wuh ripest savas vesh' hanging, keh'sei ish-veh ne', mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh vi' wuh ogsu's el'ru, heh bade ish-veh yokul. Tonk'peh wuh pi' ogsu vesh' mau nuh' kobat tor meskaraya wuh lap, heh lu wuh masuk'veh kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, ish-veh sprang pla' va'ashiv, heh wuh ogsu vesh' tossed vi' wuh sov k' ish-veh. Lu au had tevan-tor ne' va'ashiv rik' dash, wuh masuk'veh leralmin-tor: 'ra nam-tor nash? Ma du ri karik'es hiyet tor meskaraya wuh kobat pi'gel?' 'tra' nam-tor rai fam t' karik'es, ' kilko-tor wuh pi' ogsu. 'tor du nah-tor ik kupi nam-tor sovek-vel tor wuh sasu vi has kwul-tor ne' stehkuh na' veh salur? I leapt abru' wuh lap fai'ei wuh huntsmen nam-tor shooting ne' tra' svi' wuh pi'laptra. Spen-tor u' i did, kuv du mokuhlek tor ish-veh.' wuh masuk'veh tor wuh attempt tonk'peh au kupi ri prah abru' wuh lap, heh hafau hanging svi' wuh khlup, ni ik svi' nash isha wuh ogsu potau wuh upper el'ru. Wuh masuk'veh leralmin-tor: 'kuv du nam-tor such wuh valiant katravahsu, sarlah k' me vi' etwel suk-tauk heh spend wuh mu-yor k' etek.' wuh pi' ogsu vesh' willing, heh zahal-tor ish-veh. Lu au went vi' wuh tauk, vath masuk'veh vesh' sitting tra' k' wuh yon, heh tik t' au had wuh roasted sheep svi' ish-veh el'ru heh vesh' eating ish-veh. Wuh pi' ogsu glazhau pauk heh nahp: 'ish-veh nam-tor mau weht spacious la' do svi' t'nash-veh zup-shal.' wuh masuk'veh gluvau ish-veh wuh sar-tak, heh leralmin-tor au vesh' tor ti ne' svi' ish-veh heh yuk. Wuh sar-tak, however, vesh' nuh' suk' na' wuh pi' ogsu; au did ri ti ne' svi' ish-veh, tonk'peh crept vi' wuh teruk. Lu ish-veh vesh' midnight, heh wuh masuk'veh nahp ik wuh pi' ogsu vesh' lying svi' wuh ralash yuk, au prah abru, nem-tor wuh lo'uk shek-tukh mofek, tresahk k'fai wuh sar-tak k' veh salur, heh nahp au had shahtau ska' wuh grasshopper na' rom. K' wuh earliest gad-keshtan wuh masuk'veh went vi' wuh laptra, heh had ved yen-tor wuh pi' ogsu, lu ek' na' wuh'wak au lates-tor abru tor au ved merrily heh boldly. Wuh masuk'veh vesh' terrified, au vesh' kwes ik au would kwul au ek' tevik, heh sahr-tor maf svi' wuh lo'uk brax. Wuh pi' ogsu went onwards, kwon-hau-ov zahalik ish-veh sha' sfekau han. Po' au had lates-tor na' wuh akarshif, sarlah ish-veh tor wuh courtyard t' wuh royal palace, heh u' au olau weary, au ti ne' fi' wuh yar heh tevan-tor asleep. Whilst au ti tra', wuh sutra sarlah heh inspected ish-veh fi' ek' vla, heh telv-tor fi' ish-veh girdle: 'stehkuh na' veh shad-kisheya.' 'ah!' leralmin-tor au, 'ra tor wuh lo'uk warrior aitlun la' svi' wuh midst t' sochya? Au bolau nam-tor wuh mighty s'haile.' au went heh tor'pra ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh u' ish-veh opinion ik kuv t'naehm dang shaya si', nash would nam-tor wuh weighty heh useful sasu vi ought fi' rai khrosahp tor nam-tor kal-tor tor trashu. Wuh counsel sanoi wuh sa-te'kru, heh au satau veh t' ish-veh courtiers tor wuh pi' ogsu tor nufai ish-veh askital dvin lu au awoke. Wuh kevet-dutar hafau standing k' wuh sleeper, bek-tor abi' au sakadau ish-veh sikrus heh tu'ash ish-veh bezhun, heh yi zhelesh tor ish-veh nash mnah. 'na' nash maut utvau ma sarlah nash-veh la', ' wuh ogsu kilko-tor, 'i am pok tor svi-tor wuh sa-te'kru's dvin.' au vesh' therefore honourably poprah, heh wuh special kelek vesh' assigned ish-veh. Wuh ask'ersu, however, vesh' eku tehnat wuh pi' ogsu, heh istau ish-veh wuh thousand miles maf. 'ra nam-tor tor nam-tor wuh shaht t' nash?' au leralmin-tor among themselves. 'kuv etek quarrel k' ish-veh, heh au kwul-tor pa' ish-veh, stehkuh t' etek dungi tevan na' kanok salur; ri veh t' etek mokuhlek lamok tehnat ish-veh.' sarlah au therefore tor wuh klopaya, betook themselves svi' wuh ak'shem tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh eit'jae na' ish-veh dismissal. 'etek nam-tor ri dator, ' leralmin-tor au, 'tor stay k' wuh sasu vi stau stehkuh na' veh shad-kisheya.' wuh sa-te'kru vesh' sorry ik na' wuh sake t' veh au dang pak-tor ek' ish-veh faithful dvinsu, istau ik au had worla eku bezhun fi' wuh ogsu, heh would willingly ma vesh' rid t' ish-veh va'ashiv. Tonk'peh au did ri venture tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh dismissal, na' au dreaded lest au dang kwul ish-veh heh ek' ish-veh sutra tevik, heh shi himself fi' wuh royal throne. Au nahp pa' ish-veh na' wuh akarshif, heh na' kim-shah afer-tor rom counsel. Au satau tor wuh pi' ogsu heh aisha ish-veh tor nam-tor informed ik u' au vesh' wuh lo'uk warrior, au had veh ya'akash tor tor tor ish-veh. Svi' wuh laptra t' ish-veh shasol ha-tor dahkuh masuk'veh, vi aisha lo'uk mischief k' ish-veh robbing, murdering, ravaging, heh yontau, heh kling kupi betaya au rik' putting himself svi' tehvar t' tevakh. Kuv wuh ogsu conquered heh pustau aifa dahkuh masuk'veh, au would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh goh ko-fu tor ko-telsu, heh ulef t' ish-veh kingdom u' wuh dowry, likewise teh horsemen dang hal-tor k' ish-veh tor gol-tor ish-veh. 'ik would indeed nam-tor wuh tok-ti vel na' wuh sasu spo' me!' nahp wuh pi' ogsu. 'veh nam-tor ri nufau wuh vaksurik princess heh ulef wuh kingdom kanok gad t' veh's ha'kiv!' 'oh, ha, ' au kilko-tor, 'i dungi ak nessau wuh masuk'veh, heh ri tor require wuh gol'nev t' wuh hundred horsemen tor tor ish-veh; au vi mokuhlek kwul stehkuh k' veh salur has rai bolaya tor nam-tor kwes t' dahkuh.' wuh pi' ogsu went forth, heh wuh hundred horsemen zahal-tor ish-veh. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh outskirts t' wuh laptra, au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh zahelsu: 'aishan stay waiting la', i sa'awek dungi ak shaht ska' wuh masuk'veh.' yi au bounded vi' wuh laptra heh glazhau pa' gas'rak heh losrak. Po' wuh du' au pakashogau fi' masuk'veh. Au ti sleeping ne' wuh lap, heh snored ni ik wuh khlup pral-tor abru heh ne'. Wuh pi' ogsu, ri idle, hoknau dahkuh pocketsful t' kov, heh k' aifa sasu-tor abru wuh lap. Lu au vesh' halfway abru, au trel-tor ne' k' wuh khlup, abi' au hayal-tor aishan abru' wuh sleepers, heh yi kal-tor veh kov po' wuh'ashiv tevan fi' wuh thasek t' veh t' wuh masuk'veh. Na' wuh akarshif wuh masuk'veh olau nothing, tonk'peh na' kim-shah au awoke, kwitau ish-veh comrade, heh leralmin-tor: 'po nam-tor du knocking me?' 'du bolau nam-tor dreaming, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath, 'i am ri knocking du.' au laid themselves ne' tor yuk va'ashiv, heh yi wuh ogsu threw wuh kov ne' fi' wuh dahr. 'ra nam-tor wuh meaning t' nash?' maf-tor wuh vath 'po nam-tor du pelting me?' 'i am ri pelting du, ' kilko-tor wuh wuh'rak, growling. Au disputed pa' ish-veh na' wuh wak, tonk'peh u' au vesh' weary au kal-tor wuh tukh shom, heh ish-veh bezhun a'ing wuh'wak weht. Wuh pi' ogsu began ish-veh zhagra va'ashiv, picked si' wuh biggest kov, heh threw ish-veh k' ek' ish-veh lau fi' wuh thasek t' wuh wuh'rak masuk'veh. 'ik nam-tor nuh' rasahkos!' maf-tor au, heh sprang abru spo' wuh madman, heh kwitau ish-veh besu tehnat wuh lap abi' ish-veh hutau.
