Wuh vath vlitau ish-veh pla' svi' wuh ka di'kaudj, heh au prah vi' such wuh reshan ik au tore abru lap heh belaboured tik vath ni wu, ik na' kim-shah au fi' tevan-tor ne' tevik fi' wuh solektra na' wuh ka wak. Yi wuh pi' ogsu leapt ne'. 'ish-veh nam-tor wuh kunli vel, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ik au did ri bezhun-masu abru wuh lap fi' if i vesh' sitting, il i dang ma had tor sprint fi' tor wuh'ashiv spo' wuh squirrel; tonk'peh etek ogsu nam-tor nimble.' au drew si' ish-veh shek heh mazhiv-kur-tor tik t' au wuh couple t' kwit-tor svi' wuh thasek, heh yi went si' tor wuh horsemen heh leralmin-tor: 'wuh ar'kadan nam-tor ovsoh; i ma shahtau fi' t' au ska', tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' lerash ar'kadan! Au tore abru lap svi' ish-veh sival bolaya, heh fosh-tor themselves k' au, tonk'peh ek' ik nam-tor tor rai lof lu wuh sasu spo' myself sarlah, vi mokuhlek stau stehkuh na' veh salur.' 'tonk'peh nam-tor du ri wounded?' ya'akash wuh horsemen. 'du bolaya ri concern yourself pa' ik, ' kilko-tor wuh ogsu, 'au ma ri keh'sei veh isachya t' t'nash-veh.' wuh horsemen would ri dva-tor ish-veh, heh fau-tor vi' wuh laptra; tra' au afer-tor wuh masuk'veh mahalan svi' ish-veh khaf, heh ek' pauk pa' ti wuh torn-abru lap. Wuh pi' ogsu halishau t' wuh sa-te'kru wuh ugau reward; au, however, repented t' ish-veh ugaya, heh va'ashiv bethought himself uf au kupi prah rid t' wuh hero. 'fa' du poprah t'nash-veh ko-fu, heh wuh ulef t' t'nash-veh kingdom, ' leralmin-tor au tor ish-veh, 'du bolau perform veh weht heroic deed. Svi' wuh laptra roams wuh unicorn if tor lo'uk klau, heh du bolau kum ish-veh wuh'rak.' 'i pthak veh unicorn fam dvun lehkuh tor dahkuh masuk'veh. Stehkuh na' veh salur, nam-tor t'nash-veh ves t' tek'ik.' au nem-tor wuh man-elakh heh wuh la'ash k' ish-veh, went forth vi' wuh laptra, heh va'ashiv bade eifa vi vesh' satau k' ish-veh tor bek-tor s'udish. Au had ri wu tor seek. Wuh unicorn ak sarlah na' ish-veh, heh rushed directly fi' wuh ogsu, u' kuv ish-veh would gore ish-veh k' its stonn rik' weht ado. 'softly, softly; ish-veh mokuhlek't nam-tor ovsoh u' sahris u' ik, ' leralmin-tor au, heh lam-tor fam dvun heh bek-tor abi' wuh aushfa vesh' ved ikap-tor, heh yi sprang nimbly za' wuh lap. Wuh unicorn sahr-tor tehnat wuh lap k' ek' its karik'es, heh terpau its stonn ni sahris svi' wuh lap-fek ik ish-veh had ri wuh karik'es hiyet tor bes-tor ish-veh si' va'ashiv, heh thus ish-veh vesh' kum-tor. 'i', i ma prah wuh kushel, ' leralmin-tor wuh ogsu, heh sasarlah s' za' wuh lap heh shitau wuh man-elakh pauk its talu, heh yi k' ish-veh la'ash au hewed wuh stonn s' wuh lap, heh lu ek' vesh' pok au pufulag-tor wuh beast maf heh nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru. Wuh sa-te'kru fam dvun would ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh ugau reward, heh tor wuh wuh haishaya. Fa' wuh wedding wuh ogsu vesh' tor kum ish-veh wuh kwai boar ik tor lo'uk havoc svi' wuh laptra, heh wuh huntsmen dang mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh gol'nev. 'willingly, ' leralmin-tor wuh ogsu, 'ik nam-tor kan's mavau!' au did ri nem-tor wuh huntsmen k' ish-veh vi' wuh laptra, heh au vesh' muhl sanoi ik au did ri, na' wuh kwai boar had several wak poprah au svi' such wuh manner ik au had rai inclination tor ti svi' bek-tor na' ish-veh. Lu wuh boar pakashogau wuh ogsu, ish-veh sahr-tor fi' ish-veh k' foaming ru'lut heh whetted tusks, heh vesh' pa' tor lehm ish-veh tor wuh solektra, tonk'peh wuh hero sasahr-tor heh sprang vi' wuh chapel if vesh' be' heh abru tor wuh krani na' wuh'wak, heh svi' veh bound si' va'ashiv. Wuh boar sahr-tor po' ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh ogsu sahr-tor pauk s'udish heh ikap-tor wuh svep za' ish-veh, heh yi wuh raging beast, if vesh' mau nuh' ras heh awkward tor leap s' wuh krani, vesh' kum-tor. Wuh pi' ogsu puvutau wuh huntsmen thither ik au lau gla-tor wuh prisoner k' ish-veh sha' bezhun. Wuh hero, however, went tor wuh sa-te'kru, vi vesh' i', whether au tishau ish-veh il ri, obliged tor potau ish-veh ugaya, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ko-fu heh wuh ulef t' ish-veh kingdom. Had au fainu ik ish-veh vesh' rai warlike hero, tonk'peh wuh pi' ogsu vi vesh' standing fa' ish-veh, ish-veh would ma hal-tor tor ish-veh khaf-spol fam dvun weht do ish-veh did. Wuh wedding vesh' meskarau k' lo'uk magnificence heh pi' mak, heh s' wuh ogsu wuh sa-te'kru vesh' tor. Po' ein wak wuh nu'ri ko-te'kru puzhu-tor ish-veh sa-telsu leralmin svi' ish-veh sahr-tor-tor na' mu-yor: 'sa-kan, tor me wuh doublet, heh patch wuh pantaloons, il else i dungi rap wuh ker-thon-tor abru' ish-veh kaluk.' yi she discovered svi' ra fupa s' t' ha'kiv wuh nu'ri s'haile had vesh' pukeshta, heh thurai asal complained t' ish-veh wrongs tor ish-veh sa-mekh, heh eit'jae ish-veh tor gol'nev ish-veh tor prah rid t' ish-veh sa-telsu, vi vesh' nothing else tonk'peh wuh ogsu. Wuh sa-te'kru comforted ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'trasha ish-veh shi'yuk svep tu'ash nash mu-yor, heh t'nash-veh dvinsu dungau lamok s'udish, heh lu au has tevan-tor asleep dungau hal-tor svi', bind ish-veh, heh nem-tor ish-veh fi' dohn wuh hali if dungau lesh ish-veh vi' wuh eik panu.' wuh kosu vesh' satisfied k' nash; tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru's fo-wein-bearer, vi had puzhu-tor ek', vesh' friendly k' wuh nu'ri s'haile, heh informed ish-veh t' wuh bosh besau. 'i'll shitau wuh wufkau vi' ik business, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi' ogsu. Na' mu-yor au went tor sar-tak k' ish-veh ko-telsu na' wuh tsuri wak, heh lu she nahp ik au had tevan-tor asleep, she prah abru, tu'ash wuh svep, heh yi ti ne' va'ashiv. Wuh pi' ogsu, vi vesh' goh pretending tor nam-tor asleep, began tor lit'dhae svi' wuh pa'shik spes: 'sa-kan, tor me wuh doublet heh patch me wuh pantaloons, il i dungi rap wuh ker-thon-tor abru' ish-veh kaluk. I smote stehkuh na' veh salur. I pustau dahkuh masuk'veh, i katau maf veh unicorn, heh kum-tor wuh kwai boar, heh am i tor pthak eifa vi nam-tor standing s'udish wuh tvi-shal.' lu aifa sasu puzhu-tor wuh ogsu speaking thus, au vesh' overcome k' wuh lo'uk dread, heh sahr-tor u' kuv wuh kwai huntsman vesh' za' au, heh rim t' au would venture sovek-vel further tehnat ish-veh. Ni wuh pi' ogsu vesh' heh hafau wuh sa-te'kru tor wuh shaht t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Hansel heh gretel lerash k' wuh lo'uk laptra dwelt wuh ri donku-tor lapan-cutter k' ish-veh ko-telsu heh ish-veh dahkuh kanu. Wuh sa-kan vesh' puvutau hansel heh wuh ko-kan gretel. Au had pi' tor zeshaya heh tor shaya, heh wuh'wak lu lo'uk fam tevan-tor fi' wuh solektra, au kupi rai longer procure kauk kanok-gadik kap. I' lu au nahp abru' nash k' mu-yor svi' ish-veh sar-tak, heh tossed pa' svi' ish-veh anxiety, au groaned heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh ko-telsu: 'ra nam-tor tor shetau t' etek? Uf nam-tor etek tor yem-tor etwel ri donku-tor kanu, lu etek rai longer ma sovek-vel kauk na' ourselves?' 'i'll var-tor du ra, sa-telsu, ' kilko-tor wuh kosu, 'lehkuh-mal fa-gad asal etek dungi nem-tor wuh kanu si' vi' wuh laptra tor wilat ish-veh nam-tor wuh thickest; tra' etek dungi ta'hal wuh yon na' au, heh mazhiv-kur-tor tik t' au veh weht krus t' kap, heh yi etek dungi hal-tor tor etwel ar'kadan heh trasha au sa'awek. Au dungi ri talal wuh yut ha-kel va'ashiv, heh etek dungau nam-tor rid t' au.' 'rai, ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'i dungi ri tor ik; uf mokuhlek i lesh tor trasha t'nash-veh kanu sa'awek svi' wuh laptra?--wuh kwai animals would ak sarlah heh bezhun-masu au tor krus.' 'o, du duhsu!' leralmin-tor she, 'yi etek bolau ek' kehkuh tev-tor t' avon, du lau u' muhl sov-hali wuh planks na' etwel tevikeh-natuhn, ' heh she losrak ish-veh rai sochya abi' au consented. 'tonk'peh i olau maut sorry na' wuh ri donku-tor kanu, ek' wuh ka, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu. Wuh dahkuh kanu had isha ri vesh' kup tor yuk na' avon, heh had puzhu-tor ra ish-veh stepmother had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh sa-mekh. Gretel wept sfith(-) bezhun-masu, heh leralmin-tor tor hansel: 'i' ek' nam-tor abru' k' etek.' 'nam'uh hizhuk, gretel, ' leralmin-tor hansel, 'ri tor flakosh yourself, i dungi ak talal wuh yut tor gol'nev etek.' heh lu wuh hinek sular-ves had tevan-tor asleep, au prah abru, shitau fi' ish-veh pi' tor-pal, tu'ash wuh svep ne', heh crept s'udish. Wuh aikum min-tor brightly, heh wuh wan-kur da if ti svi' khom t' wuh kelek glittered spo' yeht haul-tukh qsu'lit. Hansel stooped heh tukh-tor wuh pi' abru'lik t' ish-veh tor-pal k' u' wehk u' au kupi prah svi'. Yi au went pla' heh leralmin-tor tor gretel: 'nam-tor comforted, tal-kam pi' ko-kai, heh yuk svi' sochya, oekon dungi ri forsake etek, ' heh au ti ne' va'ashiv svi' ish-veh sar-tak. Lu gad dawned, tonk'peh fa' wuh yel had risen, wuh kosu sarlah heh awoke wuh dahkuh kanu, taran: 'prah abru, du sluggards! Etek nam-tor going vi' wuh laptra tor zaprah lapan.' she mazhiv-kur-tor tik wuh pi' krus t' kap, heh leralmin-tor: 'tra' nam-tor vel na' ish-veh aru-yem, tonk'peh ri tor yokul ish-veh abru fa' yi, na' du dungi prah nothing else.' gretel nem-tor wuh kap ne' ish-veh apron, u' hansel had wuh da svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Yi au ek' eku si' teretuhr fi' wuh yut tor wuh laptra. Lu au had lates-tor wuh pen wak, hansel lam-tor fam dvun heh peeped pla' na' wuh kelek, heh did ni va'ashiv heh va'ashiv. Ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor: 'hansel, ra nam-tor du looking na' tra' heh staying za' na'? Vlitau attention, heh ri tor yen-tor uf tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh mal.' 'ah, sa-mekh, ' leralmin-tor hansel, 'i am looking na' t'nash-veh pi' wan-kur aushfa, if nam-tor sitting abru fi' wuh kamu, heh aitlu tor leralmin goodbye tor me.' wuh ko-telsu leralmin-tor: 'duhsu, ik nam-tor ri ish-veh pi' aushfa, ik nam-tor wuh asal yel if nam-tor shining fi' wuh vuzh-mev.' hansel, however, had ri vesh' looking pla' na' wuh aushfa, tonk'peh had vesh' constantly throwing veh t' wuh wan-kur da-kov s' ish-veh abru'lik fi' wuh fau-yut. Lu au had pulau wuh svitan t' wuh laptra, wuh sa-mekh leralmin-tor: 'i', kanu, tuh abru ein lapan, heh i dungi ta'hal wuh yon ik du lau ri nam-tor samu.' hansel heh gretel hoknau brushwood teretuhr, u' pid u' wuh pi' kunel. Wuh brushwood vesh' lighted, heh lu wuh yai vesh' yontau maut pid, wuh kosu leralmin-tor: 'i', kanu, ti yourselves ne' k' wuh yon heh shom, etek dungi hal-tor vi' wuh laptra heh tresahk ein lapan. Lu etek ma ovsoh, etek dungi sarlah pla' heh zaprah du maf.' hansel heh gretel hayal-tor k' wuh yon, heh lu aru sarlah, tik ate wuh pi' krus t' kap, heh u' au puzhu-tor wuh shad-kisheya t' wuh lapan-la'ash au pudva-tor ik ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' be'. Ish-veh vesh' ri wuh la'ash, however, tonk'peh wuh khlup if au had terau tor wuh withered lap if wuh salan vesh' blowing pla'rak heh fa'rak. Heh u' au had vesh' sitting such wuh wu wak, ish-veh bezhun a'ing k' zung, heh au tevan-tor sahris asleep. Lu na' kim-shah au awoke, ish-veh vesh' already gu'gelik mu-yor. Gretel began tor maf heh leralmin-tor: 'uf nam-tor etek tor prah s' wuh laptra i'?' tonk'peh hansel comforted ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'aishan bek-tor wuh pi', abi' wuh aikum has risen, heh yi etek dungi ak talal wuh yut.' heh lu wuh bosh aikum had risen, hansel nem-tor ish-veh pi' ko-kai k' wuh el'ru, heh zahal-tor wuh da if min-tor spo' newly-coined haul-tukh krus, heh gluvau au wuh yut. Au lates-tor wuh bosh mu-yor wu, heh k' shaya t' gad sarlah wuh'wak weht tor ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek. Au knocked na' wuh svep, heh lu wuh kosu tu'ash ish-veh heh gla-tor ik ish-veh vesh' hansel heh gretel, she leralmin-tor: 'du naughty kanu, po ma du yuk-tor ni wu svi' wuh laptra?--etek nahp du vesh' worla coming pla' na' ek'!' wuh sa-mekh, however, rejoiced, na' ish-veh had tresahk ish-veh tor wuh khaf-spol tor trasha au za' sa'awek. Ri wu afterwards, tra' vesh' wuh'wak weht lo'uk fam throughout wuh solektra, heh wuh kanu puzhu-tor ish-veh ko-mekh taran na' mu-yor tor ish-veh sa-mekh: 'kanok-vei nam-tor yokul va'ashiv, etek ma veh ulef loaf losrak, heh ik nam-tor wuh shaht. Wuh kanu bolau hal-tor, etek dungi nem-tor au weh-irak vi' wuh lapan, ni ik au dungi ri talal ish-veh yut si' va'ashiv; tra' nam-tor rai vath tvai t' saving ourselves!' wuh sasu's khaf-spol vesh' ras, heh au nahp: 'ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rom na' du tor thresh wuh kim-shah mouthful k' ish-veh kanu.' wuh kosu, however, would shroi tor nothing ik au had tor leralmin, tonk'peh scolded heh reproached ish-veh. Au vi leralmin-tor wuh bolau leralmin b, likewise, heh u' au had yielded wuh wuh'rak wak, au had tor tor ni wuh dahr wak isha. Wuh kanu, however, vesh' fam dvun kum'i heh had puzhu-tor wuh conversation. Lu wuh hinek sular-ves vesh' asleep, hansel va'ashiv prah abru, heh aitlu tor hal-tor si' heh abrashau da u' au had ovsoh fa', tonk'peh wuh kosu had klacha wuh svep, heh hansel kupi ri prah si'. Nevertheless au comforted ish-veh pi' ko-kai, heh leralmin-tor: 'ri tor maf, gretel, hal-tor tor yuk quietly, wuh rom oekon dungi gol'nev etek.' lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal sarlah wuh kosu, heh nem-tor wuh kanu s' ish-veh sar-tak. Ish-veh krus t' kap vesh' putan-tor tor au, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' fam dvun smaller do wuh wak fa'. Fi' wuh yut vi' wuh laptra hansel snaipau ish-veh svi' ish-veh abru'lik, heh k'ashiv lam-tor fam dvun heh threw wuh morsel fi' wuh solektra. 'hansel, po tor du pehkaya heh glazhau pauk?' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'hal-tor fi'.' 'i am looking pla' na' t'nash-veh pi' pigeon if nam-tor sitting fi' wuh kamu, heh aitlu tor leralmin goodbye tor me, ' kilko-tor hansel. 'duhsu!' leralmin-tor wuh kosu, 'ik nam-tor ri ish-veh pi' pigeon, ik nam-tor wuh asal yel ik nam-tor shining fi' wuh vuzh-mev.' hansel, however pi' k' pi', threw ek' wuh crumbs fi' wuh yut. Wuh kosu pufulag-tor wuh kanu fam dvun deeper vi' wuh laptra, wilat au had worla svi' ish-veh ha-tor vesh' fa'. Yi wuh lo'uk yon vesh' va'ashiv tor, heh wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor: 'aishan hayal-tor tra', du kanu, heh lu du nam-tor zungor du lau yuk wuh pi'; etek nam-tor going vi' wuh laptra tor tresahk lapan, heh svi' wuh khru lu etek nam-tor ovsoh, etek dungi sarlah heh zaprah du maf.' lu ish-veh vesh' aru, gretel thresh-tor ish-veh krus t' kap k' hansel, vi had scattered ish-veh k' wuh yut. Yi au tevan-tor asleep heh khru be' dvun-tor, tonk'peh kling sarlah tor wuh ri donku-tor kanu. Au did ri kum'i abi' ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik mu-yor, heh hansel comforted ish-veh pi' ko-kai heh leralmin-tor: 'aishan bek-tor, gretel, abi' wuh aikum she-tor, heh yi etek dungau gla-tor wuh crumbs t' kap if i ma strewn pa', au dungi gluvaya etek etwel yut ha-kel va'ashiv.' lu wuh aikum sarlah au eku si', tonk'peh au afer-tor rai crumbs, na' wuh wehk thousands t' kushel if hash-tor pa' svi' wuh lapan heh vunai had picked au ek' abru. Hansel leralmin-tor tor gretel: 'etek dungau ak talal wuh yut, ' tonk'peh au did ri talal ish-veh. Au lates-tor wuh bosh mu-yor heh ek' wuh thurai gad nuh' s' asal till khru, tonk'peh au did ri prah s' wuh laptra, heh vesh' maut k'avon, na' au had nothing tor yokul tonk'peh dahkuh il rehkuh nei-savas, if grew fi' wuh solektra. Heh u' au vesh' ni weary ik ish-veh mal would lesh au rai longer, au ti ne' ne'rak wuh lap heh tevan-tor asleep. Ish-veh vesh' i' rehkuh asal opi' au had losrak ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek. Au began tor lates va'ashiv, tonk'peh au kwon-hau-ov sarlah deeper vi' wuh laptra, heh kuv gol'nev did ri sarlah ak, au bolau tev-tor t' avon heh weariness. Lu ish-veh vesh' mid-gad, gla-tor au wuh vaksurik izh-wan-kur kushel sitting fi' wuh bough, if sang ni delightfully ik au lam-tor fam dvun heh shroi tor ish-veh. Heh lu its song vesh' abru', ish-veh sak-tor its rala heh flew maf fa' au, heh au zahal-tor ish-veh abi' au pulau wuh pi' kelek, fi' wuh kamu t' if ish-veh alighted; heh lu au betau wuh pi' kelek gla-tor au ik ish-veh vesh' torvau t' kap heh wein-tor k' cakes, tonk'peh ik wuh krani vesh' t' pa'shik slor-tukh. 'etek dungi eku tor ar'kadan fi' ik, ' leralmin-tor hansel, 'heh ma wuh rom yem. I dungi yokul wuh zeshau t' wuh kamu, heh du gretel, mokuhlek yokul ein t' wuh krani, ish-veh dungi zahvan slor.' hansel pulau abru abru', heh shau ska' wuh pi' t' wuh kamu tor ar'kadan uf ish-veh zahv-tor, heh gretel leant tehnat wuh krani heh nibbled na' wuh panes. Yi wuh mos spes maf-tor s' wuh parlour: 'nibble, nibble, gnaw, vi nam-tor nibbling na' t'nash-veh pi' kelek?' wuh kanu kilko-tor: 'wuh salan, wuh salan, wuh sha-ka-ri-pukeshta salan, ' heh went fi' eating rik' disturbing themselves. Hansel, vi tishau wuh zahvan t' wuh kamu, tore ne' wuh lo'uk krus t' ish-veh, heh gretel kwitau si' wuh bosh t' veh pauk krani-pane, hayal-tor ne', heh tizh-tor herself k' ish-veh. Suddenly wuh svep tu'ash, heh wuh kosu u' hinek u' wuh kunel, vi nenikau herself fi' crutches, sarlah creeping si'. Hansel heh gretel vesh' ni terribly koltha ik au kal-tor tevan ra au had svi' ish-veh el'ru. Wuh hinek kosu, however, nodded ish-veh patam, heh leralmin-tor: 'oh, du tal-kam kanu, vi has katau du la'? Tor sarlah svi', heh stay k' me. Rai klau dungau pavesh-tor tor du.' she nem-tor au fi' k' wuh el'ru, heh pufulag-tor au vi' ish-veh pi' kelek. Yi rom yem-tukh vesh' eku fa' au, thas heh pancakes, k' slor-tukh, savas, heh kov-sayas. Afterwards dahkuh takov pi' sar-tak vesh' wein-tor k' sok'i wan-kur linen, heh hansel heh gretel ti ne' svi' au, heh nahp au vesh' svi' sha-ka-ri. Wuh hinek kosu had goh pretended tor nam-tor ni ves; she vesh' svi' reality wuh wicked witch, vi ti svi' bek-tor na' kanu, heh had goh torvau wuh pi' kelek t' kap svi' zek tor entice au tra'. Lu wuh kan tevan-tor vi' ish-veh tepul, she pustau ish-veh, pufas-tor heh ate ish-veh, heh ik vesh' wuh gadzhak gad k' ish-veh. Witches ma yon-kur bezhun, heh fam yehat gla-tor irak, tonk'peh au ma wuh keen scent spo' wuh beasts, heh nam-tor aware lu komihn beings bes-tor be'. Lu hansel heh gretel sarlah vi' ish-veh neighbourhood, she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor k' malice, heh leralmin-tor mockingly: 'i ma au, au dungau ri stron me va'ashiv!' lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal fa' wuh kanu vesh' kum'i, she vesh' already abru, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh fi' t' au sleeping heh looking ni takov, k' ish-veh plump heh rosy nak she muttered tor herself: 'ik dungi nam-tor wuh dainty mouthful!' yi she seized hansel k' ish-veh shrivelled el'ru, lesh ish-veh vi' wuh pi' tihet, heh klacha ish-veh svi' za' wuh grated svep. Shei u' au lau, ish-veh would ri gol'nev ish-veh. Yi she went tor gretel, hutau ish-veh till she awoke, heh maf-tor: 'prah abru, kas'el vel, zaprah ein masu, heh fas-tor vel rom na' ish-veh sa-kai, au nam-tor svi' wuh tihet s'udish, heh nam-tor tor nam-tor tor thelik. Lu au nam-tor thelik, i dungi yokul ish-veh.' gretel began tor tusa bitterly, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ek' svi' vain, na' she vesh' punekwitau tor tor ra wuh wicked witch khartau. Heh i' wuh buhfik yem-tukh vesh' pufas-tor na' ri donku-tor hansel, tonk'peh gretel prah nothing tonk'peh crab-fo. Kanok asal wuh kosu crept tor wuh pi' tihet, heh maf-tor: 'hansel, sakadaya si' ish-veh ozh ik i lau olau kuv du dungi ak nam-tor thelik.' hansel, however, sakadau si' wuh pi' hinek tor ish-veh, heh wuh hinek kosu, vi had neik-ha'khlup bezhun, kupi ri gla-tor ish-veh, heh nahp ish-veh vesh' hansel's ozh, heh vesh' astonished ik tra' vesh' rai yut t' fattening ish-veh. Lu kehkuh wehk gad had hal-tor k', heh hansel fam dvun hafau wonil, she vesh' seized k' impatience heh would ri bek-tor sovek longer. 'i', yi, gretel, ' she maf-tor tor wuh ko-kan, 'stir yourself, heh katau ein masu. Kal-tor hansel nam-tor thelik il galat, fa-gad i dungi stau ish-veh, heh fas-tor ish-veh.' ah, uf wuh ri donku-tor pi' ko-kai did lament lu she had tor zaprah wuh masu, heh uf ish-veh bezhun-masu did yumaya ne' ish-veh nak! 'tal-kam oekon, tor gol'nev etek, ' she maf-tor. 'kuv wuh kwai beasts svi' wuh laptra had tonk'peh katau etek, etek dang na' sovek tav ma tev-tor teretuhr.' 'aishan potau ish-veh ralash tor yourself, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu, 'ish-veh skil-tor't gol'nev du na' ek'.' lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, gretel had tor hal-tor si' heh geldau abru wuh fas-matuhlek k' wuh masu, heh ta'hal wuh yon. 'etek dungi leipau wuh'rak, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu, 'i ma already falek-tor wuh fasek, heh kneaded wuh ned.' she kwitau ri donku-tor gretel si' tor wuh fasek, s' if yai t' yon vesh' already darting. 'creep svi', ' leralmin-tor wuh witch, 'heh gla-tor kuv ish-veh nam-tor properly falek-tor, ni ik etek mokuhlek shitau wuh kap svi'.' heh wuh'wak gretel vesh' svi'udish, she intended tor ikap-tor wuh fasek heh kal-tor ish-veh leipau svi' ish-veh, heh yi she would yokul ish-veh, nuh'. Tonk'peh gretel gla-tor ra she had svi' kashek, heh leralmin-tor: 'i ri tor fai-tor uf i am tor tor ish-veh; uf tor i prah svi'?' 'silly kushel, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu. 'wuh svep nam-tor suk' hiyet; aishan glazhau, i mokuhlek prah svi' myself!' heh she crept abru heh kwit ish-veh patam vi' wuh fasek. Yi gretel mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh kwitaya ik drove ish-veh irak vi' ish-veh, heh ikap-tor wuh shek-tukh svep, heh terau wuh terk. Oh! Yi she began tor vlut ved horribly, tonk'peh gretel sahr-tor maf heh wuh godless witch vesh' miserably yontau tor tevakh. Gretel, however, sahr-tor spo' igen-wesh tor hansel, tu'ash ish-veh pi' tihet, heh maf-tor: 'hansel, etek nam-tor korsau! Wuh hinek witch nam-tor tevik!' yi hansel sprang spo' wuh kushel s' its kraisek lu wuh svep nam-tor tu'ash. Uf au did rejoice heh nartaya tik vath, heh tam pa' heh shok tik vath! Heh u' au had rai longer sovek bolaya tor pthak ish-veh, au went vi' wuh witch's kelek, heh svi' kanok teruk tra' lam-tor tuf bosh t' pearls heh ek'zer. 'aifa nam-tor irak weh-rom do da!' leralmin-tor hansel, heh kwit vi' ish-veh abru'lik whatever kupi nam-tor prah svi', heh gretel leralmin-tor: 'i, nuh', dungi nem-tor vel ha-kel k' me, ' heh boshau ish-veh pinafore bosh. 'tonk'peh i' etek bolau nam-tor ska', ' leralmin-tor hansel, 'ik etek lau prah s' wuh witch's laptra.' lu au had lates-tor na' dahkuh wadan, sarlah au tor wuh lo'uk sakadaya t' masu. 'etek fam yehat tuhs, ' leralmin-tor hansel, 'gla-tor nash-veh rai ash'ya-plank, heh rai mesut.' 'heh tra' nam-tor isha rai mes-hali, ' kilko-tor gretel, 'tonk'peh wuh wan-kur duck nam-tor mahalan tra': kuv i ya'akash ish-veh, she dungi gol'nev etek abru'.' yi she maf-tor: 'pi' duck, pi' duck, dost thou gla-tor, hansel heh gretel nam-tor waiting na' thee? Tra''s worla wuh plank, il mesut svi' glan, nem-tor etek mes' fi' thy pla' ni wan-kur.' wuh duck sarlah tor au, heh hansel hayal-tor himself fi' its pla', heh var-tor ish-veh ko-kai tor hayal-tor k' ish-veh. 'rai, ' kilko-tor gretel, 'ik dungi nam-tor nuh' ras na' wuh pi' duck; she dungau nem-tor etek mes', veh po' wuh vath.' wuh rom pi' duck did ni, heh lu au vesh' wuh'wak safely mes' heh had lates-tor na' wuh pen wak, wuh laptra seemed tor nam-tor weht heh weht familiar tor au, heh na' wu-vath gla-tor au s' afar ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek. Yi au began tor sahr-tor, rushed vi' wuh parlour, heh threw themselves pauk ish-veh sa-mekh's talu. Wuh sasu had ri fainu veh kunli wadan opi' au had losrak wuh kanu svi' wuh laptra; wuh kosu, however, vesh' tevik. Gretel emptied ish-veh pinafore abi' pearls heh taluhk kov sahr-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal, heh hansel threw veh handful po' wuh'ashiv s' ish-veh abru'lik tor hau tor au. Yi ek' anxiety vesh' na' wuh shaht, heh au ha-tor teretuhr svi' buhfik happiness. T'nash-veh var nam-tor ovsoh, tra' sahr-tor wuh aushfa; whosoever kum-tor ish-veh, lau tor himself wuh suk' ausachya taik s' ish-veh. Wuh aushfa, wuh kushel, heh wuh kahm wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak, wuh aushfa, wuh kushel, heh wuh kahm, svi-tor vi' partnership heh eku abru kelek teretuhr. Na' wuh akarshif ek' went muhl; au ha-tor svi' lo'uk comfort, heh smusma ni irak u' kup tor hau considerably tor ish-veh mahr-kel. Wuh kushel's gu-vam vesh' tor hash-tor kanok-gadik vi' wuh lapan heh katau svi' hal-tukh; wuh aushfa zaprah wuh masu, heh wuh kahm gla-tor tor wuh fasan. Lu sutra nam-tor nuh' muhl ska' au kwon-hau-ov palikau tor wu na' vel uzh. Heh ni sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun, ik wuh kushel, du' si' veh gad, ragel-tor wuh katravahsu kushel, tor ik au boastfully expatiated fi' wuh marom'es t' ish-veh household arrangements. Tonk'peh wuh vath kushel sneered na' ish-veh na' hasu wuh ri donku-tor simpleton, vi did ek' wuh lerash ar'kadan, du' wuh vath dahkuh stayed na' ha-kel heh had wuh rom wak t' ish-veh. Na', lu wuh aushfa had tor wuh yon heh zaprah svi' wuh masu, she kupi retire vi' ish-veh pi' tvi-shal heh shom abi' ish-veh vesh' wak tor eku wuh pasu. Wuh kahm had goh tor glantau wuh sunil tor gla-tor ik wuh yem-tukh vesh' properly pufas-tor, heh lu ish-veh vesh' be' aru-yem-wak, au aishan threw himself vi' wuh broth, il padukau svi' heh si' among wuh sazh rehkuh il kehkuh wak, heh tra' au vesh', buttered, heh salted, heh pok tor nam-tor dvin-tor. Yi, lu wuh kushel sarlah ha-kel heh had laid aside ish-veh burden, au hayal-tor ne' tor pasu, heh lu au had shahtau ish-veh yem, au kupi yuk ish-veh boshaya till wuh zahalik asal: heh ik vesh' really wuh maut delightful ha'kiv. Vi-yumuk k' eifa remarks, wuh kushel thurai asal klee'fah tor katau svi' wuh lapan, telling wuh vath ik au had vesh' ish-veh dvinsu wu hiyet, heh had vesh' wuh duhsu vi' wuh bargain, heh ik ish-veh vesh' i' wak tor tor wuh rubah, heh tor ar'kadan ein vath yut t' arranging wuh ar'kadan. Eit'jae heh pray u' wuh aushfa heh wuh kahm lau, ish-veh vesh' t' rai nam-tor-tor; wuh kushel hafau trensu t' wuh situation, heh wuh venture had tor nam-tor tor. Au therefore drew lots, heh ish-veh tevan-tor tor wuh kahm tor katau svi' wuh lapan, tor wuh aushfa tor fas-tor, heh tor wuh kushel tor zaprah wuh masu. Heh i' ra pavesh-tor? Wuh kahm palikau svi' psthan t' lapan, wuh kushel tor wuh yon, heh wuh aushfa shitau fi' wuh sunil, heh yi aifa dahkuh bek-tor till wuh kahm fun-tor k' wuh hal-tukh na' wuh zahalik gad. Tonk'peh wuh kahm hafau ni wu maf, ik au became uneasy, heh wuh kushel flew si' tor ragel-tor ish-veh. Au had ri flown irak, however, lu sarlah ish-veh mes' wuh dog vi, having ragel-tor wuh kahm, had fudau ish-veh u' ish-veh legitimate booty, heh ni seized heh vitem-tor ish-veh. Wuh kushel complained tor wuh dog t' nash sai-famik-limuk-tor robbery, tonk'peh nothing au leralmin-tor vesh' t' sovek avail, na' wuh dog kilko-tor ik au afer-tor riyeht credentials fi' wuh kahm, heh ik vesh' wuh utvau ish-veh ha'kiv had vesh' forfeited. Au abrashau wuh lapan, heh flew sadly ha-kel, heh var-tor wuh aushfa ek' au had gla-tor heh puzhu-tor. Au vesh' fi' maut unhappy, tonk'peh sep-wafikh tor tor wuh buhfik t' vel heh tor hafau k' veh wuh'ashiv. Ni i' wuh kushel eku wuh pasu, heh wuh aushfa glazhau po' wuh yem-tukh heh, wishing tor dator ish-veh svi' wuh ka yut u' wuh kahm, k' rolling svi' heh si' among wuh sazh tor alem heh butter au, she spen-tor vi' wuh sunil; tonk'peh she pehkau pen wu fa' she pulau wuh lanet, having already parted ri goh k' ish-veh wadi heh isachya, tonk'peh isha k' ha'kiv. Presently wuh kushel sarlah svi' heh aitlu tor dvin-tor abru wuh aru-yem, tonk'peh au kupi nowhere gla-tor wuh fas-tor. Svi' ish-veh vikayek heh flurry, au threw wuh lapan la' heh tra' pa' wuh lan-tol, puvutau heh pstha, tonk'peh rai fas-tor vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor. Yi ein t' wuh lapan ik had vesh' carelessly lehm-tor ne', kum-tor yon heh began tor yon. Wuh kushel hastened tor zaprah ein masu, tonk'peh ish-veh pail tevan-tor vi' wuh muhl, heh au po' ish-veh, heh u' au vesh' unable tor recover himself, au vesh' mastevau. Ko-mekh holle wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak tra' vesh' wuh kir'an vi had dahkuh daughters; veh t' au vesh' vaksurik heh industrious, wuh vath watosh heh kas'el. Wuh ko-mekh, however, ashau wuh watosh heh kas'el veh buhfik, fai'ei she vesh' ish-veh sha' ko-fu, heh ni wuh vath, vi vesh' goh ish-veh stepdaughter, vesh' tor tor tor ek' wuh ar'kadan t' wuh kelek, heh vesh' ved wuh cinderella t' wuh skan. Ish-veh stepmother satau ish-veh si' kanok gad tor hayal-tor k' wuh muhl svi' wuh pid fau-yut, tra' tor padan abi' she tor ish-veh ozh khafau. I' ish-veh chanced veh gad ik ein khaf tevan-tor fi' tor wuh magu, heh u' wuh ko-kan pehkau abru' wuh muhl tor pu-tor ish-veh ska', wuh magu suddenly sprang si' t' ish-veh el'ru heh tevan-tor vi' wuh muhl. She sahr-tor ha-kel maf-tor tor var-tor t' ish-veh misfortune, tonk'peh ish-veh stepmother stariben harshly tor ish-veh, heh po' giving ish-veh wuh khrashik scolding, leralmin-tor unkindly, 'u' du ma kal-tor wuh magu tevan vi' wuh muhl du lau hal-tor yourself heh zaprah ish-veh si'.' wuh ko-kan went pla' tor wuh muhl ri fai-tor ra tor tor, heh na' kim-shah svi' ish-veh flakosh she spen-tor vi' wuh masu po' wuh magu. She vokau nothing weht abi' she awoke heh afer-tor herself svi' wuh vaksurik ne-yartra, bosh t' sunshine, heh k' countless svai svai-tu-ashya svi' kanok kharat. She lates-tor abru' wuh ne-yartra, heh presently sarlah ish-veh fi-tor wuh leipausu's fasek bosh t' kap, heh wuh loaves lit'dhae tor ish-veh, 'nem-tor etek si', nem-tor etek si', il alas! Etek dungau nam-tor yontau tor wuh cinder; etek vesh' leipau k'fai wu ago.' ni she nem-tor wuh kap-hilek heh drew au ek' si'. She went fi' wuh pi' weh-irak, till sarlah ish-veh tor wuh lap bosh t' savas. 'hutau me, hutau me, i pray, ' maf-tor wuh lap; 't'nash-veh savas, veh heh ek', nam-tor piyah.' ni she hutau wuh lap, heh wuh savas sarlah tevan-tor ne' fi-tor ish-veh spo' sov-masu; tonk'peh she fator shaking abi' tra' vesh' ri wuh single savas losrak fi-tor ish-veh. Yi she carefully hoknau wuh savas teretuhr svi' wuh tuh heh lates-tor fi' va'ashiv. Wuh thurai vel sarlah ish-veh tor vesh' wuh pi' kelek, heh tra' gla-tor ish-veh wuh hinek kosu looking si', k' such suk zud, ik she vesh' terrified, heh da-tor tor sahr-tor maf. Tonk'peh wuh hinek kosu puvutau po' ish-veh, 'ra nam-tor du kwes t', tal-kam kan? Stay k' me; kuv du dungi tor wuh ar'kadan t' t'nash-veh kelek properly na' me, i dungi tor du maut kunli. Du bolau nam-tor maut tun-bosh, however, tor tor t'nash-veh sar-tak svi' wuh gas'rak yut, na' i istaya du kwon-hau-ov tor hutau ish-veh thoroughly, ni ik wuh kan hash-tor pa'; yi au leralmin, ne' tra' svi' wuh panu, ik ish-veh nam-tor snowing; na' i am ko-mekh holle.' wuh hinek kosu stariben ni kindly, ik wuh ko-kan summoned abru courage heh sep-wafikh tor svi-tor vi' ish-veh dvin. She nem-tor tun tor tor kanok-vei fupa s' wuh hinek kosu's nufai-tor heh kanok wak she tor wuh sar-tak she hutau ish-veh k' ek' ish-veh lau, ni ik wuh kan flew pa' spo' ni wehk snowflakes. Wuh hinek kosu vesh' u' rom u' ish-veh zhit: she worla stariben angrily tor ish-veh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh roast heh kan-tor kahm kanok gad. Ni she stayed fi' k' ko-mekh holle na' ein wak, heh yi she began tor tor'ovau unhappy. She kupi ri palikauk var-tor po she olau maf, tonk'peh she became d'wonil na' kim-shah t' lo'uk longing tor hal-tor ha-kel; yi she fai-tor she vesh' homesick, hi she vesh' wuh thousand wak weh-rom ska' k' ko-mekh holle do k' ish-veh ko-mekh heh ko-kai. Po' waiting awhile, she went tor ko-mekh holle heh leralmin-tor, 'i am ni homesick, ik i fam yehat stay k' du sovek longer, na' hi i am ni kunli la', i bolau fun tor t'nash-veh sha' sutra.' yi ko-mekh holle leralmin-tor, 'i am sanoi ik du dang aitlun tor hal-tor pla' tor ish-veh sha' sutra, heh u' du ma dvin-tor me ni muhl heh faithfully, i dungi nem-tor du ha-kel myself.' thereupon she pufulag-tor wuh ko-kan k' wuh el'ru abru tor wuh sax'ksei temep-sharu. Wuh temep vesh' tu'ash, heh u' wuh ko-kan be' dvun-tor k'fai, wuh mashulayek t' pi-maat-tukh tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh, heh wuh pi-maat-tukh clung tor ish-veh, ni ik she vesh' wein-tor k' ish-veh s' patam tor ash'ya. 'ik nam-tor wuh reward na' ish-veh industry, ' leralmin-tor ko-mekh holle, heh u' she stariben she handed ish-veh wuh magu if she had eku-tor vi' wuh muhl. Wuh temep vesh' yi a'ing, heh wuh ko-kan afer-tor herself pla' svi' wuh hinek panu beyik ish-veh ko-mekh's kelek. U' she svi-tor wuh courtyard, wuh cock vi vesh' perched fi' wuh muhl, puvutau si': 'cock-wuh-doodle-doo! Ish-veh pi-maat-kur ko-fu's sarlah pla' tor du.' yi she went svi' tor ish-veh ko-mekh heh ko-kai, heh u' she vesh' ni richly wein-tor k' pi-maat-tukh, au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh lamekh welcome. She related tor au ek' ik had pavesh-tor, heh lu wuh ko-mekh puzhu-tor uf she had sarlah k' ish-veh lo'uk don-tak, she nahp she dang spo' ish-veh watosh, kas'el ko-fu tor hal-tor heh ar'kadan ish-veh fortune. Ni she tor wuh ko-kai hal-tor heh hayal-tor k' wuh muhl heh padan, heh wuh ko-kan pricked ish-veh ozh heh kwit ish-veh el'ru vi' wuh thorn-bush, ni ik she lau eku ein khaf fi' tor wuh magu; yi she threw ish-veh vi' wuh muhl, heh spen-tor svi' herself. Spo' ish-veh ko-kai she awoke svi' wuh vaksurik ne-yartra, heh lates-tor abru' ish-veh till sarlah ish-veh tor wuh fasek. 'nem-tor etek si', nem-tor etek si', il alas! Etek dungau nam-tor yontau tor wuh cinder; etek vesh' leipau k'fai wu ago, ' maf-tor wuh loaves u' fa'. Tonk'peh wuh kas'el ko-kan kilko-tor, 'tor du nah-tor i am going tor kitork t'nash-veh el'ru na' du?' heh lates-tor fi'. Presently sarlah ish-veh tor wuh savas-lap. 'hutau me, hutau me, i pray; t'nash-veh savas, veh heh ek', nam-tor piyah, ' ish-veh maf-tor. Tonk'peh she goh kilko-tor, 'wuh nice vel tor ya'akash me tor tor, veh t' wuh savas lau tevan fi' t'nash-veh patam, ' heh be' dvun-tor fi'. Na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor ko-mekh holle's kelek, heh u' she had puzhu-tor ek' pa' wuh suk zud s' ish-veh ko-kai, she vesh' ri kwes t' au, heh engaged herself rik' vohtaya tor wuh hinek kosu. Wuh wuh'rak gad she vesh' maut obedient heh industrious, heh pidesh herself tor sanoi ko-mekh holle, na' she nahp t' wuh pi-maat-tukh she dang prah svi' fun. Wuh thurai gad, however, she began tor dawdle abru' ish-veh ar'kadan, heh wuh wuh gad she vesh' weht idle fam dvun; yi she began tor ti svi' sar-tak svi' wuh asal heh klee'fah tor prah abru. Weh-rasahkos fam dvun, she neglected tor tor wuh hinek kosu's sar-tak properly, heh forgot tor hutau ish-veh ni ik wuh kan lau hash-tor pa'. Ni ko-mekh holle maut ak prah zungor t' ish-veh, heh var-tor ish-veh she lau hal-tor. Wuh kas'el ko-kan vesh' delighted na' nash, heh nahp tor herself, 'wuh pi-maat-tukh dungi ak nam-tor t'nash-veh.' ko-mekh holle pufulag-tor ish-veh, u' she had pufulag-tor ish-veh ko-kai, tor wuh sax'ksei temep-sharu; tonk'peh u' she vesh' be' dvun-tor k'fai, instead t' wuh mashulayek t' pi-maat-tukh, wuh lo'uk bucketful t' ralash sarlah pouring abru' ish-veh. 'ik nam-tor svi' fun na' ish-veh dvin, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu, heh she ikap-tor wuh temep. Ni wuh kas'el ko-kan had tor hal-tor ha-kel wein-tor k' ralash, heh wuh cock fi' wuh muhl puvutau si' u' gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh: 'cock-wuh-doodle-doo! Ish-veh kitork ko-fu's sarlah pla' tor du.' tonk'peh, ar'kadan ra she would, she kupi ri prah wuh ralash ska' heh ish-veh terpau tor ish-veh u' wu u' she ha-tor. Pi' yon-kur-taik [pi' yon-kur riding fash] wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak tra' vesh' wuh tal-kam pi' ko-kan vi vesh' ashau k' kanok-veh vi glazhau na' ish-veh, tonk'peh danik t' ek' k' ish-veh ko'mekh-il, heh tra' vesh' nothing ik she would ri ma putan-tor tor wuh kan. Wuh'wak she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh pi' taik t' yon-kur velvet, if suited ish-veh ni muhl ik she would worla sai-vel-tor sovek-kitok; ni she vesh' kwon-hau-ov puvutau 'pi' yon-kur-taik.' veh gad ish-veh ko-mekh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'sarlah, pi' yon-kur-taik, la' nam-tor wuh krus t' cake heh wuh mashek t' wine; nem-tor au tor ish-veh ko'mekh-il, she nam-tor has-bosh heh kobat, heh au dungi tor ish-veh rom. Eku si' fa' ish-veh prah fal, heh lu du nam-tor going, lates nicely heh quietly heh ri tor sahr-tor ska' wuh yut, il du lau tevan heh shaya wuh mashek, heh yi ish-veh ko'mekh-il dungi prah nothing; heh lu du hal-tor vi' ish-veh tvi-shal, ri tor yen-tor tor leralmin, "rom asal", heh ri tor peep vi' kanok teruk fa' du tor ish-veh.' 'i dungi nem-tor lo'uk tun, ' leralmin-tor pi' yon-kur-taik tor ish-veh ko-mekh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh. Wuh ko'mekh-il ha-tor si' svi' wuh lapan, ulef wuh league s' wuh pi'kahr, heh aishan u' pi' yon-kur-taik svi-tor wuh lapan, wuh wolf ragel-tor ish-veh. Yon-kur-taik did ri fai-tor ra wuh wicked creature au vesh', heh vesh' mokov kwes t' ish-veh. 'rom gad, pi' yon-kur-taik, ' leralmin-tor au. 'nemaiyo kindly, wolf.' 'whither maf ni lehkuh-mal, pi' yon-kur-taik?' 'tor t'nash-veh ko'mekh-il's.' 'ra ma du prah svi' ish-veh apron?' 'cake heh wine; za-gad vesh' leipaun-gad, ni ri donku-tor has-bosh ko'mekh-il nam-tor tor ma vel rom, tor tor ish-veh stronger.' 'wilat tor ish-veh ko'mekh-il ha-tor, pi' yon-kur-taik?' 'wuh rom yonuk t' wuh league weh-irak fi' svi' wuh lapan; ish-veh kelek lam-tor ne' wuh rehkuh suk oak-lap, wuh kov-sayas-lap nam-tor aishan ne'; du surely bolau fai-tor ish-veh, ' kilko-tor pi' yon-kur-taik. Wuh wolf nahp tor himself: 'ra wuh sival nu'ri creature! Ra wuh nice plump mouthful--she dungi nam-tor weh-rom tor yokul do wuh hinek kosu. I bolau bae'cok craftily, ni u' tor kum fi'.' ni au lates-tor na' wuh pen wak k' wuh vla t' pi' yon-kur-taik, heh yi au leralmin-tor: 'gla-tor, pi' yon-kur-taik, uf takov wuh svai nam-tor pa' la'--po tor du ri glazhau pauk? I dva-tor, nuh', ik du ri tor zhu-tor uf sweetly wuh pi' kushel nam-tor uralaun; du lates gravely bi' u' kuv du vesh' going tor shi'oren, du' kanok-vei else si' la' svi' wuh lapan nam-tor merry.' pi' yon-kur-taik ashenau ish-veh bezhun, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh sunbeams taman la' heh tra' k'fai wuh lap, heh takov svai growing kanok-wilat, she nahp: 'suppose i nem-tor ko'mekh-il wuh sluk nosegay; ik would sanoi ish-veh nuh'. Ish-veh nam-tor ni lehkuh-mal svi' wuh gad ik i dungau fam dvun prah tra' svi' rom wak'; heh ni she sahr-tor s' wuh yut vi' wuh lapan tor glazhau na' svai. Heh whenever she had picked veh, she fancied ik gla-tor ish-veh wuh fam dvun prettier veh weh-irak fi', heh sahr-tor po' ish-veh, heh ni prah deeper heh deeper vi' wuh lapan. Meanwhile wuh wolf sahr-tor zehik tor wuh ko'mekh-il's kelek heh knocked na' wuh svep. 'vi nam-tor tra'?' 'pi' yon-kur-taik, ' kilko-tor wuh wolf. 'she nam-tor bringing cake heh wine; tu'ash wuh svep.' 'abertau wuh kuhr, ' puvutau si' wuh ko'mekh-il, 'i am nuh' kobat, heh fam yehat prah abru.' wuh wolf abertau wuh kuhr, wuh svep sprang tu'ash, heh rik' taran wuh zhit au went zehik tor wuh ko'mekh-il's sar-tak, heh katau ish-veh. Yi au shitau fi' ish-veh sai-vel, sai-vel-tor himself svi' ish-veh taik laid himself svi' sar-tak heh drew wuh curtains. Pi' yon-kur-taik, however, had vesh' sahran pa' picking svai, heh lu she had hoknau ni wehk ik she kupi lesh rai weht, she vokau ish-veh ko'mekh-il, heh eku si' fi' wuh yut tor ish-veh. She vesh' ak'wikmun tor talal wuh cottage-svep standing tu'ash, heh lu she went vi' wuh tvi-shal, she had such wuh flekh olaya ik she leralmin-tor tor herself: 'oh tal-kam! Uf uneasy i olau nash-gad, heh na' vath wak i spo' hasu k' ko'mekh-il ni mau.' she puvutau si': 'rom asal, ' tonk'peh poprah rai kilko-srashiv; ni she went tor wuh sar-tak heh drew pla' wuh curtains. Tra' ti ish-veh ko'mekh-il k' ish-veh taik seshau irak abru' ish-veh limuk, heh looking maut flekh. 'oh! Ko'mekh-il, ' she leralmin-tor, 'ra suk' kaluk du ma!' 'wuh weh-rom tor zhu-tor du k', t'nash-veh kan, ' vesh' wuh kilko. 'tonk'peh, ko'mekh-il, ra suk' bezhun du ma!' she leralmin-tor. 'wuh weh-rom tor gla-tor du k', t'nash-veh tal-kam.' 'tonk'peh, ko'mekh-il, ra suk el'ru du ma!' 'wuh weh-rom tor teraya-martaya du k'.' 'oh! Tonk'peh, ko'mekh-il, ra wuh terrible suk' ru'lut du ma!' 'wuh weh-rom tor yokul du k'!' heh scarcely had wuh wolf leralmin-tor nash, do k' veh bound au vesh' s' sar-tak heh vitem-tor abru yon-kur-taik. Lu wuh wolf had appeased ish-veh yeht-avon, au ti ne' va'ashiv svi' wuh sar-tak, tevan-tor asleep heh began tor snore maut ral. Wuh huntsman vesh' aishan be' dvun-tor wuh kelek, heh nahp tor himself: 'uf wuh hinek kosu nam-tor snoring! I bolau aishan gla-tor kuv she aitlu sovek-vel.' ni au went vi' wuh tvi-shal, heh lu au sarlah tor wuh sar-tak, gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh wolf vesh' lying svi' ish-veh. 'tor i talal du la', du hinek sinner!' leralmin-tor au. 'i ma wu sought du!' yi aishan u' au vesh' going tor yon na' ish-veh, ish-veh paresh-tor tor ish-veh ik wuh wolf lau ma katau wuh ko'mekh-il, heh ik she lau fam dvun nam-tor korsau, ni au did ri yon, tonk'peh nem-tor wuh shif t' scissors, heh began tor tresahk tu'ash wuh skaun-sa'haf t' wuh sleeping wolf. Lu au had tor dahkuh snips, gla-tor ish-veh wuh pi' yon-kur-taik shining, heh yi au tor dahkuh snips weht, heh wuh pi' ko-kan sprang si', maf-tor: 'ah, uf koltha i ma vesh'! Uf gu'gelik ish-veh vesh' svi'udish wuh wolf'; heh po' ik wuh aged ko'mekh-il sasarlah alive isha, tonk'peh scarcely kup tor esh-tor. Yon-kur-taik, however, sahris zaprah lo'uk kov k' if au boshau wuh wolf's nehg, heh lu au awoke, au aitlu tor sahr-tor maf, tonk'peh wuh kov vesh' ni ras ik au neshau na' wuh'wak, heh tevan-tor tevik. Yi ek' rehkuh vesh' delighted. Wuh huntsman drew ska' wuh wolf's wadi heh went ha-kel k' ish-veh; wuh ko'mekh-il ate wuh cake heh drank wuh wine if yon-kur-taik had katau, heh zaprah-tor, tonk'peh yon-kur-taik nahp tor herself: 'u' wu u' i ha-tor, i dungi worla k' myself trasha wuh yut, tor sahr-tor vi' wuh lapan, lu t'nash-veh ko-mekh has zadik me tor tor ni.' ish-veh isha related ik wuh'wak lu yon-kur-taik vesh' va'ashiv taking cakes tor wuh hinek ko'mekh-il, wuh'ashiv wolf stariben tor ish-veh, heh ar'kada tor entice ish-veh s' wuh yut. Yon-kur-taik, however, vesh' fi' ish-veh klashausu, heh went zehik fa'rak fi' ish-veh yut, heh var-tor ish-veh ko'mekh-il ik she had ragel-tor wuh wolf, heh ik au had leralmin-tor 'rom asal' tor ish-veh, tonk'peh k' such wuh wicked glazhau svi' ish-veh bezhun, ik kuv au had ri vesh' fi' wuh tsuri fau-yut she vesh' ac'ruth au would ma yokul ish-veh abru. 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko'mekh-il, 'etek dungi ikap-tor wuh svep, ik au lau ri sarlah svi'.' ak afterwards wuh wolf knocked, heh maf-tor: 'tu'ash wuh svep, ko'mekh-il, i am pi' yon-kur-taik, heh am bringing du ein cakes.' tonk'peh au did ri stariben, il tu'ash wuh svep, ni wuh zhai-kur-hisahk vazgau dah'wak il thrice pauk wuh kelek, heh na' kim-shah spen-tor fi' wuh kamu, intending tor bek-tor abi' yon-kur-taik went ha-kel svi' wuh khru, heh yi tor vazgau po' ish-veh heh katau ish-veh svi' wuh mu'khlup'es. Tonk'peh wuh ko'mekh-il gla-tor ra vesh' svi' ish-veh nahp. Svi' khom t' wuh kelek vesh' wuh lo'uk kov trough, ni she leralmin-tor tor wuh kan: 'nem-tor wuh pail, yon-kur-taik; i tor ein kahm za-gad, ni lesh wuh masu svi' if i kan-tor au tor wuh trough.' yon-kur-taik lesh abi' wuh lo'uk trough vesh' ved bosh. Yi wuh fnish-tor t' wuh kahm pulau wuh wolf, heh au sniffed heh peeped ne', heh na' kim-shah sakadau si' ish-veh talu ni irak ik au kupi rai longer potau ish-veh footing heh began tor trel, heh trel-tor ne' s' wuh kamu zehik vi' wuh lo'uk trough, heh vesh' mastevau. Tonk'peh yon-kur-taik went joyously ha-kel, heh kling ek'wak did sovek-vel tor klau ish-veh va'ashiv. Wuh robber bridegroom tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh miller vi had veh vaksurik ko-fu, heh u' she vesh' grown abru, au vesh' anxious ik she dang nam-tor muhl telik heh tanilau na'. Au leralmin-tor tor himself, 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor wuh wuh'rak suitable sasu vi sarlah heh ya'akash na' ish-veh el'ru.' ri wu po' wuh suitor saudau, heh u' au saudau tor nam-tor maut don-ka heh wuh miller kupi gla-tor nothing svi' ish-veh k' if tor talal lafot, au betrothed ish-veh ko-fu tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh ko-kan did ri palutunau wuh sasu u' wuh ko-kan ought tor palutunau ish-veh betrothed sa-telsu. She did ri olau ik she kupi sahrafel ish-veh, heh she kupi ri glazhau na' ish-veh il nah-tor t' ish-veh rik' wuh inward ak'shem-hutau. Veh gad au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'du ma ri wi vlitau me wuh yaret, hi etek ma vesh' betrothed na' ein wak.' 'i ri tor fai-tor wilat ish-veh kelek nam-tor, ' she kilko-tor. 't'nash-veh kelek nam-tor si' tra' svi' wuh gu'gelik laptra, ' au leralmin-tor. She ar'kada tor tobeg herself k' taran ik she would ri nam-tor kup tor talal wuh yut thither. Ish-veh betrothed goh kilko-tor, 'du bolau sarlah heh gla-tor me thurai gad; i ma already invited be'hai'la na' ik gad, heh ik du lau ri lafosh wuh yut, i dungi strew vitush bi' wuh yut.' lu gad sarlah, heh ish-veh vesh' wak na' wuh ko-kan tor palikaya, wuh olaya t' dread sarlah abru' ish-veh if she kupi ri danau, heh ik she lau nam-tor kup tor talal ish-veh yut va'ashiv, she boshau ish-veh abru'lik k' peas heh lentils tor sprinkle fi' wuh solektra u' she went bi'. Fi' reaching wuh entrance tor wuh laptra she afer-tor wuh yut strewed k' vitush, heh aifa she zahal-tor, throwing ne' ein peas fi' either vla t' ish-veh na' kanok ash she nem-tor. She lates-tor wuh bosh gad abi' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh deepest, darkest krus t' wuh laptra. Tra' gla-tor ish-veh wuh lonely kelek, looking ni grim heh mysterious, ik ish-veh did ri sanoi ish-veh na' ek'. She ash-tor svi'udish, tonk'peh ri wuh soul vesh' tor nam-tor gla-tor, heh wuh lo'uk silence reigned throughout. Suddenly wuh spes maf-tor: 'da-tor pla', da-tor pla', nu'ri maiden rom, svizh-tor ri svi' nash murderers' lair.' wuh ko-kan glazhau abru heh gla-tor ik wuh spes sarlah s' wuh kushel hanging svi' wuh kraisek fi' wuh temok. Va'ashiv ish-veh maf-tor: 'da-tor pla', da-tor pla', nu'ri maiden rom, svizh-tor ri svi' nash murderers' lair.' wuh ko-kan be' dvun-tor fi', going s' tvi-shal tor tvi-shal t' wuh kelek, tonk'peh au vesh' ek' herbosh, heh fam dvun gla-tor ish-veh kling. Na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor wuh cellar, heh tra' hayal-tor wuh maut, maut hinek kosu, vi kupi ri potau ish-veh patam s' shaking. 'mokuhlek du var-tor me, ' ya'akash wuh ko-kan, 'kuv t'nash-veh betrothed sa-telsu ha-tor la'?' 'ah, du ri donku-tor kan, ' kilko-tor wuh hinek kosu, 'ra wuh shi na' du tor sarlah tor! Nash nam-tor wuh murderers' den. Du nah-tor yourself wuh ugau bride, heh ik ish-veh kal'i'farr dungi ak nem-tor shi, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor k' tevakh ik du dungi potau ish-veh kal'i'farr gadzhak. Glazhau, tor gla-tor du ik suk fas-matuhlek t' masu if i am obliged tor potau fi' wuh yon! U' ak u' au ma du svi' ish-veh tepul au dungi stau du rik' mercy, heh fas-tor heh yokul du, na' au nam-tor eaters t' sasu. Kuv i did ri nem-tor pity fi' du heh korsau du, du would nam-tor pakik.' thereupon wuh hinek kosu pufulag-tor ish-veh za' wuh suk cask, if ved ip-sut ish-veh s' zan-tor. 'potau u' fam dvun u' wuh aushfa, ' she leralmin-tor; 'ri tor dvun il stariben, il ish-veh dungi nam-tor ek' abru' k' du. Tonight, lu wuh robbers nam-tor ek' asleep, etek dungi sasahr-tor teretuhr. I ma wu vesh' waiting na' wuh opportunity tor stron.' wuh zhit vesh' hardly s' ish-veh ru'lut lu wuh godless hali-sutra fun-tor, dragging wuh'ashiv nu'ri ko-kan bi' k' au. Au vesh' ek' mon-tor, heh vlitau rai heed tor ish-veh maf-tor heh lamentations. Au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wine tor mon, rehkuh bezhun-zaneshu bosh, veh t' wan-kur wine, veh t' yon-kur, heh veh t' kin-kur, heh k' ik ish-veh khaf-spol mazhiv-kur-tor yut heh she tev-tor. Yi au tore ska' ish-veh dainty sai-vel, laid ish-veh fi' wuh pasu, heh tresahk ish-veh vaksurik ak'shem vi' krus, heh sprinkled alem fi-tor ish-veh. Wuh ri donku-tor betrothed ko-kan crouched trembling heh shuddering za' wuh cask, na' gla-tor ish-veh ra wuh terrible buk had vesh' intended na' ish-veh k' wuh robbers. Veh t' au i' pubeglanau wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov fam dvun remaining fi' wuh wuhr-ozh t' wuh riyeht-stau ko-kan, heh u' au kupi ri bes-tor ish-veh ska' easily, au nem-tor wuh hatchet heh tresahk ska' wuh ozh; tonk'peh wuh ozh sprang vi' wuh sov, heh tevan-tor za' wuh cask vi' wuh lap t' wuh ko-kan vi vesh' hiding tra'. Wuh robber nem-tor wuh ta'hal heh began looking na' ish-veh, tonk'peh au kupi ri talal ish-veh. 'ma du glazhau za' wuh suk cask?' leralmin-tor veh t' wuh vath. Tonk'peh wuh hinek kosu puvutau si', 'sarlah heh yokul ish-veh mu'yor-yem, heh kal-tor wuh vel nam-tor till fa-gad; wuh ozh skil-tor't sahr-tor maf.' 'wuh hinek kosu nam-tor gas'rak, ' leralmin-tor wuh robbers, heh au ceased looking na' wuh ozh heh hayal-tor ne'. Wuh hinek kosu yi rish-tor wuh sleeping draught k' ish-veh wine, heh fa' wu au vesh' ek' lying fi' wuh lan-tol t' wuh cellar, sahris asleep heh snoring. U' ak u' wuh ko-kan vesh' assured t' nash, sarlah ish-veh s' za' wuh cask. She vesh' obliged tor ash abru' wuh ak'shem t' wuh sleepers, vi vesh' lying ikap-tor teretuhr, heh kanok moment she vesh' boshau k' uzhau dread lest she dang awaken au. Tonk'peh oekon gol-tor ish-veh, ni ik she be' dvun-tor safely abru' au, heh yi she heh wuh hinek kosu went upstairs, tu'ash wuh svep, heh hastened u' sahris u' au kupi s' wuh murderers' den. Au afer-tor wuh vitush scattered k' wuh salan, tonk'peh wuh peas heh lentils had tehkau, heh grown sufficiently abru' wuh solektra, tor kakhartausu au svi' wuh moonlight bi' wuh yut. Ek' mu-yor wu au lates-tor, heh ish-veh vesh' asal fa' au pulau wuh mill. Yi wuh ko-kan var-tor ish-veh sa-mekh ek' ik had pavesh-tor. Wuh gad sarlah ik had vesh' teslau na' wuh kal'i'farr. Wuh bridegroom lasha heh isha wuh suk apc'koik t' be'hai'la, na' wuh miller had taken tun tor invite ek' ish-veh t'hylara heh relations. U' au hayal-tor na' wuh gadzhak, tik be'hai'la svi' da-tor vesh' ya'akash tor var-tor wuh var; wuh bride hayal-tor fam dvun heh did ri leralmin wuh zhit. 'heh du, t'nash-veh ashaya, ' leralmin-tor wuh bridegroom, turning tor ish-veh, 'nam-tor tra' rai var du fai-tor? Var-tor etek vel.' 'i dungi var-tor du wuh sahr-tor, yi, ' leralmin-tor wuh bride. 'i went sa'awek k'fai wuh laptra heh sarlah na' kim-shah tor wuh kelek; ri wuh soul sos talal k'svi, tonk'peh wuh kushel ik vesh' hanging svi' wuh kraisek fi' wuh temok maf-tor: 'da-tor pla', da-tor pla', nu'ri maiden rom, svizh-tor ri svi' nash murderers' lair.' heh va'ashiv wuh dahr wak ish-veh leralmin-tor aifa zhit.' 't'nash-veh ashal-veh, nash nam-tor goh wuh sahr-tor.' 'i went fi' k'fai wuh kelek s' tvi-shal tor tvi-shal, tonk'peh au vesh' ek' herbosh, heh kanok-vei vesh' ni grim heh mysterious. Na' kim-shah i went ne' tor wuh cellar, heh tra' hayal-tor wuh maut, maut hinek kosu, vi kupi ri potau ish-veh patam fam dvun. I ya'akash ish-veh kuv t'nash-veh betrothed ha-tor la', heh she kilko-tor, "ah, du ri donku-tor kan, du nam-tor sarlah tor wuh murderers' den; ish-veh betrothed tor indeed ha-tor la', tonk'peh au dungi stau du rik' mercy heh afterwards fas-tor heh yokul du."' 't'nash-veh ashal-veh, nash nam-tor goh wuh sahr-tor.' 'wuh hinek kosu ip-sut me za' wuh suk cask, heh scarcely had she ovsoh nash lu wuh robbers fun-tor ha-kel, dragging wuh nu'ri ko-kan bi' k' au. Au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rehkuh ves t' wine tor mon, wan-kur, yon-kur, heh kin-kur, heh k' ik she tev-tor.' 't'nash-veh ashal-veh, nash nam-tor goh wuh sahr-tor.' 'yi au tore ska' ish-veh dainty sai-vel, heh tresahk ish-veh vaksurik ak'shem vi' krus heh sprinkled alem fi-tor ish-veh.' 't'nash-veh ashal-veh, nash nam-tor goh wuh sahr-tor.' 'heh veh t' wuh robbers gla-tor ik tra' vesh' wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov fam dvun losrak fi' ish-veh ozh, heh u' ish-veh vesh' rihagik tor bes-tor ska', au nem-tor wuh hatchet heh tresahk ska' ish-veh ozh; tonk'peh wuh ozh sprang vi' wuh sov heh tevan-tor za' wuh lo'uk cask vi' t'nash-veh lap. Heh la' nam-tor wuh ozh k' wuh mokov.' heh k' aifa zhit wuh bride drew forth wuh ozh heh shewed ish-veh tor wuh assembled be'hai'la. Wuh bridegroom, vi du' nash recital had grown tevalik spoh, abru heh ar'kada tor stron, tonk'peh wuh be'hai'la seized ish-veh heh meskarau ish-veh sahris. Au tefu ish-veh abru tor yeht-gav, heh au heh ek' ish-veh murderous zhel vesh' condemned tor tevakh na' ish-veh wicked deeds. Tom kaur-ozh wuh ri donku-tor woodman hayal-tor svi' ish-veh cottage veh mu-yor, smoking ish-veh mev k' wuh yon-shal, du' ish-veh ko-telsu hayal-tor k' ish-veh vla spinning. 'uf lonely ish-veh nam-tor, ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor au, u' au puffed si' wuh wu tcha t' vuzh, 'na' du heh me tor hayal-tor la' k' ourselves, rik' sovek kanu tor mavau pa' heh amuse etek du' vath sutra seem ni kunli heh merry k' ish-veh kanu!' 'ra du leralmin nam-tor maut yeht, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu, sighing, heh turning pauk ish-veh halek; 'uf kunli dang i nam-tor kuv i had tonk'peh veh kan! Kuv ish-veh vesh' ek'wak ni pi'--nay, kuv ish-veh vesh' rai bigger do t'nash-veh kaur-ozh--i dang nam-tor maut kunli, heh ashaya ish-veh dearly.' i'--shaik u' du lau nah-tor ish-veh--sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun ik nash rom kosu's istaya vesh' fulfilled, aishan svi' wuh maut yut she had istau ish-veh; na', ri wu afterwards, she had wuh pi' sa-kan, vi vesh' ved muhl-bosh heh karik, tonk'peh vesh' ri mau bigger do t'nash-veh kaur-ozh. Ni au leralmin-tor, 'muhl, etek fam yehat leralmin etek ma ri prah ra etek istau na', heh, pi' u' au nam-tor, etek dungi ashaya ish-veh dearly.' heh au puvutau ish-veh thomas kaur-ozh. Au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh plenty t' yem-tukh, wi na' ek' au kupi tor au worla grew bigger, tonk'peh potau aishan wuh ka suk'es u' au had vesh' lu au vesh' pukeshta. Fam dvun, ish-veh bezhun vesh' nasik heh sparkling, heh au ak gluvau himself tor nam-tor wuh clever pi' katravahsu, vi kwon-hau-ov fai-tor muhl ra au vesh' pa'. Veh gad, u' wuh woodman vesh' getting pok tor hal-tor vi' wuh lapan tor tresahk hal-tukh, au leralmin-tor, 'i istaya i had ein-veh tor katau wuh hal po' me, na' i aitlun tor tor haste.' 'oh, sa-mekh, ' maf-tor tom, 'i dungi nem-tor tun t' ik; wuh hal dungau nam-tor svi' wuh lapan k' wuh wak du aitlun ish-veh.' yi wuh woodman abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh leralmin-tor, 'uf mokuhlek ik nam-tor? Du fam yehat pulau abru tor wuh jarel's bridle.' 'worla kashek ik, sa-mekh, ' leralmin-tor tom; 'kuv t'nash-veh ko-mekh dungi goh harness wuh jarel, i dungi prah vi' ish-veh kaluk heh var-tor ish-veh if yut tor hal-tor.' 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'etek dungi ar'kadan na' wuh'wak.' lu wuh wak sarlah wuh ko-mekh harnessed wuh jarel tor wuh hal, heh shitau tom vi' ish-veh kaluk; heh u' au hayal-tor tra' wuh pi' sasu var-tor wuh beast uf tor hal-tor, maf-tor si', 'hal-tor fi'!' heh 'pehkaya!' u' au aitlu: heh thus wuh jarel went fi' aishan u' muhl u' kuv wuh woodman had driven ish-veh himself vi' wuh lapan. Ish-veh pavesh-tor ik u' wuh jarel vesh' going wuh pi' nuh' sahris, heh tom vesh' calling si', 'kogavik! Kogavik!' dahkuh ri-fainusu sarlah abru. 'ra wuh shaik vel ik nam-tor!' leralmin-tor veh: 'tra' nam-tor wuh hal going bi', heh i zhu-tor wuh carter talking tor wuh jarel, tonk'peh wi i mokuhlek gla-tor kling.' 'ik nam-tor queer, indeed, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath; 'kal-tor etek zahal-tor wuh hal, heh gla-tor wilat ish-veh hal-tor.' ni au went fi' vi' wuh lapan, till na' kim-shah sarlah au tor wuh shi wilat wuh woodman vesh'. Yi tom kaur-ozh, seeing ish-veh sa-mekh, maf-tor si', 'gla-tor, sa-mekh, la' i am k' wuh hal, ek' gas'rak heh safe! I' nem-tor me ne'!' ni ish-veh sa-mekh nem-tor meskaraya t' wuh jarel k' veh el'ru, heh k' wuh vath nem-tor ish-veh sa-fu s' wuh jarel's kaluk, heh shitau ish-veh ne' fi-tor wuh terp, wilat au hayal-tor u' merry u' du sanoi. Wuh dahkuh ri-fainusu vesh' ek' nash wak looking fi', heh did ri fai-tor ra tor leralmin na' wonder. Na' kim-shah veh nem-tor wuh vath aside, heh leralmin-tor, 'ik pi' urchin dungi tor etwel fortune, kuv etek mokuhlek prah ish-veh, heh lesh ish-veh pa' s' kahr tor kahr u' wuh gluvaya; etek bolau mahr-tor ish-veh.' ni au went abru tor wuh woodman, heh ya'akash ish-veh ra au would nem-tor na' wuh pi' sasu. 'au dungi nam-tor weh-rom ska', ' leralmin-tor au, 'k' etek do k' du.' 'i skil-tor't makau ish-veh na' ek', ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh; 't'nash-veh sha' kahm heh khaf nam-tor dearer tor me do ek' wuh haul-tukh heh pi-maat-tukh svi' wuh panu.' tonk'peh tom, khaf-spol t' wuh bargain au aitlu tor tor, crept abru ish-veh sa-mekh's tor-pal tor ish-veh tipan heh zhal-tor svi' ish-veh kaluk, 'nem-tor wuh donku, sa-mekh, heh kal-tor au ma me; i'll ak sarlah pla' tor du.' ni wuh woodman na' kim-shah leralmin-tor au would makau tom tor wuh ri-fainusu na' wuh suk krus t' pi-maat-tukh, heh au vlitau wuh price. 'wilat would du spo' tor hayal-tor?' leralmin-tor veh t' au. 'oh, shitau me fi' wuh rim t' ish-veh taik; ik dungi nam-tor wuh nice tanaf-shi'gluvaun na' me; i mokuhlek lates pa' tra' heh gla-tor wuh shasol u' etek hal-tor bi'.' ni au did u' au istau; heh lu tom had taken trasha t' ish-veh sa-mekh au nem-tor ish-veh maf k' au. Au halovau fi' till ish-veh began tor nam-tor dusky, heh yi wuh pi' sasu leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor me prah ne', i'm zungor.' ni wuh sasu nem-tor ska' ish-veh taik, heh shitau ish-veh ne' fi' wuh solek-vihk t' terra, svi' wuh ploughed vunai k' wuh vla t' wuh fau-yut. Tonk'peh tom sahr-tor pa' svi' wuh furrows, heh na' kim-shah trel-tor vi' wuh hinek aushfa-razh. 'rom mu-yor, t'nash-veh trensu!' leralmin-tor au, 'i'm ska'! Kashek heh glazhau nasik po' me wuh thurai wak.' yi au sahr-tor na' wuh'wak tor wuh shi, heh poked wuh shahtau t' ish-veh terpau vi' wuh aushfa-razh, tonk'peh ek' svi' vain; tom goh ukrau weh-irak heh weh-irak svi'; heh na' kim-shah ish-veh became ved gu'gelik, ni ik au vesh' punekwitau tor hal-tor ish-veh yut rik' ish-veh prize, u' sulky u' kupi nam-tor. Lu tom afer-tor au vesh' hal-tor, au sasarlah t' ish-veh hiding-shi. 'ra tehvar-bosh walking ish-veh nam-tor, ' leralmin-tor au, 'svi' nash ploughed vunai! Kuv i vesh' tor tevan s' veh t' aifa lo'uk solek-vihk, i dang undoubtedly shaya t'nash-veh talu.' na' kim-shah, k' rom kunli, au afer-tor wuh suk herbosh snail-fo. 'nash nam-tor kunli, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i mokuhlek yuk la' maut muhl'; heh svi' au crept. Aishan u' au vesh' tevan-tor asleep, au puzhu-tor dahkuh sasu be' dvun-tor k', chatting teretuhr; heh veh leralmin-tor tor wuh vath, 'uf mokuhlek etek rob ik don-ka parson's kelek t' ish-veh haul-tukh heh pi-maat-tukh?' 'i'll var-tor du!' maf-tor tom. 'ra ralash vesh' ik?' leralmin-tor wuh pi'tak, koltha; 'i'm sure i puzhu-tor ein-veh stariben.' au lam-tor fam dvun listening, heh tom leralmin-tor, 'nem-tor me k' du, heh i'll ak gluvaya du uf tor prah wuh parson's donku.' 'tonk'peh wilat nam-tor du?' leralmin-tor au. 'glazhau pa' fi' wuh solektra, ' kilko-tor au, 'heh shroi wilat wuh ralash sarlah s'.' na' kim-shah wuh pi'tak afer-tor ish-veh si', heh abertau ish-veh abru svi' ish-veh el'ru. 'du pi' urchin!' au leralmin-tor, 'ra mokuhlek du tor na' etek?' 'po, i mokuhlek prah svi' wuh shek-tukh krani-mofek t' wuh parson's kelek, heh lehm du si' whatever du aitlun.' 'ik's wuh rom nahp, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi'tak; 'sarlah bi', etek dungau gla-tor ra du mokuhlek tor.' lu sarlah au tor wuh parson's kelek, tom trel-tor k'fai wuh krani-mofek vi' wuh tvi-shal, heh yi puvutau si' u' ral u' au kupi vlei, 'dungi du ma ek' ik nam-tor la'?' na' nash wuh pi'tak vesh' koltha, heh leralmin-tor, 'softly, softly! Stariben neik, ik du lau ri awaken anybody.' tonk'peh tom seemed u' kuv au did ri ken-tor au, heh bawled si' va'ashiv, 'uf mau dungi du ma? Dungau i lehm ish-veh ek' si'?' i' wuh fas-tor ti svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal; heh khaf-spol wuh ralash she ashenau herself abru svi' ish-veh sar-tak heh shroi. Meantime wuh pi'tak vesh' koltha, heh sahr-tor ska' wuh pi' yut; tonk'peh na' kim-shah au plucked abru ish-veh khaf-spol, heh leralmin-tor, 'wuh pi' urchin nam-tor goh trying tor tor duhsu t' etek.' ni sarlah au pla' heh zhal-tor softly tor ish-veh, taran, 'i' kal-tor etek ma rai weht t' ish-veh roguish kha'wal; tonk'peh lehm etek si' ein t' wuh donku.' yi tom puvutau si' u' ral u' au kupi, 'maut muhl! Meskaraya ish-veh el'ru! La' sarlah ish-veh.' wuh fas-tor puzhu-tor nash ved eiktra, ni she sprang s' sar-tak, heh sahr-tor tor tu'ash wuh svep. Wuh pi'tak sahr-tor ska' u' kuv wuh wolf vesh' na' ish-veh harr: heh wuh maid, having groped pa' heh afer-tor nothing, went maf na' wuh ta'hal. K' wuh wak sarlah ish-veh pla', tom had trel-tor ska' vi' wuh aushfa-kel; heh lu she had glazhau pa' heh pstha kanok razh heh teruk, heh afer-tor kling, she went tor sar-tak, thinking she bolau ma vesh' dreaming k' ish-veh bezhun tu'ash. Wuh pi' sasu ukrau pa' svi' wuh hay-loft, heh na' kim-shah afer-tor wuh snug shi tor shaht ish-veh mu-yor's shom svi'; ni au laid himself ne', meaning tor yuk till gad-ha'khlup, heh yi talal ish-veh yut ha-kel tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh. Tonk'peh alas! Uf woefully au vesh' undone! Ra tuhsau heh sorrows pavesh-tor tor etek ek' svi' nash panu! Wuh fas-tor prah abru lehkuh-mal, fa' gad-keshtan, tor yem-tor wuh aushfa; heh going zehik tor wuh hay-loft, lesh maf wuh suk uzh'a'lek t' hay, k' wuh pi' sasu svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh, sahris asleep. Au fam dvun, however, yuk-tor fi', heh did ri kum'i till au afer-tor himself svi' wuh ru'lut t' wuh aushfa; na' wuh fas-tor had shitau wuh hay vi' wuh aushfa's rick, heh wuh aushfa had taken tom abru svi' wuh mouthful t' ish-veh. 'rom fam-wuh-gad!' leralmin-tor au, 'uf sarlah i tor tumble vi' wuh mill?' tonk'peh au ak afer-tor si' wilat au really vesh'; heh vesh' punekwitau ki' ek' ish-veh wits pa' ish-veh, ik au lau ri prah svi' wuh aushfa's zud, heh ni nam-tor plesh-tor tor tevakh. Na' kim-shah ne' au went vi' ish-veh skaun-sa'haf. 'ish-veh nam-tor rather gu'gelik, ' leralmin-tor au; 'au forgot tor torvau krani svi' nash tvi-shal tor kal-tor wuh yel svi'; wuh ha'fek would nam-tor rai rasahkos vel.' hi au tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh rasahkos kunli, au did ri spo' ish-veh ha-shal na' ek'; heh wuh rasahkos t' ish-veh vesh', ik weht heh weht hay vesh' kwon-hau-ov coming ne', heh wuh ret losrak na' ish-veh became smaller heh smaller. Na' kim-shah au lit'dhae u' ral u' au kupi, 'ri tor katau me sovek weht hay! Ri tor katau me sovek weht hay!' wuh maid pavesh-tor tor nam-tor aishan yi milking wuh aushfa; heh khaf-spol ein-veh stariben, tonk'peh seeing kling, heh wi hasu ved sure ish-veh vesh' wuh ka spes ik she had puzhu-tor svi' wuh mu-yor, she vesh' ni koltha ik she tevan-tor ska' ish-veh stool, heh overset wuh thas-pail. U' ak u' she kupi pick herself abru s' wuh kitek, she sahr-tor ska' u' sahris u' she kupi tor ish-veh trensu wuh parson, heh leralmin-tor, 'osu, osu, wuh aushfa nam-tor talking!' tonk'peh wuh parson leralmin-tor, 'kosu, thou tanaf surely mad!' however, au went k' ish-veh vi' wuh aushfa-kelek, tor ar'kadan heh gla-tor ra vesh' wuh tukh. Scarcely had au eku ash'ya fi' wuh threshold, lu tom puvutau si', 'ri tor katau me sovek weht hay!' yi wuh parson himself vesh' koltha; heh thinking wuh aushfa vesh' surely bewitched, var-tor ish-veh sasu tor stau ish-veh fi' wuh gla-tor. Ni wuh aushfa vesh' pustau, heh tresahk abru; heh wuh skaun-sa'haf, svi' if tom ti, vesh' lehm-tor si' fi-tor wuh dunghill. Tom ak eku himself tor ar'kadan tor prah si', if vesh' ri wuh maut hagik task; tonk'peh na' kim-shah, aishan u' au had tor tvi-shal tor prah ish-veh patam si', sluk has-bosh-kunli befell ish-veh. Wuh k'avon wolf sprang si', heh vitem-tor abru wuh bosh skaun-sa'haf, k' tom svi' ish-veh, na' veh gulp, heh sahr-tor maf. Tom, however, vesh' fam dvun ri disheartened; heh thinking wuh wolf would ri ritishaya having ein chat k' ish-veh u' au vesh' going bi', au puvutau si', 't'nash-veh rom t'hy'la, i mokuhlek gluvaya du wuh khinik skasau.' 'wilat's ik?' leralmin-tor wuh wolf. 'svi' such heh such wuh kelek, ' leralmin-tor tom, describing ish-veh sha' sa-mekh's kelek. 'du mokuhlek ukrau k'fai wuh smash-mev vi' wuh af'tum heh yi vi' wuh pantry, heh tra' du dungi talal cakes, ham, kahm, samu kahm, roast pig, savas-dumplings, heh kanok-vei ik ish-veh khaf-spol mokuhlek istaya.' wuh wolf did ri aitlun tor nam-tor ya'akash dah'wak; ni ik maut mu-yor au went tor wuh kelek heh ukrau k'fai wuh smash-mev vi' wuh af'tum, heh yi vi' wuh pantry, heh ate heh drank tra' tor ish-veh khaf-spol's content. U' ak u' au had had hiyet au aitlu tor prah maf; tonk'peh au had yokul ni mau ik au kupi ri hal-tor si' k' wuh ka yut sarlah ish-veh svi'. Nash vesh' aishan ra tom had reckoned fi-tor; heh i' au began tor eku abru wuh lo'uk saul, tor ek' wuh ralash au kupi. 'dungi du nam-tor hagik?' leralmin-tor wuh wolf; 'du'll awaken kanok-veh svi' wuh kelek kuv du tor such wuh clatter.' 'ra's ik tor me?' leralmin-tor wuh pi' sasu; 'du ma had ish-veh frolic, i' i've wuh kashek tor nam-tor merry myself'; heh au began, uralaun heh shouting u' ral u' au kupi. Wuh woodman heh ish-veh ko-telsu, hasu awakened k' wuh ralash, peeped k'fai wuh treshaya svi' wuh svep; tonk'peh lu gla-tor au wuh wolf vesh' tra', du lau muhl suppose ik au vesh' sadly koltha; heh wuh woodman sahr-tor na' ish-veh la'ash, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ko-telsu wuh urokesor. 'tor du hafau, ' leralmin-tor wuh woodman, 'heh lu i ma knocked ish-veh fi' wuh patam du bolau tres ish-veh abru k' wuh urokesor.' tom puzhu-tor ek' nash, heh lit'dhae, 'sa-mekh, sa-mekh! I am la', wuh wolf has vitem-tor me.' heh ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor, 'sha-ka-ri nam-tor krol-tor! Etek ma afer-tor etwel tal-kam kan va'ashiv'; heh au var-tor ish-veh ko-telsu ri tor nam-tor-tor wuh urokesor na' pthak she dang dash-tor ish-veh. Yi au mokh-tor wuh lo'uk salur, heh kwul-tor wuh wolf fi' wuh patam, heh pustau ish-veh fi' wuh gla-tor! Heh lu au vesh' tevik au tresahk tu'ash ish-veh ak'shem, heh eku tommy elik. 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'ra ptha etek ma had na' du!' 'ha, sa-mekh, ' kilko-tor au; 'i ma travelled ek' abru' wuh panu, i nah-tor, svi' veh yut il vath, opi' etek parted; heh i' i am maut glad tor sarlah ha-kel heh prah sluk sov va'ashiv.' 'po, wilat ma du vesh'?' leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh. 'i ma vesh' svi' wuh aushfa-razh--heh svi' wuh snail-fo--heh ne' wuh aushfa's drahk--heh svi' wuh wolf's nehg; heh wi la' i am va'ashiv, safe heh ralash.' 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor au, 'du nam-tor sarlah pla', heh etek dungi ri makau du va'ashiv na' ek' wuh don-tak svi' wuh panu.' yi au teraya-martaya heh shok-tor ish-veh tal-kam pi' sa-fu, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh plenty tor yokul heh mon, na' au vesh' maut k'avon; heh yi au zaprah uzh sai-vel na' ish-veh, na' ish-veh hinek ones had vesh' ved spoiled fi' ish-veh halovaya. Ni trensu kaur-ozh stayed na' ha-kel k' ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh, svi' sochya; na' hi au had vesh' ni lo'uk wuh traveller, heh had ovsoh heh gla-tor ni wehk tok-ti vel, heh vesh' tishau hiyet t' telling wuh bosh var, au kwon-hau-ov sep-wafikh ik, po' ek', tra''s rai shi spo' ha-kel! Rumpelstiltskin k' wuh vla t' wuh lapan, svi' wuh shasol wuh wu yut ska', sahr-tor wuh tok-ti pilash t' masu; heh fi-tor wuh pilash tra' lam-tor wuh mill. Wuh miller's kelek vesh' beyik, heh wuh miller, du bolau fai-tor, had wuh maut vaksurik ko-fu. She vesh', moreover, maut shrewd heh clever; heh wuh miller vesh' ni yaut t' ish-veh, ik au veh gad var-tor wuh sa-te'kru t' wuh solektra, vi nam-tor-tor tor sarlah heh shi'kar svi' wuh lapan, ik ish-veh ko-fu kupi padan pi-maat-tukh s' terp. I' nash sa-te'kru vesh' maut tishau t' donku; heh lu au puzhu-tor wuh miller's boast ish-veh greediness vesh' ashenau, heh au satau na' wuh ko-kan tor nam-tor katau fa' ish-veh. Yi au pufulag-tor ish-veh tor wuh tvi-shal svi' ish-veh palace wilat tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk tuh t' terp, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh spinning-halek, heh leralmin-tor, 'ek' nash bolau nam-tor pada-tor vi' pi-maat-tukh fa' asal, u' du ashaya ish-veh ha'kiv.' ish-veh vesh' svi' vain ik wuh ri donku-tor maiden leralmin-tor ik ish-veh vesh' goh wuh silly boast t' ish-veh sa-mekh, na' ik she kupi tor rai such vel u' padan terp vi' pi-maat-tukh: wuh tvi-shal svep vesh' klacha, heh she vesh' losrak sa'awek. She hayal-tor ne' svi' veh teruk t' wuh tvi-shal, heh began tor bewail ish-veh lerash buk; lu fi' wuh sudden wuh svep tu'ash, heh wuh droll-looking pi' sasu hobbled svi', heh leralmin-tor, 'rom morrow tor du, t'nash-veh rom lass; ra nam-tor du weeping na'?' 'alas!' leralmin-tor she, 'i bolau padan nash terp vi' pi-maat-tukh, heh i fai-tor ri uf.' 'ra dungi du mazhiv-kur-tor me, ' leralmin-tor wuh hobgoblin, 'tor tor ish-veh na' du?' 't'nash-veh necklace, ' kilko-tor wuh maiden. Au nem-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh zhit, heh hayal-tor himself ne' tor wuh halek, heh whistled heh sang: 'pauk pa', pauk pa', lo heh behold! Magu maf, magu maf, terp vi' pi-maat-tukh!' heh pauk pa' wuh halek went merrily; wuh ar'kadan vesh' sahris ovsoh, heh wuh terp vesh' ek' pada-tor vi' pi-maat-tukh. Lu wuh sa-te'kru sarlah heh gla-tor nash, au vesh' greatly astonished heh sanoi; tonk'peh ish-veh khaf-spol grew fam dvun weht greedy t' nazh-kap, heh au ikap'uh t'du ru'lut wuh ri donku-tor miller's ko-fu va'ashiv k' wuh sluk task. Yi she fai-tor ri ra tor tor, heh hayal-tor ne' wuh'wak weht tor tusa; tonk'peh wuh kobsu ak tu'ash wuh svep, heh leralmin-tor, 'ra dungi du mazhiv-kur-tor me tor tor ish-veh task?' 'wuh mokov fi' t'nash-veh ozh, ' leralmin-tor she. Ni ish-veh pi' t'hy'la nem-tor wuh mokov, heh began tor ar'kadan na' wuh halek va'ashiv, heh whistled heh sang: 'pauk pa', pauk pa', lo heh behold! Magu maf, magu maf, terp vi' pi-maat-tukh!' till, wu fa' asal, ek' vesh' ovsoh va'ashiv. Wuh sa-te'kru vesh' greatly delighted tor gla-tor ek' nash glittering treasure; tonk'peh fam dvun au had ri hiyet: ni au nem-tor wuh miller's ko-fu tor wuh wi larger tuh, heh leralmin-tor, 'ek' nash bolau nam-tor pada-tor tonight; heh kuv ish-veh nam-tor, du dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-te'kru.' u' ak u' she vesh' sa'awek ik kobsu sarlah svi', heh leralmin-tor, 'ra dungi du mazhiv-kur-tor me tor padan pi-maat-tukh na' du nash wuh wak?' 'i ma nothing losrak, ' leralmin-tor she. 'yi leralmin du dungi mazhiv-kur-tor me, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi' sasu, 'wuh wuh'rak pi' kan ik du lau ma lu du nam-tor ko-te'kru.' 'ik lau worla nam-tor, ' nahp wuh miller's ko-fu: heh u' she fai-tor rai vath yut tor prah ish-veh task ovsoh, she leralmin-tor she would tor ra au ya'akash. Pauk went wuh halek va'ashiv tor wuh hinek song, heh wuh manikin wuh'wak weht pada-tor wuh tuh vi' pi-maat-tukh. Wuh sa-te'kru sarlah svi' wuh asal, heh, finding ek' au aitlu, vesh' punekwitau tor potau ish-veh zhit; ni au telik wuh miller's ko-fu, heh she really became ko-te'kru. Na' wuh keshtan t' ish-veh wuh'rak pi' kan she vesh' maut glad, heh forgot wuh kobsu, heh ra she had leralmin-tor. Tonk'peh veh gad sarlah ish-veh vi' ish-veh tvi-shal, wilat she vesh' sitting mavaun k' ish-veh kan-bu, heh shitau ish-veh svi' kashek t' ish-veh. Yi she grieved sorely na' ish-veh misfortune, heh leralmin-tor she would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ek' wuh don-tak t' wuh kingdom kuv au would kal-tor ish-veh ska', tonk'peh svi' vain; till na' kim-shah ish-veh bezhun-masu softened ish-veh, heh au leralmin-tor, 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du rehkuh gad' takov, heh kuv du' ik wak du var-tor me t'nash-veh ahm, du dungau potau ish-veh kan.' i' wuh ko-te'kru ti kum'i ek' mu-yor, thinking t' ek' wuh shaik ahm ik she had ek'wak puzhu-tor; heh she satau skladasu ek' abru' wuh solektra tor talal si' uzh ones. Wuh thurai gad wuh pi' sasu sarlah, heh she began k' timothy, ichabod, benjamin, jeremiah, heh ek' wuh ahm she kupi vokau; tonk'peh tor ek' heh tik t' au au leralmin-tor, 'madam, ik nam-tor ri t'nash-veh ahm.' wuh dahr gad she began k' ek' wuh comical ahm she kupi zhu-tor t', bandy-mal, hunchback, pi'tak-shanks, heh ni fi'; tonk'peh wuh pi' gentleman fam dvun leralmin-tor tor kanok veh t' au, 'madam, ik nam-tor ri t'nash-veh ahm.' wuh wuh gad veh t' wuh skladasu sarlah pla', heh leralmin-tor, 'i ma travelled dahkuh gad rik' khaf-spol t' sovek vath ahm; tonk'peh za-gad, u' i vesh' climbing wuh pid kunel, among wuh lap t' wuh laptra wilat wuh fox heh wuh hare nufai tik vath rom mu-yor, vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh pi' hut; heh fa' wuh hut yontau wuh yon; heh pauk pa' wuh yon wuh funny pi' kobsu vesh' taman fi-tor veh mal, heh uralaun: "merrily wuh gadzhak i'll tor. Nash-gad i'll fas-tor, fa-gad leipau; merrily i'll tam heh uralau, na' thurai gad dungi wuh ri-fainusu katau. Pi' tor t'nash-veh t'sai sahr-tor rumpelstiltskin nam-tor t'nash-veh ahm!" lu wuh ko-te'kru puzhu-tor nash she spen-tor na' mak, heh u' ak u' ish-veh pi' t'hy'la sarlah she hayal-tor ne' fi-tor ish-veh throne, heh puvutau ek' ish-veh kelek pauk tor tizh-tor wuh mihrsh; heh wuh nurse lam-tor k' ish-veh vla k' wuh kan-bu svi' ish-veh kar, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' ved pok tor nam-tor putan-tor abru. Yi wuh pi' sasu began tor chuckle na' wuh nahp t' having wuh ri donku-tor kan, tor nem-tor ha-kel k' ish-veh tor ish-veh hut svi' wuh lapan; heh au lit'dhae, 'i', t'sai, ra nam-tor t'nash-veh ahm?' 'nam-tor ish-veh john?' ya'akash she. 'rai, madam!' 'nam-tor ish-veh tom?' 'rai, madam!' 'nam-tor ish-veh jemmy?' 'ish-veh nam-tor ri.' 'mokuhlek ish-veh ahm nam-tor rumpelstiltskin?' leralmin-tor wuh t'sai slyly. 'ein witch var-tor du ik!--ein witch var-tor du ik!' maf-tor wuh pi' sasu, heh dashed ish-veh gas'rak ash'ya svi' wuh reshan ni glu vi' wuh lan-tol, ik au vesh' punekwitau tor ti meskaraya t' ish-veh k' fi' el'ru tor seshaya ish-veh si'. Yi au tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh yut ska', du' wuh nurse abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh wuh kan-bu crowed; heh ek' wuh kelek jeered na' ish-veh na' having had ni mau trouble na' nothing, heh leralmin-tor, 'etek istaya du wuh maut rom asal, heh wuh merry gadzhak, mr rumplestiltskin!' clever gretel tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh fas-tor ahmau gretel, vi sai-vel-tor ash'el k' yon-kur timut, heh lu she lates-tor si' k' au fi', she da-tor herself nash yut heh ik, vesh' ved kunli heh nahp: 'du certainly nam-tor wuh takov ko-kan!' heh lu sarlah ish-veh ha-kel she drank, svi' ish-veh gladness t' khaf-spol, wuh draught t' wine, heh u' wine teporilau wuh aitlun tor yokul, she zahv-tor wuh buhfik t' whatever she vesh' fasan abi' she vesh' satisfied, heh leralmin-tor: 'wuh fas-tor bolau fai-tor ra wuh yem-tukh nam-tor spo'.' sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun ik wuh trensu veh gad leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'gretel, tra' nam-tor wuh be'hai'la coming nash khru; dator me dahkuh fowls maut daintily.' 'i dungi gla-tor tor ish-veh, trensu, ' kilko-tor gretel. She pustau dahkuh fowls, scalded au, plucked au, shitau au fi' wuh spit, heh na' khru eku au fa' wuh yon, ik au lau roast. Wuh fowls began tor da-tor khav-kur, heh vesh' nearly pok, tonk'peh wuh be'hai'la had ri wi lasha. Yi gretel puvutau si' tor ish-veh trensu: 'kuv wuh be'hai'la tor ri sarlah, i bolau nem-tor wuh fowls maf s' wuh yon, tonk'peh ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh sin heh wuh mesh kuv au nam-tor ri yokul wuh moment au nam-tor na' ish-veh juiciest.' wuh trensu leralmin-tor: 'i dungi sahr-tor myself, heh zaprah wuh be'hai'la.' lu wuh trensu had da-tor ish-veh pla', gretel laid wuh spit k' wuh fowls fi' veh vla, heh nahp: 'standing ni wu k' wuh yon tra', tor veh wadashaya heh thirsty; vi fai-tor lu au dungi sarlah? Meanwhile, i dungi sahr-tor vi' wuh cellar, heh nem-tor wuh mon.' she sahr-tor ne', eku wuh mashek, leralmin-tor: 'oekon kudau ish-veh na' du, gretel, ' heh nem-tor wuh rom mon, heh nahp ik wine dang yumaya fi', heh dang ri nam-tor svi-shau, heh nem-tor wi wuh'ashiv hearty draught. Yi she went heh shitau wuh fowls ne' va'ashiv tor wuh yon, basted au, heh drove wuh spit merrily pauk. Tonk'peh u' wuh roast kahm smelt ni rom, gretel nahp: 'vel lau nam-tor riyeht, ish-veh ought tor nam-tor zahv-tor!' she estuhl ish-veh k' ish-veh ozh, heh leralmin-tor: 'ah! Uf rom fowls nam-tor! Ish-veh certainly nam-tor wuh sin heh wuh mesh ik au nam-tor ri yokul na' wuh gas'rak wak!' she sahr-tor tor wuh krani, tor gla-tor kuv wuh trensu vesh' ri coming k' ish-veh be'hai'la, tonk'peh gla-tor ish-veh kling, heh went pla' tor wuh fowls heh nahp: 'veh t' wuh rala nam-tor yontau! I had weh-rom nem-tor ish-veh ska' heh yokul ish-veh.' ni she tresahk ish-veh ska', ate ish-veh, heh tizh-tor ish-veh, heh lu she had ovsoh, she nahp: 'wuh vath bolau hal-tor ne' nuh', il else trensu dungi glantau ik vel nam-tor missing.' lu wuh dahkuh rala vesh' yokul, she went heh glazhau na' ish-veh trensu, heh did ri gla-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh suddenly paresh-tor tor ish-veh: 'vi fai-tor? Au nam-tor sos'eh ri coming na' ek', heh ma da-tor svi' ein-wilat.' yi she leralmin-tor: 'muhl, gretel, tizh-tor yourself, veh kushel has vesh' tresahk vi', nem-tor wuh'ashiv mon, heh yokul ish-veh abru entirely; lu ish-veh nam-tor yokul du dungi ma ein sochya, po dang oekon's rom mazhiv-kur nam-tor spoilt?' ni she sahr-tor vi' wuh cellar va'ashiv, nem-tor wuh masuk' mon heh ate abru wuh veh kahm svi' lo'uk glee. Lu veh t' wuh kahm vesh' vitem-tor ne', heh fam dvun ish-veh trensu did ri sarlah, gretel glazhau na' wuh vath heh leralmin-tor: 'ra veh nam-tor, wuh vath dang nam-tor likewise, wuh dahkuh hal-tor teretuhr; ra's gas'rak na' wuh veh nam-tor gas'rak na' wuh vath; i nah-tor kuv i vesh' tor nem-tor wuh'ashiv draught ish-veh would tor me rai klau.' ni she nem-tor wuh'ashiv hearty mon, heh kal-tor wuh dahr kahm zahal-tor wuh wuh'rak. Du' she vesh' tor wuh danik t' ish-veh, ish-veh trensu sarlah heh maf-tor: 'brax abru, gretel, wuh be'hai'la nam-tor coming directly po' me!' 'ha, osu, i dungi ak dvin-tor abru, ' kilko-tor gretel. Meantime wuh trensu glazhau tor gla-tor ik wuh pasu vesh' properly laid, heh nem-tor wuh lo'uk lipau, wherewith au vesh' going tor skrim-tor wuh kahm, heh sharpened ish-veh fi' wuh ash-tor. Presently wuh be'hai'la sarlah, heh knocked politely heh courteously na' wuh kelek-svep. Gretel sahr-tor, heh glazhau tor gla-tor vi vesh' tra', heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh be'hai'la, she shitau ish-veh ozh tor ish-veh bru-lar heh leralmin-tor: 'hush! Hush! Hal-tor maf u' sahris u' du mokuhlek, kuv t'nash-veh trensu kum-tor du ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh weh-rasahkos na' du; au certainly did ya'akash du tor mu'yor-yem, tonk'peh ish-veh intention nam-tor tor tresahk ska' ish-veh dahkuh kaluk. Aishan shroi uf au nam-tor sharpening wuh lipau na' ish-veh!' wuh be'hai'la puzhu-tor wuh sharpening, heh hurried ne' wuh ash-tor va'ashiv u' sahris u' au kupi. Gretel vesh' ri idle; she sahr-tor screaming tor ish-veh trensu, heh maf-tor: 'du ma invited wuh tok-ti be'hai'la!' 'po, gretel? Ra tor du tvai k' ik?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor she, 'au has taken wuh kahm if i vesh' aishan going tor dvin-tor abru, ska' wuh dish, heh has sahr-tor maf k' au!' 'ik's wuh nice trick!' leralmin-tor ish-veh trensu, heh lamented wuh tok-ti kahm. 'kuv au had tonk'peh losrak me veh, ni ik vel hafau na' me tor yokul.' au puvutau tor ish-veh tor pehkaya, tonk'peh wuh be'hai'la pretended ri tor zhu-tor. Yi au sahr-tor po' ish-veh k' wuh lipau fam dvun svi' ish-veh el'ru, maf-tor: 'aishan veh, aishan veh, ' meaning ik wuh be'hai'la dang trasha ish-veh aishan veh kahm, heh ri nem-tor fi'. Wuh be'hai'la, however, nahp rai vathru do ik au vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru veh t' ish-veh kaluk, heh sahr-tor u' kuv yon vesh' yontau ne' ish-veh, svi' zek tor nem-tor au fi' k' ish-veh. Wuh hinek sasu heh ish-veh grandson tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh maut hinek sasu, t'vi bezhun had shetau neik-ha'khlup, ish-veh kaluk pasik t' khaf-spol, ish-veh mal-nef trembled, heh lu au hayal-tor na' pasu au kupi hardly meskaraya wuh floku, heh spilt wuh broth fi-tor wuh pasu-sai il kal-tor ish-veh sahr-tor s' ish-veh ru'lut. Ish-veh sa-fu heh ish-veh sa-fu's ko-telsu vesh' spa'ash na' nash, ni wuh hinek sa'mekh'al na' kim-shah had tor hayal-tor svi' wuh teruk za' wuh stove, heh au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh yem-tukh svi' wuh earthenware yerak, heh ri kauk hiyet t' ish-veh. Heh au nam-tor-tor tor glazhau na' wuh pasu k' ish-veh bezhun bosh t' bezhun-masu. Wuh'wak, nuh', ish-veh trembling el'ru kupi ri meskaraya wuh yerak, heh ish-veh tevan-tor tor wuh solektra heh shau. Wuh nu'ri ko-telsu scolded ish-veh, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor nothing heh goh spes-tevan. Yi au katau ish-veh wuh wooden yerak na' wuh zamu ulef-pence, s' if au had tor yokul. Au vesh' wuh'wak sitting thus lu wuh pi' grandson t' kehkuh tevun hinek began tor hoknau teretuhr ein bits t' lapan fi-tor wuh solektra. 'ra nam-tor du doing tra'?' ya'akash wuh sa-mekh.
