'i am tor wuh pi' trough, ' kilko-tor wuh kan, 'na' sa-mekh heh ko-mekh tor yokul s' lu i am suk'.' wuh sasu heh ish-veh ko-telsu glazhau na' tik vath na' wuh du', heh presently began tor maf. Yi au nem-tor wuh hinek sa'mekh'al tor wuh pasu, heh henceforth kwon-hau-ov kal-tor ish-veh yokul k' au, heh likewise leralmin-tor nothing kuv au did nes wuh pi' t' sovek-vel. Wuh pi' peasant tra' vesh' wuh ac'ruth pi'kahr wherein kling ha-tor tonk'peh really don-ka peasants, heh aishan veh ri donku-tor veh, ik au puvutau wuh pi' peasant. Au had ri kauk ni mau u' wuh aushfa, heh fam dvun lehkuh donku tor mahr-tor veh, heh wi au heh ish-veh ko-telsu did ni istaya ki' veh. Veh gad au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'shroi, i ma wuh rom idea, tra' nam-tor etwel gossip wuh carpenter, au dungau tor etek wuh wooden vaukh, heh kras ish-veh khav-kur, ni ik ish-veh glazhau spo' sovek vath, heh svi' wak ish-veh dungi certainly prah suk' heh nam-tor wuh aushfa.' wuh kosu isha tishau wuh idea, heh ish-veh gossip wuh carpenter tresahk heh planed wuh vaukh, heh kras-tor ish-veh u' ish-veh ought tor nam-tor, heh tor ish-veh k' its patam hanging ne' u' kuv ish-veh vesh' eating. Thurai asal lu wuh aushfa vesh' hasu driven si', wuh pi' peasant puvutau wuh aushfa-kuht svi' heh leralmin-tor: 'glazhau, i ma wuh pi' vaukh tra', tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor fam dvun pi' heh has tor nam-tor lesh.' wuh aushfa-kuht leralmin-tor: 'ek' gas'rak, ' heh nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar heh lesh ish-veh tor wuh pasture, heh eku ish-veh among wuh yar. Wuh pi' vaukh kwon-hau-ov hafau standing spo' veh if vesh' eating, heh wuh aushfa-kuht leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh dungi ak sahr-tor k' itself, aishan glazhau uf ish-veh yokul already!' na' mu-yor lu au vesh' going tor yetur wuh kuht ha-kel va'ashiv, au leralmin-tor tor wuh vaukh: 'kuv du mokuhlek lamok tra' heh yokul ish-veh boshaya, du mokuhlek isha hal-tor fi' ish-veh kehkuh mal; i ri tor tun tor zaseshau du ha-kel va'ashiv svi' t'nash-veh kar.' tonk'peh wuh pi' peasant lam-tor na' ish-veh svep, heh bek-tor na' ish-veh pi' vaukh, heh lu wuh aushfa-kuht drove wuh aushfa k'fai wuh pi'kahr, heh wuh vaukh vesh' missing, au inquired wilat ish-veh vesh'. Wuh aushfa-kuht kilko-tor: 'ish-veh nam-tor fam dvun standing si' tra' eating. Ish-veh would ri pehkaya heh sarlah k' etek.' tonk'peh wuh pi' peasant leralmin-tor: 'oh, tonk'peh i bolau ma t'nash-veh beast pla' va'ashiv.' yi au went pla' tor wuh ne-yartra teretuhr, tonk'peh ein-veh had stolen wuh vaukh, heh ish-veh vesh' hal-tor. Wuh aushfa-kuht leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh bolau ma sahr-tor maf.' wuh peasant, however, leralmin-tor: 'ri tor var-tor me ik, ' heh pufulag-tor wuh aushfa-kuht fa' wuh mayor, vi na' ish-veh carelessness condemned ish-veh tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh peasant wuh aushfa na' wuh vaukh if had sahr-tor maf. Heh i' wuh pi' peasant heh ish-veh ko-telsu had wuh aushfa na' if au had ni wu istau, heh au vesh' heartily glad, tonk'peh au had rai yem-tukh na' ish-veh, heh kupi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh nothing tor yokul, ni ish-veh ak had tor nam-tor pustau. Au salted wuh kahm, heh wuh peasant went vi' wuh kahr heh aitlu tor makau wuh wadi tra', ni ik au lau mahr-tor wuh uzh vaukh k' wuh proceeds. Fi' wuh yut au be' dvun-tor k' wuh mill, heh tra' hayal-tor wuh raven k' pushau rala, heh s' pity au nem-tor ish-veh heh wrapped ish-veh svi' wuh wadi. Tonk'peh u' wuh igen-va grew ni rasahkos heh tra' vesh' wuh sahriv t' sov-masu heh salan, au kupi hal-tor rai weh-irak, heh da-tor pla' tor wuh mill heh eit'jae na' rau-nol. Wuh miller's ko-telsu vesh' sa'awek svi' wuh kelek, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh peasant: 'ti yourself fi' wuh terp tra', ' heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shihvek t' kap heh thuhk. Wuh peasant ate ish-veh, heh ti ne' k' ish-veh wadi be' ish-veh, heh wuh kosu nahp: 'au nam-tor zungor heh has hal-tor tor yuk.' svi' wuh meantime sarlah wuh parson; wuh miller's ko-telsu poprah ish-veh muhl, heh leralmin-tor: 't'nash-veh sa-telsu nam-tor si', ni etek dungi ma wuh gadzhak.' wuh peasant shroi, heh lu au puzhu-tor au variben pa' feasting au vesh' smertau ik au had vesh' punekwitau tor tor izaya k' wuh shihvek t' kap heh thuhk. Yi wuh kosu dvin-tor abru kehkuh natya vel, roast kahm, yarmok, cakes, heh wine. Aishan u' au vesh' pa' tor hayal-tor ne' heh yokul, tra' vesh' wuh knocking s'udish. Wuh kosu leralmin-tor: 'oh, heavens! Ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu!' she sahris ip-sut wuh roast kahm svi'udish wuh tiled stove, wuh wine ne' wuh trak, wuh yarmok fi' wuh sar-tak, wuh cakes ne' ish-veh, heh wuh parson svi' wuh tsorayek fi' wuh porch. Yi she tu'ash wuh svep na' ish-veh sa-telsu, heh leralmin-tor: 'itaren sha-ka-ri, du nam-tor pla' va'ashiv! Tra' nam-tor such wuh sahriv, ish-veh glazhau u' kuv wuh panu vesh' coming tor wuh shaht.' wuh miller gla-tor wuh peasant lying fi' wuh terp, heh ya'akash, 'ra nam-tor ik katravahsu doing tra'?' 'ah, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu, 'wuh ri donku-tor knave sarlah svi' wuh sahriv heh sov-masu, heh eit'jae na' rau-nol, ni i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh zeshau t' kap heh thuhk, heh gluvau ish-veh wilat wuh terp vesh'.' wuh sasu leralmin-tor: 'i ma rai objection, tonk'peh nam-tor sahris heh prah me vel tor yokul.' wuh kosu leralmin-tor: 'tonk'peh i ma nothing tonk'peh kap heh thuhk.' 'i am contented k' sovek-vel, ' kilko-tor wuh sa-telsu, 'ni irak u' i am concerned, kap heh thuhk dungi tor, ' heh glazhau na' wuh peasant heh leralmin-tor: 'sarlah heh yokul ein weht k' me.' wuh peasant did ri require tor nam-tor invited dah'wak, tonk'peh prah abru heh ate. Po' nash wuh miller gla-tor wuh wadi svi' if wuh raven vesh', lying fi' wuh solektra, heh ya'akash: 'ra ma du tra'?' wuh peasant kilko-tor: 'i ma wuh soothsayer svi'udish ish-veh.' 'mokuhlek au fa-ariben sovek-vel tor me?' leralmin-tor wuh miller. 'po ri?' kilko-tor wuh peasant: 'tonk'peh au goh leralmin-tor kehkuh vel, heh wuh fifth au potau tor himself.' wuh miller vesh' curious, heh leralmin-tor: 'kal-tor ish-veh fa-ariben vel na' wuh'wak.' yi wuh peasant k'hy wuh raven's patam, ni ik au croaked heh tor wuh ralash spo' krr, krr. Wuh miller leralmin-tor: 'ra did au leralmin?' wuh peasant kilko-tor: 'svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, au leralmin-tor ik tra' nam-tor ein wine ipik ne' wuh trak.' 'kudau me!' maf-tor wuh miller, heh went tra' heh afer-tor wuh wine. 'i' hal-tor fi', ' leralmin-tor au. Wuh peasant tor wuh raven croak va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor: 'svi' wuh dahr shi, au leralmin-tor ik tra' nam-tor ein roast kahm svi' wuh tiled stove.' 'fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit!' maf-tor wuh miller, heh went thither, heh afer-tor wuh roast kahm. Wuh peasant tor wuh raven prophesy fam dvun weht, heh leralmin-tor: 'thirdly, au leralmin-tor ik tra' nam-tor ein yarmok fi' wuh sar-tak.' 'ik would nam-tor wuh tok-ti vel!' maf-tor wuh miller, heh went tra' heh afer-tor wuh yarmok. Na' kim-shah wuh peasant k'hy wuh raven wuh'wak weht till au croaked, heh leralmin-tor: 'fourthly, au leralmin-tor ik tra' nam-tor ein cakes ne' wuh sar-tak.' 'ik would nam-tor wuh tok-ti vel!' maf-tor wuh miller, heh glazhau tra', heh afer-tor wuh cakes. Heh i' wuh dahkuh hayal-tor ne' tor wuh pasu teretuhr, tonk'peh wuh miller's ko-telsu vesh' koltha tor tevakh, heh went tor sar-tak heh nem-tor ek' wuh tal-muv k' ish-veh. Wuh miller would ma tishau mau tor fai-tor wuh fifth, tonk'peh wuh pi' peasant leralmin-tor: 'wuh'rak, etek dungi sahris yokul wuh kehkuh vel, na' wuh fifth nam-tor vel rasahkos.' ni au ate, heh po' ik au bargained uf mau wuh miller vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor na' wuh fifth prophecy, abi' au sep-wafikh fi' rehkuh hundred talers. Yi wuh peasant wuh'wak weht k'hy wuh raven's patam till au croaked loudly. Wuh miller ya'akash: 'ra did au leralmin?' wuh peasant kilko-tor: 'au leralmin-tor ik wuh e'shua nam-tor hiding s'udish tra' svi' wuh tsorayek fi' wuh porch.' wuh miller leralmin-tor: 'wuh e'shua bolau hal-tor si', ' heh tu'ash wuh kelek-svep; yi wuh kosu vesh' punekwitau tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh tal-muv, heh wuh peasant unlocked wuh tsorayek. Wuh parson sahr-tor si' u' sahris u' au kupi, heh wuh miller leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh vesh' yeht; vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh nesh-kur rascal k' t'nash-veh sha' bezhun.' wuh peasant, however, tor ska' thurai asal k' gad-keshtan k' wuh rehkuh hundred talers. Na' ha-kel wuh pi' peasant gradually puspusau si'; au torvau wuh vaksurik kelek, heh wuh peasants leralmin-tor: 'wuh pi' peasant has certainly vesh' tor wuh shi wilat pi-maat-kur izh tevan-tor, heh sutra lesh wuh pi-maat-tukh ha-kel svi' hilek.' yi wuh pi' peasant vesh' katau fa' wuh mayor, heh bidden tor leralmin s' whence ish-veh don-tak sarlah. Au kilko-tor: 'i makau t'nash-veh aushfa's wadi svi' wuh kahr, na' rehkuh hundred talers.' lu wuh peasants puzhu-tor ik, au nuh' istau tor tizh-tor nash lo'uk pinkaunu, heh sahr-tor ha-kel, pustau ek' ish-veh aushfa, heh stripped ska' ish-veh wadi svi' zek tor makau au svi' wuh kahr tor wuh greatest advantage. Wuh mayor, however, leralmin-tor: 'tonk'peh t'nash-veh dvinsu bolau hal-tor wuh'rak.' lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh merchant svi' wuh kahr, au did ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh weht do dahkuh talers na' wuh wadi, heh lu wuh vath sarlah, au did ri mazhiv-kur-tor au ni mau, heh leralmin-tor: 'ra mokuhlek i tor k' ek' aifa wadi?' yi wuh peasants vesh' smertau ik wuh pi' peasant dang ma thus outwitted au, aitlu tor nem-tor vengeance fi' ish-veh, heh accused ish-veh t' nash treachery fa' wuh mayor. Wuh innocent pi' peasant vesh' unanimously sentenced tor tevakh, heh vesh' tor nam-tor padukau vi' wuh masu, svi' wuh subok tilau bosh t' razh. Au vesh' pufulag-tor forth, heh wuh priest vesh' katau vi vesh' tor leralmin wuh shivak na' ish-veh soul. Wuh vath vesh' ek' obliged tor retire tor wuh ir, heh lu wuh peasant glazhau na' wuh priest, au recognized wuh sasu vi had vesh' k' wuh miller's ko-telsu. Au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'i eku du elik s' wuh tsorayek, eku me elik s' wuh subok.' na' nash ka moment abru sarlah, k' wuh treit t' sheep, wuh maut shepherd ik wuh peasant fai-tor had wu vesh' wishing tor nam-tor mayor, ni au maf-tor k' ek' ish-veh lau: 'rai, i dungi ri tor ish-veh; kuv wuh bosh panu insists fi' ish-veh, i dungi ri tor ish-veh!' wuh shepherd khaf-spol ik, sarlah abru tor ish-veh, heh ya'akash: 'ra nam-tor du pa'? Ra nam-tor ish-veh ik du dungi ri tor?' wuh peasant leralmin-tor: 'au aitlun tor tor me mayor, kuv i dungi tonk'peh shitau myself svi' wuh subok, tonk'peh i dungi ri tor ish-veh.' wuh shepherd leralmin-tor: 'kuv nothing weht do ik nam-tor needful svi' zek tor nam-tor mayor, i would prah vi' wuh subok na' wuh'wak.' wuh peasant leralmin-tor: 'kuv du dungi prah svi', du dungi nam-tor mayor.' wuh shepherd vesh' willing, heh prah svi', heh wuh peasant ikap-tor wuh fik ne' fi' ish-veh; yi au nem-tor wuh shepherd's treit na' himself, heh drove ish-veh maf. Wuh parson went tor wuh patreitan, heh afsakau ik wuh shivak had vesh' leralmin-tor. Yi sarlah au heh padukau wuh subok na' wuh masu. Lu wuh subok began tor padukau, wuh shepherd maf-tor: 'i am ved willing tor nam-tor mayor.' au pudva-tor rai vathru do ik ish-veh vesh' wuh peasant vi vesh' taran nash, heh kilko-tor: 'ik nam-tor ra etek intend, tonk'peh wuh'rak du dungau glazhau pa' du wuh pi' ne' ne' tra', ' heh au padukau wuh subok ne' vi' wuh masu. Po' ik wuh peasants went ha-kel, heh u' au vesh' entering wuh pi'kahr, wuh pi' peasant isha sarlah quietly svi', driving wuh treit t' sheep heh looking ved contented. Yi wuh peasants vesh' astonished, heh leralmin-tor: 'peasant, s' whence tor sarlah du? Ma du sasarlah t' wuh masu?' 'ha, truly, ' kilko-tor wuh peasant, 'i sank glu, glu ne', abi' na' kim-shah i prah tor wuh lanet; i kwitau wuh lanet s' wuh subok, heh crept si', heh tra' vesh' takov ne-yartra fi' if wuh su'etek t' lambs vesh' feeding, heh s' thence i katau nash treit maf k' me.' leralmin-tor wuh peasants: 'nam-tor tra' sovek weht tra'?' 'oh, ha, ' leralmin-tor au, 'weht do i kupi aitlun.' yi wuh peasants tor abru ish-veh kashkau ik au nuh' would zaprah ein sheep na' themselves, wuh treit apiece, tonk'peh wuh mayor leralmin-tor: 'sarlah nash-veh wuh'rak.' ni au went tor wuh masu teretuhr, heh aishan yi tra' vesh' ein t' wuh pi' fleecy wan svi' wuh pla-kur igen, if nam-tor puvutau pi' lambs, heh au vesh' haul-tor svi' wuh masu, whereupon wuh peasants maf-tor: 'etek already gla-tor wuh sheep ne' ne'!' wuh mayor hish-tor fa'rak heh leralmin-tor: 'i dungi hal-tor ne' wuh'rak, heh glazhau pa' me, heh kuv vel ugaya muhl i'll vutau du.' ni au spen-tor svi'; splash! Went wuh masu; ish-veh sounded u' kuv au vesh' calling au, heh wuh bosh patreitan taul-tor svi' po' ish-veh u' veh sasu. Yi wuh entire pi'kahr vesh' tevik, heh wuh pi' peasant, u' lad heir, became wuh don-ka sasu. Frederick heh catherine tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh sasu puvutau frederick: au had wuh ko-telsu t'vi ahm vesh' catherine, heh au had ri wu vesh' telik. Veh gad frederick leralmin-tor. 'kate! I am going tor ar'kadan svi' wuh vunai; lu sarlah nash-veh pla' i dungau nam-tor k'avon ni kal-tor me ma vel nice pufas-tor, heh wuh rom draught t' ale.' 'maut muhl, ' leralmin-tor she, 'ish-veh dungau ek' nam-tor pok.' lu aru-yem-wak drew nigh, catherine nem-tor wuh nice steak, if vesh' ek' wuh kahm she had, heh shitau ish-veh fi' wuh yon tor pol-tor. Wuh steak ak began tor glazhau khav-kur, heh tor crackle svi' wuh sunil; heh catherine lam-tor k' k' wuh snauk heh da-tor ish-veh: yi she leralmin-tor tor herself, 'wuh steak nam-tor siyah pok, i lau u' muhl hal-tor tor wuh cellar na' wuh ale.' ni she losrak wuh sunil fi' wuh yon heh nem-tor wuh suk mashek heh went vi' wuh cellar heh tapped wuh ale cask. Wuh naliveh sahr-tor vi' wuh mashek heh catherine lam-tor looking fi'. Na' kim-shah ish-veh popped vi' ish-veh patam, 'wuh dog nam-tor ri ikap'uh t'du ru'lut--au lau nam-tor sahran maf k' wuh steak; ik's muhl nahp t'.' ni abru she sahr-tor s' wuh cellar; heh sure hiyet wuh rascally cur had prah wuh steak svi' ish-veh ru'lut, heh vesh' tor ska' k' ish-veh. Maf sahr-tor catherine, heh maf sahr-tor wuh dog mes' wuh vunai: tonk'peh au sahr-tor faster do she, heh terpau beyik wuh steak. 'ish-veh's ek' hal-tor, heh "ra mokuhlek't nam-tor bohrau bolau nam-tor palesh-tor", ' leralmin-tor catherine. Ni she da-tor pauk; heh u' she had sahr-tor wuh rom yut heh vesh' zungor, she lates-tor ha-kel leisurely tor samuyau herself. I' ek' nash wak wuh ale vesh' sahran nuh', na' catherine had ri da-tor wuh cock; heh lu wuh mashek vesh' bosh wuh liquor sahr-tor fi-tor wuh lan-tol till wuh cask vesh' herbosh. Lu she prah tor wuh cellar kaiden gla-tor ish-veh ra had pavesh-tor. 't'nash-veh yel!' leralmin-tor she, 'ra dungau i tor tor potau frederick s' seeing ek' nash slopping pa'?' ni she nahp wuh du'; heh na' kim-shah vokau ik tra' vesh' wuh sa'haf t' tok-ti yem bought na' wuh kim-shah rom, heh ik kuv she sprinkled nash abru' wuh lan-tol ish-veh would suck abru wuh ale nicely. 'ra wuh kunli vel, ' leralmin-tor she, 'ik etek potau ik yem! Etek ma i' wuh rom nam-tor-tor na' ish-veh.' ni maf she went na' ish-veh: tonk'peh she khartau tor eku ish-veh ne' aishan fi-tor wuh lo'uk mashek bosh t' naliveh, heh upset ish-veh; heh thus ek' wuh ale ik had vesh' korsau vesh' eku mahalan fi' wuh lan-tol isha. 'ah! Muhl, ' leralmin-tor she, 'lu veh hal-tor wuh'ashiv lau u' muhl zahal-tor.' yi she strewed wuh yem ek' pa' wuh cellar, heh vesh' ved sanoi k' ish-veh cleverness, heh leralmin-tor, 'uf maut pu heh sok'i ish-veh glazhau!' na' aru frederick sarlah ha-kel. 'i', ko-telsu, ' maf-tor au, 'ra ma du na' aru-yem?' 'o frederick!' kilko-tor she, 'i vesh' fasan du wuh steak; tonk'peh du' i went ne' tor bes-tor wuh ale, wuh dog sahr-tor maf k' ish-veh; heh du' i sahr-tor po' ish-veh, wuh ale sahr-tor si'; heh lu i went tor pseth abru wuh ale k' wuh sa'haf t' yem ik etek prah na' wuh rom, i upset wuh mashek: tonk'peh wuh cellar nam-tor i' ved pseth, heh glazhau ni sok'i!' 'kate, kate, ' leralmin-tor au, 'uf kupi du tor ek' nash?' po did du trasha wuh steak tor pol-tor, heh wuh ale tor sahr-tor, heh yi spoil ek' wuh yem?' 'po, frederick, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i did ri fai-tor i vesh' doing riyeht; du dang ma var-tor me fa'.' wuh sa-telsu nahp tor himself, 'kuv t'nash-veh ko-telsu khartau tukh thus, i bolau glazhau nasik myself.' i' au had wuh rom deal t' pi-maat-tukh svi' wuh kelek: ni au leralmin-tor tor catherine, 'ra takov kin-kur gonaf aifa nam-tor! I dungau shitau au vi' wuh natuhn heh visolektau au svi' wuh bah-ker; tonk'peh nem-tor tun ik du worla hal-tor be' il meddle k' au.' 'rai, frederick, ' leralmin-tor she, 'ik i worla dungi.' u' ak u' au vesh' hal-tor, tra' sarlah k' ein pedlars k' earthenware math heh dishes, heh au ya'akash ish-veh whether she would mahr-tor. 'oh tal-kam me, i dang spo' tor mahr-tor maut mau, tonk'peh i ma rai donku: kuv du had sovek nam-tor-tor na' kin-kur gonaf, i lau deal k' du.' 'kin-kur gonaf!' leralmin-tor au: 'kal-tor etek ma wuh glazhau na' au.' 'hal-tor vi' wuh bah-ker heh hil-tor wilat i var-tor du, heh du dungi talal wuh kin-kur gonaf: i dare ri hal-tor myself.' ni wuh rogues went: heh lu au afer-tor ra aifa kin-kur gonaf vesh', au nem-tor au ek' maf, heh losrak ish-veh plenty t' math heh dishes. Yi she eku au ek' pa' wuh kelek na' wuh gluvaya: heh lu frederick sarlah pla', au lit'dhae, 'kate, ra ma du vesh' doing?' 'gla-tor, ' leralmin-tor she, 'i ma bought ek' aifa k' ish-veh kin-kur gonaf: tonk'peh i did ri esta au myself; wuh pedlars went themselves heh hil-tor au abru.' 'ko-telsu, ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor frederick, 'ra wuh takov krus t' ar'kadan du ma tor! Eifa kin-kur gonaf vesh' ek' t'nash-veh donku: uf sarlah du tor tor such wuh vel?' 'po, ' kilko-tor she, 'i did ri fai-tor tra' vesh' sovek klau svi' ish-veh; du dang ma var-tor me.' catherine lam-tor musing na' wuh du', heh na' kim-shah leralmin-tor tor ish-veh sa-telsu, 'hark ye, frederick, etek dungi ak prah wuh pi-maat-tukh pla': kal-tor etek sahr-tor po' wuh pi'tak.' 'muhl, etek dungi ar'kadan, ' kilko-tor au; 'tonk'peh nem-tor ein butter heh thuhk k' du, ik etek lau ma vel tor yokul k' wuh yut.' 'maut muhl, ' leralmin-tor she; heh au eku si': heh u' frederick lates-tor wuh fastest, au losrak ish-veh ko-telsu ein yut za'. 'ish-veh tor ri tukh, ' nahp she: 'lu etek da-tor pla', i dungau nam-tor ni mau nearer ha-kel do au.' presently sarlah ish-veh tor wuh fik t' wuh kunel, ne' wuh vla t' if tra' vesh' wuh fau-yut ni wonil ik wuh hal halek kwon-hau-ov chafed wuh lap fi' tik vla u' au be' dvun-tor. 'ah, gla-tor i', ' leralmin-tor she, 'uf au ma bruised heh wounded eifa ri donku-tor lap; au dungi worla prah muhl.' ni she nem-tor pity fi' au, heh tor nam-tor-tor t' wuh butter tor elmin au ek', ni ik wuh halek lau ri dash-tor au ni mau. Du' she vesh' doing nash ves office veh t' ish-veh thuhk tevan-tor s' wuh ki'haf, heh padukau ne' wuh kunel. Catherine glazhau, tonk'peh kupi ri gla-tor wilat ish-veh had hal-tor; ni she leralmin-tor, 'muhl, i suppose wuh vath dungi hal-tor wuh ka yut heh talal du; au has younger mal do i ma.' yi she padukau wuh vath thuhk po' ish-veh; heh maf ish-veh went, kling fai-tor wilat, ne' wuh kunel. Tonk'peh she leralmin-tor she supposed ik au fai-tor wuh fau-yut, heh would zahal-tor ish-veh, heh she kupi ri stay tra' ek' gad waiting na' au. Na' kim-shah she overtook frederick, vi aitlu ish-veh tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh vel tor yokul. Yi she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh pseth kap. 'wilat nam-tor wuh butter heh thuhk?' leralmin-tor au. 'oh!' kilko-tor she, 'i nam-tor-tor wuh butter tor elmin eifa ri donku-tor lap ik wuh halek chafed ni: heh veh t' wuh thuhk sahr-tor maf ni i satau wuh vath po' ish-veh tor talal ish-veh, heh i suppose au nam-tor fi' fi' wuh fau-yut teretuhr ein-wilat.' 'ra wuh kushel du nam-tor tor tor such silly vel!' leralmin-tor wuh sa-telsu. 'uf mokuhlek du leralmin ni?' leralmin-tor she; 'i am sure du worla var-tor me ri.' au ate wuh pseth kap teretuhr; heh frederick leralmin-tor, 'kate, i rok du klacha wuh svep safe lu sarlah du maf.' 'rai, ' kilko-tor she, 'du did ri var-tor me.' 'yi hal-tor ha-kel, heh tor ish-veh i' fa' etek hal-tor sovek weh-irak, ' leralmin-tor frederick, 'heh katau k' du vel tor yokul.' catherine did u' au var-tor ish-veh, heh nahp tor herself k' wuh yut, 'frederick aitlu vel tor yokul; tonk'peh i ri tor nah-tor au nam-tor maut tishau t' butter heh thuhk: i'll katau ish-veh wuh sa'haf t' tok-ti kov-sayas, heh wuh sfith-masu, na' i ma k'ashiv gla-tor ish-veh nem-tor ein.' lu she pulau ha-kel, she terkau wuh pla' svep, tonk'peh wuh khom svep she nem-tor ska' wuh tu'adayek, heh leralmin-tor, 'frederick var-tor me tor klachek wuh svep, tonk'peh surely ish-veh mokuhlek nowhere nam-tor ni safe kuv i nem-tor ish-veh k' me.' ni she nem-tor ish-veh wak k' wuh yut; heh lu she overtook ish-veh sa-telsu she maf-tor si', 'tra', frederick, tra' nam-tor wuh svep itself, du lau glantau ish-veh u' carefully u' du sanoi.' 'alas! Alas!' leralmin-tor au, 'ra wuh clever ko-telsu i ma! I satau du tor tor wuh kelek sahris, heh du nem-tor wuh svep maf, ni ik kanok-veh lau hal-tor svi' heh si' u' au sanoi--however, u' du ma katau wuh svep, du dungau lesh ish-veh pa' k' du na' ish-veh kusut-tor.' 'maut muhl, ' kilko-tor she, 'i'll lesh wuh svep; tonk'peh i'll ri lesh wuh kov-sayas heh sfith-masu mashek isha--ik would nam-tor nuh' mau t' wuh tus; ni kuv du sanoi, i'll terau au tor wuh svep.' frederick veling tor rai objection tor ik dotor, heh au eku ska' vi' wuh lapan tor glazhau na' wuh pi'tak; tonk'peh au kupi ri talal au: heh lu ish-veh grew gu'gelik, au sasu-tor abru vi' wuh lap tor spend wuh mu-yor tra'. Scarcely vesh' au abru, do vi dang sarlah k' tonk'peh wuh maut rogues au vesh' looking na'. Au vesh' svi' yeht'es lo'uk rascals, heh belonged tor ik mohrn t' sutra vi talal vel fa' au nam-tor pakik; au vesh' zungor; ni au hayal-tor ne' heh tor wuh yon ne' wuh maut lap wilat frederick heh catherine vesh'. Frederick trel-tor ne' fi' wuh vath vla, heh abrashau ein kov. Yi au sasu-tor abru va'ashiv, heh ar'kada tor kwul wuh pi'tak fi' wuh patam k' au: tonk'peh au goh leralmin-tor, 'ish-veh bolau nam-tor be' asal, na' wuh salan hutau wuh fir-savas ne'.' catherine, vi had wuh svep fi' ish-veh tipan, began tor nam-tor maut zungor; tonk'peh she nahp ish-veh vesh' wuh kov-sayas fi-tor ish-veh ik vesh' ni ras: ni she leralmin-tor softly, 'frederick, i bolau kal-tor wuh kov-sayas hal-tor.' 'rai, ' kilko-tor au, 'ri i', au dungi discover etek.' 'i mokuhlek't gol'nev ik: au bolau hal-tor.' 'muhl, yi, tor haste heh lehm au ne', kuv du dungi.' yi maf rattled wuh kov-sayas ne' among wuh boughs heh veh t' wuh pi'tak maf-tor, 'kudau me, ish-veh nam-tor hailing.' wuh pi' du' po', catherine nahp wuh svep vesh' fam dvun maut ras: ni she zhal-tor tor frederick, 'i bolau lehm wuh sfith-masu ne'.' 'pray ri tor, ' kilko-tor au, 'ish-veh dungi discover etek.' 'i mokuhlek't gol'nev ik, ' leralmin-tor she, 'hal-tor ish-veh bolau.' ni she mukau ek' wuh sfith-masu ne'; heh wuh pi'tak leralmin-tor, 'ra wuh ras asal-masu tra' nam-tor!' na' kim-shah ish-veh popped vi' catherine's patam ik ish-veh vesh' wuh svep itself ik vesh' ni ras ek' wuh wak: ni she zhal-tor, 'frederick, i bolau lehm wuh svep ne' ak.' tonk'peh au eit'jae heh prayed ish-veh ri tor tor ni, na' au vesh' sure ish-veh would svik-tor au. 'la' hal-tor, however, ' leralmin-tor she: heh ne' went wuh svep k' such wuh clatter fi-tor wuh pi'tak, ik au maf-tor si' 'riyeht-staya!' heh ri fai-tor ra vesh' coming, sahr-tor maf u' sahris u' au kupi, heh losrak ek' wuh pi-maat-tukh. Ni lu frederick heh catherine sarlah ne', tra' au afer-tor ek' ish-veh donku safe heh ralash. Sweetheart roland tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh kosu vi vesh' wuh yeht witch heh had dahkuh daughters, veh watosh heh wicked, heh nash-veh she ashau fai'ei she vesh' ish-veh sha' ko-fu, heh veh vaksurik heh rom, heh nash-veh she fnu-ven, fai'ei she vesh' ish-veh stepdaughter. Wuh stepdaughter wuh'wak had wuh takov apron, if wuh vath fancied ni mau ik she became envious, heh var-tor ish-veh ko-mekh ik she bolau heh would ma ik apron. 'nam'uh hizhuk, t'nash-veh kan, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu, 'heh du dungau ma ish-veh. Ish-veh stepsister has wu nazh-tor tevakh; tonight lu she nam-tor asleep dungi-sarlah nash-veh heh tresahk ish-veh patam ska'. Goh nam-tor tun-bosh ik du nam-tor na' wuh irak vla t' wuh sar-tak, heh kwitaya ish-veh muhl tor wuh khom.' ish-veh would ma vesh' ek' abru' k' wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan kuv she had ri aishan yi vesh' standing svi' wuh teruk, heh puzhu-tor kanok-vei. Ek' gad wu she dared ri hal-tor s' svep, heh lu bedtime had sarlah, wuh witch's ko-fu prah vi' sar-tak wuh'rak, ni u' tor ti na' wuh irak vla, tonk'peh lu she vesh' asleep, wuh vath kwitau ish-veh kogavik tor wuh khom, heh nem-tor na' herself wuh shi na' wuh pla', beyik wuh temok. Svi' wuh mu-yor, wuh hinek kosu sarlah creeping svi', she meskarau wuh la'ash svi' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru, heh olau k' ish-veh losrak tor gla-tor kuv sovek-veh vesh' lying na' wuh s'udish, heh yi she ruskarau wuh la'ash k' fi' el'ru, heh tresahk ish-veh sha' kan's patam ska'. Lu she had hal-tor maf, wuh ko-kan prah abru heh went tor ish-veh sweetheart, vi vesh' puvutau roland, heh knocked na' ish-veh svep. Lu au sasarlah, she leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'shroi, dearest roland, etek bolau hash-tor svi' ek' haste; t'nash-veh stepmother aitlu tor stau me, tonk'peh has kwul-tor ish-veh sha' kan. Lu gad-ha'khlup sarlah, heh gla-tor ish-veh ra she has ovsoh, etek dungau nam-tor pakik.' 'tonk'peh, ' leralmin-tor roland, 'i counsel du wuh'rak tor nem-tor maf ish-veh magic wand, il etek fam yehat stron kuv she pursues etek.' wuh maiden zaprah wuh magic wand, heh she nem-tor wuh tevik ko-kan's patam heh eku-tor rehkuh eku-tor t' khaf fi' wuh solektra, veh svi' khom t' wuh sar-tak, veh svi' wuh af'tum, heh veh fi' wuh kaiden. Yi she hurried maf k' ish-veh lover. Lu wuh hinek witch prah abru thurai asal, she puvutau ish-veh ko-fu, heh aitlu tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh apron, tonk'peh she did ri sarlah. Yi wuh witch maf-tor: 'wilat nam-tor du?' 'la', fi' wuh kaiden, i am sweeping, ' kilko-tor wuh wuh'rak eku t' khaf. Wuh hinek kosu went si', tonk'peh gla-tor kling fi' wuh kaiden, heh maf-tor va'ashiv: 'wilat nam-tor du?' 'la' svi' wuh af'tum, i am warming myself, ' maf-tor wuh dahr eku t' khaf. She went vi' wuh af'tum, tonk'peh afer-tor kling. Yi she maf-tor va'ashiv: 'wilat nam-tor du?' 'ah, la' svi' wuh sar-tak, i am sleeping, ' maf-tor wuh wuh eku t' khaf. She went vi' wuh tvi-shal tor wuh sar-tak. Ra did she gla-tor tra'? Ish-veh sha' kan, t'vi patam she had tresahk ska', bathed svi' ish-veh khaf. Wuh witch tevan-tor vi' wuh shaukaush, sprang tor wuh krani, heh u' she kupi glazhau forth ved irak vi' wuh panu, she pakashogau ish-veh stepdaughter hurrying maf k' ish-veh sweetheart roland. 'ik dungau ri gol'nev du, ' maf-tor she, 'kauk kuv du ma prah wuh wu yut ska', du dungau fam dvun ri stron me.' she shitau fi' ish-veh wehk-league kluf, svi' if she wein-tor wuh wadan's lates na' kanok ash, heh ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' she overtook au. Wuh ko-kan, however, lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh hinek kosu striding na' ish-veh, rubai, k' ish-veh magic wand, ish-veh sweetheart roland vi' wuh suk'muzh, heh herself vi' wuh duck mahalan svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh. Wuh witch shitau herself fi' wuh gef, threw breadcrumbs svi', heh went tor shaht-fam trouble tor entice wuh duck; tonk'peh wuh duck did ri kal-tor herself nam-tor enticed, heh wuh hinek kosu had tor hal-tor ha-kel na' mu-yor u' she had sarlah. Na' nash wuh ko-kan heh ish-veh sweetheart roland resumed ish-veh malatik shid va'ashiv, heh au lates-tor fi' wuh bosh mu-yor abi' gad-keshtan. Yi wuh maiden rubai herself vi' wuh vaksurik svai if lam-tor svi' wuh midst t' wuh briar labah, heh ish-veh sweetheart roland vi' wuh fiddler. Ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' wuh witch sarlah striding abru na' au, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh ralash-tanafsu: 'tal-kam ralash-tanafsu, sos pluck ik vaksurik svai na' myself?' 'oh, ha, ' au kilko-tor, 'i dungi mavau tor du du' du tor ish-veh.' u' she vesh' hastily creeping vi' wuh labah heh vesh' aishan going tor pluck wuh svai, fai-tor perfectly muhl vi wuh svai vesh', au began tor mavau, heh whether she would il ri, she vesh' punekwitau tor tam, na' ish-veh vesh' wuh magical tam. Wuh faster au mavau, wuh weht khrashik sikar vesh' she punekwitau tor tor, heh wuh thorns tore ish-veh sai-vel s' ish-veh ak'shem, heh pricked ish-veh heh wounded ish-veh till she bled, heh u' au did ri pehkaya, she had tor tam till she ti tevik fi' wuh solektra. U' au vesh' i' eku elik, roland leralmin-tor: 'i' i dungi hal-tor tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh heh arrange na' wuh wedding.' 'yi svi' wuh meantime i dungi stay la' heh bek-tor na' du, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-kan, 'heh ik kling lau recognize me, i dungi rubah myself vi' wuh yon-kur kov landmark.' yi roland went maf, heh wuh ko-kan lam-tor spo' wuh yon-kur landmark svi' wuh vunai heh bek-tor na' ish-veh k'diwa. Tonk'peh lu roland prah ha-kel, au tevan-tor vi' wuh snares t' wuh'ashiv, vi ni sem-tor ish-veh ik au forgot wuh maiden. Wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan hafau tra' wuh akarshif, tonk'peh na' wu-vath, u' au did ri fun na' ek', she vesh' maf, heh rubai herself vi' wuh svai, heh nahp: 'ein-veh dungi surely sarlah nash yut, heh sahr-tor me ne'.' ish-veh befell, however, ik wuh shepherd potau ish-veh sheep svi' wuh vunai heh gla-tor wuh svai, heh u' ish-veh vesh' ni takov, plucked ish-veh, nem-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh, heh laid ish-veh maf svi' ish-veh tuf. S' ik wak forth, flekh vel pavesh-tor svi' wuh shepherd's kelek. Lu au arose svi' wuh asal, ek' wuh ar'kadan vesh' already ovsoh, wuh tvi-shal vesh' swept, wuh pasu heh wu-ku-san pu-tor, wuh yon svi' wuh hearth vesh' lighted, heh wuh masu vesh' zaprah, heh na' aru, lu sarlah ish-veh ha-kel, wuh pasu vesh' laid, heh wuh rom aru-yem dvin-tor. Au kupi ri conceive uf nash sarlah tor be' dvun, na' au worla gla-tor wuh komihn hasu svi' ish-veh kelek, heh kling kupi ma ip-sut himself svi' ish-veh. Au vesh' certainly sanoi k' nash rom attendance, tonk'peh fam dvun na' kim-shah au vesh' ni kwes ik au went tor wuh kau-bosh kosu heh ya'akash na' ish-veh na'shikh. Wuh kau-bosh kosu leralmin-tor: 'tra' nam-tor ein enchantment za' ish-veh, shroi maut lehkuh-mal ein asal kuv sovek-vel nam-tor dvun-tor svi' wuh tvi-shal, heh kuv gla-tor du sovek-vel, rai tukh ra ish-veh nam-tor, lehm wuh wan-kur sai abru' ish-veh, heh yi wuh magic dungi nam-tor pehkau.' wuh shepherd did u' she bade ish-veh, heh thurai asal aishan u' gad dawned, gla-tor ish-veh wuh tuf tu'ash, heh wuh svai sasarlah. Swiftly au sprang na' ish-veh, heh threw wuh wan-kur sai abru' ish-veh. Instantly wuh mesuvulaya sarlah tor wuh shaht, heh wuh vaksurik ko-kan lam-tor fa' ish-veh, vi nafai-tor tor ish-veh ik she had vesh' wuh svai, heh ik abru tor nash wak she had attended tor ish-veh kelek-keeping. She var-tor ish-veh ish-veh var, heh u' she sanoi ish-veh au ya'akash ish-veh kuv she would marry ish-veh, tonk'peh she kilko-tor: 'rai, ' na' she aitlu tor hafau faithful tor ish-veh sweetheart roland, hi au had deserted ish-veh. Nevertheless, she ugau ri tor hal-tor maf, tonk'peh tor fator keeping kelek na' wuh shepherd. Heh i' wuh wak drew be' lu roland's wedding vesh' tor nam-tor u'thet, heh yi, fupa s' wuh hinek custom svi' wuh shasol, ish-veh vesh' tor'pra ik ek' wuh ko-kan vesh' tor nam-tor la' na' ish-veh, heh uralau svi' dor t' wuh bridal shif. Lu wuh faithful maiden puzhu-tor t' nash, she grew ni maf ik she nahp ish-veh khaf-spol would shaya, heh she would ri hal-tor thither, tonk'peh wuh vath ko-kan sarlah heh nem-tor ish-veh. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh da-tor tor uralau, she ash-tor pla', abi' na' kim-shah she vesh' wuh goh veh losrak, heh yi she kupi ri klee'fah. Tonk'peh lu she began ish-veh song, heh ish-veh pulau roland's kaluk, au sprang abru heh maf-tor: 'i fai-tor wuh spes, ik nam-tor wuh yeht bride, i dungi ma rai vath!' kanok-vei au had yen-tor, heh if had vanished s' ish-veh kashek, had suddenly sarlah ha-kel va'ashiv tor ish-veh khaf-spol. Yi wuh faithful maiden meskarau ish-veh wedding k' ish-veh sweetheart roland, heh tushat sarlah tor wuh shaht heh mak began. Snowdrop ish-veh vesh' wuh svitan t' karil, lu wuh sax'ksei wef t' izh vesh' tevan-tor pa', ik wuh ko-te'kru t' wuh shasol wehk thousand miles ska' hayal-tor working na' ish-veh krani. Wuh nentu t' wuh krani vesh' tor t' tok-ti nesh-kur ebony, heh u' she hayal-tor looking si' fi-tor wuh izh, she pricked ish-veh ozh, heh rehkuh eku-tor t' khaf tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh. Yi she gazed thoughtfully fi-tor wuh yon-kur eku-tor ik sprinkled wuh wan-kur izh, heh leralmin-tor, 'would ik t'nash-veh pi' ko-fu lau nam-tor u' wan-kur u' ik izh, u' yon-kur u' ik khaf, heh u' nesh-kur u' nash ebony windowframe!' heh ni wuh pi' ko-kan really did tor'ovau abru; ish-veh wadi vesh' u' wan-kur u' izh, ish-veh nak u' rosy u' wuh khaf, heh ish-veh isachya u' nesh-kur u' ebony; heh she vesh' puvutau snowdrop. Tonk'peh nash ko-te'kru tev-tor; heh wuh sa-te'kru ak telik wuh'ashiv ko-telsu, vi became ko-te'kru, heh vesh' maut vaksurik, tonk'peh ni vain ik she kupi ri lesh tor nah-tor ik sovek-veh kupi nam-tor handsomer do she vesh'. She had wuh pu'a looking-makh, tor if she nam-tor-tor tor hal-tor, heh yi she would gaze fi-tor herself svi' ish-veh, heh leralmin: 'var-tor me, makh, var-tor me yeht! T' ek' wuh t'sai svi' wuh solektra, vi nam-tor fairest, var-tor me, vi?' heh wuh makh had kwon-hau-ov kilko-tor: 'thou, ko-te'kru, tanaf wuh fairest svi' ek' wuh solektra.' tonk'peh snowdrop grew weht heh weht vaksurik; heh lu she vesh' stehkuh tevun hinek she vesh' u' ugelik u' wuh gad, heh fairer do wuh ko-te'kru herself. Yi wuh makh veh gad kilko-tor wuh ko-te'kru, lu she went tor glazhau svi' ish-veh u' tsuri: 'thou, ko-te'kru, tanaf rom, heh beauteous tor gla-tor, tonk'peh snowdrop nam-tor lovelier irak do thee!' lu she puzhu-tor nash she da-tor spoh k' reshan heh envy, heh puvutau tor veh t' ish-veh dvinsu, heh leralmin-tor, 'nem-tor snowdrop maf vi' wuh eik lapan, ik i lau worla gla-tor ish-veh sovek weht.' yi wuh dvinsu pufulag-tor ish-veh maf; tonk'peh ish-veh khaf-spol klimtau lu snowdrop eit'jae ish-veh tor spare ish-veh ha'kiv, heh au leralmin-tor, 'i dungi ri dash-tor du, thou takov kan.' ni au losrak ish-veh k' herself; heh hi au nahp ish-veh danik kesik ik wuh kwai beasts would bezhun-masu ish-veh svi' krus, au olau u' kuv wuh lo'uk rasath vesh' taken ska' ish-veh khaf-spol lu au had tor abru ish-veh kashek ri tor stau ish-veh tonk'peh tor trasha ish-veh tor ish-veh buk, k' wuh pavesh t' ein-veh finding heh saving ish-veh. Yi ri donku-tor snowdrop czar-tor bi' k'fai wuh lapan svi' lo'uk pthak; heh wuh kwai beasts roared pa' ish-veh, tonk'peh rim did ish-veh sovek klau. Svi' wuh khru sarlah ish-veh tor wuh cottage among wuh kunel, heh went svi' tor shom, na' ish-veh pi' ash'ya would lesh ish-veh rai further. Kanok-vei vesh' spruce heh pu svi' wuh cottage: fi' wuh pasu vesh' sak-tor wuh wan-kur sai, heh tra' vesh' stehkuh pi' math, stehkuh pi' loaves, heh stehkuh pi' bezhun-zaneshu k' wine svi' au; heh stehkuh lipau heh snauk laid svi' zek; heh k' wuh temok lam-tor stehkuh pi' sar-tak. U' she vesh' maut k'avon, she picked wuh pi' krus t' tik loaf heh drank wuh maut pi' wine s' tik makh; heh po' ik she nahp she would ti ne' heh shom. Ni she ar'kada ek' wuh pi' sar-tak; tonk'peh veh vesh' nuh' wu, heh wuh'ashiv vesh' nuh' pen, till na' kim-shah wuh seventh suited ish-veh: heh tra' she laid herself ne' heh went tor yuk. K' heh k' svi' sarlah wuh trensu t' wuh cottage. I' au vesh' stehkuh pi' dwarfs, ik ha-tor among wuh suk'kunel, heh hil-tor heh pstha na' pi-maat-tukh. Au lighted abru ish-veh stehkuh ha'gelek, heh gla-tor na' wuh'wak ik ek' vesh' ri gas'rak. Wuh wuh'rak leralmin-tor, 'vi has vesh' sitting fi' t'nash-veh stool?' wuh dahr, 'vi has vesh' eating ska' t'nash-veh math?' wuh wuh, 'vi has vesh' picking t'nash-veh kap?' wuh fourth, 'vi has vesh' meddling k' t'nash-veh floku?' wuh fifth, 'vi has vesh' handling t'nash-veh snauk?' wuh sixth, 'vi has vesh' tresahk-tor k' t'nash-veh lipau?' wuh seventh, 'vi has vesh' drinking t'nash-veh wine?' yi wuh wuh'rak glazhau pauk heh leralmin-tor, 'vi has vesh' lying fi' t'nash-veh sar-tak?' heh wuh shom sarlah sahran tor ish-veh, heh kanok-veh lit'dhae ik somebody had vesh' fi-tor ish-veh sar-tak. Tonk'peh wuh seventh gla-tor snowdrop, heh puvutau ek' ish-veh brethren tor sarlah heh gla-tor ish-veh; heh au lit'dhae k' wonder heh astonishment heh katau ish-veh ha'gelek tor glazhau na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'rom heavens! Ra wuh lovely kan she nam-tor!' heh au vesh' maut glad tor gla-tor ish-veh, heh nem-tor tun ri tor wake ish-veh; heh wuh seventh kobsu yuk-tor wuh wadan k' tik t' wuh vath dwarfs svi' da-tor, till wuh mu-yor vesh' hal-tor. Svi' wuh asal snowdrop var-tor au ek' ish-veh var; heh au pitied ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor kuv she would potau ek' vel svi' zek, heh fas-tor heh pu-tor heh knit heh padan na' au, she lau stay wilat she vesh', heh au would nem-tor rom tun t' ish-veh. Yi au went si' ek' gad wu tor ish-veh ar'kadan, seeking na' pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh svi' wuh suk'kunel: tonk'peh snowdrop vesh' losrak na' ha-kel; heh au vikau ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'wuh ko-te'kru dungi ak talal si' wilat du nam-tor, ni nem-tor tun heh kal-tor kling svi'.' tonk'peh wuh ko-te'kru, i' ik she nahp snowdrop vesh' tevik, pudva-tor ik she bolau nam-tor wuh handsomest t'sai svi' wuh solektra; heh she went tor ish-veh makh heh leralmin-tor: 'var-tor me, makh, var-tor me yeht! T' ek' wuh t'sai svi' wuh solektra, vi nam-tor fairest, var-tor me, vi?' heh wuh makh kilko-tor: 'thou, ko-te'kru, tanaf wuh fairest svi' ek' nash solektra: tonk'peh abru' wuh kunel, svi' wuh greenwood duvek, wilat wuh stehkuh dwarfs ish-veh kelek ma tor, tra' snowdrop nam-tor hiding ish-veh patam; heh she nam-tor lovelier irak, o ko-te'kru! Do thee.' yi wuh ko-te'kru vesh' maut mau koltha; na' she fai-tor ik wuh makh kwon-hau-ov stariben wuh yeht'es, heh vesh' sure ik wuh dvinsu had pusvik-tor ish-veh. Heh she kupi ri lesh tor nah-tor ik sovek-veh ha-tor vi vesh' weht vaksurik do she vesh'; ni she sai-vel-tor herself abru u' wuh hinek pedlar, heh went ish-veh yut abru' wuh kunel, tor wuh shi wilat wuh dwarfs dwelt. Yi she knocked na' wuh svep, heh maf-tor, 'tok-ti wares tor makau!' snowdrop glazhau si' na' wuh krani, heh leralmin-tor, 'rom gad, rom kosu! Ra ma du tor makau?' 'rom wares, tok-ti wares, ' leralmin-tor she; 'laces heh bobbins t' ek' colours.' 'i dungi kal-tor wuh hinek t'sai svi'; she seems tor nam-tor wuh maut rom wihfelau t' ak'shem, ' nahp snowdrop, u' she sahr-tor ne' heh unbolted wuh svep. 'kudau me!' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu, 'uf badly ish-veh stays nam-tor laced! Kal-tor me lace au abru k' veh t' t'nash-veh nice uzh laces.' snowdrop did ri sahr-tor t' sovek mischief; ni she lam-tor fa' wuh hinek kosu; tonk'peh she eku tor ar'kadan ni nimbly, heh seshau wuh lace ni wufik, ik snowdrop's esh vesh' pehkau, heh she tevan-tor ne' u' kuv she vesh' tevik. 'tra''s wuh shaht tor ek' thy vaksur, ' leralmin-tor wuh spiteful ko-te'kru, heh went maf ha-kel. Svi' wuh khru wuh stehkuh dwarfs sarlah ha-kel; heh i bolaya ri leralmin uf grieved au vesh' tor gla-tor ish-veh faithful snowdrop sakadau si' fi-tor wuh solektra, u' kuv she vesh' ved tevik. However, au abertau ish-veh abru, heh lu au afer-tor ra ailed ish-veh, au tresahk wuh lace; heh svi' wuh pi' wak she began tor esh-tor, heh maut ak sarlah tor ha'kiv va'ashiv. Yi au leralmin-tor, 'wuh hinek kosu vesh' wuh ko-te'kru herself; nem-tor tun wuh'ashiv wak, heh kal-tor kling svi' lu etek nam-tor maf.' lu wuh ko-te'kru prah ha-kel, she went zehik tor ish-veh makh, heh stariben tor ish-veh u' fa'; tonk'peh tor ish-veh lo'uk tushat ish-veh fam dvun leralmin-tor: 'thou, ko-te'kru, tanaf wuh fairest svi' ek' nash solektra: tonk'peh abru' wuh kunel, svi' wuh greenwood duvek, wilat wuh stehkuh dwarfs ish-veh kelek ma tor, tra' snowdrop nam-tor hiding ish-veh patam; heh she nam-tor lovelier irak, o ko-te'kru! Do thee.' yi wuh khaf sahr-tor samu svi' ish-veh khaf-spol k' spite heh malice, tor gla-tor ik snowdrop fam dvun ha-tor; heh she sai-vel-tor herself abru va'ashiv, tonk'peh svi' ved wuh'ashiv sai-vel s' wuh veh she sai-vel-tor fa', heh nem-tor k' ish-veh wuh poisoned dref. Lu she pulau wuh dwarfs' cottage, she knocked na' wuh svep, heh maf-tor, 'tok-ti wares tor makau!' tonk'peh snowdrop leralmin-tor, 'i dare ri kal-tor sovek-veh svi'.' yi wuh ko-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'goh glazhau na' t'nash-veh vaksurik dref!' heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh poisoned veh. Heh ish-veh glazhau ni takov, ik she nem-tor ish-veh abru heh shitau ish-veh vi' ish-veh isachya tor ar'kadan ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh moment ish-veh estuhl ish-veh patam, wuh gisam vesh' ni powerful ik she tevan-tor ne' senseless. 'tra' du lau ti, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-te'kru, heh went ish-veh yut. Tonk'peh k' rom kunli wuh dwarfs sarlah svi' maut lehkuh-mal ik khru; heh lu gla-tor au snowdrop lying fi' wuh solektra, au nahp ra had pavesh-tor, heh ak afer-tor wuh poisoned dref. Heh lu au nem-tor ish-veh maf she prah muhl, heh var-tor au ek' ik had be' dvun-tor; heh au vikau ish-veh wuh'wak weht ri tor tu'ash wuh svep tor sovek-veh. Meantime wuh ko-te'kru went ha-kel tor ish-veh makh, heh hutau k' reshan lu she telv-tor wuh maut ka kilko-srashiv u' fa'; heh she leralmin-tor, 'snowdrop dungau tev-tor, kuv ish-veh kodona me t'nash-veh ha'kiv.' ni she went k' herself vi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh prah pok wuh poisoned savas: wuh s'udish glazhau maut rosy heh tempting, tonk'peh whoever zahv-tor ish-veh vesh' sure tor tev-tor. Yi she sai-vel-tor herself abru u' wuh peasant's ko-telsu, heh travelled abru' wuh kunel tor wuh dwarfs' cottage, heh knocked na' wuh svep; tonk'peh snowdrop shitau ish-veh patam s' wuh krani heh leralmin-tor, 'i dare ri kal-tor sovek-veh svi', na' wuh dwarfs ma var-tor me ri.' 'tor u' du sanoi, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek kosu, 'tonk'peh na' sovek tav nem-tor nash takov savas; i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh du.' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor snowdrop, 'i dare ri nem-tor ish-veh.' 'du silly ko-kan!' kilko-tor wuh vath, 'ra nam-tor du kwes t'? Tor du nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor poisoned? Sarlah! Tor du yokul veh krus, heh i dungi yokul wuh vath.' i' wuh savas vesh' ni tor abru ish-veh vla vesh' rom, hi wuh vath vla vesh' poisoned. Yi snowdrop vesh' mau tempted tor zahvan, na' wuh savas glazhau ni maut nice; heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh hinek kosu yokul, she kupi bek-tor rai longer. Tonk'peh she had scarcely shitau wuh krus vi' ish-veh ru'lut, lu she tevan-tor ne' tevik fi-tor wuh solektra. 'nash wak nothing dungi korsau thee, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-te'kru; heh she went ha-kel tor ish-veh makh, heh na' kim-shah ish-veh leralmin-tor: 'thou, ko-te'kru, tanaf wuh fairest t' ek' wuh rom.' heh yi ish-veh wicked khaf-spol vesh' glad, heh u' kunli u' such wuh khaf-spol kupi nam-tor. Lu khru sarlah, heh wuh dwarfs had hal-tor ha-kel, au afer-tor snowdrop lying fi' wuh solektra: rai esh sarlah s' ish-veh bru-lar, heh au vesh' kwes ik she vesh' ved tevik. Au abertau ish-veh abru, heh dref-tor ish-veh isachya, heh pu-tor ish-veh limuk k' wine heh masu; tonk'peh ek' vesh' svi' vain, na' wuh pi' ko-kan seemed ved tevik. Ni au laid ish-veh ne' fi-tor wuh bier, heh ek' stehkuh glantau heh bewailed ish-veh rehkuh bosh gad; heh yi au nahp au would visolektau ish-veh: tonk'peh ish-veh nak vesh' fam dvun rosy; heh ish-veh limuk glazhau aishan u' ish-veh did du' she vesh' alive; ni au leralmin-tor, 'etek dungi worla visolektau ish-veh svi' wuh samu solektra.' heh au tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn t' makh, ni ik au lau fam dvun glazhau na' ish-veh, heh kitau fi-tor ish-veh svi' pi-maat-kur nuhm ra ish-veh ahm vesh', heh ik she vesh' wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu. Heh wuh tevikeh-natuhn vesh' eku among wuh kunel, heh veh t' wuh dwarfs kwon-hau-ov hayal-tor k' ish-veh heh glantau. Heh wuh kushel t' wuh sov sarlah nuh', heh bemoaned snowdrop; heh wuh'rak t' ek' sarlah wuh owl, heh yi wuh raven, heh na' kim-shah wuh dove, heh hayal-tor k' ish-veh vla. Heh thus snowdrop ti na' wuh wu, akarshif, heh fam dvun goh glazhau u' hi she vesh' asleep; na' she vesh' kauk i' u' wan-kur u' izh, heh u' yon-kur u' khaf, heh u' nesh-kur u' ebony. Na' kim-shah wuh prince sarlah heh puvutau na' wuh dwarfs' kelek; heh gla-tor ish-veh snowdrop, heh telv-tor ra vesh' written svi' pi-maat-kur nuhm. Yi au nufau wuh dwarfs donku, heh prayed heh besought au tor kal-tor ish-veh nem-tor ish-veh maf; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor, 'etek dungi ri krus k' ish-veh na' ek' wuh pi-maat-tukh svi' wuh panu.' na' kim-shah, however, au had pity fi' ish-veh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh tevikeh-natuhn; tonk'peh wuh moment au abertau ish-veh abru tor lesh ish-veh ha-kel k' ish-veh, wuh krus t' savas tevan-tor s' svi' ish-veh bru-lar, heh snowdrop awoke, heh leralmin-tor, 'wilat am i?' heh wuh prince leralmin-tor, 'thou tanaf ved safe k' me.' yi au var-tor ish-veh ek' ik had pavesh-tor, heh leralmin-tor, 'i ashaya du irak weh-rom do ek' wuh panu; ni sarlah k' me tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh's palace, heh du dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu.' heh snowdrop consented, heh went ha-kel k' wuh prince; heh kanok-vei vesh' prah pok k' lo'uk pomp heh splendour na' ish-veh wedding. Tor wuh gadzhak vesh' ya'akash, among wuh shom, snowdrop's hinek nemut wuh ko-te'kru; heh u' she vesh' sai-vel-tor herself svi' tok-ti don-ka sai-vel, she glazhau svi' wuh makh heh leralmin-tor: 'var-tor me, makh, var-tor me yeht! T' ek' wuh t'sai svi' wuh solektra, vi nam-tor fairest, var-tor me, vi?' heh wuh makh kilko-tor: 'thou, t'sai, tanaf loveliest la', i ween; tonk'peh lovelier irak nam-tor wuh uzh-tor ko-te'kru.' lu she puzhu-tor nash she palikau k' reshan; tonk'peh ish-veh envy heh curiosity vesh' ni lo'uk, ik she kupi ri gol'nev setting si' tor gla-tor wuh bride. Heh lu she prah tra', heh gla-tor ik ish-veh vesh' rai vath do snowdrop, vi, u' she nahp, had vesh' tevik wuh wu du', she khluhkau k' reshan, heh tevan-tor ne' heh tev-tor: tonk'peh snowdrop heh wuh prince ha-tor heh reigned kunling abru' ik solektra wehk, wehk tevun; heh sometimes au went abru vi' wuh suk'kunel, heh vlitau wuh yaret tor wuh pi' dwarfs, vi had vesh' ni ves tor snowdrop svi' ish-veh wak t' bolaya. Wuh faf-kur tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh ko-te'kru tor ik oekon had putan-tor rai kanu. Kanok asal she went vi' wuh bah-ker heh prayed tor oekon svi' sha-ka-ri tor bestow fi' ish-veh wuh sa-fu il wuh ko-fu. Yi wuh ha'su s' sha-ka-ri sarlah tor ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'nam-tor na' shom, du dungau ma wuh sa-fu k' wuh tepul t' wishing, ni ik whatsoever svi' wuh panu au istau na', ik dungau au ma.' yi she went tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh var-tor ish-veh wuh joyful tidings, heh lu wuh wak vesh' sarlah she mazhiv-kur-tor keshtan tor wuh sa-fu, heh wuh sa-te'kru vesh' boshau k' gladness. Kanok asal she went k' wuh kan tor wuh bah-ker wilat wuh kwai beasts vesh' potau, heh pu-tor herself tra' svi' wuh pa'shik pilash. Ish-veh pavesh-tor wuh'wak lu wuh kan vesh' wuh pi' older, ik ish-veh vesh' lying svi' ish-veh kar heh she tevan-tor asleep. Yi sarlah wuh hinek fas-tor, vi fai-tor ik wuh kan had wuh tepul t' wishing, heh vazgau ish-veh maf, heh au nem-tor wuh hen, heh tresahk ish-veh svi' krus, heh eku-tor ein t' its khaf fi' wuh ko-te'kru's apron heh fi' ish-veh sai-vel. Yi au lesh wuh kan maf tor wuh tsat shi, wilat wuh nurse vesh' obliged tor suckle ish-veh, heh au sahr-tor tor wuh sa-te'kru heh accused wuh ko-te'kru t' having kal-tor ish-veh kan tor nam-tor taken s' ish-veh k' wuh kwai beasts. Lu wuh sa-te'kru gla-tor wuh khaf fi' ish-veh apron, au pudva-tor nash, tevan-tor vi' such wuh shaukaush ik au ordered wuh pid kispek tor nam-tor torvau, svi' if neither yel il aikum kupi nam-tor gla-tor heh had ish-veh ko-telsu shitau vi' ish-veh, heh walled abru. La' she vesh' tor stay na' stehkuh tevun rik' kahm il mon, heh tev-tor t' avon. Tonk'peh oekon satau dahkuh ha'su s' sha-ka-ri svi' wuh shid t' wan-kur doves, if flew tor ish-veh dah'wak wuh gad, heh lesh ish-veh yem-tukh abi' wuh stehkuh tevun vesh' abru'. Wuh fas-tor, however, nahp tor himself: 'kuv wuh kan has wuh tepul t' wishing, heh i am la', au lau maut easily prah me vi' trouble.' ni au losrak wuh palace heh went tor wuh sa-kan, vi vesh' already suk' hiyet tor stariben, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'istaya na' wuh vaksurik palace na' yourself k' wuh bah-ker, heh ek' else ik pertains tor ish-veh.' scarcely vesh' wuh zhit si' t' wuh sa-kan's ru'lut, lu kanok-vei vesh' tra' ik au had istau na'. Po' wuh du' wuh fas-tor leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'ish-veh nam-tor ri muhl na' du tor nam-tor ni sa'awek, istaya na' wuh takov ko-kan u' wuh besu.' yi wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu istau na' veh, heh she iyi lam-tor fa' ish-veh, heh vesh' weht vaksurik do sovek krassu kupi ma kras-tor ish-veh. Wuh dahkuh mavau teretuhr, heh ashau tik vath k' ek' ish-veh khaf-spol, heh wuh hinek fas-tor went si' hunting spo' wuh nobleman. Wuh nahp paresh-tor tor ish-veh, however, ik wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu lau ein gad istaya tor nam-tor k' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh thus katau ish-veh vi' lo'uk peril. Ni au went si' heh nem-tor wuh maiden aside, heh leralmin-tor: 'tonight lu wuh sa-kan nam-tor asleep, hal-tor tor ish-veh sar-tak heh taul nash lipau vi' ish-veh khaf-spol, heh katau me ish-veh khaf-spol heh lahv, heh kuv du tor ri tor ish-veh, du dungau pak-tor ish-veh ha'kiv.' thereupon au went maf, heh lu au fun-tor thurai gad she had ri ovsoh ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 'po dang i foshuhl wuh khaf t' wuh innocent sa-kan vi has worla klau sovek-veh?' wuh fas-tor wuh'wak weht leralmin-tor: 'kuv du ri tor tor ish-veh, ish-veh dungau kodona du ish-veh sha' ha'kiv.' lu au had hal-tor maf, she had wuh pi' hind katau tor ish-veh, heh ordered ish-veh tor nam-tor pustau, heh nem-tor ish-veh khaf-spol heh lahv, heh laid au fi' wuh math, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh hinek sasu coming, she leralmin-tor tor wuh sa-kan: 'ti ne' svi' ish-veh sar-tak, heh bes-tor wuh sai-vel abru' du.' yi wuh wicked wretch sarlah svi' heh leralmin-tor: 'wilat nam-tor wuh sa-kan's khaf-spol heh lahv?' wuh ko-kan pulau wuh math tor ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu threw ska' wuh quilt, heh leralmin-tor: 'du hinek sinner, po did du aitlun tor stau me? I' dungi i pronounce thy zhit-bal. Du dungau shetau wuh nesh-kur wil'tei heh ma wuh pi-maat-tukh hmoi'neks pauk ish-veh talu, heh dungau yokul yontau kastik-kov, till wuh yai thorau forth s' ish-veh drahk.' heh lu au had spoken aifa zhit, wuh hinek sasu vesh' rubai vi' wuh wil'tei dog, heh had wuh pi-maat-tukh hmoi'neks pauk ish-veh talu, heh wuh fas-tor vesh' ordered tor katau abru ein ha-tor kastik-kov, heh aifa au ate, abi' wuh yai shau forth s' ish-veh drahk. Wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu hafau tra' wuh pen du' longer, heh au nahp t' ish-veh ko-mekh, heh wondered kuv she vesh' fam dvun alive. Na' wu-vath au leralmin-tor tor wuh maiden: 'i dungi hal-tor ha-kel tor t'nash-veh sha' shasol; kuv du dungi hal-tor k' me, i dungi tanilau na' du.' 'ah, ' she kilko-tor, 'wuh yut nam-tor ni wu, heh ra dungau i tor svi' wuh flekh solektra wilat i am ri-fainu?' u' she did ri seem ved willing, heh u' au kupi ri nam-tor parted s' tik vath, au istau ik she lau nam-tor rubai vi' wuh vaksurik faf-kur, heh nem-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh. Yi au went maf tor ish-veh sha' shasol, heh wuh wil'tei had tor sahr-tor po' ish-veh. Au went tor wuh kispek svi' if ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' confined, heh u' ish-veh vesh' ni pid, au istau na' wuh pu'uth if would pulau abru tor wuh maut fik. Yi au mounted abru heh glazhau svi'udish, heh maf-tor: 'k'diwa ko-mekh, t'sai ko-te'kru, nam-tor du fam dvun alive, il nam-tor du tevik?' she kilko-tor: 'i ma aishan yokul, heh am fam dvun satisfied, ' na' she nahp wuh ha'su vesh' tra'. Leralmin-tor au: 'i am ish-veh tal-kam sa-fu, ik wuh kwai beasts vesh' leralmin-tor ki' torn s' ish-veh kar; tonk'peh i am alive fam dvun, heh dungi ak eku du elik.' yi au tev-tor va'ashiv, heh went tor ish-veh sa-mekh, heh aisha himself tor nam-tor tor'pra u' wuh flekh huntsman, heh ya'akash kuv au kupi nufai ish-veh dvin. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor ha, kuv au vesh' skilful heh kupi prah zhagra na' ish-veh, au dang sarlah tor ish-veh, tonk'peh ik deer had worla taken abru ish-veh ha-shal svi' sovek krus t' wuh kahkrus il shasol. Yi wuh huntsman ugau tor procure u' mau zhagra na' ish-veh u' au kupi possibly nam-tor-tor na' wuh royal pasu. Ni au summoned ek' wuh huntsmen teretuhr, heh bade au hal-tor si' vi' wuh laptra k' ish-veh. Heh au went k' au heh tor au shid wuh lo'uk da-kuv, tu'ash na' veh shaht wilat au stationed himself, heh began tor istaya. Dah-teh deer heh weht sarlah sahran svi'udish wuh da-kuv na' wuh'wak, heh wuh huntsmen pohshaya au. Yi au vesh' ek' shitau fi' sheh-leh shasol hal, heh driven ha-kel tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh na' wuh'wak au vesh' kup tor lan-tol ish-veh pasu k' zhagra, po' having had rim na' ek' na' tevun. I' wuh sa-te'kru olau lo'uk mak na' nash, heh khartau ik ish-veh entire household dang yokul k' ish-veh thurai gad, heh tor wuh lo'uk gadzhak. Lu au vesh' ek' assembled teretuhr, au leralmin-tor tor wuh huntsman: 'u' du nam-tor ni clever, du dungau hayal-tor k' me.' au kilko-tor: 's'haile sa-te'kru, ish-veh majesty bolau tobeg me, i am wuh ri donku-tor huntsman.' tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru insisted fi' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 'du dungau hayal-tor k' me, ' abi' au did ish-veh. Whilst au vesh' sitting tra', au nahp t' ish-veh dearest ko-mekh, heh istau ish-veh t' wuh sa-te'kru's principal dvinsu would palikau tor stariben t' ish-veh, heh would ya'akash uf ish-veh vesh' faring k' wuh ko-te'kru svi' wuh kispek, heh kuv she vesh' alive fam dvun, il had perished. Hardly had au shidau wuh istaya do wuh marshal began, heh leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh majesty, etek ha-tor joyously la', tonk'peh uf nam-tor wuh ko-te'kru living svi' wuh kispek? Nam-tor she fam dvun alive, il has she tev-tor?' tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru kilko-tor: 'she kal-tor t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-fu nam-tor torn tor krus k' kwai beasts; i dungi ri ma ish-veh ahmau.' yi wuh huntsman arose heh leralmin-tor: 'gracious s'haile sa-mekh she nam-tor alive fam dvun, heh i am ish-veh sa-fu, heh i vesh' ri lesh maf k' kwai beasts, tonk'peh k' ik wretch wuh hinek fas-tor, vi tore me s' ish-veh kar lu she vesh' asleep, heh sprinkled ish-veh apron k' wuh khaf t' wuh kahm.' thereupon au nem-tor wuh dog k' wuh pi-maat-kur hmoi'neks, heh leralmin-tor: 'ik nam-tor wuh wretch!' heh aisha ha-tor kastik-kov tor nam-tor katau, heh aifa wuh dog vesh' compelled tor katau fa' wuh glan t' ek', abi' yai thorau forth s' its drahk. Fi' nash wuh huntsman ya'akash wuh sa-te'kru kuv au would spo' tor gla-tor wuh dog svi' ish-veh yeht shid, heh istau ish-veh pla' vi' wuh shid t' wuh fas-tor, svi' if au lam-tor iyi, k' ish-veh wan-kur apron, heh ish-veh lipau k' ish-veh vla. Lu wuh sa-te'kru gla-tor ish-veh au tevan-tor vi' wuh shaukaush, heh ordered ish-veh tor nam-tor vishizhau vi' wuh deepest dungeon. Yi wuh huntsman stariben further heh leralmin-tor: 'sa-mekh, dungi gla-tor du wuh maiden vi katau me abru ni tenderly heh vi vesh' afterwards tor riyeht-staya me, tonk'peh did ri tor ish-veh, hi ish-veh sha' ha'kiv nerau fi' ish-veh?' wuh sa-te'kru kilko-tor: 'ha, i would spo' tor gla-tor ish-veh.' wuh sa-fu leralmin-tor: 'danik gracious sa-mekh, i dungi gluvaya ish-veh tor du svi' wuh shid t' wuh vaksurik svai, ' heh au kwit ish-veh el'ru vi' ish-veh abru'lik heh katau forth wuh faf-kur, heh shitau ish-veh fi' wuh royal pasu, heh ish-veh vesh' ni vaksurik ik wuh sa-te'kru had worla gla-tor veh tor kaik ish-veh. Yi wuh sa-fu leralmin-tor: 'i' dungi i gluvaya ish-veh tor du svi' ish-veh sha' shid, ' heh istau ik she lau shetau wuh maiden, heh she lam-tor tra' looking ni vaksurik ik rai krassu kupi ma tor ish-veh glazhau weht ni. Heh wuh sa-te'kru satau dahkuh waiting-maids heh dahkuh attendants vi' wuh kispek, tor zaprah wuh ko-te'kru heh katau ish-veh tor wuh royal pasu. Tonk'peh lu she vesh' pufulag-tor svi' she ate nothing, heh leralmin-tor: 'wuh gracious heh merciful oekon vi has nenikau me svi' wuh kispek, dungi ak eku me elik.' she ha-tor rehkuh gad weht, heh yi tev-tor kunling, heh lu she vesh' visolektau, wuh dahkuh wan-kur doves if had katau ish-veh yem-tukh tor wuh kispek, heh vesh' ha'su t' sha-ka-ri, zahal-tor ish-veh ak'shem heh hayal-tor themselves fi' ish-veh shi'vukhut. Wuh aged sa-te'kru ordered wuh fas-tor tor nam-tor torn svi' kehkuh krus, tonk'peh tushat consumed wuh sa-te'kru's sha' khaf-spol, heh au ak tev-tor. Ish-veh sa-fu telik wuh vaksurik maiden ik au had katau k' ish-veh u' wuh svai svi' ish-veh abru'lik, heh whether au nam-tor fam dvun alive il ri, nam-tor fainu tor oekon. Clever elsie tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh sasu vi had wuh ko-fu vi vesh' puvutau clever elsie. Heh lu she had grown abru ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor: 'etek dungi prah ish-veh telik.' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-mekh, 'kuv goh ein-veh would sarlah vi would ma ish-veh.' na' wu-vath wuh sasu sarlah kwi' heh wooed ish-veh, vi vesh' puvutau hans; tonk'peh au stipulated ik clever elsie dang nam-tor really klon. 'oh, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'she has plenty t' rom kash-ral'; heh wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor: 'oh, she mokuhlek gla-tor wuh salan coming abru wuh yut, heh zhu-tor wuh hash-tor coughing.' 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor hans, 'kuv she nam-tor ri really klon, i skil-tor't ma ish-veh.' lu au vesh' sitting na' aru-yem heh had yokul, wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor: 'elsie, hal-tor vi' wuh cellar heh zaprah ein naliveh.' yi clever elsie nem-tor wuh pitcher s' wuh temok, went vi' wuh cellar, heh tapped wuh lid brax u' she went, ni ik wuh wak lau ri saudau wu. Lu she vesh' ne' she zaprah herself wuh ku-san, heh eku ish-veh fa' wuh subok ni ik she had rai bolaya tor stoop, heh did ri dash-tor ish-veh pla' il tor herself sovek ri-gishu dash. Yi she shitau wuh mokuhlek fa' ish-veh, heh da-tor wuh sayumak, heh du' wuh naliveh vesh' sahran she would ri kal-tor ish-veh bezhun nam-tor idle, tonk'peh glazhau abru na' wuh temok, heh po' mau peering la' heh tra', gla-tor wuh pick-la'ash exactly abru' ish-veh, if wuh masons had accidentally losrak tra'. Yi clever elsie began tor tusa heh leralmin-tor: 'kuv i prah hans, heh etek ma wuh kan, heh au tor'ovau suk', heh etek satau ish-veh vi' wuh cellar la' tor bes-tor naliveh, yi wuh pick-la'ash dungi tevan fi' ish-veh patam heh stau ish-veh.' yi she hayal-tor heh wept heh shei k' ek' wuh karik'es t' ish-veh ak'shem, abru' wuh misfortune if ti fa' ish-veh. Eifa upstairs bek-tor na' wuh mon, tonk'peh clever elsie fam dvun did ri sarlah. Yi wuh kosu leralmin-tor tor wuh dvinsu: 'aishan hal-tor ne' vi' wuh cellar heh gla-tor wilat elsie nam-tor.' wuh maid went heh afer-tor ish-veh sitting svi' khom t' wuh subok, screaming loudly. 'elsie po tor du tusa?' ya'akash wuh maid. 'ah, ' she kilko-tor, 'ma i ri utvau tor tusa? Kuv i prah hans, heh etek ma wuh kan, heh au tor'ovau suk', heh has tor bes-tor naliveh la', wuh pick-la'ash dungi sos'eh tevan fi' ish-veh patam, heh stau ish-veh.' yi leralmin-tor wuh maid: 'ra wuh clever elsie etek ma!' heh hayal-tor ne' be' ish-veh heh began loudly tor tusa abru' wuh misfortune. Po' wuh du', u' wuh maid did ri sarlah pla', heh eifa upstairs vesh' thirsty na' wuh naliveh, wuh sasu leralmin-tor tor wuh sa-kan: 'aishan hal-tor ne' vi' wuh cellar heh gla-tor wilat elsie heh wuh ko-kan nam-tor.' wuh sa-kan went ne', heh tra' hayal-tor clever elsie heh wuh ko-kan fi' weeping teretuhr. Yi au ya'akash: 'po nam-tor du weeping?' 'ah, ' leralmin-tor elsie, 'ma i ri utvau tor tusa? Kuv i prah hans, heh etek ma wuh kan, heh au tor'ovau suk', heh has tor bes-tor naliveh la', wuh pick-la'ash dungi tevan fi' ish-veh patam heh stau ish-veh.' yi leralmin-tor wuh sa-kan: 'ra wuh clever elsie etek ma!' heh hayal-tor ne' k' ish-veh, heh likewise began tor vlut loudly. Upstairs au bek-tor na' wuh sa-kan, tonk'peh u' au fam dvun did ri fun, wuh sasu leralmin-tor tor wuh kosu: 'aishan hal-tor ne' vi' wuh cellar heh gla-tor wilat elsie nam-tor!' wuh kosu went ne', heh afer-tor ek' rehkuh svi' wuh midst t' ish-veh lamentations, heh inquired ra vesh' wuh aishan; yi elsie var-tor ish-veh isha ik ish-veh fa-wak kan vesh' tor nam-tor pustau k' wuh pick-la'ash, lu ish-veh grew suk' heh had tor bes-tor naliveh, heh wuh pick-la'ash tevan-tor ne'. Yi leralmin-tor wuh ko-mekh likewise: 'ra wuh clever elsie etek ma!' heh hayal-tor ne' heh wept k' au. Wuh sasu upstairs bek-tor wuh pen wak, tonk'peh u' ish-veh ko-telsu did ri sarlah pla' heh ish-veh mag grew ek'wak greater, au leralmin-tor: 'i bolau hal-tor vi' wuh cellar myself heh gla-tor wilat elsie nam-tor.' tonk'peh lu au prah vi' wuh cellar, heh au vesh' ek' sitting teretuhr maf-tor, heh au puzhu-tor wuh utvau, heh ik elsie's kan vesh' wuh aishan, heh wuh elsie lau sos'eh katau veh vi' wuh panu ein gad, heh ik au lau nam-tor pustau k' wuh pick-la'ash, kuv au dang pavesh-tor tor nam-tor sitting ne'rak ish-veh, bestan naliveh aishan na' wuh maut wak lu ish-veh tevan-tor ne', au maf-tor: 'oh, ra wuh clever elsie!' heh hayal-tor ne', heh likewise wept k' au. Wuh bridegroom stayed upstairs sa'awek na' wuh akarshif; yi u' kling would sarlah pla' au nahp: 'au bolau nam-tor waiting na' me ne': i nuh' bolau hal-tor tra' heh gla-tor ra au nam-tor pa'.' lu au prah ne', wuh kaukuh t' au vesh' sitting screaming heh lamenting ved piteously, tik si'-doing wuh vath. 'ra misfortune has pavesh-tor yi?' ya'akash au. 'ah, tal-kam hans, ' leralmin-tor elsie, 'kuv etek marry tik vath heh ma wuh kan, heh au nam-tor suk', heh etek sos'eh satau ish-veh la' tor bes-tor vel tor mon, yi wuh pick-la'ash if has vesh' losrak abru tra' lau dash ish-veh shi'nahp si' kuv ish-veh vesh' tor tevan ne', ni ma etek ri utvau tor tusa?' 'sarlah, ' leralmin-tor hans, 'weht understanding do ik nam-tor ri bolau na' t'nash-veh household, u' du nam-tor such wuh clever elsie, i dungi ma du, ' heh seized ish-veh el'ru, nem-tor ish-veh upstairs k' ish-veh, heh telik ish-veh. Po' hans had had ish-veh ein wak, au leralmin-tor: 'ko-telsu, i am going si' tor ar'kadan heh pinkau ein donku na' etek; hal-tor vi' wuh vunai heh tresahk wuh corn ik etek lau ma ein kap.' 'ha, tal-kam hans, i dungi tor ik.' po' hans had hal-tor maf, she pufas-tor herself ein rom broth heh nem-tor ish-veh vi' wuh vunai k' ish-veh. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh vunai she leralmin-tor tor herself: 'ra dungau i tor; dungau i tresahk wuh'rak, il dungau i yokul wuh'rak? Oh, i dungi yokul wuh'rak.' yi she drank ish-veh cup t' broth heh lu she vesh' fully satisfied, she wuh'wak weht leralmin-tor: 'ra dungau i tor? Dungau i tresahk wuh'rak, il dungau i yuk wuh'rak? I dungi yuk wuh'rak.' yi she ti ne' among wuh corn heh tevan-tor asleep. Hans had vesh' na' ha-kel na' wuh akarshif, tonk'peh elsie did ri sarlah; yi leralmin-tor au: 'ra wuh clever elsie i ma; she nam-tor ni industrious ik she tor ri kauk sarlah ha-kel tor yokul.' tonk'peh lu khru sarlah heh she fam dvun stayed maf, hans went si' tor gla-tor ra she had tresahk, tonk'peh nothing vesh' tresahk, heh she vesh' lying among wuh corn asleep. Yi hans hastened ha-kel heh katau wuh fowler's vis k' pi' kus-vakh heh geldau ish-veh pauk pa' ish-veh, heh she fam dvun went fi' sleeping. Yi au sahr-tor ha-kel, ikap-tor wuh kelek-svep, heh hayal-tor ne' svi' ish-veh ku-san heh ar'kada. Na' wu-vath, lu ish-veh vesh' ved gu'gelik, clever elsie awoke heh lu she prah abru tra' vesh' wuh jingling ek' pauk pa' ish-veh, heh wuh kus-vakh rang na' tik ash if she nem-tor. Yi she vesh' alarmed, heh became uncertain whether she really vesh' clever elsie il ri, heh leralmin-tor: 'nam-tor ish-veh i, il nam-tor ish-veh ri i?' tonk'peh she fai-tor ri ra kilko-srashiv tor tor tor nash, heh lam-tor na' wuh wak svi' vet; na' wu-vath she nahp: 'i dungi hal-tor ha-kel heh ya'akash kuv ish-veh nam-tor i, il kuv ish-veh nam-tor ri i, au dungi nam-tor sure tor fai-tor.' she sahr-tor tor wuh svep t' ish-veh sha' kelek, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ikap-tor; yi she knocked na' wuh krani heh maf-tor: 'hans, nam-tor elsie k'svi?' 'ha, ' kilko-tor hans, 'she nam-tor k'svi.' hereupon she vesh' terrified, heh leralmin-tor: 'ah, heavens! Yi ish-veh nam-tor ri i, ' heh went tor wuh'ashiv svep; tonk'peh lu wuh sutra puzhu-tor wuh jingling t' wuh kus-vakh au would ri tu'ash ish-veh, heh she kupi prah svi' nowhere. Yi she sahr-tor s' wuh pi'kahr, heh kling has gla-tor ish-veh opi'. Wuh miser svi' wuh bush wuh uroshitausu had wuh faithful heh diligent dvinsu, vi had ar'kada lerash na' ish-veh rehkuh tevun, rik' having vesh' vlitau sovek wages. Na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh vi' wuh sasu's patam ik au would ri hal-tor fi' thus rik' vlitau sovek longer; ni au went tor ish-veh trensu, heh leralmin-tor, 'i ma ar'kada lerash na' du wuh wu wak, i dungi sahrafel tor du tor mazhiv-kur-tor me ra i nazh ki' na' t'nash-veh trouble.' wuh uroshitausu vesh' wuh maf miser, heh fai-tor ik ish-veh sasu vesh' maut velik-hearted; ni au nem-tor si' threepence, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh na' kanok tevun's dvin wuh qsu'lit. Wuh ri donku-tor katravahsu nahp ish-veh vesh' wuh lo'uk deal t' donku tor ma, heh leralmin-tor tor himself, 'po dang i ar'kadan lerash, heh ha-tor la' fi' rasahkos panavau sovek longer? I mokuhlek i' haolvaya vi' wuh eik panu, heh tor myself merry.' k' ik au shitau ish-veh donku vi' ish-veh sa'haf, heh eku si', roaming abru' kunel heh ku-li. U' au jogged bi' abru' wuh vunai, uralaun heh taman, wuh pi' kobsu ragel-tor ish-veh, heh ya'akash ish-veh ra tor ish-veh ni merry. 'po, ra dang tor me ne'-hearted?' leralmin-tor au; 'i am ralash svi' muhl'es heh don-ka svi' sa'haf, ra dang i palutunau? I ma korsau abru t'nash-veh rehkuh tevun' pinkaunu heh ma ish-veh ek' safe svi' t'nash-veh abru'lik.' 'uf mau lau ish-veh sarlah tor?' leralmin-tor wuh pi' sasu. 'bosh threepence, ' kilko-tor wuh countryman. 'i istaya du would mazhiv-kur-tor au tor me, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath; 'i am maut ri donku-tor.' yi wuh sasu pitied ish-veh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ek' au had; heh wuh pi' kobsu leralmin-tor svi' fun, 'u' du ma such wuh ves trau khaf-spol, i dungi vahl du rehkuh istau--veh na' kanok qsu'lit; ni dvel-tor whatever du spo'.' yi wuh countryman rejoiced na' ish-veh rom kunli, heh leralmin-tor, 'i spo' wehk vel weh-rom do donku: wuh'rak, i dungi ma wuh kes-wun ik dungi katau ne' kanok-vei i pohshau na'; secondly, wuh fiddle ik dungi eku kanok-veh taman ik zhu-tor me mavau fi-tor ish-veh; heh thirdly, i dang spo' ik kanok-veh dang vahl ra i ya'akash.' wuh kobsu leralmin-tor au dang ma ish-veh rehkuh istau; ni au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh kes-wun heh fiddle, heh went ish-veh yut. Etwel trau t'hy'la halovau fi' ish-veh yut nuh'; heh kuv au vesh' merry fa', au vesh' i' lehkuh wak weht ni. Au had ri hal-tor irak fa' au ragel-tor wuh hinek miser: beyik au lam-tor wuh lap, heh fi' wuh topmost pi'gel hayal-tor wuh thrush uralaun maf danik joyfully. 'oh, ra wuh takov kushel!' leralmin-tor wuh miser; 'i would mazhiv-kur-tor wuh lo'uk deal t' donku ki' such wuh veh.' 'kuv ik's ek', ' leralmin-tor wuh countryman, 'i dungi ak katau ish-veh ne'.' yi au nem-tor abru ish-veh kes-wun, heh ne' tevan-tor wuh thrush vi' wuh bushes na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh lap. Wuh miser crept vi' wuh bush tor talal ish-veh; tonk'peh directly au had prah vi' wuh svitan, ish-veh besu nem-tor abru ish-veh fiddle heh mavau maf, heh wuh miser began tor tam heh sikar pa', capering higher heh higher svi' wuh sov. Wuh thorns ak began tor bezhun-masu ish-veh sai-vel till au ek' geldau svi' a'cit pa' ish-veh, heh au himself vesh' ek' scratched heh wounded, ni ik wuh khaf sahr-tor ne'. 'oh, na' sha-ka-ri's sake!' maf-tor wuh miser, 'trensu! Trensu! Pray kal-tor wuh fiddle sa'awek. Ra ma i ovsoh tor nazh nash?' 'thou hast hohl-tor wehk wuh ri donku-tor soul ikap-tor hiyet, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath; 'thou tanaf goh latva thy reward': ni au mavau abru wuh'ashiv tvelkau. Yi wuh miser began tor eit'jae heh ugaya, heh nufau donku na' ish-veh liberty; tonk'peh au did ri sarlah abru tor wuh ralash-tanafsu's price na' ein wak, heh au tam-tor ish-veh bi' brisker heh brisker, heh wuh miser nufai higher heh higher, till na' kim-shah au nufau wuh pauk hundred t' florins ik au had svi' ish-veh sa'haf, heh had aishan nazh-tor k' cheating ein ri donku-tor katravahsu. Lu wuh countryman gla-tor ni mau donku, au leralmin-tor, 'i dungi sep-wafikh tor ish-veh mnah.' ni au nem-tor wuh sa'haf, shitau abru ish-veh fiddle, heh travelled fi' maut sanoi k' ish-veh bargain. Meanwhile wuh miser crept s' wuh bush ulef-sai-fam heh svi' wuh piteous plight, heh began tor ponder uf au dang nem-tor ish-veh revenge, heh dvin-tor ish-veh tab-ma besu ein trick. Na' kim-shah au went tor wuh judge, heh complained ik wuh rascal had robbed ish-veh t' ish-veh donku, heh beaten ish-veh vi' wuh bargain; heh ik wuh katravahsu vi did ish-veh lesh wuh kes-wun na' ish-veh pla' heh wuh fiddle geldau pauk ish-veh talu. Yi wuh judge satau si' ish-veh officers tor katau abru wuh accused wherever au dang talal ish-veh; heh au vesh' ak kum-tor heh katau abru tor nam-tor ar'kada. Wuh miser began tor var-tor ish-veh var, heh leralmin-tor au had vesh' robbed t' ish-veh donku. 'rai, du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh me na' mavaun wuh tvelkau tor du.' leralmin-tor wuh countryman; tonk'peh wuh judge var-tor ish-veh ik vesh' ri kesik, heh tresahk wuh tukh pen k' ordering ish-veh ska' tor wuh geld-stau-nentu. Ni maf au vesh' taken; tonk'peh u' au lam-tor fi' wuh ash-tor au leralmin-tor, 't'nash-veh s'haile judge, vahl me veh kim-shah ya'akash.' 'sovek-vel tonk'peh thy ha'kiv, ' kilko-tor wuh vath. 'rai, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i ri tor ya'akash t'nash-veh ha'kiv; goh tor kal-tor me mavau fi-tor t'nash-veh fiddle na' wuh kim-shah wak.' wuh miser lit'dhae, 'oh, rai! Rai! Na' sha-ka-ri's sake ri tor shroi tor ish-veh! Ri tor shroi tor ish-veh!' tonk'peh wuh judge leralmin-tor, 'ish-veh nam-tor goh nash wuh'wak, au dungi ak ma ovsoh.' wuh kla-min vesh', au kupi ri klee'fah wuh ya'akash, fi' khrosahp t' wuh kobsu's wuh mazhiv-kur. Yi wuh miser leralmin-tor, 'bind me sahris, bind me sahris, na' pity's sake.' tonk'peh wuh countryman seized ish-veh fiddle, heh kwul-tor abru wuh tvelkau, heh na' wuh wuh'rak pitoh judge, clerks, heh jailer vesh' svi' dvunel; ek' began capering, heh kling kupi meskaraya wuh miser. Na' wuh dahr pitoh wuh hangman kal-tor ish-veh prisoner hal-tor, heh tam-tor isha, heh k' wuh wak au had mavau wuh wuh'rak mofek t' wuh tvelkau, ek' vesh' taman teretuhr--judge, kelek, heh miser, heh ek' wuh sutra vi had zahal-tor tor glazhau fi'. Palikauk wuh vel vesh' merry heh vaksurik hiyet; tonk'peh lu ish-veh had hal-tor fi' wuh du', heh tra' seemed tor nam-tor rai shaht t' mavaun il taman, au began tor lit'dhae, heh eit'jae ish-veh tor trasha ska'; tonk'peh au pehkau ri wuh whit wuh weht na' ish-veh entreaties, till wuh judge ri goh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh ha'kiv, tonk'peh ugau tor fun ish-veh wuh hundred florins. Yi au puvutau tor wuh miser, heh leralmin-tor, 'var-tor etek i', du vagabond, wilat du prah ik pi-maat-tukh, il i dungau mavau fi' na' ish-veh amusement goh, ' 'i vazgau ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh miser svi' wuh la'es t' ek' wuh sutra; 'i nafai-tor ik i vazgau ish-veh, heh ik du pinkau ish-veh fairly.' yi wuh countryman pehkau ish-veh fiddle, heh losrak wuh miser tor nem-tor ish-veh shi na' wuh geld-stau-nentu. Ashputtel wuh ko-telsu t' wuh don-ka sasu tevan-tor has-bosh; heh lu she olau ik ish-veh shaht drew nigh, she puvutau ish-veh goh ko-fu tor ish-veh sar-tak-vla, heh leralmin-tor, 'kwon-hau-ov nam-tor wuh rom ko-kan, heh i dungi glazhau ne' s' sha-ka-ri heh paluntunau du.' ak afterwards she ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun heh tev-tor, heh vesh' visolektau svi' wuh bah-ker; heh wuh pi' ko-kan went kanok gad tor ish-veh shi'vukhut heh wept, heh vesh' kwon-hau-ov rom heh ves tor ek' pa' ish-veh. Heh wuh izh tevan-tor heh sak-tor wuh vaksurik wan-kur covering abru' wuh shi'vukhut; tonk'peh k' wuh wak wuh sikar sarlah, heh wuh yel had klimtau ish-veh maf va'ashiv, ish-veh sa-mekh had telik wuh'ashiv ko-telsu. Nash uzh ko-telsu had dahkuh daughters t' ish-veh sha', ik she katau ha-kel k' ish-veh; au vesh' rom svi' limuk tonk'peh flalik na' khaf-spol, heh ish-veh vesh' i' wuh sorry wak na' wuh ri donku-tor pi' ko-kan. 'ra tor wuh rom-na'-nothing aitlun svi' wuh parlour?' leralmin-tor au; 'au vi would yokul kap dang wuh'rak pinkau ish-veh; maf k' wuh af'tum-maid!' yi au nem-tor maf ish-veh tok-ti sai-vel, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh hinek zhai-kur pelal tor shitau fi', heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh, heh da-tor ish-veh vi' wuh af'tum. Tra' she vesh' punekwitau tor tor lerash ar'kadan; tor shen lehkuh-mal fa' gad-ha'khlup, tor katau wuh masu, tor tor wuh yon, tor fas-tor heh tor pu-tor. Isha ik, wuh ko-kai plagued ish-veh svi' ek' wihfelau t' yut, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh. Svi' wuh khru lu she vesh' zungor, she had rai sar-tak tor ti ne' fi', tonk'peh vesh' tor tor ti k' wuh hearth among wuh vitush; heh u' nash, veling, tor ish-veh kwon-hau-ov grazhiv heh kitork, au puvutau ish-veh ashputtel. Ish-veh pavesh-tor wuh'wak ik wuh sa-mekh vesh' going tor wuh rom, heh ya'akash ish-veh ko-telsu's daughters ra au dang katau au. 'tok-ti sai-vel, ' leralmin-tor wuh wuh'rak; 'pearls heh lerash-khush, ' maf-tor wuh dahr. 'i', kan, ' leralmin-tor au tor ish-veh sha' ko-fu, 'ra dungi du ma?' 'wuh wuh'rak pi'gel, tal-kam sa-mekh, ik brushes tehnat ish-veh taik lu du da-tor ish-veh limuk tor sarlah homewards, ' leralmin-tor she. Yi au bought na' wuh wuh'rak dahkuh wuh tok-ti sai-vel heh pearls heh lerash-khush au had ya'akash na': heh fi' ish-veh yut ha-kel, u' au fau-tor k'fai wuh yar-kur pi'laptra, wuh hazel pi'gel brushed tehnat ish-veh, heh siyah kwitau ska' ish-veh taik: ni au shau ish-veh ska' heh katau ish-veh maf; heh lu au prah ha-kel au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh ko-fu. Yi she nem-tor ish-veh, heh went tor ish-veh ko-mekh's shi'vukhut heh kastkau ish-veh tra'; heh maf-tor ni mau ik ish-veh vesh' mashau k' ish-veh bezhun-masu; heh tra' ish-veh grew heh became wuh tok-ti lap. Rehkuh wak kanok gad she went tor ish-veh heh maf-tor; heh ak wuh pi' kushel sarlah heh torvau its ha-kel fi-tor wuh lap, heh variben k' ish-veh, heh paluntunau ish-veh, heh katau ish-veh whatever she istau na'. I' ish-veh pavesh-tor ik wuh sa-te'kru t' ik solektra meskarau wuh gadzhak, if vesh' tor kim-shah rehkuh gad; heh s' eifa vi sarlah tor ish-veh ish-veh sa-fu vesh' tor dvel-tor wuh bride na' himself. Ashputtel's dahkuh ko-kai vesh' ya'akash tor sarlah; ni au puvutau ish-veh abru, heh leralmin-tor, 'i', dref etwel isachya, achut etwel ash'el, heh tie etwel sashes na' etek, na' etek nam-tor going tor tam na' wuh sa-te'kru's gadzhak.' yi she did u' she vesh' var-tor; tonk'peh lu ek' vesh' ovsoh she kupi ri gol'nev maf-tor, na' she nahp tor herself, she dang ni ma tishau ki' hal-tor k' au tor wuh rin'k'n; heh na' kim-shah she eit'jae ish-veh ko-mekh maut lerash tor kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor. 'du, ashputtel!' leralmin-tor she; 'du vi ma nothing tor sai-vel-tor, rai sai-vel na' ek', heh vi fam yehat kauk tam--du aitlun tor hal-tor tor wuh rin'k'n? Heh lu she potau fi' begging, she leralmin-tor na' kim-shah, tor prah rid t' ish-veh, 'i dungi lehm nash dishful t' peas vi' wuh vitush-tuh, heh kuv svi' dahkuh wadan' wak du ma picked au ek' si', du dungau hal-tor tor wuh gadzhak nuh'.' yi she threw wuh peas ne' among wuh vitush, tonk'peh wuh pi' maiden sahr-tor si' na' wuh pla' svep vi' wuh bah-ker, heh lit'dhae: 'hither, hither, k'fai wuh igen, turtle-doves heh linnets, hash-tor! Blackbird, thrush, heh chaffinch sa-ka-ashausu, hither, hither, haste maf! Veh heh ek' sarlah gol'nev me, sahris! Haste ye, haste ye!--pick, pick, pick!' yi wuh'rak sarlah dahkuh wan-kur doves, hashan svi' na' wuh af'tum krani; thurai sarlah dahkuh turtle-doves; heh po' au sarlah ek' wuh pi' kushel ne' sha-ka-ri, chirping heh fluttering svi': heh au flew ne' vi' wuh vitush. Heh wuh pi' doves stooped ish-veh patam ne' heh eku tor ar'kadan, pick, pick, pick; heh yi wuh vath began tor pick, pick, pick: heh among au ek' au ak picked si' ek' wuh rom kap-yar, heh shitau ish-veh vi' wuh dish tonk'peh losrak wuh vitush. Wu fa' wuh shaht t' wuh wadan wuh ar'kadan vesh' ved ovsoh, heh ek' flew si' va'ashiv na' wuh krani. Yi ashputtel katau wuh dish tor ish-veh ko-mekh, overjoyed na' wuh nahp ik i' she dang hal-tor tor wuh rin'k'n. Tonk'peh wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor, 'rai, rai! Du slut, du ma rai sai-vel, heh fam yehat tam; du dungau ri hal-tor.' heh lu ashputtel eit'jae maut lerash tor hal-tor, she leralmin-tor, 'kuv du mokuhlek svi' veh wadan's wak pick dahkuh t' eifa dishes t' peas s' wuh vitush, du dungau hal-tor nuh'.' heh thus she nahp she dang k'puu prah rid t' ish-veh. Ni she hutau dahkuh dishes t' peas vi' wuh vitush. Tonk'peh wuh pi' maiden went si' vi' wuh bah-ker na' wuh pla' t' wuh kelek, heh lit'dhae u' fa': 'hither, hither, k'fai wuh igen, turtle-doves heh linnets, hash-tor! Blackbird, thrush, heh chaffinch sa-ka-ashausu, hither, hither, haste maf! Veh heh ek' sarlah gol'nev me, sahris! Haste ye, haste ye!--pick, pick, pick!' yi wuh'rak sarlah dahkuh wan-kur doves svi' na' wuh af'tum krani; thurai sarlah dahkuh turtle-doves; heh po' au sarlah ek' wuh pi' kushel ne' sha-ka-ri, chirping heh spen-tor pa'. Heh au flew ne' vi' wuh vitush; heh wuh pi' doves shitau ish-veh patam ne' heh eku tor ar'kadan, pick, pick, pick; heh yi wuh vath began pick, pick, pick; heh au shitau ek' wuh rom kap-yar vi' wuh dishes, heh losrak ek' wuh vitush. Fa' ulef wuh wadan's wak ek' vesh' ovsoh, heh si' au flew va'ashiv. Heh yi ashputtel nem-tor wuh dishes tor ish-veh ko-mekh, rejoicing tor nah-tor ik she dang i' hal-tor tor wuh rin'k'n. Tonk'peh ish-veh ko-mekh leralmin-tor, 'ish-veh nam-tor ek' t' rai nam-tor-tor, du fam yehat hal-tor; du ma rai sai-vel, heh fam yehat tam, heh du would goh shitau etek tor mesh': heh ska' she went k' ish-veh dahkuh daughters tor wuh rin'k'n. I' lu ek' vesh' hal-tor, heh kling losrak na' ha-kel, ashputtel went sorrowfully heh hayal-tor ne' ne' wuh hazel-lap, heh lit'dhae: 'hutau, hutau, hazel-lap, pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh abru' me!' yi ish-veh t'hy'la wuh kushel flew s' wuh lap, heh katau wuh pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh sai-vel na' ish-veh, heh slippers t' spangled silk; heh she shitau au fi', heh zahal-tor ish-veh ko-kai tor wuh gadzhak. Tonk'peh au did ri fai-tor ish-veh, heh nahp ish-veh bolau nam-tor ein flekh princess, she glazhau ni tok-ti heh vaksurik svi' ish-veh don-ka sai-vel; heh au worla wuh'wak nahp t' ashputtel, taking ish-veh na' vahl ik she vesh' safe na' ha-kel svi' wuh kitek. Wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu ak sarlah abru tor ish-veh, heh nem-tor ish-veh k' wuh el'ru heh tam-tor k' ish-veh, heh kling else: heh au worla losrak ish-veh el'ru; tonk'peh lu sovek-veh else sarlah tor ya'akash ish-veh tor tam, au leralmin-tor, 'nash t'sai nam-tor taman k' me.' thus au tam-tor till wuh tab-ma wadan t' wuh mu-yor; heh yi she aitlu tor hal-tor ha-kel: heh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu leralmin-tor, 'i dungau hal-tor heh nem-tor tun t' du tor ish-veh ha-kel'; na' au aitlu tor gla-tor wilat wuh vaksurik maiden ha-tor. Tonk'peh she trel-tor maf s' ish-veh, unawares, heh sahr-tor ska' na' ha-kel; heh u' wuh prince zahal-tor ish-veh, she spen-tor abru vi' wuh pigeon-kelek heh ikap-tor wuh svep. Yi au bek-tor till ish-veh sa-mekh sarlah ha-kel, heh var-tor ish-veh ik wuh ri-fainu maiden, vi had vesh' na' wuh gadzhak, had ip-sut herself svi' wuh pigeon-kelek. Tonk'peh lu au had pushau tu'ash wuh svep au afer-tor kling k'svi; heh u' sarlah au pla' vi' wuh kelek, ashputtel vesh' lying, u' she kwon-hau-ov did, svi' ish-veh kitork pelal k' wuh vitush, heh ish-veh neik-ha'khlup pi' ha'gelek vesh' yontau svi' wuh vuzh-mev.
