Na' she had sahr-tor u' sahris u' she kupi k'fai wuh pigeon-kelek heh fi' tor wuh hazel-lap, heh had tra' taken ska' ish-veh vaksurik sai-vel, heh shitau au ne'rak wuh lap, ik wuh kushel lau lesh au maf, heh had lain ne' va'ashiv svi' wuh vitush svi' ish-veh pi' zhai-kur pelal. Wuh thurai gad lu wuh gadzhak vesh' va'ashiv meskarau, heh ish-veh sa-mekh, ko-mekh, heh ko-kai vesh' hal-tor, ashputtel went tor wuh hazel-lap, heh leralmin-tor: 'hutau, hutau, hazel-lap, pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh abru' me!' heh wuh kushel sarlah heh katau wuh fam dvun finer sai-vel do wuh veh she had worn wuh gad fa'. Heh lu sarlah ish-veh svi' ish-veh tor wuh rin'k'n, kanok-veh wondered na' ish-veh vaksur: tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu, vi vesh' waiting na' ish-veh, nem-tor ish-veh k' wuh el'ru, heh tam-tor k' ish-veh; heh lu sovek-veh ya'akash ish-veh tor tam, au leralmin-tor u' fa', 'nash t'sai nam-tor taman k' me.' lu mu-yor sarlah she aitlu tor hal-tor ha-kel; heh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu zahal-tor la' u' fa', ik au lau gla-tor vi' ra kelek she went: tonk'peh she sprang maf s' ish-veh ek' na' wuh'wak vi' wuh bah-ker za' ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek. Svi' nash bah-ker lam-tor wuh tok-ti suk savas-lap bosh t' piyah savas; heh ashputtel, ri fai-tor wilat tor ip-sut herself, spen-tor abru vi' ish-veh rik' hasu gla-tor. Yi wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu pakik glan t' ish-veh, heh kupi ri talal si' wilat she vesh' hal-tor, tonk'peh bek-tor till ish-veh sa-mekh sarlah ha-kel, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'wuh ri-fainu t'sai vi tam-tor k' me has trel-tor maf, heh i nah-tor she bolau ma sprung vi' wuh savas-lap.' wuh sa-mekh nahp tor himself, 'mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor ashputtel?' ni au had wuh la'ash katau; heh au tresahk ne' wuh lap, tonk'peh afer-tor kling fi-tor ish-veh. Heh lu sarlah au pla' vi' wuh af'tum, tra' ti ashputtel among wuh vitush; na' she had trel-tor ne' fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh lap, heh lesh ish-veh vaksurik sai-vel pla' tor wuh kushel na' wuh hazel-lap, heh yi shitau fi' ish-veh pi' zhai-kur pelal. Wuh wuh gad, lu ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh heh ko-kai vesh' hal-tor, she went va'ashiv vi' wuh bah-ker, heh leralmin-tor: 'hutau, hutau, hazel-lap, pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh abru' me!' yi ish-veh ves t'hy'la wuh kushel katau wuh sai-vel fam dvun finer do wuh former veh, heh slippers if vesh' ek' t' pi-maat-tukh: ni ik lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh gadzhak kling fai-tor ra tor leralmin, na' wonder na' ish-veh vaksur: heh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu tam-tor k' kling tonk'peh ish-veh; heh lu sovek-veh else ya'akash ish-veh tor tam, au leralmin-tor, 'nash t'sai nam-tor t'nash-veh tersu, osu.' lu mu-yor sarlah she aitlu tor hal-tor ha-kel; heh wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu would hal-tor k' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor tor himself, 'i dungi ri pak-tor ish-veh nash wak'; tonk'peh, however, she va'ashiv trel-tor maf s' ish-veh, hi svi' such wuh brax ik she eku-tor ish-veh losrak pi-maat-kur slipper fi-tor wuh kaiden. Wuh prince nem-tor wuh ash'el, heh went wuh thurai gad tor wuh sa-te'kru ish-veh sa-mekh, heh leralmin-tor, 'i dungi nem-tor na' t'nash-veh ko-telsu wuh t'sai ik nash pi-maat-kur slipper nunau.' yi fi' wuh ko-kai vesh' overjoyed tor zhu-tor ish-veh; na' au had vaksurik ash'ya, heh had rai vet ik au kupi sai-vel-tor wuh pi-maat-kur slipper. Wuh eldest went wuh'rak vi' wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh slipper vesh', heh aitlu tor ar'kadan ish-veh fi', heh wuh ko-mekh lam-tor k'. Tonk'peh ish-veh lo'uk gof kupi ri hal-tor vi' ish-veh, heh wuh ash'el vesh' altogether mau nuh' pi' na' ish-veh. Yi wuh ko-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh lipau, heh leralmin-tor, 'worla kashek, tresahk ish-veh ska'; lu du nam-tor ko-te'kru du dungi ri tun pa' gof; du dungi ri aitlun tor lates.' ni wuh silly ko-kan tresahk ska' ish-veh lo'uk gof, heh thus lerakhovau fi' wuh ash'el, heh went tor wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu. Yi au nem-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh bride, heh eku ish-veh be' ish-veh fi' ish-veh jarel, heh fau-tor maf k' ish-veh homewards. Tonk'peh fi' ish-veh yut ha-kel au had tor be' dvun k' wuh hazel-lap ik ashputtel had kastkau; heh fi' wuh khlup hayal-tor wuh pi' dove uralaun: 'pla' va'ashiv! Pla' va'ashiv! Glazhau tor wuh ash'el! Wuh ash'el nam-tor nuh' pi', heh ri tor na' du! Prince! Prince! Glazhau va'ashiv na' thy bride, na' she's ri wuh yeht veh ik hayal-tor k' thy vla.' yi wuh prince prah ne' heh glazhau na' ish-veh ash'ya; heh gla-tor ish-veh, k' wuh khaf ik salash s' ish-veh, ra wuh trick she had mavau ish-veh. Ni au da-tor ish-veh jarel pauk, heh katau wuh riyeht bride pla' tor ish-veh ha-kel, heh leralmin-tor, 'nash nam-tor ri wuh gas'rak bride; kal-tor wuh vath ko-kai ar'kadan heh shitau fi' wuh slipper.' yi she went vi' wuh tvi-shal heh prah ish-veh ash'ya vi' wuh ash'el, ek' tonk'peh wuh timut, if vesh' nuh' suk. Tonk'peh ish-veh ko-mekh lerakhovau ish-veh svi' till wuh khaf sarlah, heh nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu: heh au eku ish-veh u' ish-veh bride k' ish-veh vla fi' ish-veh jarel, heh fau-tor maf k' ish-veh. Tonk'peh lu sarlah au tor wuh hazel-lap wuh pi' dove hayal-tor tra' fam dvun, heh sang: 'pla' va'ashiv! Pla' va'ashiv! Glazhau tor wuh ash'el! Wuh ash'el nam-tor nuh' pi', heh ri tor na' du! Prince! Prince! Glazhau va'ashiv na' thy bride, na' she's ri wuh yeht veh ik hayal-tor k' thy vla.' yi au glazhau ne', heh gla-tor ik wuh khaf salash ni mau s' wuh ash'el, ik ish-veh wan-kur stockings vesh' ved yon-kur. Ni au da-tor ish-veh jarel heh katau ish-veh isha pla' va'ashiv. 'nash nam-tor ri wuh yeht bride, ' leralmin-tor au tor wuh sa-mekh; 'ma du rai vath daughters?' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor au; 'tra' nam-tor goh wuh pi' kitork ashputtel la', wuh kan t' t'nash-veh wuh'rak ko-telsu; i am sure she fam yehat nam-tor wuh bride.' wuh prince var-tor ish-veh tor satau ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor, 'rai, rai, she nam-tor mau nuh' kitork; she dungi ri dare tor gluvaya herself.' however, wuh prince would ma ish-veh sarlah; heh she wuh'rak pu-tor ish-veh limuk heh el'ru, heh yi went svi' heh curtsied tor ish-veh, heh au pulau ish-veh wuh pi-maat-kur slipper. Yi she nem-tor ish-veh om'toi ash'el ska' ish-veh losrak ash'ya, heh shitau fi' wuh pi-maat-kur slipper; heh ish-veh fitted ish-veh u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' tor na' ish-veh. Heh lu au drew be' heh glazhau na' ish-veh limuk au fai-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'nash nam-tor wuh gas'rak bride.' tonk'peh wuh ko-mekh heh fi' wuh ko-kai vesh' koltha, heh da-tor spoh k' reshan u' au nem-tor ashputtel fi' ish-veh jarel, heh fau-tor maf k' ish-veh. Heh lu sarlah au tor wuh hazel-lap, wuh wan-kur dove sang: 'ha-kel! Ha-kel! Glazhau na' wuh ash'el! Princess! Wuh ash'el vesh' tor na' du! Prince! Prince! Nem-tor ha-kel thy bride, na' she nam-tor wuh yeht veh ik hayal-tor k' thy vla!' heh lu wuh dove had ovsoh its song, sarlah ish-veh hashan, heh perched fi-tor ish-veh gas'rak tipan, heh ni went ha-kel k' ish-veh. Wuh wan-kur oluhk wuh akarshif ago tra' ha-tor wuh sa-te'kru vi vesh' famed na' ish-veh kau k'fai ek' wuh solektra. Nothing vesh' ipik s' ish-veh, heh ish-veh seemed u' kuv ro'fori t' wuh danik tsat vel vesh' katau tor ish-veh k'fai wuh sov. Tonk'peh au had wuh flekh custom; kanok gad po' aru-yem, lu wuh pasu vesh' pa'shu, heh kling else vesh' la', wuh trusty dvinsu had tor katau ish-veh veh weht dish. Ish-veh vesh' wein-tor, however, heh kauk wuh dvinsu did ri fai-tor ra vesh' svi' ish-veh, neither did sovek-veh fai-tor, na' wuh sa-te'kru worla nem-tor ska' wuh wein tor yokul t' ish-veh abi' au vesh' ved sa'awek. Nash had hal-tor fi' na' wuh akarshif, lu veh gad wuh dvinsu, vi nem-tor maf wuh dish, vesh' overcome k' such curiosity ik au kupi ri gol'nev carrying wuh dish vi' ish-veh tvi-shal. Lu au had carefully klacha wuh svep, au abertau abru wuh wein, heh gla-tor wuh wan-kur oluhk lying fi' wuh dish. Tonk'peh lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh au kupi ri wafu himself wuh sanosh t' tasting ish-veh, ni au tresahk t' wuh pi' zeshau heh shitau ish-veh vi' ish-veh ru'lut. Rai sooner had ish-veh estuhl ish-veh lahv do au puzhu-tor wuh flekh zhalan t' pi' spes s'udish ish-veh krani. Au went heh shroi, heh yi pubeglanau ik ish-veh vesh' wuh sparrows vi vesh' chattering teretuhr, heh telling veh wuh'ashiv t' ek' ves t' vel if au had gla-tor svi' wuh vunai heh lapan. Eating wuh oluhk had putan-tor ish-veh tepul t' understanding wuh gen-lis t' animals. I' ish-veh ni pavesh-tor ik fi' nash maut gad wuh ko-te'kru pakik ish-veh danik vaksurik mokov, heh suspicion t' having stolen ish-veh tevan-tor fi-tor nash trusty dvinsu, vi vesh' kal-tor tor hal-tor kanok-wilat. Wuh sa-te'kru ordered wuh sasu tor nam-tor katau fa' ish-veh, heh threatened k' reshnek zhit ik vita au kupi fa' wuh morrow sasfekau wuh pi'tak, au himself dang nam-tor glazhau fi-tor u' guilty heh fitor. Svi' vain au afsakau ish-veh innocence; au vesh' dismissed k' rai weh-rom kilko-srashiv. Svi' ish-veh trouble heh pthak au went ne' vi' wuh courtyard heh nem-tor nahp uf tor gol'nev himself s' ish-veh trouble. I' ein ducks vesh' sitting teretuhr quietly k' wuh brook heh taking ish-veh shom; heh, whilst au vesh' tor ish-veh kan mos k' ish-veh dun, au vesh' having wuh confidential conversation teretuhr. Wuh dvinsu lam-tor k' heh shroi. Au vesh' telling veh wuh'ashiv t' ek' wuh shitau wilat au had vesh' waddling pa' ek' wuh asal, heh ra rom yem-tukh au had afer-tor; heh veh leralmin-tor svi' wuh pitiful molu: 'vel ti ras fi' t'nash-veh skaun-sa'haf; u' i vesh' eating svi' haste i vitem-tor wuh mokov if ti ne' wuh ko-te'kru's krani.' wuh dvinsu na' wuh'wak seized ish-veh k' wuh talu, lesh ish-veh tor wuh af'tum, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh fas-tor: 'la' nam-tor wuh tok-ti duck; pray, stau ish-veh.' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh fas-tor, heh rasathau ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru; 'she has spared rai trouble tor fatten herself, heh has vesh' waiting tor nam-tor roasted wu hiyet.' ni au tresahk ska' ish-veh patam, heh u' she vesh' hasu sai-vel-tor na' wuh spit, wuh ko-te'kru's mokov vesh' afer-tor svi'udish ish-veh. Wuh dvinsu kupi i' easily skan-tor ish-veh innocence; heh wuh sa-te'kru, tor tor amends na' wuh riyeht, kal-tor ish-veh tor ya'akash wuh favour, heh ugau ish-veh wuh buhfik shi svi' wuh kelek ik au kupi istaya na'. Wuh dvinsu klee'fah kanok-vei, heh goh ya'akash na' wuh jarel heh ein donku na' travelling, u' au had wuh kashek tor gla-tor wuh panu heh hal-tor pa' wuh pi'. Lu ish-veh ya'akash vesh' vahl au eku si' fi' ish-veh yut, heh veh gad sarlah tor wuh muzh, wilat au gla-tor rehkuh aluk kum-tor svi' wuh reeds heh gasping na' masu. I', hi ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor ik aluk nam-tor dumb, au puzhu-tor au lamenting ik au bolau perish ni miserably, heh, u' au had wuh ves khaf-spol, au prah ska' ish-veh jarel heh shitau wuh rehkuh prisoners pla' vi' wuh masu. Au leapt k' delight, shitau si' ish-veh patam, heh maf-tor tor ish-veh: 'etek dungi vokau du heh repay du na' saving etek!' au fau-tor fi', heh po' wuh du' ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik au puzhu-tor wuh spes svi' wuh mazhiv na' ish-veh ash'ya. Au shroi, heh puzhu-tor wuh ant-sa-te'kru complain: 'po fam yehat sular-ves, k' ish-veh om'toi beasts, potau ska' etwel ak'shem? Ik stupid jarel, k' ish-veh ras hoofs, has vesh' treading ne' t'nash-veh sutra rik' mercy!' ni au da-tor fi' tor wuh vla yut heh wuh ant-sa-te'kru lit'dhae tor ish-veh: 'etek dungi vokau du--veh rom da-tor nazh-tor wuh'ashiv!' wuh yut pufulag-tor ish-veh vi' wuh lapan, heh tra' gla-tor ish-veh dahkuh hinek ravens standing k' ish-veh ha-kel, heh throwing si' ish-veh nu'ri ones. 'si' k' du, du idle, rom-na'-nothing creatures!' maf-tor au; 'etek fam yehat talal yem-tukh na' du sovek longer; du nam-tor suk' hiyet, heh mokuhlek tanilau na' yourselves.' tonk'peh wuh ri donku-tor nu'ri ravens ti fi-tor wuh solektra, flapping ish-veh rala, heh maf-tor: 'oh, ra helpless chicks etek nam-tor! Etek bolau izaya na' ourselves, heh wi etek fam yehat hash-tor! Ra mokuhlek etek tor, tonk'peh ti la' heh starve?' ni wuh rom nu'ri katravahsu alighted heh pustau ish-veh jarel k' ish-veh shek, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor au na' yem-tukh. Yi sarlah au spen-tor abru tor ish-veh, satisfied ish-veh avon, heh maf-tor: 'etek dungi vokau du--veh rom da-tor nazh-tor wuh'ashiv!' heh i' au had tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh sha' mal, heh lu au had lates-tor wuh wu yut, sarlah ish-veh tor wuh suk kahr. Tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk ralash heh patreitan svi' wuh yut, heh wuh sasu fau-tor abru fi' horseback, maf-tor aloud: 'wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu aitlu wuh sa-telsu; tonk'peh whoever seeks ish-veh el'ru bolau perform wuh lerash task, heh kuv au tor ri navau au dungi forfeit ish-veh ha'kiv.' wehk had already tor wuh attempt, tonk'peh svi' vain; nevertheless lu wuh youth gla-tor wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu au vesh' ni overcome k' ish-veh lo'uk vaksur ik au forgot ek' tehvar, went fa' wuh sa-te'kru, heh afsakau himself wuh suitor. Ni au vesh' pufulag-tor si' tor wuh masutra, heh wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov vesh' lehm-tor vi' ish-veh, fa' ish-veh bezhun; yi wuh sa-te'kru ordered ish-veh tor zaprah nash mokov abru s' wuh lanet t' wuh masutra, heh hau: 'kuv sarlah du abru va'ashiv rik' ish-veh du dungi nam-tor lehm-tor svi' va'ashiv heh va'ashiv abi' du perish svi' wuh pral.' ek' wuh sutra grieved na' wuh handsome youth; yi au went maf, leaving ish-veh sa'awek k' wuh masutra. Au lam-tor fi' wuh gef heh panah-tor ra au dang tor, lu suddenly gla-tor ish-veh rehkuh aluk sarlah mahalan na' ish-veh, heh au vesh' wuh maut aluk t'vi ha-tor au had korsau. Wuh veh svi' wuh svitan meskarau wuh mussel svi' its ru'lut, if ish-veh laid fi' wuh gef na' wuh youth's ash'ya, heh lu au had taken ish-veh abru heh tu'ash ish-veh, tra' ti wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov svi' wuh fo. Bosh t' mak au nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru heh gishu ik au would vahl ish-veh wuh ugau reward. Tonk'peh lu wuh yaut princess pakashogau ik au vesh' ri ish-veh kaik svi' keshtan, she scorned ish-veh, heh required ish-veh wuh'rak tor perform wuh'ashiv task. She went ne' vi' wuh bah-ker heh strewed k' ish-veh sha' el'ru lehkuh sacksful t' millet-nei fi' wuh yar; yi she leralmin-tor: 'fa-gad asal fa' ug'yel-shen aifa bolau nam-tor abrashau, heh ri wuh single kap-yar nam-tor wanting.' wuh youth hayal-tor ne' svi' wuh bah-ker heh panah-tor uf ish-veh lau nam-tor tor-yehat tor perform nash task, tonk'peh au kupi nah-tor t' nothing, heh tra' au hayal-tor sorrowfully awaiting wuh shaya t' gad, lu au dang nam-tor pufulag-tor tor tevakh. Tonk'peh u' ak u' wuh wuh'rak ha'zehl t' wuh yel min-tor vi' wuh bah-ker gla-tor ish-veh ek' wuh lehkuh sa'haf standing vla k' vla, ved bosh, heh ri wuh single kap-yar vesh' missing. Wuh ant-sa-te'kru had sarlah svi' wuh mu-yor k' thousands heh thousands t' ants, heh wuh grateful creatures had k' lo'uk industry abrashau ek' wuh millet-nei heh hoknau au vi' wuh sa'haf. Presently wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu herself sarlah ne' vi' wuh bah-ker, heh vesh' putaurau tor gla-tor ik wuh nu'ri sasu had ovsoh wuh task she had putan-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh she kupi ri wi conquer ish-veh yaut khaf-spol, heh leralmin-tor: 'hi au has performed fi' wuh tasks, au dungau ri nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu abi' au had katau me wuh savas s' wuh lap t' ha'kiv.' wuh youth did ri fai-tor wilat wuh lap t' ha'kiv lam-tor, tonk'peh au eku si', heh would ma hal-tor fi' na' ek'wak, u' wu u' ish-veh mal would lesh ish-veh, hi au had rai rok t' finding ish-veh. Po' au had czar-tor k'fai rehkuh kingdoms, sarlah ish-veh veh khru tor wuh lapan, heh ti ne' ne' wuh lap tor yuk. Tonk'peh au puzhu-tor wuh rustling svi' wuh khlup, heh wuh pi-maat-kur savas tevan-tor vi' ish-veh el'ru. Na' wuh ka wak rehkuh ravens flew ne' tor ish-veh, perched themselves fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef, heh leralmin-tor: 'etek nam-tor wuh rehkuh nu'ri ravens ik du korsau s' starving; lu etek had grown suk', heh puzhu-tor ik du vesh' seeking wuh pi-maat-kur savas, etek flew abru' wuh masutra tor wuh shaht t' wuh panu, wilat wuh lap t' ha'kiv lam-tor, heh ma katau du wuh savas.' wuh youth, bosh t' mak, eku si' homewards, heh nem-tor wuh pi-maat-kur savas tor wuh sa-te'kru's vaksurik ko-fu, vi had i' rai weht tobeg-tor losrak tor tor. Au tresahk wuh savas t' ha'kiv svi' dahkuh heh ate ish-veh teretuhr; heh yi ish-veh khaf-spol became bosh t' ashaya na' ish-veh, heh au ha-tor svi' undisturbed happiness tor wuh lo'uk ya'shakhuv. Wuh wolf heh wuh stehkuh pi' kan tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh hinek vralt vi had stehkuh pi' kan, heh ashau au k' ek' wuh ashaya t' wuh ko-mekh na' ish-veh kanu. Veh gad she aitlu tor hal-tor vi' wuh laptra heh zaprah ein yem-tukh. Ni she puvutau ek' stehkuh tor ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'tal-kam kanu, i ma tor hal-tor vi' wuh laptra, nam-tor fi' ish-veh klashausu tehnat wuh wolf; kuv sarlah ish-veh svi', au dungi katau du ek'--wadi, isachya, heh kanok-vei. Wuh wretch k'ashiv pastau himself, tonk'peh du dungi fai-tor ish-veh na' wuh'wak k' ish-veh rough spes heh ish-veh nesh-kur ash'ya.' wuh kan leralmin-tor: 'tal-kam ko-mekh, etek dungi nem-tor rom tun t' ourselves; du lau hal-tor maf rik' sovek anxiety.' yi wuh hinek veh bleated, heh went fi' ish-veh yut k' wuh hagik kashek. Ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' ein-veh knocked na' wuh kelek-svep heh puvutau: 'tu'ash wuh svep, tal-kam kanu; ish-veh ko-mekh nam-tor la', heh has katau vel pla' k' ish-veh na' tik t' du.' tonk'peh wuh pi' kan fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' wuh wolf, k' wuh rough spes. 'etek dungi ri tu'ash wuh svep, ' maf-tor au, 'du nam-tor ri etwel ko-mekh. She has wuh mos, vaksurik spes, tonk'peh ish-veh spes nam-tor rough; du nam-tor wuh wolf!' yi wuh wolf went maf tor wuh shopkeeper heh bought himself wuh lo'uk vihk t' gav, ate nash heh tor ish-veh spes mos k' ish-veh. Yi sarlah ish-veh pla', knocked na' wuh svep t' wuh kelek, heh puvutau: 'tu'ash wuh svep, tal-kam kanu, ish-veh ko-mekh nam-tor la' heh has katau vel pla' k' ish-veh na' tik t' du.' tonk'peh wuh wolf had laid ish-veh nesh-kur paws tehnat wuh krani, heh wuh kanu gla-tor au heh maf-tor: 'etek dungi ri tu'ash wuh svep, etwel ko-mekh has ri nesh-kur ash'ya spo' du: du nam-tor wuh wolf!' yi wuh wolf sahr-tor tor wuh leipausu heh leralmin-tor: 'i ma dash-tor t'nash-veh ash'ya, tetaya ein ned abru' au na' me.' heh lu wuh leipausu had tetau ish-veh ash'ya abru', au sahr-tor tor wuh miller heh leralmin-tor: 'strew ein wan-kur yem abru' t'nash-veh ash'ya na' me.' wuh miller nahp tor himself: 'wuh wolf aitlu tor tehs-tor ein-veh, ' heh klee'fah; tonk'peh wuh wolf leralmin-tor: 'kuv du dungi ri tor ish-veh, i dungi katau du.' yi wuh miller vesh' kwes, heh tor ish-veh paws wan-kur na' ish-veh. Truly, nash nam-tor wuh yut t' mankind. Ni i' wuh wretch went na' wuh wuh wak tor wuh kelek-svep, knocked na' ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'tu'ash wuh svep na' me, kanu, ish-veh tal-kam pi' ko-mekh has sarlah ha-kel, heh has katau kanok veh t' du vel pla' s' wuh laptra k' ish-veh.' wuh pi' kan maf-tor: 'wuh'rak gluvaya etek ish-veh paws ik etek lau fai-tor kuv du nam-tor etwel tal-kam pi' ko-mekh.' yi au shitau ish-veh paws svi' k'fai wuh krani heh lu wuh kan gla-tor ik au vesh' wan-kur, au pudva-tor ik ek' au leralmin-tor vesh' yeht, heh tu'ash wuh svep. Tonk'peh vi dang sarlah svi' tonk'peh wuh wolf! Au vesh' terrified heh aitlu tor ip-sut themselves. Veh sprang ne' wuh pasu, wuh dahr vi' wuh sar-tak, wuh wuh vi' wuh stove, wuh fourth vi' wuh af'tum, wuh fifth vi' wuh cupboard, wuh sixth ne' wuh washing-yerak, heh wuh seventh vi' wuh wak-vel-nuf. Tonk'peh wuh wolf afer-tor au ek', heh nam-tor-tor rai lo'uk hali-kal; veh po' wuh vath au vitem-tor au ne' ish-veh drahk. Wuh youngest, vi vesh' svi' wuh wak-vel-nuf, vesh' wuh goh veh au did ri talal. Lu wuh wolf had satisfied ish-veh yeht-avon au nem-tor himself ska', laid himself ne' ne' wuh lap svi' wuh yar-kur ne-yartra s'udish, heh began tor yuk. Ak afterwards wuh hinek vralt sarlah ha-kel va'ashiv s' wuh laptra. Ah! Ra wuh glan gla-tor ish-veh tra'! Wuh kelek-svep lam-tor eik tu'ash. Wuh pasu, ku-san, heh wu-ku-san vesh' lehm-tor ne', wuh washing-yerak ti pushau tor krus, heh wuh quilts heh trak vesh' seshau ska' wuh sar-tak. She sought ish-veh kanu, tonk'peh au vesh' nowhere tor nam-tor afer-tor. She puvutau au veh po' wuh'ashiv k' ahm, tonk'peh kling kilko-tor. Na' kim-shah, lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh youngest, wuh mos spes maf-tor: 'tal-kam ko-mekh, i am svi' wuh wak-vel-nuf.' she nem-tor wuh kan si', heh ish-veh var-tor ish-veh ik wuh wolf had sarlah heh had yokul ek' wuh vath. Yi du lau glenonau uf she wept abru' ish-veh ri donku-tor kanu. Na' wu-vath svi' ish-veh tushat she went si', heh wuh youngest kan sahr-tor k' ish-veh. Lu sarlah au tor wuh ne-yartra, tra' ti wuh wolf k' wuh lap heh snored ni ral ik wuh khlup hutau. She glazhau na' ish-veh fi' kanok vla heh gla-tor ik vel vesh' dvun-tor heh struggling svi' ish-veh gorged nehg. 'ah, heavens, ' she leralmin-tor, 'nam-tor ish-veh tor-yehat ik t'nash-veh ri donku-tor kanu ik au has vitem-tor ne' na' ish-veh mu'yor-yem, mokuhlek nam-tor fam dvun alive?' yi wuh kan had tor sahr-tor ha-kel heh zaprah scissors, heh wuh og-lum heh og-elakh, heh wuh vralt tresahk tu'ash wuh stislak's skaun-sa'haf, heh hardly had she tor veh tresahk, do veh pi' kan kwit its patam si', heh lu she had tresahk weh-irak, ek' shehkuh sprang si' veh po' wuh'ashiv, heh vesh' ek' fam dvun alive, heh had dashau rai dash whatever, na' svi' ish-veh greediness wuh stislak had vitem-tor au ne' bosh. Ra rejoicing tra' vesh'! Au nartau ish-veh tal-kam ko-mekh, heh spen-tor spo' wuh ogsu na' ish-veh wedding. Wuh ko-mekh, however, leralmin-tor: 'i' hal-tor heh glazhau na' ein suk' kov, heh etek dungi boshaya wuh wicked beast's skaun-sa'haf k' au du' au nam-tor fam dvun asleep.' yi wuh stehkuh kan zaseshau wuh kov thither k' ek' threshan, heh shitau u' wehk t' au vi' nash skaun-sa'haf u' au kupi prah svi'; heh wuh ko-mekh og-tor ish-veh abru va'ashiv svi' wuh greatest haste, ni ik au vesh' ri aware t' sovek-vel heh worla wuh'wak stirred. Lu wuh wolf na' wu-vath had had ish-veh boshaya t' yuk, au prah fi' ish-veh mal, heh u' wuh kov svi' ish-veh skaun-sa'haf tor ish-veh maut thirsty, au aitlu tor hal-tor tor wuh muhl tor mon. Tonk'peh lu au began tor lates heh tor dvun pa', wuh kov svi' ish-veh skaun-sa'haf knocked tehnat tik vath heh rattled. Yi maf-tor au: 'ra rumbles heh tumbles tehnat t'nash-veh ri donku-tor hinek? I nahp 'twas shehkuh kan, tonk'peh ish-veh olau spo' suk' kov.' heh lu au prah tor wuh muhl heh stooped abru' wuh masu tor mon, wuh ras kov tor ish-veh tevan svi', heh au mastevau miserably. Lu wuh stehkuh kan gla-tor ik, sarlah au sahran tor wuh gla-tor heh maf-tor aloud: 'wuh wolf nam-tor tevik! Wuh wolf nam-tor tevik!' heh tam-tor na' mak pauk pa' wuh muhl k' ish-veh ko-mekh. Wuh ko-te'kru bee dahkuh sa-te'kru' sa-fu wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak went vi' wuh panu tor seek ish-veh fortunes; tonk'peh au ak tevan-tor vi' wuh wasteful duhik yut t' living, ni ik au kupi ri fun ha-kel va'ashiv. Yi ish-veh sa-kai, vi vesh' wuh pi' insignificant kobsu, went si' tor seek na' ish-veh sa-kai: tonk'peh lu au had afer-tor au au goh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh, tor nah-tor ik au, vi vesh' ni nu'ri heh velik, dang ar'kadan tor haolvaya k'fai wuh panu, lu au, vi vesh' ni mau wiser, had vesh' unable tor prah fi'. However, au ek' eku si' fi' ish-veh halovaya teretuhr, heh sarlah na' kim-shah tor wuh ant-kunel. Wuh dahkuh tela'at sa-kai would ma seshau ish-veh ne', svi' zek tor gla-tor uf wuh ri donku-tor ants svi' ish-veh kolthak would sahr-tor pa' heh lesh ska' ish-veh yu-mur. Tonk'peh wuh pi' kobsu leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor wuh ri donku-tor vel tizh-tor themselves, i dungi ri dash du tor trouble au.' ni fi' au went, heh sarlah tor wuh suk'muzh wilat wehk wehk ducks vesh' mahalan pa'. Wuh dahkuh sa-kai aitlu tor kum dahkuh, heh roast au. Tonk'peh wuh kobsu leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor wuh ri donku-tor vel tizh-tor themselves, du dungau ri stau au.' thurai sarlah au tor wuh bees'-ha-kel svi' wuh hollow lap, heh tra' vesh' ni mau honey ik ish-veh sahr-tor ne' wuh lap-fek; heh wuh dahkuh sa-kai aitlu tor ta'hal wuh yon ne' wuh lap heh stau wuh bees, ni u' tor prah ish-veh honey. Tonk'peh wuh kobsu meskarau au pla', heh leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor wuh takov ravot tizh-tor themselves, i fam yehat kal-tor du yontau au.' na' wu-vath wuh rehkuh sa-kai sarlah tor wuh castle: heh u' au be' dvun-tor k' wuh stables gla-tor au tok-ti jarel standing tra', tonk'peh ek' vesh' t' marble, heh rai sasu vesh' tor nam-tor gla-tor. Yi au went k'fai ek' wuh tvi-shal, till au sarlah tor wuh svep fi' if vesh' rehkuh klachek: tonk'peh svi' wuh svitan t' wuh svep vesh' wuh wicket, ni ik au kupi glazhau vi' wuh thurai tvi-shal. Tra' gla-tor au wuh pi' zhai-kur hinek sasu sitting na' wuh pasu; heh au puvutau tor ish-veh wuh'wak il dah'wak, tonk'peh au did ri zhu-tor: however, au puvutau wuh wuh wak, heh yi au she-tor heh sasarlah tor au. Au leralmin-tor nothing, tonk'peh nem-tor meskaraya t' au heh pufulag-tor au tor wuh vaksurik pasu wein-tor k' ek' wihfelau t' rom vel: heh lu au had yokul heh mon-tor, au gluvau tik t' au tor wuh sar-tak-tvi-shal. Wuh thurai asal sarlah ish-veh tor wuh eldest heh nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh marble pasu, wilat tra' vesh' rehkuh tablets, containing wuh khrosahp t' wuh tvai k' if wuh castle lau nam-tor disenchanted. Wuh wuh'rak tablet leralmin-tor: 'svi' wuh lapan, ne' wuh yekuhl, ti wuh thousand pearls t' wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu; au bolau ek' nam-tor afer-tor: heh kuv veh nam-tor missing k' eku t' yel, au vi seeks au dungi nam-tor da-tor vi' marble.' wuh eldest sa-kai eku si', heh sought na' wuh pearls wuh bosh gad: tonk'peh wuh khru sarlah, heh au had ri afer-tor wuh wuh'rak hundred: ni au vesh' da-tor vi' kov u' wuh tablet had fa-ariben. Wuh thurai gad wuh dahr sa-kai undertook wuh task; tonk'peh au navau rai weh-rom do wuh wuh'rak; na' au kupi goh talal wuh dahr hundred t' wuh pearls; heh therefore au nuh' vesh' da-tor vi' kov. Na' kim-shah sarlah wuh pi' kobsu's da-tor; heh au glazhau svi' wuh yekuhl; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ni lerash tor talal wuh pearls, heh wuh job vesh' ni tiresome!--ni au hayal-tor ne' fi-tor wuh kov heh maf-tor. Heh u' au hayal-tor tra', wuh sa-te'kru t' wuh ants (t'vi ha'kiv au had korsau) sarlah tor gol'nev ish-veh, k' kaukuh thousand ants; heh ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' au had afer-tor ek' wuh pearls heh laid au svi' wuh tuh. Wuh dahr tablet leralmin-tor: 'wuh tal-muv t' wuh princess's sar-tak-tvi-shal bolau nam-tor aluk-kum-tor abru s' wuh suk'muzh.' heh u' wuh kobsu sarlah tor wuh rihk t' ish-veh, gla-tor ish-veh wuh dahkuh ducks t'vi ha-tor au had korsau mahalan pa'; heh au taul-tor ne' heh ak katau svi' wuh tal-muv s' wuh lanet. Wuh wuh task vesh' wuh hardest. Ish-veh vesh' tor dvel-tor si' wuh youngest heh wuh buhfik t' wuh sa-te'kru's rehkuh daughters. I' au vesh' ek' vaksurik, heh ek' exactly kahkwa: tonk'peh au vesh' var-tor ik wuh eldest had yokul wuh krus t' slor-tukh, wuh thurai ein slor syrup, heh wuh youngest wuh spoonful t' honey; ni au vesh' tor guess if ish-veh vesh' ik had yokul wuh honey. Yi sarlah wuh ko-te'kru t' wuh bees, vi had vesh' korsau k' wuh pi' kobsu s' wuh yon, heh she ar'kada wuh bru-lar t' ek' rehkuh; tonk'peh na' kim-shah she hayal-tor fi-tor wuh bru-lar t' wuh veh ik had yokul wuh honey: heh ni wuh kobsu fai-tor if vesh' wuh youngest. Thus wuh spell vesh' pushau, heh ek' vi had vesh' da-tor vi' kov awoke, heh nem-tor ish-veh proper shidau. Heh wuh kobsu telik wuh youngest heh wuh buhfik t' wuh princesses, heh vesh' sa-te'kru po' ish-veh sa-mekh's tevakh; tonk'peh ish-veh dahkuh sa-kai telik wuh vath dahkuh ko-kai. Wuh elves heh wuh shoemaker tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh shoemaker, vi ar'kada maut lerash heh vesh' maut trau: tonk'peh fam dvun au kupi ri pinkau hiyet tor ha-tor fi-tor; heh na' kim-shah ek' au had svi' wuh panu vesh' hal-tor, korsau aishan duf hiyet tor tor veh shif t' ash'el. Yi au tresahk ish-veh duf si', ek' pok tor tor abru wuh thurai gad, meaning tor shen lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal tor ish-veh ar'kadan. Ish-veh conscience vesh' pa'shik heh ish-veh khaf-spol ta'hal amidst ek' ish-veh troubles; ni au went peaceably tor sar-tak, losrak ek' ish-veh tun-tor tor sha-ka-ri, heh ak tevan-tor asleep. Svi' wuh asal po' au had leralmin-tor ish-veh prayers, au hayal-tor himself ne' tor ish-veh ar'kadan; lu, tor ish-veh lo'uk wonder, tra' lam-tor wuh ash'el ek' pok tor, fi-tor wuh pasu. Wuh rom sasu fai-tor ri ra tor leralmin il nah-tor na' such wuh shaik vel aisha. Au glazhau na' wuh workmanship; tra' vesh' ri veh riyeht og svi' wuh bosh job; ek' vesh' ni pu heh yeht, ik ish-veh vesh' ved wuh masterpiece. Wuh ka gad wuh klepovausu sarlah svi', heh wuh ash'el suited ish-veh ni muhl ik au willingly vlitau wuh price higher do tsuri na' au; heh wuh ri donku-tor shoemaker, k' wuh donku, bought duf hiyet tor tor dahkuh shif weht. Svi' wuh khru au tresahk si' wuh ar'kadan, heh went tor sar-tak lehkuh-mal, ik au lau prah abru heh palikau betimes thurai gad; tonk'peh au vesh' korsau ek' wuh trouble, na' lu au prah abru svi' wuh asal wuh ar'kadan vesh' ovsoh pok tor ish-veh el'ru. Ak svi' sarlah klepovausu, vi vlitau ish-veh handsomely na' ish-veh goods, ni ik au bought duf hiyet na' kehkuh shif weht. Au tresahk si' wuh ar'kadan va'ashiv overnight heh afer-tor ish-veh ovsoh svi' wuh asal, u' fa'; heh ni ish-veh went fi' na' ein wak: ra vesh' prah pok svi' wuh khru vesh' kwon-hau-ov ovsoh k' gad-keshtan, heh wuh rom sasu ak became smusma-tor heh muhl ska' va'ashiv. Veh khru, pa' christmas-wak, u' au heh ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' sitting abru' wuh yon chatting teretuhr, au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'i dang spo' tor hayal-tor abru heh glantau tonight, ik etek lau gla-tor vi ish-veh nam-tor ik sarlah heh tor t'nash-veh ar'kadan na' me.' wuh ko-telsu tishau wuh nahp; ni au losrak wuh ta'hal yontau, heh ip-sut themselves svi' wuh teruk t' wuh tvi-shal, za' wuh curtain ik vesh' geldau abru tra', heh glantau ra would pavesh-tor. U' ak u' ish-veh vesh' midnight, tra' sarlah svi' dahkuh pi' sai-fam dwarfs; heh au hayal-tor themselves fi-tor wuh shoemaker's wu-ku-san, nem-tor abru ek' wuh ar'kadan ik vesh' tresahk si', heh began tor ply k' ish-veh wuhr-ozh, stitching heh rapping heh tapping maf na' such wuh tav, ik wuh shoemaker vesh' ek' wonder, heh kupi ri nem-tor ish-veh bezhun ska' au. Heh fi' au went, till wuh job vesh' ved ovsoh, heh wuh ash'el lam-tor pok na' nam-tor-tor fi-tor wuh pasu. Nash vesh' wu fa' gad-keshtan; heh yi au bustled maf u' sahris u' igen-wesh. Wuh thurai gad wuh ko-telsu leralmin-tor tor wuh shoemaker. 'aifa pi' wights ma tor etek don-ka, heh etek ought tor nam-tor itar-bosh tor au, heh tor au wuh rom da-tor kuv etek mokuhlek. I am ved sorry tor gla-tor au sahr-tor pa' u' au tor; heh indeed ish-veh nam-tor ri maut tevan, na' au ma nothing fi-tor ish-veh pla'dor tor potau ska' wuh samu. I'll var-tor du ra, i dungi tor tik t' au wuh sav'el, heh wuh tor-pal heh waistcoat, heh wuh shif t' pantaloons vi' wuh bargain; heh tor du tor tik t' au wuh pi' shif t' ash'el.' wuh nahp sanoi wuh rom cobbler maut mau; heh veh khru, lu ek' wuh vel vesh' pok, au laid au fi' wuh pasu, instead t' wuh ar'kadan ik au nam-tor-tor tor tresahk si', heh yi went heh ip-sut themselves, tor glantau ra wuh pi' elves would tor. Pa' midnight svi' sarlah au, taman heh skipping, spen-tor pauk wuh tvi-shal, heh yi went tor hayal-tor ne' tor ish-veh ar'kadan u' tsuri; tonk'peh lu au gla-tor wuh sai-vel lying na' au, au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh chuckled, heh seemed mightily delighted. Yi au sai-vel-tor themselves svi' wuh twinkling t' wuh bezhun, heh tam-tor heh capered heh sprang pa', u' merry u' kupi nam-tor; till na' kim-shah au tam-tor si' na' wuh svep, heh maf abru' wuh yar-kur. Wuh rom couple gla-tor au rai weht; tonk'peh kanok-vei went muhl k' au s' ik wak fa'rak, u' wu u' au ha-tor. Wuh juniper-lap wu, wu ago, ein dah-leh-teh tevun il ni, tra' ha-tor wuh don-ka sasu k' wuh rom heh vaksurik ko-telsu. Au ashau tik vath dearly, tonk'peh sorrowed mau ik au had rai kanu. Ni greatly did au aitlun ki' veh, ik wuh ko-telsu prayed na' ish-veh gad heh mu-yor, tonk'peh fam dvun au hafau childless. Svi' khom t' wuh kelek tra' vesh' wuh kelek, svi' if grew wuh juniper-lap. Veh karil's gad wuh ko-telsu lam-tor ne' wuh lap tor puhnk ein savas, heh u' she vesh' puhnk-tor au, she tresahk ish-veh ozh, heh wuh khaf tevan-tor fi' wuh izh. 'ah, ' spes-tevan wuh kosu heavily, 'kuv i had tonk'peh wuh kan, u' yon-kur u' khaf heh u' wan-kur u' izh, ' heh u' she stariben wuh zhit, ish-veh khaf-spol grew ta'hal k'svi ish-veh, heh ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik ish-veh istaya vesh' vahl, heh she fun-tor tor wuh kelek olaya glad heh comforted. Wuh tevun-krus be' dvun-tor, heh wuh izh had ek' sasaudau; yi wuh'ashiv tevun-krus went k', heh ek' wuh terra vesh' yar-kur. Ni wuh tevun-krus zahal-tor veh wuh'ashiv, heh wuh'rak wuh lap budded svi' wuh lapan, heh ak wuh yar-kur khlup grew bali intertwined, heh yi wuh blossoms began tor tevan. Wuh'wak va'ashiv wuh ko-telsu lam-tor ne' wuh juniper-lap, heh ish-veh vesh' ni bosh t' slor scent ik ish-veh khaf-spol leaped na' mak, heh she vesh' ni overcome k' ish-veh happiness, ik she tevan-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef. Presently wuh savas became pauk heh pesik, heh she vesh' glad heh na' sochya; tonk'peh lu au vesh' fully piyah she picked wuh nei-savas heh ate eagerly t' au, heh yi she grew maf heh has-bosh. Wuh pi' du' later she puvutau ish-veh sa-telsu, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, weeping. 'kuv i tev-tor, visolektau me ne' wuh juniper-lap.' yi she olau comforted heh kunli va'ashiv, heh fa' wuh'ashiv tevun-krus had be' dvun-tor she had wuh pi' kan, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' u' wan-kur u' izh heh u' yon-kur u' khaf, ish-veh mak vesh' ni lo'uk ik she tev-tor. Ish-veh sa-telsu visolektau ish-veh ne' wuh juniper-lap, heh wept bitterly na' ish-veh. K' degrees, however, ish-veh sorrow grew lehkuh, heh hi na' wak au fam dvun grieved abru' ish-veh pak, au vesh' kup tor hal-tor pa' u' tsuri, heh later fi' au telik va'ashiv. Au i' had wuh pi' ko-fu pukeshta tor ish-veh; wuh kan t' ish-veh wuh'rak ko-telsu vesh' wuh sa-kan, vi vesh' u' yon-kur u' khaf heh u' wan-kur u' izh. Wuh ko-mekh ashau ish-veh ko-fu maut mau, heh lu she glazhau na' ish-veh heh yi glazhau na' wuh sa-kan, ish-veh tilau ish-veh khaf-spol tor nah-tor ik au would kwon-hau-ov lamok svi' wuh yut t' ish-veh sha' kan, heh she vesh' continually thinking uf she kupi prah wuh bosh t' wuh veltra na' ish-veh. Nash ek'rasah nahp nem-tor mat t' ish-veh weht heh weht, heh tor ish-veh kloshah maut unkindly tor wuh sa-kan. She drove ish-veh s' shi tor shi k' cuffings heh buffetings, ni ik wuh ri donku-tor kan went pa' svi' pthak, heh had rai sochya s' wuh wak au losrak shi'oren tor wuh wak au went pla'. Veh gad wuh pi' ko-fu sarlah sahran tor ish-veh ko-mekh svi' wuh mahr-kel-tvi-shal, heh leralmin-tor, 'ko-mekh, mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh savas.' 'ha, t'nash-veh kan, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu, heh she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh vaksurik savas s' wuh tuf; wuh tuf had wuh maut ras lid heh wuh suk shek-tukh klachek. 'ko-mekh, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi' ko-fu va'ashiv, 'lau ri sa-kai ma veh nuh'?' wuh ko-mekh vesh' reshnek na' nash, tonk'peh she kilko-tor, 'ha, lu au sasarlah t' shi'oren.' aishan yi she glazhau s' wuh krani heh gla-tor ish-veh coming, heh ish-veh seemed u' kuv wuh ek'rasah tam'a svi-tor vi' ish-veh, na' she snatched wuh savas si' t' ish-veh pi' ko-fu's el'ru, heh leralmin-tor, 'du dungau ri ma veh fa' ish-veh sa-kai.' she threw wuh savas vi' wuh tuf heh ikap-tor ish-veh tor. Wuh pi' sa-kan i' sarlah svi', heh wuh ek'rasah tam'a svi' wuh ko-telsu tor ish-veh leralmin kindly tor ish-veh, 't'nash-veh sa-fu, dungi du ma wuh savas?' tonk'peh she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh wicked glazhau. 'ko-mekh, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-kan, 'uf dreadful du glazhau! Ha, mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh savas.' wuh nahp sarlah tor ish-veh ik she would stau ish-veh. 'sarlah k' me, ' she leralmin-tor, heh she abertau abru wuh lid t' wuh tuf; 'nem-tor veh si' na' yourself.' heh u' au keh'sei abru' tor tor ni, wuh ek'rasah tam'a urged ish-veh, heh tevul! Ne' went wuh lid, heh ska' went wuh pi' sa-kan's patam. Yi she vesh' overwhelmed k' pthak na' wuh nahp t' ra she had ovsoh. 'kuv goh i mokuhlek prevent sovek-veh fai-tor ik i did ish-veh, ' she nahp. Ni she went upstairs tor ish-veh tvi-shal, heh nem-tor wuh wan-kur handkerchief s' ish-veh fik zish-nef; yi she eku wuh sa-kan's patam va'ashiv fi' ish-veh tipan, heh bound ish-veh k' wuh handkerchief ni ik nothing kupi nam-tor gla-tor, heh shitau ish-veh fi' wuh ku-san k' wuh svep k' wuh savas svi' ish-veh el'ru. Ak po' nash, pi' marleen sarlah abru tor ish-veh ko-mekh vi vesh' stirring wuh sunil t' boiling masu abru' wuh yon, heh leralmin-tor, 'ko-mekh, sa-kai nam-tor sitting k' wuh svep k' wuh savas svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh au glazhau ni spoh; heh lu i ya'akash ish-veh tor mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh savas, au did ri kilko-srashiv, heh ik koltha me.' 'hal-tor tor ish-veh va'ashiv, ' leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, 'heh kuv au tor ri kilko-srashiv, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh natuhn fi' wuh kaluk.' ni pi' marleen went, heh leralmin-tor, 'sa-kai, mazhiv-kur-tor me ik savas, ' tonk'peh au did ri leralmin wuh zhit; yi she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh natuhn fi' wuh kaluk, heh ish-veh patam padukau ska'. She vesh' ni terrified na' nash, ik she sahr-tor maf-tor heh screaming tor ish-veh ko-mekh. 'oh!' she leralmin-tor, 'i ma knocked ska' sa-kai's patam, ' heh yi she wept heh wept, heh nothing would pehkaya ish-veh. 'ra ma du ovsoh!' leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, 'tonk'peh kling bolau fai-tor pa' ish-veh, ni du bolau potau silence; ra nam-tor ovsoh mokuhlek't nam-tor undone; etek dungi tor ish-veh vi' puddings.' heh she nem-tor wuh pi' sa-kan heh tresahk ish-veh abru, tor ish-veh vi' puddings, heh shitau ish-veh svi' wuh sunil. Tonk'peh marleen lam-tor looking fi', heh wept heh wept, heh ish-veh bezhun-masu tevan-tor vi' wuh sunil, ni ik tra' vesh' rai bolaya t' alem. Presently wuh sa-mekh sarlah ha-kel heh hayal-tor ne' tor ish-veh aru-yem; au ya'akash, 'wilat nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-fu?' wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor nothing, tonk'peh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh suk dish t' nesh-kur pudding, heh marleen fam dvun wept rik' ceasing. Wuh sa-mekh va'ashiv ya'akash, 'wilat nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-fu?' 'oh, ' kilko-tor wuh ko-telsu, 'au nam-tor hal-tor vi' wuh shasol tor ish-veh ko-mekh's lo'uk sa-kuk; au nam-tor going tor stay tra' ein wak.' 'ra has au hal-tor tra' na', heh au worla kauk leralmin-tor goodbye tor me!' 'muhl, au tishau hasu tra', heh au var-tor me au dang nam-tor maf ved shehkuh wehk gad; au nam-tor muhl glazhau po' tra'.' 'i olau maut unhappy pa' ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-telsu, 'svi' nuf ish-veh dang ri nam-tor ek' gas'rak, heh au ought ki' leralmin-tor goodbye tor me.' k' nash au went fi' k' ish-veh aru-yem, heh leralmin-tor, 'pi' marleen, po tor du tusa? Sa-kai dungi ak nam-tor pla'.' yi au ya'akash ish-veh ko-telsu na' weht pudding, heh u' au ate, au threw wuh hinek ne' wuh pasu. Pi' marleen went upstairs heh nem-tor ish-veh buhfik silk handkerchief s' ish-veh lanet zish-nef, heh svi' ish-veh she wrapped ek' wuh hinek s' ne' wuh pasu heh lesh au s'udish, heh ek' wuh wak she did nothing tonk'peh tusa. Yi she laid au svi' wuh yar-kur yar ne' wuh juniper-lap, heh she had rai sooner ovsoh ni, yi ek' ish-veh sadness seemed tor trasha ish-veh, heh she wept rai weht. Heh i' wuh juniper-lap began tor dvun, heh wuh khlup pral-tor pla'rak heh fa'rak, wuh'rak maf s' veh wuh'ashiv, heh yi teretuhr va'ashiv, u' ish-veh lau nam-tor ein-veh clapping ish-veh el'ru na' mak. Po' nash wuh mist sarlah pauk wuh lap, heh svi' wuh midst t' ish-veh tra' vesh' wuh yontau u' t' yon, heh s' wuh yon tra' flew wuh vaksurik kushel, ik she-tor pid vi' wuh sov, uralaun magnificently, heh lu ish-veh kupi rai weht nam-tor gla-tor, wuh juniper-lap lam-tor tra' u' fa', heh wuh silk handkerchief heh wuh hinek vesh' hal-tor. Pi' marleen i' olau u' lighthearted heh kunli u' kuv ish-veh sa-kai vesh' fam dvun alive, heh she went pla' tor wuh kelek heh hayal-tor ne' cheerfully tor wuh pasu heh ate. Wuh kushel flew maf heh alighted fi' wuh kelek t' wuh goldsmith heh began tor uralau: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; she laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' wuh goldsmith vesh' svi' ish-veh zup-shal tor wuh pi-maat-tukh naf-elakh, lu au puzhu-tor wuh song t' wuh kushel fi' ish-veh kamu. Au nahp ish-veh ni vaksurik ik au prah abru heh sahr-tor si', heh u' au tuhsau wuh threshold au pakik veh t' ish-veh slippers. Tonk'peh au sahr-tor fi' vi' wuh svitan t' wuh yut, k' wuh slipper fi' veh ash'ya heh wuh ash'ai fi' wuh vath; au fam dvun had fi' ish-veh apron, heh fam dvun meskarau wuh pi-maat-tukh naf-elakh heh wuh pincers svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh ni au lam-tor gazing abru na' wuh kushel, du' wuh yel sarlah shining brightly ne' fi' wuh yut. 'kushel, ' au leralmin-tor, 'uf beautifully du uralau! Uralau me ik song va'ashiv.' 'nay, ' leralmin-tor wuh kushel, 'i ri tor uralau dah'wak na' nothing. Mazhiv-kur-tor ik pi-maat-tukh naf-elakh, heh i dungi uralau ish-veh du va'ashiv.' 'la' nam-tor wuh naf-elakh, nem-tor ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh goldsmith. 'goh uralau me ik va'ashiv.' wuh kushel flew ne' heh nem-tor wuh pi-maat-tukh naf-elakh svi' ish-veh gas'rak spahk, heh yi au alighted va'ashiv svi' khom t' wuh goldsmith heh sang: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; she laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' yi au flew maf, heh settled fi' wuh kamu t' wuh shoemaker's kelek heh sang: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; she laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' wuh shoemaker puzhu-tor ish-veh, heh au spen-tor abru heh sahr-tor si' svi' ish-veh sav'el-sleeves, heh lam-tor looking abru na' wuh kushel fi' wuh kamu k' ish-veh el'ru abru' ish-veh bezhun tor potau himself s' hasu blinded k' wuh yel. 'kushel, ' au leralmin-tor, 'uf beautifully du uralau!' yi au puvutau k'fai wuh svep tor ish-veh ko-telsu: 'ko-telsu, sasarlah; la' nam-tor wuh kushel, sarlah heh glazhau na' ish-veh heh zhu-tor uf beautifully ish-veh uralau.' yi au puvutau ish-veh ko-fu heh wuh kanu, yi wuh apprentices, ko-kan heh sa-kan, heh au ek' sahr-tor abru wuh yut tor glazhau na' wuh kushel, heh gla-tor uf splendid ish-veh vesh' k' its yon-kur heh yar-kur kan, heh its talu spo' burnished pi-maat-tukh, heh bezhun spo' dahkuh ugelik yel svi' its patam. 'kushel, ' leralmin-tor wuh shoemaker, 'uralau me ik song va'ashiv.' 'nay, ' kilko-tor wuh kushel, 'i ri tor uralau dah'wak na' nothing; du bolau mazhiv-kur-tor me vel.' 'ko-telsu, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'hal-tor vi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal; fi' wuh upper nef du dungi gla-tor wuh shif t' yon-kur ash'el; katau au tor me.' wuh ko-telsu went svi' heh zaprah wuh ash'el. 'tra', kushel, ' leralmin-tor wuh shoemaker, 'i' uralau me ik song va'ashiv.' wuh kushel flew ne' heh nem-tor wuh yon-kur ash'el svi' ish-veh losrak spahk, heh yi au went pla' tor wuh kamu heh sang: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; she laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' lu au had shahtau, au flew maf. Au had wuh naf-elakh svi' ish-veh gas'rak spahk heh wuh ash'el svi' ish-veh losrak, heh au flew gas'rak maf tor wuh mill, heh wuh mill went 'click clack, click clack, click clack.' svi'udish wuh mill vesh' dah-leh t' wuh miller's sasu hewing wuh kov, heh u' au went 'hick hack, hick hack, hick hack, ' wuh mill went 'click clack, click clack, click clack.' wuh kushel settled fi' wuh lime-lap svi' khom t' wuh mill heh sang: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; yi veh t' wuh sasu losrak ska', t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; dahkuh weht sasu losrak ska' heh shroi, t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; yi kehkuh weht losrak ska', she laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti i' tra' vesh' goh ohkuh na' ar'kadan, ne'rak heh i' goh kaukuh, wuh juniper-lap. Heh i' goh veh, kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' yi au glazhau abru heh wuh kim-shah veh had losrak ska' ar'kadan. 'kushel, ' au leralmin-tor, 'ra wuh vaksurik song ik nam-tor du uralau! Kal-tor me zhu-tor ish-veh nuh'; uralau ish-veh va'ashiv.' 'nay, ' kilko-tor wuh kushel, 'i ri tor uralau dah'wak na' nothing; mazhiv-kur-tor me ik millstone, heh i dungi uralau ish-veh va'ashiv.' 'kuv ish-veh belonged tor me sa'awek, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'du dang ma ish-veh.' 'ha, ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath: 'kuv au dungi uralau va'ashiv, au mokuhlek ma ish-veh.' wuh kushel sarlah ne', heh ek' wuh dah-leh millers eku tor heh abertau abru wuh kov k' wuh ha-zehl; yi wuh kushel shitau ish-veh patam k'fai wuh razh heh nem-tor wuh kov pauk ish-veh talu spo' wuh hmoi'neks, heh flew pla' k' ish-veh tor wuh lap heh sang-- 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; she laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' heh lu au had shahtau ish-veh song, au sak-tor ish-veh rala, heh k' wuh naf-elakh svi' ish-veh gas'rak spahk, wuh ash'el svi' ish-veh losrak, heh wuh millstone pauk ish-veh talu, au flew gas'rak maf tor ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek. Wuh sa-mekh, wuh ko-mekh, heh pi' marleen vesh' having ish-veh aru-yem. 'uf lighthearted i olau, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'ni sanoi heh cheerful.' 'heh i, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-mekh, 'i olau ni uneasy, u' kuv wuh ras rahm-sahriv vesh' coming.' tonk'peh pi' marleen hayal-tor heh wept heh wept. Yi wuh kushel sarlah hashan na' wuh kelek heh settled fi' wuh kamu. 'i tor olau ni kunli, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'heh uf beautifully wuh yel min-tor; i olau aishan u' kuv i vesh' going tor gla-tor wuh hinek t'hy'la va'ashiv.' 'ah!' leralmin-tor wuh ko-telsu, 'heh i am ni bosh t' flakosh heh uneasiness ik t'nash-veh zud chatter, heh i olau u' kuv tra' vesh' wuh yon svi' t'nash-veh os-khaf-mev, ' heh she tore tu'ash ish-veh sai-vel; heh ek' wuh du' pi' marleen hayal-tor svi' wuh teruk heh wept, heh wuh math fi' ish-veh mal-nef vesh' masupik k' ish-veh bezhun-masu. Wuh kushel i' flew tor wuh juniper-lap heh began uralaun: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; wuh ko-mekh ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun heh ish-veh kaluk, ik she lau gla-tor heh zhu-tor nothing, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh roaring ralash svi' ish-veh kaluk spo' ik t' wuh khrashik sahriv, heh svi' ish-veh bezhun wuh yontau heh flashing spo' igen-wesh: t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; 'glazhau, ko-mekh, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'na' wuh vaksurik kushel ik nam-tor uralaun ni magnificently; heh uf lamekh heh ugelik wuh yel nam-tor, heh ra wuh delicious scent t' bar-kas svi' wuh sov!' t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; yi pi' marleen laid ish-veh patam ne' fi' ish-veh mal-nef heh sobbed. 'i bolau hal-tor s'udish heh gla-tor wuh kushel nearer, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu. 'ah, ri tor hal-tor!' maf-tor wuh ko-telsu. 'i olau u' kuv wuh bosh kelek vesh' svi' yai!' tonk'peh wuh sasu went si' heh glazhau na' wuh kushel. She laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' k' ik wuh kushel kal-tor tevan wuh pi-maat-tukh naf-elakh, heh ish-veh tevan-tor aishan pauk wuh sasu's talu, ni ik ish-veh fitted ish-veh exactly. Au went svi'udish, heh leralmin-tor, 'gla-tor, ra wuh splendid kushel ik nam-tor; au has putan-tor me nash vaksurik pi-maat-tukh naf-elakh, heh glazhau ni vaksurik himself.' tonk'peh wuh ko-telsu vesh' svi' such pthak heh trouble, ik she tevan-tor fi' wuh lan-tol, heh ish-veh taik tevan-tor s' ish-veh patam. Yi wuh kushel began va'ashiv: 't'nash-veh ko-mekh pustau ish-veh pi' sa-fu; 'ah me!' maf-tor wuh ko-telsu, 'kuv i vesh' tonk'peh wuh thousand ash'ya ne'rak wuh terra, ik i lau ri zhu-tor ik song.' t'nash-veh sa-mekh grieved lu i vesh' hal-tor; yi wuh kosu tevan-tor ne' va'ashiv u' kuv tevik. T'nash-veh ko-kai ashau me buhfik t' ek'; 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor pi' marleen, 'i dungi hal-tor si' nuh' heh gla-tor kuv wuh kushel dungi mazhiv-kur-tor me sovek-vel.' ni she went si'. She laid ish-veh kerchief abru' me, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh hinek ik au lau ti heh au threw ne' wuh ash'el tor ish-veh, ne'rak wuh juniper-lap kywitt, kywitt, ra wuh vaksurik kushel am i!' heh she i' olau ved kunli heh lighthearted; she shitau fi' wuh ash'el heh tam-tor heh spen-tor pa' svi' au. 'i vesh' ni miserable, ' she leralmin-tor, 'lu i sasarlah, tonk'peh ik has ek' be' dvun-tor maf; ik nam-tor indeed wuh splendid kushel, heh au has putan-tor me wuh shif t' yon-kur ash'el.' wuh ko-telsu sprang abru, k' ish-veh isachya standing si' s' ish-veh patam spo' yai t' yon. 'yi i dungi hal-tor si' nuh', ' she leralmin-tor, 'heh gla-tor kuv ish-veh dungi lighten t'nash-veh misery, na' i olau u' kuv wuh panu vesh' coming tor wuh shaht.' tonk'peh u' she tuhsau wuh threshold, tevul! Wuh kushel threw wuh millstone ne' fi' ish-veh patam, heh she vesh' plesh-tor tor tevakh. Wuh sa-mekh heh pi' marleen puzhu-tor wuh ralash heh sahr-tor si', tonk'peh au goh gla-tor mist heh yai heh yon rising s' wuh gla-tor, heh lu aifa had be' dvun-tor, tra' lam-tor wuh pi' sa-kai, heh au nem-tor wuh sa-mekh heh pi' marleen k' wuh el'ru; yi au ek' rehkuh rejoiced, heh went svi'udish teretuhr heh hayal-tor ne' tor ish-veh aru-yem heh ate. Wuh turnip tra' vesh' dahkuh sa-kai vi vesh' fi' ask'ersu; wuh veh vesh' don-ka heh wuh vath ri donku-tor. Wuh ri donku-tor sasu nahp au would ar'kadan tor weh-rom himself; ni, pulling ska' ish-veh yon-kur tor-pal, au became wuh bahsu, heh hil-tor ish-veh solektra muhl, heh sowed turnips. Lu wuh nei sarlah abru, tra' vesh' veh kastik bigger do ek' wuh shom; heh ish-veh potau getting larger heh larger, heh seemed u' kuv ish-veh would worla cease growing; ni ik ish-veh lau ma vesh' puvutau wuh prince t' turnips na' tra' worla vesh' such wuh veh gla-tor fa', heh worla dungi va'ashiv. Na' kim-shah ish-veh vesh' ni suk' ik ish-veh boshau wuh hal, heh dahkuh oxen kupi hardly bes-tor ish-veh; heh wuh bahsu fai-tor ri ra svi' wuh panu tor tor k' ish-veh, il whether ish-veh would nam-tor wuh kudaya il wuh curse tor ish-veh. Veh gad au leralmin-tor tor himself, 'ra dungau i tor k' ish-veh? Kuv i makau ish-veh, ish-veh dungi katau rai weht do wuh'ashiv; heh na' eating, wuh pi' turnips nam-tor weh-rom do nash; wuh buhfik vel sos'eh nam-tor tor lesh ish-veh heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru u' wuh ulidar t' respect.' yi au yoked ish-veh oxen, heh drew wuh turnip tor wuh kelek, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru. 'ra wuh wonderful vel!' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru; 'ki'gla-tor nash-veh wehk flekh vel, tonk'peh such wuh stislak u' nash i worla gla-tor. Wilat did du prah wuh nei? Il nam-tor ish-veh goh ish-veh rom kunli? Kuv ni, du nam-tor wuh yeht kan t' fortune.' 'ah, rai!' kilko-tor wuh bahsu, 'i am rai kan t' fortune; i am wuh ri donku-tor ask'ersu, vi worla kupi prah hiyet tor ha-tor fi-tor; ni i laid aside t'nash-veh yon-kur tor-pal, heh eku tor ar'kadan, tilling wuh solektra. I ma wuh sa-kai, vi nam-tor don-ka, heh ish-veh majesty fai-tor ish-veh muhl, heh ek' wuh panu fai-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh fai'ei i am ri donku-tor, kanok-veh yen-tor me.' wuh sa-te'kru yi nem-tor pity fi' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'du dungau nam-tor ri donku-tor rai longer. I dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du ni mau ik du dungau nam-tor kauk richer do ish-veh sa-kai.' yi au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh pi-maat-tukh heh shasol heh patreitau, heh tor ish-veh ni don-ka ik ish-veh sa-kai's fortune kupi mokov nam-tor tcok'at k' ish-veh. Lu wuh sa-kai puzhu-tor t' ek' nash, heh uf wuh turnip had tor wuh bahsu ni don-ka, au envied ish-veh sorely, heh bethought himself uf au kupi contrive tor prah wuh ka rom fortune na' himself. However, au satalau tor khartau weht cleverly do ish-veh sa-kai, heh prah teretuhr wuh don-ka la' t' pi-maat-tukh heh tok-ti jarel na' wuh sa-te'kru; heh nahp au bolau ma wuh mau larger mazhiv-kur svi' fun; na' kuv ish-veh sa-kai had poprah ni mau na' goh wuh turnip, ra bolau ish-veh la' nam-tor don? Wuh sa-te'kru nem-tor wuh mazhiv-kur maut graciously, heh leralmin-tor au fai-tor ri ra tor mazhiv-kur-tor svi' fun weht taluhk heh wonderful do wuh lo'uk turnip; ni wuh ask'ersu vesh' punekwitau tor shitau ish-veh vi' wuh hal, heh zaseshau ish-veh ha-kel k' ish-veh. Lu au pulau ha-kel, au fai-tor ri fi-tor ik tor krau ish-veh reshan heh spite; heh na' wu-vath wicked nahp sarlah vi' ish-veh patam, heh au resolved tor stau ish-veh sa-kai. Ni au hired ein villains tor riyeht-staya ish-veh; heh having shown au wilat tor ti svi' ambush, au went tor ish-veh sa-kai, heh leralmin-tor, 'tal-kam sa-kai, i ma afer-tor wuh ipik treasure; kal-tor etek hal-tor heh hil-tor ish-veh abru, heh thresh ish-veh svi' etek.' wuh vath had rai suspicions t' ish-veh roguery: ni au went si' teretuhr, heh u' au vesh' travelling bi', wuh murderers rushed si' fi-tor ish-veh, bound ish-veh, heh vesh' going tor geldau ish-veh fi' wuh lap. Tonk'peh whilst au vesh' getting ek' pok, au puzhu-tor wuh sahr-tor t' wuh jarel na' wuh ir, if ni koltha au ik au kwitau ish-veh prisoner talu heh tipan teretuhr vi' wuh sa'haf, heh swung ish-veh abru k' wuh elakh tor wuh lap, wilat au losrak ish-veh dangling, heh sahr-tor maf. Meantime au ar'kada heh ar'kada maf, till au tor wuh razh suk hiyet tor shitau si' ish-veh patam. Lu wuh horseman sarlah abru, au skan-tor tor nam-tor wuh orensu, wuh merry katravahsu, vi vesh' journeying bi' fi' ish-veh nag, heh uralaun u' au went. U' ak u' wuh sasu svi' wuh sa'haf gla-tor ish-veh be' dvun-tor ne' wuh lap, au lit'dhae, 'rom asal! Rom asal tor thee, t'nash-veh t'hy'la!' wuh orensu glazhau pa' kanok-wilat; heh seeing kling, heh ri fai-tor wilat wuh spes sarlah s', lit'dhae, 'vi calls me?' yi wuh sasu svi' wuh lap kilko-tor, 'abertau abru thine bezhun, na' behold la' i hayal-tor svi' wuh sa'haf t' kau; la' ma i, svi' wuh pen wak, oren-tor lo'uk heh wondrous vel. Tcok'at tor nash ku-san, ek' wuh learning t' wuh shi'oren nam-tor u' herbosh sov. Wuh pi' longer, heh i dungau fai-tor ek' ik sasu mokuhlek fai-tor, heh dungau sarlah forth wiser do wuh wisest t' mankind. La' i discern wuh glat heh dvunel t' wuh heavens heh wuh yel; wuh tor-gav ik tash wuh salan; wuh su'etek t' wuh mazhiv fi' wuh seashore; wuh hakausu t' wuh has-bosh; wuh virtues t' ek' simples, t' kushel, heh t' taluhk kov. Wert thou tonk'peh wuh'wak la', t'nash-veh t'hy'la, hi wouldst olau heh sha' wuh tepul t' fai-tukh. Wuh orensu shroi tor ek' nash heh wondered mau; na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor, 'blessed nam-tor wuh gad heh wadan lu i afer-tor du; fam yehat du contrive tor kal-tor me vi' wuh sa'haf na' wuh pi' du'?' yi wuh vath kilko-tor, u' kuv maut unwillingly, 'wuh pi' ret i lau kal-tor thee tor hayal-tor la', kuv thou wilt reward me muhl heh entreat me kindly; tonk'peh thou bolau tarry wi wuh wadan ne', till i ma oren-tor ein pi' tukh ik nam-tor wi ri-fainu tor me.' ni wuh orensu hayal-tor himself ne' heh bek-tor wuh du'; tonk'peh wuh wak geldau ras fi-tor ish-veh, heh au eit'jae earnestly ik au lau she-tor forthwith, na' ish-veh mag na' fai-tukh vesh' lo'uk. Yi wuh vath pretended tor mazhiv-kur-tor yut, heh leralmin-tor, 'thou bolau kal-tor wuh sa'haf t' kau tev-tor, k' untying yonder elakh, heh yi thou shalt svi-tor.' ni wuh orensu kal-tor ish-veh ne', tu'ash wuh sa'haf, heh eku ish-veh elik. 'i' yi, ' maf-tor au, 'kal-tor me she-tor sahris.' u' au began tor shitau himself vi' wuh sa'haf timut wuh'rak, 'bek-tor wuh du', ' leralmin-tor wuh bahsu, 'ik nam-tor ri wuh yut.' yi au kwitau ish-veh svi' patam wuh'rak, tied abru wuh sa'haf, heh ak swung abru wuh searcher po' kau dangling svi' wuh sov. 'uf nam-tor ish-veh k' thee, t'hy'la?' leralmin-tor au, 'dost thou ri olau ik kau sarlah unto thee? Shom tra' svi' sochya, till thou tanaf wuh wiser sasu do thou wert.' ni taran, au sahr-tor ska' fi' wuh orensu's nag, heh losrak wuh ri donku-tor katravahsu tor hoknau kau till somebody dang sarlah heh kal-tor ish-veh ne'. Clever hans wuh ko-mekh t' hans leralmin-tor: 'whither maf, hans?' hans kilko-tor: 'tor gretel.' 'kloshah muhl, hans.' 'oh, i'll kloshah muhl. Goodbye, ko-mekh.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans sarlah tor gretel. 'rom gad, gretel.' 'rom gad, hans. Ra tor du katau ik nam-tor rom?' 'i katau nothing, i aitlun ki' vel putan-tor me.' gretel presents hans k' wuh og-lum, hans leralmin-tor: 'goodbye, gretel.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans nem-tor wuh og-lum, terpau ish-veh vi' wuh hay-hal, heh zahal-tor wuh hal ha-kel. 'rom khru, ko-mekh.' 'rom khru, hans. Wilat ma du vesh'?' 'k' gretel.' 'ra did du nem-tor ish-veh?' 'nem-tor nothing; had vel putan-tor me.' 'ra did gretel mazhiv-kur-tor du?' 'mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh og-lum.' 'wilat nam-tor wuh og-lum, hans?' 'terpau svi' wuh hay-hal.' 'ik vesh' has-bosh ovsoh, hans. Du dang ma terpau wuh og-lum svi' ish-veh sleeve.' 'worla kashek, i'll tor weh-rom thurai wak.' 'whither maf, hans?' 'tor gretel, ko-mekh.' 'kloshah muhl, hans.' 'oh, i'll kloshah muhl. Goodbye, ko-mekh.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans sarlah tor gretel. 'rom gad, gretel.' 'rom gad, hans. Ra tor du katau ik nam-tor rom?' 'i katau nothing. I aitlun ki' vel putan-tor tor me.' gretel presents hans k' wuh lipau. 'goodbye, gretel.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans nem-tor wuh lipau, terpau ish-veh svi' ish-veh sleeve, heh hal-tor ha-kel. 'rom khru, ko-mekh.' 'rom khru, hans. Wilat ma du vesh'?' 'k' gretel.' ra did du nem-tor ish-veh?' 'nem-tor ish-veh nothing, she mazhiv-kur-tor me vel.' 'ra did gretel mazhiv-kur-tor du?' 'mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh lipau.' 'wilat nam-tor wuh lipau, hans?' 'terpau svi' t'nash-veh sleeve.' 'ik's has-bosh ovsoh, hans, du dang ma shitau wuh lipau svi' ish-veh abru'lik.' 'worla kashek, dungi tor weh-rom thurai wak.' 'whither maf, hans?' 'tor gretel, ko-mekh.' 'kloshah muhl, hans.' 'oh, i'll kloshah muhl. Goodbye, ko-mekh.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans sarlah tor gretel. 'rom gad, gretel.' 'rom gad, hans. Ra rom vel tor du katau?' 'i katau nothing, i aitlun vel putan-tor me.' gretel presents hans k' wuh nu'ri vralt. 'goodbye, gretel.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans nem-tor wuh vralt, ties its mal, heh shitau ish-veh svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Lu au prah ha-kel ish-veh nam-tor suffocated. 'rom khru, ko-mekh.' 'rom khru, hans. Wilat ma du vesh'?' 'k' gretel.' 'ra did du nem-tor ish-veh?' 'nem-tor nothing, she mazhiv-kur-tor me vel.' 'ra did gretel mazhiv-kur-tor du?' 'she mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh vralt.' 'wilat nam-tor wuh vralt, hans?' 'shitau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh abru'lik.' 'ik vesh' has-bosh ovsoh, hans, du dang ma shitau wuh man-elakh pauk wuh vralt's talu.' 'worla kashek, dungi tor weh-rom thurai wak.' 'whither maf, hans?' 'tor gretel, ko-mekh.' 'kloshah muhl, hans.' 'oh, i'll kloshah muhl. Goodbye, ko-mekh.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans sarlah tor gretel. 'rom gad, gretel.' 'rom gad, hans. Ra rom vel tor du katau?' 'i katau nothing, i aitlun vel putan-tor me.' gretel presents hans k' wuh krus t' bacon. 'goodbye, gretel.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans nem-tor wuh bacon, ties ish-veh tor wuh man-elakh, heh zaseshau ish-veh maf za' ish-veh. Wuh dogs sarlah heh katau wuh bacon. Lu au prah ha-kel, au has wuh man-elakh svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh tra' nam-tor rai longer sovek-vel hanging fi' tor ish-veh. 'rom khru, ko-mekh.' 'rom khru, hans. Wilat ma du vesh'?' 'k' gretel.' 'ra did du nem-tor ish-veh?' 'i nem-tor ish-veh nothing, she mazhiv-kur-tor me vel.' 'ra did gretel mazhiv-kur-tor du?' 'mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh zeshau t' bacon.' 'wilat nam-tor wuh bacon, hans?' 'i tied ish-veh tor wuh man-elakh, katau ish-veh ha-kel, dogs nem-tor ish-veh.' 'ik vesh' has-bosh ovsoh, hans, du dang ma lesh wuh bacon fi' ish-veh patam.' 'worla kashek, dungi tor weh-rom thurai wak.' 'whither maf, hans?' 'tor gretel, ko-mekh.' 'kloshah muhl, hans.' 'i'll kloshah muhl. Goodbye, ko-mekh.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans sarlah tor gretel. 'rom gad, gretel.' 'rom gad, hans, ra rom vel tor du katau?' 'i katau nothing, tonk'peh would ma vel putan-tor.' gretel presents hans k' wuh vaukh. 'goodbye, gretel.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans nem-tor wuh vaukh, shitau ish-veh fi' ish-veh patam, heh wuh vaukh kicks ish-veh limuk. 'rom khru, ko-mekh.' 'rom khru, hans. Wilat ma du vesh'?' 'k' gretel.' 'ra did du nem-tor ish-veh?' 'i nem-tor nothing, tonk'peh had vel putan-tor me.' 'ra did gretel mazhiv-kur-tor du?' 'wuh vaukh.' 'wilat ma du wuh vaukh, hans?' 'i eku ish-veh fi' t'nash-veh patam heh ish-veh kicked t'nash-veh limuk.' 'ik vesh' has-bosh ovsoh, hans, du dang ma pufulag-tor wuh vaukh, heh shitau ish-veh svi' wuh stall.' 'worla kashek, dungi tor weh-rom thurai wak.' 'whither maf, hans?' 'tor gretel, ko-mekh.' 'kloshah muhl, hans.' 'i'll kloshah muhl. Goodbye, ko-mekh.' 'goodbye, hans.' hans sarlah tor gretel. 'rom gad, gretel.' 'rom gad, hans. Ra rom vel tor du katau?' 'i katau nothing, tonk'peh would ma vel putan-tor.' gretel leralmin-tor tor hans: 'i dungi hal-tor k' du.' hans nem-tor gretel, ties ish-veh tor wuh man-elakh, fulag-tor ish-veh tor wuh rack, heh binds ish-veh sahris. Yi hans hal-tor tor ish-veh ko-mekh. 'rom khru, ko-mekh.' 'rom khru, hans. Wilat ma du vesh'?' 'k' gretel.' 'ra did du nem-tor ish-veh?' 'i nem-tor ish-veh nothing.' 'ra did gretel mazhiv-kur-tor du?' 'she mazhiv-kur-tor me nothing, sarlah ish-veh k' me.' 'wilat ma du losrak gretel?' 'i pufulag-tor ish-veh k' wuh man-elakh, tied ish-veh tor wuh rack, heh scattered ein yar na' ish-veh.' 'ik vesh' has-bosh ovsoh, hans, du dang ma vishizhau friendly bezhun fi' ish-veh.' 'worla kashek, dungi tor weh-rom.' hans went vi' wuh tihet, tresahk si' ek' wuh vaukh' heh sheep's bezhun, heh threw au svi' gretel's limuk. Yi gretel became reshnek, tore herself thal heh sahr-tor maf, heh vesh' rai longer wuh bride t' hans. Wuh rehkuh gen-lis wuh aged tum-tor wuh'wak ha-tor svi' switzerland, vi had wuh goh sa-fu, tonk'peh au vesh' stupid, heh kupi oren-tor nothing. Yi leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh: 'hark du, t'nash-veh sa-fu, ar'kadan u' i dungi i mokuhlek prah nothing vi' ish-veh patam. Du bolau hal-tor s' hence, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du vi' wuh tun t' wuh u'thet trensu, vi dungau gla-tor ra au mokuhlek tor k' du.' wuh youth vesh' satau vi' wuh flekh kahr, heh hafau wuh bosh tevun k' wuh trensu. Na' wuh shaht t' nash wak, sarlah ish-veh ha-kel va'ashiv, heh ish-veh sa-mekh ya'akash: 'i', t'nash-veh sa-fu, ra ma du oren-tor?' 'sa-mekh, i ma oren-tor ra wuh dogs leralmin lu au kas-wadi.' 's'haile ma mercy fi' etek!' maf-tor wuh sa-mekh; 'nam-tor ik ek' du ma oren-tor? I dungi satau du vi' wuh'ashiv kahr, tor wuh'ashiv trensu.' wuh youth vesh' taken thither, heh stayed wuh tevun k' nash trensu likewise. Lu sarlah ish-veh pla' wuh sa-mekh va'ashiv ya'akash: 't'nash-veh sa-fu, ra ma du oren-tor?' au kilko-tor: 'sa-mekh, i ma oren-tor ra wuh kushel leralmin.' yi wuh sa-mekh tevan-tor vi' wuh reshan heh leralmin-tor: 'oh, du pakik sasu, du ma spent wuh taluhk wak heh oren-tor nothing; nam-tor du ri kafusik tor saudau fa' t'nash-veh bezhun? I dungi satau du tor wuh wuh trensu, tonk'peh kuv du oren-tor nothing nash wak isha, i dungi rai longer nam-tor ish-veh sa-mekh.' wuh youth hafau wuh bosh tevun k' wuh wuh trensu isha, heh lu sarlah ish-veh ha-kel va'ashiv, heh ish-veh sa-mekh inquired: 't'nash-veh sa-fu, ra ma du oren-tor?' au kilko-tor: 'tal-kam sa-mekh, i ma nash tevun oren-tor ra wuh git'woa croak.' yi wuh sa-mekh tevan-tor vi' wuh danik furious reshan, sprang abru, puvutau ish-veh sutra thither, heh leralmin-tor: 'nash sasu nam-tor rai longer t'nash-veh sa-fu, i yetur ish-veh forth, heh a'fic du tor nem-tor ish-veh si' vi' wuh laptra, heh stau ish-veh.' au nem-tor ish-veh forth, tonk'peh lu au dang ma pustau ish-veh, au kupi ri tor ish-veh na' pity, heh kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, heh au tresahk wuh bezhun heh lahv s' wuh deer ik au lau lesh au tor wuh hinek sasu u' wuh token. Wuh youth czar-tor fi', heh po' ein wak sarlah tor wuh klomak wilat au eit'jae na' wuh mu-yor's lodging. 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh s'haile t' wuh castle, 'kuv du dungi be' dvun wuh mu-yor ne' tra' svi' wuh hinek kispek, hal-tor thither; tonk'peh i vikau du, ish-veh nam-tor na' wuh peril t' ish-veh ha'kiv, na' ish-veh nam-tor bosh t' kwai dogs, if kas-wadi heh vlut rik' stopping, heh na' ac'ruth wadan wuh sasu has tor nam-tor putan-tor tor au, ik au na' wuh'wak katau.' wuh bosh kahkrus vesh' svi' sorrow heh dismay fai'ei t' au, heh wi kling kupi tor sovek-vel tor pehkaya nash. Wuh youth, however, vesh' rik' pthak, heh leralmin-tor: 'aishan kal-tor me hal-tor ne' tor wuh barking dogs, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me vel ik i mokuhlek lehm tor au; au dungi tor nothing tor klau me.' u' au himself would ma ish-veh ni, au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ein yem-tukh na' wuh kwai animals, heh pufulag-tor ish-veh ne' tor wuh kispek. Lu au went svi'udish, wuh dogs did ri kas-wadi na' ish-veh, tonk'peh wagged ish-veh harr ved amicably pa' ish-veh, ate ra au eku fa' au, heh did ri dash-tor veh isachya t' ish-veh patam. Thurai asal, tor wuh astonishment t' kanok-veh, au sasarlah va'ashiv safe heh unharmed, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh s'haile t' wuh castle: 'wuh dogs ma revealed tor me, svi' ish-veh sha' gen-lis, po au dwell tra', heh katau ek'rasah fi' wuh solektra. Au nam-tor bewitched, heh nam-tor obliged tor paluntunau wuh lo'uk treasure if nam-tor ne' svi' wuh kispek, heh au mokuhlek ma rai shom abi' ish-veh nam-tor taken maf, heh i ma likewise oren-tor, s' ish-veh discourse, uf ik nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh.' yi ek' vi puzhu-tor nash rejoiced, heh wuh s'haile t' wuh castle leralmin-tor au would thanai ish-veh u' wuh sa-fu kuv au accomplished ish-veh successfully. Au went ne' va'ashiv, heh u' au fai-tor ra au had tor tor, au did ish-veh thoroughly, heh katau wuh tuf bosh t' pi-maat-tukh si' k' ish-veh. Wuh howling t' wuh kwai dogs vesh' henceforth puzhu-tor rai weht; au had sasaudau, heh wuh shasol vesh' el-tor s' wuh trouble. Po' ein wak au nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh patam ik au would haolvaya tor rome. Fi' wuh yut au be' dvun-tor k' wuh masu-kastra, svi' if wuh su'etek t' git'woa vesh' sitting croaking. Au shroi tor au, heh lu au became aware t' ra au vesh' taran, au grew maut thoughtful heh maf. Na' kim-shah au lasha svi' rome, wilat wuh pope had aishan tev-tor, heh tra' vesh' lo'uk vet among wuh cardinals u' tor ik au dang kru'minaakh u' ish-veh successor. Au na' wu-vath sep-wafikh ik wuh person dang nam-tor pudvel-tor u' pope vi dang nam-tor distinguished k' ein ekonik heh miraculous token. Heh aishan u' ik vesh' klopau fi', wuh nu'ri tum-tor svi-tor vi' wuh church, heh suddenly dahkuh izh-wan-kur doves flew fi' ish-veh tipan heh hafau sitting tra'. Wuh ecclesiastics recognized therein wuh token s' abru', heh ya'akash ish-veh fi' wuh gla-tor kuv au would nam-tor pope. Au vesh' undecided, heh fai-tor ri kuv au vesh' worthy t' nash, tonk'peh wuh doves counselled ish-veh tor tor ish-veh, heh na' wu-vath au leralmin-tor ha. Yi vesh' au anointed heh consecrated, heh thus vesh' fulfilled ra au had puzhu-tor s' wuh git'woa fi' ish-veh yut, if had ni dau ish-veh, ik au vesh' tor nam-tor ish-veh holiness wuh pope. Yi au had tor uralau wuh shivak, heh did ri fai-tor veh zhit t' ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh dahkuh doves hayal-tor continually fi' ish-veh tipan, heh leralmin-tor ish-veh ek' svi' ish-veh kaluk. Wuh fox heh wuh aushfa ish-veh pavesh-tor ik wuh aushfa ragel-tor wuh fox svi' wuh laptra, heh u' she nahp tor herself: 'au nam-tor clever heh bosh t' veshtaya, heh mau vam svi' wuh panu, ' she stariben tor ish-veh svi' wuh friendly yut. 'rom gad, tal-kam mr fox, uf nam-tor du? Uf nam-tor ek' k' du? Uf nam-tor du getting fi' svi' aifa lerash wak?' wuh fox, bosh t' ek' ves t' arrogance, glazhau na' wuh aushfa s' patam tor ash'ya, heh na' wuh akarshif did ri fai-tor whether au would mazhiv-kur-tor sovek kilko-srashiv il ri. Na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor: 'oh, du wretched hisahk-cleaner, du piebald duhsu, du k'avon aushfa-shi'ka'ree, ra mokuhlek du nam-tor thinking t'? Ma du wuh nak tor ya'akash uf i am getting fi'? Ra ma du oren-tor? Uf wehk arts tor du ken-tor?' 'i ken-tor tonk'peh veh, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa, modestly. 'ra tanaf nam-tor ik?' ya'akash wuh fox. 'lu wuh hounds nam-tor zahalik me, i mokuhlek sikar vi' wuh lap heh korsau myself.' 'nam-tor ik ek'?' leralmin-tor wuh fox. 'i am trensu t' wuh hundred arts, heh ma vi' wuh bargain wuh sackful t' cunning. Du tor me sorry na' du; sarlah k' me, i dungi saven-tor du uf sutra prah maf s' wuh hounds.' aishan yi sarlah wuh shi'ka'ree k' kehkuh dogs. Wuh aushfa sprang nimbly abru wuh lap, heh hayal-tor ne' na' wuh fik t' ish-veh, wilat wuh khlup heh motra ved ip-sut ish-veh. 'tu'ash ish-veh sa'haf, mr fox, tu'ash ish-veh sa'haf, ' maf-tor wuh aushfa tor ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh dogs had already seized ish-veh, heh vesh' holding ish-veh sahris. 'ah, mr fox, ' maf-tor wuh aushfa. 'du k' ish-veh hundred arts nam-tor losrak svi' wuh lurch! Had du vesh' kup tor qots'noi spo' me, du would ri ma pakik ish-veh ha'kiv.' wuh kehkuh clever sa-kai 'tal-kam kanu, ' leralmin-tor wuh ri donku-tor sasu tor ish-veh kehkuh sa-fu, 'i ma nothing tor mazhiv-kur-tor du; du bolau hal-tor si' vi' wuh eik panu heh ar'kadan ish-veh kunli. Palikau k' learning ein hali il wuh'ashiv, heh gla-tor uf du mokuhlek prah fi'.' ni wuh kehkuh sa-kai nem-tor ish-veh walking-terpau svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh pi' uzh'a'lek fi' ish-veh tipan, heh po' nufai-tor ish-veh sa-mekh goodbye, went ek' si' na' wuh temep teretuhr. Lu au had prah fi' ein yut sarlah au tor kehkuh crossways, tik leading tor wuh natya shasol. Yi wuh eldest leralmin-tor, 'la' etek bolau krus; tonk'peh nash gad kehkuh tevun etek dungi sarlah pla' tor nash gla-tor, heh svi' wuh meantime tik bolau ar'kadan ra au mokuhlek tor na' himself.' ni tik sa-kai went ish-veh yut; heh u' wuh eldest vesh' hastening fi' wuh sasu ragel-tor ish-veh, heh ya'akash ish-veh wilat au vesh' going, heh ra au aitlu. 'i am going tor ar'kadan t'nash-veh kunli svi' wuh panu, heh dang spo' tor palikau k' learning ein tanaf il trade, ' kilko-tor au. 'yi, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'hal-tor k' me, heh i dungi saven-tor du tor shetau wuh cunningest pi'tak ik ek'wak vesh'.' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath, 'ik nam-tor ri wuh trau calling, heh ra mokuhlek veh glazhau tor pinkau k' ish-veh svi' wuh shaht tonk'peh wuh geld-stau-nentu?' 'oh!' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'du bolaya ri pthak wuh geld-stau-nentu; na' i dungi goh saven-tor du tor vazgau ra dungi nam-tor rom zhagra: i meddle k' nothing tonk'peh ra kling else mokuhlek prah il tun sovek-vel pa', heh wilat kling mokuhlek talal du si'.' ni wuh nu'ri sasu sep-wafikh tor zahal-tor ish-veh trade, heh au ak gluvau himself ni clever, ik nothing kupi stron ish-veh ik au had wuh'wak eku ish-veh kashek fi-tor. Wuh dahr sa-kai isha ragel-tor wuh sasu, vi, lu au afer-tor si' ra au vesh' setting si' fi-tor, ya'akash ish-veh ra hali au tvai tor zahal-tor. 'i ri tor fai-tor wi, ' leralmin-tor au. 'yi sarlah k' me, heh nam-tor wuh yel-gazer. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh thol tanaf, na' nothing mokuhlek nam-tor ipik s' du, lu wuh'wak du ken-tor wuh yel.' wuh dotor sanoi ish-veh mau, heh au ak became such wuh skilful yel-gazer, ik lu au had dvin-tor si' ish-veh wak, heh aitlu tor trasha ish-veh trensu, au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh makh, heh leralmin-tor, 'k' nash du mokuhlek gla-tor ek' ik nam-tor be' dvun-tor svi' wuh igen heh fi' terra, heh nothing mokuhlek nam-tor ipik s' du.' wuh wuh sa-kai ragel-tor wuh huntsman, vi nem-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh, heh saven-tor ish-veh ni muhl ek' ik belonged tor hunting, ik au became maut clever svi' wuh hali t' wuh lapan; heh lu au losrak ish-veh trensu au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh kes-wun, heh leralmin-tor, 'whatever du pohshau na' k' nash kes-wun du dungi nam-tor sure tor kwul.' wuh youngest sa-kai likewise ragel-tor wuh sasu vi ya'akash ish-veh ra au istau tor tor. 'would ri du spo', ' leralmin-tor au, 'tor nam-tor wuh ogsu?' 'oh, rai!' leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri sasu; 'sitting tuhs-malik s' asal tor mu-yor, working pla'rak heh fa'rak k' wuh og-lum heh kushel, dungi worla saikhut me.' 'oh!' kilko-tor wuh sasu, 'ik nam-tor ri t'nash-veh wihfelau t' tailoring; sarlah k' me, heh du dungi oren-tor ved wuh'ashiv ves t' hali s' ik.' ri fai-tor ra weh-rom tor tor, sarlah ish-veh vi' wuh dotor, heh oren-tor tailoring s' wuh palikaya; heh lu au losrak ish-veh trensu, au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh og-lum, heh leralmin-tor, 'du mokuhlek og-tor sovek-vel k' nash, nam-tor ish-veh u' mos u' wuh yu-mur il u' lerash u' pishek; heh wuh joint dungi nam-tor ni tok-ti ik rai fenul dungi nam-tor gla-tor.' po' wuh ret t' kehkuh tevun, na' wuh wak sep-wafikh fi-tor, wuh kehkuh sa-kai ragel-tor na' wuh kehkuh tuhs-fau-yut; heh having welcomed tik vath, eku ska' na' ish-veh sa-mekh's ha-kel, wilat au var-tor ish-veh ek' ik had pavesh-tor tor au, heh uf tik had oren-tor ein hali. Yi, veh gad, u' au vesh' sitting fa' wuh kelek ne' wuh maut pid lap, wuh sa-mekh leralmin-tor, 'i dang spo' tor ar'kadan ra tik t' du mokuhlek tor svi' nash yut.' ni au glazhau abru, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh dahr sa-fu, 'na' wuh fik t' nash lap tra' nam-tor wuh chaffinch's ha-kel; var-tor me uf wehk yu-mur tra' nam-tor svi' ish-veh.' wuh yel-gazer nem-tor ish-veh makh, glazhau abru, heh leralmin-tor, 'kaukuh.' 'i', ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh tor wuh eldest sa-fu, 'nem-tor maf wuh yu-mur rik' letting wuh kushel ik nam-tor sitting fi-tor au heh hatching au fai-tor sovek-vel t' ra du nam-tor doing.' ni wuh cunning pi'tak sasu-tor abru wuh lap, heh katau maf tor ish-veh sa-mekh wuh kaukuh yu-mur s' ne' wuh kushel; heh ish-veh worla gla-tor il olau ra au vesh' doing, tonk'peh potau sitting fi' na' its ease. Yi wuh sa-mekh nem-tor wuh yu-mur, heh shitau veh fi' tik teruk t' wuh pasu, heh wuh fifth svi' wuh svitan, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh huntsman, 'tresahk ek' wuh yu-mur svi' dahkuh krus na' veh pohshaya.' wuh huntsman nem-tor abru ish-veh kes-wun, heh na' veh pohshaya kwul-tor ek' wuh kaukuh yu-mur u' ish-veh sa-mekh istau. 'i' sarlah ish-veh da-tor, ' leralmin-tor au tor wuh nu'ri ogsu; 'og-tor wuh yu-mur heh wuh nu'ri kushel svi' au teretuhr va'ashiv, ni neatly ik wuh pohshaya dungau ma ovsoh au rai klau.' yi wuh ogsu nem-tor ish-veh og-lum, heh og-tor wuh yu-mur u' au vesh' var-tor; heh lu au had ovsoh, wuh pi'tak vesh' satau tor nem-tor au pla' tor wuh ha-kel, heh shitau au ne' wuh kushel rik' its fai-tor ish-veh. Yi she went fi' sitting, heh hatched au: heh svi' wuh zamu gad au ukrau si', heh had goh wuh pi' yon-kur wesh mes' ish-veh talu, wilat wuh ogsu had sewn au teretuhr. 'muhl ovsoh, sa-fu!' leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu; 'du ma tor rom nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh wak, heh oren-tor vel don wuh fai-tor; tonk'peh i am sure i ri tor fai-tor if ought ki' wuh prize. Oh, ik wuh wak lau ak sarlah na' du tor da-tor ish-veh renkup'es tor ein khrosahp!' ri wu po' nash tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk bustle svi' wuh shasol; na' wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu had vesh' lesh ska' k' wuh mighty dragon, heh wuh sa-te'kru pula'tusa abru' ish-veh pak gad heh mu-yor, heh tor ish-veh fainu ik whoever katau ish-veh pla' tor ish-veh dang ma ish-veh na' wuh ko-telsu. Yi wuh kehkuh sa-kai leralmin-tor tor tik vath, 'la' nam-tor wuh pavesh na' etek; kal-tor etek ar'kadan ra etek mokuhlek tor.' heh au sep-wafikh tor gla-tor whether au kupi ri eku wuh princess elik. 'i dungi ak talal si' wilat she nam-tor, however, ' leralmin-tor wuh yel-gazer, u' au glazhau k'fai ish-veh makh; heh au ak lit'dhae, 'i gla-tor ish-veh afar ska', sitting fi-tor wuh kov svi' wuh masutra, heh i mokuhlek zamasu wuh dragon beyik, guarding ish-veh.' yi au went tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh ya'akash na' wuh hali na' himself heh ish-veh sa-kai; heh au masu-halovau teretuhr abru' wuh masutra, till sarlah au tor wuh gas'rak shi. Tra' au afer-tor wuh princess sitting, u' wuh yel-gazer had leralmin-tor, fi' wuh kov; heh wuh dragon vesh' lying asleep, k' ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh lap. 'i dare ri pohshau na' ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman, 'na' i dang stau wuh vaksurik nu'ri t'sai isha.' 'yi i dungi ar'kadan t'nash-veh renkup'es, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi'tak, heh went heh vazgau ish-veh maf s' ne' wuh dragon, ni quietly heh kogavik ik wuh beast did ri fai-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh went fi' snoring. Yi maf au hastened k' ish-veh bosh t' mak svi' ish-veh masu-hali na' wuh hali; tonk'peh ak sarlah wuh dragon roaring za' au k'fai wuh sov; na' au awoke heh din-tor wuh princess. Tonk'peh lu au prah abru' wuh masu-hali, heh aitlu tor pounce fi-tor au heh lesh ska' wuh princess, wuh huntsman nem-tor abru ish-veh kes-wun heh pohshaya ish-veh zehik k'fai wuh khaf-spol ni ik au tevan-tor ne' tevik. Au vesh' fam dvun ri safe; na' au vesh' such wuh lo'uk beast ik svi' ish-veh tevan au overset wuh masu-hali, heh au had tor mahal-tor svi' wuh tu'ash masutra fi-tor wuh zamu planks. Ni wuh ogsu nem-tor ish-veh og-lum, heh k' wuh zamu suk og shitau ein t' wuh planks teretuhr; heh au hayal-tor ne' fi-tor aifa, heh masu-halovau pa' heh hoknau abru ek' krus t' wuh masu-hali; heh yi tacked au teretuhr ni sahris ik wuh masu-hali vesh' ak pok, heh au yi pulau wuh hali heh prah ha-kel safe. Lu au had katau ha-kel wuh princess tor ish-veh sa-mekh, tra' vesh' lo'uk rejoicing; heh au leralmin-tor tor wuh kehkuh sa-kai, 'veh t' du dungau marry ish-veh, tonk'peh du bolau settle svi' yourselves if ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor.' yi tra' arose wuh quarrel svi' au; heh wuh yel-gazer leralmin-tor, 'kuv i had ri afer-tor wuh princess si', ek' ish-veh renkup'es would ma vesh' t' rai nam-tor-tor; therefore she ought tor nam-tor t'nash-veh.' 'ish-veh seeing ish-veh would ma vesh' t' rai nam-tor-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi'tak, 'kuv i had ri taken ish-veh maf s' wuh dragon; therefore she ought tor nam-tor t'nash-veh.' 'rai, she nam-tor t'nash-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman; 'na' kuv i had ri pustau wuh dragon, au would, po' ek', ma torn du heh wuh princess vi' krus.' 'heh kuv i had ri sewn wuh masu-hali teretuhr va'ashiv, ' leralmin-tor wuh ogsu, 'du would ek' ma vesh' mastevau, therefore she nam-tor t'nash-veh.' yi wuh sa-te'kru shitau svi' wuh zhit, heh leralmin-tor, 'tik t' du nam-tor gas'rak; heh u' ek' fam yehat ma wuh nu'ri t'sai, wuh buhfik yut nam-tor na' neither t' du ki' ish-veh: na' wuh yeht'es nam-tor, tra' nam-tor somebody she tishau wuh lo'uk deal weh-rom. Tonk'peh tor tor abru na' ish-veh pak, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor tik t' du, u' wuh reward na' ish-veh renkup'es, ulef wuh kingdom.' ni wuh sa-kai sep-wafikh ik nash dotor would nam-tor mau weh-rom do either quarrelling il marrying wuh t'sai vi had rai kashek ki' au. Heh wuh sa-te'kru yi mazhiv-kur-tor tor tik ulef wuh kingdom, u' au had leralmin-tor; heh au ha-tor maut kunling wuh shom t' ish-veh gad, heh nem-tor rom tun t' ish-veh sa-mekh; heh somebody nem-tor weh-rom tun t' wuh nu'ri t'sai, do tor kal-tor either wuh dragon il veh t' wuh craftsmen ma ish-veh va'ashiv. Lily heh wuh lion wuh merchant, vi had rehkuh daughters, vesh' wuh'wak setting si' fi-tor wuh halovaya; tonk'peh fa' au went au ya'akash tik ko-fu ra mazhiv-kur au dang katau pla' na' ish-veh.
