Wuh eldest istau na' pearls; wuh dahr na' ek'zer; tonk'peh wuh wuh, vi vesh' puvutau lily, leralmin-tor, 'tal-kam sa-mekh, katau me wuh she-tor.' i' ish-veh vesh' rai hagik task tor talal wuh she-tor, na' ish-veh vesh' wuh svitan t' karil; wi u' she vesh' ish-veh prettiest ko-fu, heh vesh' maut tishau t' svai, ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor au would ar'kadan ra au kupi tor. Ni au shok-tor ek' rehkuh, heh nufai au goodbye. Heh lu wuh wak sarlah na' ish-veh tor hal-tor ha-kel, au had bought pearls heh ek'zer na' wuh dahkuh eldest, tonk'peh au had sought kanok-wilat svi' vain na' wuh she-tor; heh lu au went vi' sovek bah-ker heh ya'akash na' such wuh vel, wuh sutra abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh, heh ya'akash ish-veh whether au nahp roses grew svi' izh. Nash grieved ish-veh maut mau, na' lily vesh' ish-veh dearest kan; heh u' au vesh' journeying ha-kel, thinking ra au dang katau ish-veh, sarlah ish-veh tor wuh tok-ti castle; heh pa' wuh castle vesh' wuh bah-ker, svi' veh ulef t' if ish-veh seemed tor nam-tor belaar-wak heh svi' wuh vath ulef karil. Fi' veh vla wuh finest svai vesh' svi' bosh svai, heh fi' wuh vath kanok-vei glazhau dreary heh visolektau svi' wuh izh. 'wuh kunli kwul!' leralmin-tor au, u' au puvutau tor ish-veh dvinsu, heh var-tor ish-veh tor hal-tor tor wuh vaksurik sar-tak t' roses ik vesh' tra', heh katau ish-veh maf veh t' wuh finest svai. Nash ovsoh, au vesh' riding maf muhl sanoi, lu abru sprang wuh kei lion, heh roared si', 'whoever has stolen t'nash-veh roses dungau nam-tor yokul abru alive!' yi wuh sasu leralmin-tor, 'i fai-tor ri ik wuh bah-ker belonged tor du; mokuhlek nothing korsau t'nash-veh ha'kiv?' 'rai!' leralmin-tor wuh lion, 'nothing, vita du undertake tor mazhiv-kur-tor me whatever ragel-tor du fi' ish-veh fun ha-kel; kuv du sep-wafikh tor nash, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du ish-veh ha'kiv, heh wuh she-tor nuh' na' ish-veh ko-fu.' tonk'peh wuh sasu vesh' unwilling tor tor ni heh leralmin-tor, 'ish-veh lau nam-tor t'nash-veh youngest ko-fu, vi ashau me danik, heh kwon-hau-ov sahr-tor tor ragel-tor me lu i hal-tor ha-kel.' yi wuh dvinsu vesh' greatly koltha, heh leralmin-tor, 'ish-veh lau sos'eh nam-tor goh wuh aushfa il wuh dog.' heh na' kim-shah wuh sasu yielded k' wuh ras khaf-spol, heh nem-tor wuh she-tor; heh leralmin-tor au would mazhiv-kur-tor wuh lion whatever dang ragel-tor ish-veh wuh'rak fi' ish-veh fun. Heh u' sarlah ish-veh be' ha-kel, ish-veh vesh' lily, ish-veh youngest heh dearest ko-fu, ik ragel-tor ish-veh; sarlah ish-veh sahran, heh shok-tor ish-veh, heh welcomed ish-veh ha-kel; heh lu gla-tor ish-veh ik au had katau ish-veh wuh she-tor, she vesh' fam dvun weht glad. Tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh began tor nam-tor maut sorrowful, heh tor tusa, taran, 'alas, t'nash-veh dearest kan! I ma bought nash svai na' wuh pid price, na' i ma leralmin-tor i would mazhiv-kur-tor du tor wuh kwai lion; heh lu au has du, au dungi bezhun-masu du svi' krus, heh yokul du.' yi au var-tor ish-veh ek' ik had pavesh-tor, heh leralmin-tor she dang ri hal-tor, kal-tor ra would pavesh-tor. Tonk'peh she comforted ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'tal-kam sa-mekh, wuh zhit du ma putan-tor bolau nam-tor potau; i dungi hal-tor tor wuh lion, heh soothe ish-veh: sos'eh au dungi kal-tor me sarlah safe ha-kel va'ashiv.' wuh thurai asal she ya'akash wuh yut she vesh' tor hal-tor, heh nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh went forth k' wuh vakh khaf-spol vi' wuh lapan. Tonk'peh wuh lion vesh' wuh enchanted prince. K' gad au heh ek' ish-veh kelek vesh' lions, tonk'peh svi' wuh khru au nem-tor ish-veh gas'rak shidau va'ashiv. Heh lu lily sarlah tor wuh castle, au welcomed ish-veh ni courteously ik she sep-wafikh tor marry ish-veh. Wuh wedding-gadzhak vesh' meskarau, heh au ha-tor kunling teretuhr wuh akarshif. Wuh prince vesh' goh tor nam-tor gla-tor u' ak u' khru sarlah, heh yi au meskarau ish-veh kelek; tonk'peh kanok asal au losrak ish-veh bride, heh went maf k' himself, she fai-tor ri whither, till wuh mu-yor sarlah va'ashiv. Po' ein wak au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'fa-gad tra' dungi nam-tor wuh lo'uk gadzhak svi' ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek, na' ish-veh eldest ko-kai nam-tor tor nam-tor telik; heh kuv du istaya tor hal-tor heh yaret ish-veh t'nash-veh lions dungau ras-tukh du thither.' yi she rejoiced mau na' wuh nahp t' seeing ish-veh sa-mekh wuh'wak weht, heh eku si' k' wuh lions; heh kanok-veh vesh' overjoyed tor gla-tor ish-veh, na' au had nahp ish-veh tevik wu opi'. Tonk'peh she var-tor au uf kunli she vesh', heh stayed till wuh gadzhak vesh' abru', heh yi went pla' tor wuh lapan. Ish-veh dahr ko-kai vesh' ak po' telik, heh lu lily vesh' ya'akash tor hal-tor tor wuh wedding, she leralmin-tor tor wuh prince, 'i dungi ri hal-tor sa'awek nash wak--du bolau hal-tor k' me.' tonk'peh au would ri, heh leralmin-tor ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh maut hazardous vel; na' kuv wuh least ha'zehl t' wuh torch-ta'hal dang tevan fi-tor ish-veh ish-veh enchantment would shetau fam dvun weh-rasahkos, na' au dang nam-tor rubai vi' wuh dove, heh nam-tor punekwitau tor czar pa' wuh panu na' stehkuh wu tevun. However, she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rai shom, heh leralmin-tor she would nem-tor tun rai ta'hal dang tevan fi-tor ish-veh. Ni na' kim-shah au eku si' teretuhr, heh nem-tor k' au ish-veh pi' kan; heh she dvel-tor wuh suk tvur k' bali temok na' ish-veh tor hayal-tor svi' du' wuh wedding-torches vesh' lighted; tonk'peh, unluckily, kling gla-tor ik tra' vesh' wuh treshaya svi' wuh svep. Yi wuh wedding vesh' meskarau k' lo'uk pomp, tonk'peh u' wuh ranau sarlah s' wuh church, heh be' dvun-tor k' wuh torches fa' wuh tvur, wuh maut pi' ha'zehl t' ta'hal tevan-tor fi-tor wuh prince. Svi' wuh moment au sasaudau, heh lu ish-veh ko-telsu sarlah svi' heh glazhau na' ish-veh, she afer-tor goh wuh wan-kur dove; heh ish-veh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'stehkuh tevun bolau i hash-tor abru heh ne' abru' wuh limuk t' wuh terra, tonk'peh kanok i' heh yi i dungi kal-tor tevan wuh wan-kur kan, ik dungi gluvaya du wuh yut i am going; zahal-tor ish-veh, heh na' kim-shah du lau overtake heh eku me elik.' nash leralmin-tor, au flew si' na' wuh svep, heh ri donku-tor lily zahal-tor; heh kanok i' heh yi wuh wan-kur kan tevan-tor, heh gluvau ish-veh wuh yut she vesh' tor halovaya. Thus she went roving fi' k'fai wuh eik panu, heh glazhau neither tor wuh gas'rak el'ru il tor wuh losrak, il nem-tor sovek shom, na' stehkuh tevun. Yi she began tor nam-tor glad, heh nahp tor herself ik wuh wak vesh' sahris coming lu ek' ish-veh troubles dang shaht; wi repose vesh' fam dvun irak ska', na' veh gad u' she vesh' travelling fi' she din-tor wuh wan-kur kan, heh lu she abertau abru ish-veh bezhun she kupi nowhere gla-tor wuh dove. 'i', ' nahp she tor herself, 'rai mamuk t' sasu mokuhlek nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor tor me.' ni she went tor wuh yel heh leralmin-tor, 'thou shinest kanok-wilat, fi' wuh kunel's fik heh wuh ku-li's gluder--hast thou sovek-wilat gla-tor t'nash-veh wan-kur dove?' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh yel, 'i ma ri gla-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor thee wuh tevikeh-natuhn--tu'ash ish-veh lu thy wadan t' bolaya sarlah.' ni she itaren wuh yel, heh went fi' ish-veh yut till eventide; heh lu wuh aikum arose, she maf-tor unto ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'thou shinest k'fai wuh mu-yor, abru' vunai heh pi'laptra--hast thou nowhere gla-tor t'nash-veh wan-kur dove?' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh aikum, 'i fam yehat gol'nev thee tonk'peh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor thee wuh yu-mur--shaya ish-veh lu bolaya sarlah.' yi she itaren wuh aikum, heh went fi' till wuh mu-yor-salan blew; heh she ashenau abru ish-veh spes tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'thou blowest k'fai kanok lap heh ne' kanok mor--hast thou ri gla-tor t'nash-veh wan-kur dove?' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh mu-yor-salan, 'tonk'peh i dungi ya'akash rehkuh vath salan; sos'eh gla-tor au ish-veh.' yi wuh she'rak salan heh wuh tev'rak salan sarlah, heh leralmin-tor au nuh' had ri gla-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh khu'rak salan leralmin-tor, 'ki'gla-tor nash-veh wuh wan-kur dove--au has sasahr-tor tor wuh yon-kur masutra, heh nam-tor rubai wuh'wak weht vi' wuh lion, na' wuh stehkuh tevun nam-tor be' dvun-tor maf, heh tra' au nam-tor fighting k' wuh dragon; heh wuh dragon nam-tor wuh enchanted princess, vi seeks tor dahshauk ish-veh s' du.' yi wuh mu-yor-salan leralmin-tor, 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor thee counsel. Hal-tor tor wuh yon-kur masutra; fi' wuh gas'rak gef lamok wehk fek--tum-tor au, heh lu thou comest tor wuh eleventh, shaya ish-veh ska', heh smite wuh dragon k' ish-veh; heh ni wuh lion dungi ma wuh skil, heh fi' t' au dungi saudau tor du svi' ish-veh sha' shidau. Yi glazhau pauk heh thou wilt gla-tor wuh griffin, winged spo' kushel, sitting k' wuh yon-kur masutra; spen-tor fi' tor ish-veh pla' k' thy k'diwa veh u' sahris u' tor-yehat, heh au dungi lesh du abru' wuh mashau tor ish-veh ha-kel. I dungi isha mazhiv-kur-tor thee nash kov-sayas, ' fator wuh mu-yor-salan. 'lu du nam-tor ulef-yut abru', lehm ish-veh ne', heh s' wuh mashau dungi iyi sikar abru wuh pid kov-sayas-lap fi' if wuh griffin dungi nam-tor kup tor shom, vathru au would ri ma wuh karik'es tor lesh du wuh bosh yut; kuv, therefore, thou dost yen-tor tor lehm ne' wuh kov-sayas, au dungi kal-tor du fi' tevan vi' wuh masutra.' ni etwel ri donku-tor wanderer went forth, heh afer-tor ek' u' wuh mu-yor-salan had leralmin-tor; heh she plucked wuh eleventh fek, heh smote wuh dragon, heh wuh lion forthwith became wuh prince, heh wuh dragon wuh princess va'ashiv. Tonk'peh rai sooner vesh' wuh princess sadalau s' wuh spell, do she seized wuh prince k' wuh kar heh sprang fi' tor wuh griffin's pla', heh went ska' carrying wuh prince maf k' ish-veh. Thus wuh unhappy traveller vesh' va'ashiv forsaken heh forlorn; tonk'peh she nem-tor khaf-spol heh leralmin-tor, 'u' irak u' wuh salan salur, heh ni wu u' wuh cock kushel, i dungi halovaya fi', till i talal ish-veh wuh'wak va'ashiv.' she went fi' na' wuh wu, wu yut, till na' wu-vath sarlah ish-veh tor wuh castle whither wuh princess had lesh wuh prince; heh tra' vesh' wuh gadzhak prah pok, heh she puzhu-tor ik wuh wedding vesh' pa' tor nam-tor meskarau. 'sha-ka-ri mamuk me i'!' leralmin-tor she; heh she nem-tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn ik wuh yel had putan-tor ish-veh, heh afer-tor ik k'svi ish-veh ti wuh sai-vel u' dazzling u' wuh yel itself. Ni she shitau ish-veh fi', heh went vi' wuh palace, heh ek' wuh sutra gazed fi-tor ish-veh; heh wuh sai-vel sanoi wuh bride ni mau ik she ya'akash whether ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor makau. 'ri na' pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh.' leralmin-tor she, 'tonk'peh na' kahm heh khaf.' wuh princess ya'akash ra she tvai, heh she leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor me stariben k' wuh bridegroom nash mu-yor svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor thee wuh sai-vel.' na' kim-shah wuh princess sep-wafikh, tonk'peh she var-tor ish-veh chamberlain tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh prince wuh sleeping draught, ik au lau ri zhu-tor il gla-tor ish-veh. Lu khru sarlah, heh wuh prince had tevan-tor asleep, she vesh' pufulag-tor vi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh she hayal-tor herself ne' na' ish-veh ash'ya, heh leralmin-tor: 'i ma zahal-tor thee stehkuh tevun. I ma vesh' tor wuh yel, wuh aikum, heh wuh mu-yor-salan, tor seek thee, heh na' kim-shah i ma gol-tor thee tor overcome wuh dragon. Wilt thou yi yen-tor me ved?' tonk'peh wuh prince ek' wuh wak yuk-tor ni soundly, ik ish-veh spes goh be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh, heh seemed spo' wuh whistling t' wuh salan among wuh fir-lap. Yi ri donku-tor lily vesh' pufulag-tor maf, heh punekwitau tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh pi-maat-kur sai-vel; heh lu gla-tor ish-veh ik tra' vesh' rai gol'nev na' ish-veh, she went si' vi' wuh ne-yartra, heh hayal-tor herself ne' heh wept. Tonk'peh u' she hayal-tor she bethought herself t' wuh yu-mur ik wuh aikum had putan-tor ish-veh; heh lu she shau ish-veh, tra' sahr-tor si' wuh hen heh leh-dah kahm t' pure pi-maat-tukh, ik mavau pa', heh yi nestled ne' wuh hinek veh's rala, ni u' tor shid wuh danik vaksurik glan svi' wuh panu. Heh she she-tor abru heh drove au fa' ish-veh, till wuh bride gla-tor au s' ish-veh krani, heh vesh' ni sanoi ik sarlah ish-veh forth heh ya'akash ish-veh kuv she would makau wuh kesh-travek. 'ri na' pi-maat-tukh il haul-tukh, tonk'peh na' kahm heh khaf: kal-tor me va'ashiv nash khru stariben k' wuh bridegroom svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor thee wuh bosh kesh-travek.' yi wuh princess nahp tor svik-tor ish-veh u' fa', heh sep-wafikh tor ra she ya'akash: tonk'peh lu wuh prince went tor ish-veh tvi-shal au ya'akash wuh chamberlain po wuh salan had whistled ni svi' wuh mu-yor. Heh wuh chamberlain var-tor ish-veh ek'--uf au had putan-tor ish-veh wuh sleeping draught, heh uf wuh ri donku-tor maiden had sarlah heh spoken tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh vesh' tor sarlah va'ashiv ik mu-yor. Yi wuh prince nem-tor tun tor lehm maf wuh sleeping draught; heh lu lily sarlah heh began va'ashiv tor var-tor ish-veh ra woes had befallen ish-veh, heh uf faithful heh yeht tor ish-veh she had vesh', au fai-tor ish-veh k'diwa ko-telsu's spes, heh sprang abru, heh leralmin-tor, 'du ma awakened me u' s' wuh sahr-tor, na' wuh flekh princess had lehm-tor wuh spell pa' me, ni ik i had altogether yen-tor du; tonk'peh sha-ka-ri hath satau du tor me svi' wuh kunli wadan.' heh au vazgau maf s' wuh palace k' mu-yor unawares, heh hayal-tor themselves fi' wuh griffin, vi flew pla' k' au abru' wuh yon-kur masutra. Lu au vesh' ulef-yut mes' lily kal-tor wuh kov-sayas tevan vi' wuh masu, heh iyi wuh suk kov-sayas-lap arose s' wuh masutra, whereon wuh griffin shom-tor na' wuh du', heh yi lesh au safely ha-kel. Tra' au afer-tor ish-veh kan, i' grown abru tor nam-tor comely heh rom; heh po' ek' ish-veh troubles au ha-tor kunling teretuhr tor wuh shaht t' ish-veh gad. Wuh fox heh wuh jarel wuh uroshitausu had wuh jarel ik had vesh' wuh marom faithful dvinsu tor ish-veh: tonk'peh au vesh' i' grown nuh' hinek tor ar'kadan; ni wuh uroshitausu would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh nothing weht tor yokul, heh leralmin-tor, 'i aitlun du rai longer, ni nem-tor yourself ska' s' t'nash-veh tihet; i dungau ri nem-tor du pla' va'ashiv abi' du nam-tor stronger do wuh lion.' yi au tu'ash wuh svep heh da-tor ish-veh adrift. Wuh ri donku-tor jarel vesh' maut melancholy, heh czar-tor abru heh ne' svi' wuh lapan, seeking ein pi' rau-nol s' wuh samu salan heh sov-masu. Presently wuh fox ragel-tor ish-veh: 'ra's wuh tukh, t'nash-veh t'hy'la?' leralmin-tor au, 'po tor du geldau ne' ish-veh patam heh glazhau ni lonely heh woe-begone?' 'ah!' kilko-tor wuh jarel, 'yeht-gav heh avarice worla dwell svi' veh kelek; t'nash-veh trensu has yen-tor ek' ik i ma ovsoh na' ish-veh ni wehk tevun, heh fai'ei i mokuhlek rai longer ar'kadan au has da-tor me adrift, heh leralmin-tor vita i shetau stronger do wuh lion au dungi ri nem-tor me pla' va'ashiv; ra pavesh mokuhlek i ma t' ik? Au fai-tor i ma rim, il au would ri variben ni.' however, wuh fox nufai ish-veh nam-tor t' rom cheer, heh leralmin-tor, 'i dungi gol'nev du; ti ne' tra', sakadaya yourself si' ved stegel, heh pretend tor nam-tor tevik.' wuh jarel did u' au vesh' var-tor, heh wuh fox went zehik tor wuh lion vi ha-tor svi' wuh tauk beyik, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'wuh pi' yut ska' ti wuh tevik jarel; sarlah k' me heh du lau tor wuh marom yem t' ish-veh carcase.' wuh lion vesh' greatly sanoi, heh eku ska' iyi; heh lu sarlah au tor wuh jarel, wuh fox leralmin-tor, 'du dungi ri nam-tor kup tor yokul ish-veh comfortably la'; i'll var-tor du ra--i dungi tie du sahris tor ish-veh harr, heh yi du mokuhlek bes-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh den, heh yokul ish-veh na' ish-veh el-wak.' nash na'shikh sanoi wuh lion, ni au laid himself ne' quietly na' wuh fox tor tor ish-veh sahris tor wuh jarel. Tonk'peh wuh fox khartau tor tie ish-veh mal teretuhr heh bound ek' ni lerash heh sahris ik k' ek' ish-veh karik'es au kupi ri eku himself elik. Lu wuh ar'kadan vesh' ovsoh, wuh fox clapped wuh jarel fi' wuh tipan, heh leralmin-tor, 'jip! Dobbin! Jip!' yi abru au sprang, heh dvun-tor ska', dragging wuh lion za' ish-veh. Wuh beast began tor roar heh vlei, till ek' wuh kushel t' wuh lapan flew maf na' kolthak; tonk'peh wuh jarel kal-tor ish-veh uralau fi', heh tor ish-veh yut quietly abru' wuh vunai tor ish-veh trensu's kelek. 'la' au nam-tor, trensu, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i ma prah wuh weh-rom t' ish-veh': heh lu wuh uroshitausu gla-tor ish-veh hinek dvinsu, ish-veh khaf-spol relented, heh au leralmin-tor. 'thou shalt stay svi' thy tihet heh nam-tor muhl taken tun t'.' heh ni wuh ri donku-tor hinek jarel had plenty tor yokul, heh ha-tor--till au tev-tor. Wuh pla-kur ta'hal tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh ask'ersu vi na' wehk tevun had dvin-tor wuh sa-te'kru faithfully, tonk'peh lu wuh t'naehm sarlah tor wuh shaht kupi dvin-tor rai longer fai'ei t' wuh wehk skek if au had poprah. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'du lau fun tor ish-veh ha-kel, i bolaya du rai longer, heh du dungi ri poprah sovek weht donku, na' au goh poprah wages vi renders me dvin na' au.' yi wuh ask'ersu did ri fai-tor uf tor pinkau wuh living, went maf greatly troubled, heh lates-tor wuh bosh gad, abi' svi' wuh khru au svi-tor wuh laptra. Lu mu'khlup'es sarlah fi', gla-tor ish-veh wuh ta'hal, if au went abru tor, heh sarlah tor wuh kelek wherein ha-tor wuh witch. 'tor mazhiv-kur-tor me veh mu-yor's lodging, heh wuh pi' tor yokul heh mon, ' leralmin-tor au tor ish-veh, 'il i dungau starve.' 'oho!' she kilko-tor, 'vi mazhiv-kur-tor sovek-vel tor wuh sahr-tor-maf ask'ersu? Wi dungi i nam-tor compassionate, heh nem-tor du svi', kuv du dungi tor ra i istaya.' 'ra tor du istaya?' leralmin-tor wuh ask'ersu. 'ik du dang hil-tor ek' pauk t'nash-veh bah-ker na' me, fa-gad.' wuh ask'ersu consented, heh thurai gad zup-tor k' ek' ish-veh karik'es, tonk'peh kupi ri shaht ish-veh k' wuh khru. 'gla-tor nash-veh muhl hiyet, ' leralmin-tor wuh witch, 'ik du mokuhlek tor rai weht nash-gad, tonk'peh i dungi potau du wi wuh'ashiv mu-yor, svi' vlitaya na' if du bolau fa-gad chop me wuh tus t' lapan, heh chop ish-veh pi'.' wuh ask'ersu spent wuh bosh gad svi' doing ish-veh, heh svi' wuh khru wuh witch proposed ik au dang stay veh mu-yor weht. 'fa-gad, du dungau goh tor me wuh maut trifling krus t' ar'kadan. Za' t'nash-veh kelek, tra' nam-tor wuh hinek pseth muhl, vi' if t'nash-veh ta'hal has tevan-tor, ish-veh yontau pla-kur, heh worla hal-tor si', heh du dungau katau ish-veh abru va'ashiv.' thurai gad wuh hinek kosu nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh muhl, heh kal-tor ish-veh ne' svi' wuh ki'haf. Au afer-tor wuh pla-kur ta'hal, heh tor ish-veh wuh glantokaya tor bes-tor ish-veh abru va'ashiv. She did bes-tor ish-veh abru, tonk'peh lu au sarlah be' wuh rihk, she sakadau ne' ish-veh el'ru heh aitlu tor nem-tor wuh pla-kur ta'hal maf s' ish-veh. 'rai, ' leralmin-tor au, perceiving ish-veh ek'rasah intention, 'i dungi ri mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh ta'hal abi' i am standing k' fi' ash'ya fi-tor wuh solektra.' wuh witch tevan-tor vi' wuh shaukaush, kal-tor ish-veh tevan va'ashiv vi' wuh muhl, heh went maf. Wuh ri donku-tor ask'ersu tevan-tor rik' dash fi' wuh moist solektra, heh wuh pla-kur ta'hal went fi' yontau, tonk'peh t' ra nam-tor-tor vesh' ik tor ish-veh? Gla-tor ish-veh maut muhl ik au kupi ri stron tevakh. Au hayal-tor na' wuh du' maut sorrowfully, yi suddenly au olau svi' ish-veh abru'lik heh afer-tor ish-veh tobacco mev, if vesh' fam dvun ulef bosh. 'nash dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh kim-shah sanosh, ' nahp au, seshau ish-veh si', lit ish-veh na' wuh pla-kur ta'hal heh began tor vuzh. Lu wuh vuzh had circled pa' wuh suk-tauk, suddenly wuh pi' nesh-kur kobsu lam-tor fa' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 's'haile, ra nam-tor ish-veh khartau?' 'ra t'nash-veh khartau nam-tor?' kilko-tor wuh ask'ersu, ved astonished. 'i bolau tor kanok-vei du nufai me, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi' sasu. 'rom, ' leralmin-tor wuh ask'ersu; 'yi svi' wuh wuh'rak shi gol'nev me s' nash muhl.' wuh pi' sasu nem-tor ish-veh k' wuh el'ru, heh pufulag-tor ish-veh k'fai wuh underground tvur, tonk'peh au did ri yen-tor tor nem-tor wuh pla-kur ta'hal k' ish-veh. Fi' wuh yut wuh kobsu gluvau ish-veh wuh treasures if wuh witch had tershau heh ipik tra', heh wuh ask'ersu nem-tor u' mau pi-maat-tukh u' au kupi lesh. Lu au vesh' abru', au leralmin-tor tor wuh pi' sasu: 'i' hal-tor heh bind wuh hinek witch, heh lesh ish-veh fa' wuh judge.' svi' wuh pen wak sarlah ish-veh k' spo' wuh salan, riding fi' wuh kwai tom-aushfa heh screaming frightfully. Il vesh' ish-veh wu fa' wuh pi' sasu reappeared. 'ish-veh nam-tor ek' ovsoh, ' leralmin-tor au, 'heh wuh witch nam-tor already hanging fi' wuh geld-stau-nentu. Ra further khartau has t'nash-veh s'haile?' inquired wuh kobsu. 'i', rim, ' kilko-tor wuh ask'ersu; 'du mokuhlek fun ha-kel, goh nam-tor na' el'ru iyi, kuv i summon du.' 'nothing weht nam-tor bolau do ik du dang ta'hal ish-veh mev na' wuh pla-kur ta'hal, heh i dungi saudau fa' du na' wuh'wak.' thereupon au vanished s' ish-veh glan. Wuh ask'ersu fun-tor tor wuh kahr s' if sarlah ish-veh. Au went tor wuh buhfik ha-shal, ordered himself handsome sai-vel, heh yi bade wuh landlord furnish ish-veh wuh tvi-shal u' handsome u' tor-yehat. Lu ish-veh vesh' pok heh wuh ask'ersu had taken mat t' ish-veh, au summoned wuh pi' nesh-kur manikin heh leralmin-tor: 'i ma dvin-tor wuh sa-te'kru faithfully, tonk'peh au has dismissed me, heh losrak me tor avon, heh i' i aitlun tor nem-tor t'nash-veh revenge.' 'ra am i tor tor?' ya'akash wuh pi' sasu. 'tab-ma na' mu-yor, lu wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu nam-tor svi' sar-tak, katau ish-veh la' svi' ish-veh yuk, she dungau tor dvinsu's ar'kadan na' me.' wuh manikin leralmin-tor: 'ik nam-tor wuh hagik vel na' me tor tor, tonk'peh wuh maut tehvar-bosh vel na' du, na' kuv ish-veh nam-tor discovered, du dungi panavau has-bosh.' lu leh-dah o'wak-vel had kwul-tor, wuh svep sprang tu'ash, heh wuh manikin lesh svi' wuh princess. 'aha! Nam-tor du tra'?' maf-tor wuh ask'ersu, 'prah tor ish-veh ar'kadan na' wuh'wak! Zaprah wuh fnash-vel heh fnashtaya wuh tvi-shal.' lu she had ovsoh nash, au ordered ish-veh tor sarlah tor ish-veh ku-san, heh yi au sakadau si' ish-veh ash'ya heh leralmin-tor: 'seshaya ska' t'nash-veh kluf, ' heh yi au threw au svi' ish-veh limuk, heh tor ish-veh pick au abru va'ashiv, heh sok'i heh brighten au. She, however, did kanok-vei au bade ish-veh, rik' opposition, silently heh k' ulef-ikap-tor bezhun. Lu wuh wuh'rak cock crowed, wuh manikin lesh ish-veh pla' tor wuh royal palace, heh laid ish-veh svi' ish-veh sar-tak. Thurai asal lu wuh princess arose she went tor ish-veh sa-mekh, heh var-tor ish-veh ik she had had wuh maut flekh sahr-tor. 'i vesh' lesh k'fai wuh yut k' wuh rapidity t' igen-wesh, ' leralmin-tor she, 'heh taken vi' wuh ask'ersu's tvi-shal, heh i had tor bek-tor fi-tor ish-veh spo' wuh dvinsu, fnashtaya ish-veh tvi-shal, sok'i ish-veh kluf, heh tor ek' ves t' menial ar'kadan. Ish-veh vesh' goh wuh sahr-tor, heh wi i am aishan u' zungor u' kuv i really had ovsoh kanok-vei.' 'wuh sahr-tor lau ma vesh' yeht, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh krus t' na'shikh. Boshaya ish-veh abru'lik bosh t' peas, heh tor wuh pi' razh svi' wuh abru'lik, heh yi kuv du nam-tor lesh maf va'ashiv, au dungi tevan si' heh trasha wuh yut svi' wuh yut.' tonk'peh unseen k' wuh sa-te'kru, wuh manikin vesh' standing be' ish-veh lu au leralmin-tor ik, heh puzhu-tor ek'. Na' mu-yor lu wuh sleeping princess vesh' va'ashiv lesh k'fai wuh yut, ein peas certainly did tevan s' ish-veh abru'lik, tonk'peh au tor rai yut, na' wuh crafty manikin had aishan fa' scattered peas svi' kanok yut tra' vesh'. Heh va'ashiv wuh princess vesh' compelled tor tor dvinsu's ar'kadan abi' cock-kushel. Thurai asal wuh sa-te'kru satau ish-veh sutra si' tor seek wuh yut, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ek' svi' vain, na' svi' kanok yut ri donku-tor kanu vesh' sitting, picking abru peas, heh taran: 'ish-veh bolau ma sov-mashau peas, kim-shah mu-yor.' 'etek bolau nah-tor t' vel else, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru; 'potau ish-veh ash'el fi' lu du hal-tor tor sar-tak, heh fa' sarlah du pla' s' wuh shi wilat du nam-tor taken, ip-sut veh t' au tra', i dungi ak contrive tor talal ish-veh.' wuh nesh-kur manikin puzhu-tor nash besau, heh na' mu-yor lu wuh ask'ersu va'ashiv ordered ish-veh tor katau wuh princess, revealed ish-veh tor ish-veh, heh var-tor ish-veh ik au fai-tor t' rai expedient tor counteract nash stratagem, heh ik kuv wuh ash'el vesh' afer-tor svi' wuh ask'ersu's kelek ish-veh would hal-tor badly k' ish-veh. 'tor ra i nufai du, ' kilko-tor wuh ask'ersu, heh va'ashiv nash wuh mu-yor wuh princess vesh' obliged tor ar'kadan spo' wuh dvinsu, tonk'peh fa' she went maf, she ip-sut ish-veh ash'el ne' wuh sar-tak. Thurai asal wuh sa-te'kru had wuh entire kahr pstha na' ish-veh ko-fu's ash'el. Ish-veh vesh' afer-tor na' wuh ask'ersu's, heh wuh ask'ersu himself, vi na' wuh entreaty t' wuh kobsu had hal-tor s'udish wuh temep, vesh' ak katau pla', heh lehm-tor vi' prison. Svi' ish-veh hash au had yen-tor wuh danik taluhk vel au had, wuh pla-kur ta'hal heh wuh pi-maat-tukh, heh had goh veh ducat svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Heh i' putush-tor k' naf-elakh, au vesh' standing na' wuh krani t' ish-veh dungeon, lu au chanced tor gla-tor veh t' ish-veh comrades be' dvun-tor k'. Wuh ask'ersu tapped na' wuh pane t' makh, heh lu nash sasu sarlah abru, leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'nam-tor ni ves u' tor zaprah me wuh pi' uzh'a'lek i ma losrak lying svi' wuh ha-shal, heh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh ducat na' doing ish-veh.' ish-veh comrade sahr-tor thither heh katau ish-veh ra au aitlu. U' ak u' wuh ask'ersu vesh' sa'awek va'ashiv, au lighted ish-veh mev heh summoned wuh nesh-kur manikin. 'ma rai pthak, ' leralmin-tor wuh latter tor ish-veh trensu. 'hal-tor wheresoever au nem-tor du, heh kal-tor au tor ra au dungi, goh nem-tor wuh pla-kur ta'hal k' du.' thurai gad wuh ask'ersu vesh' ar'kada, heh hi au had ovsoh nothing wicked, wuh judge condemned ish-veh tor tevakh. Lu au vesh' pufulag-tor forth tor tev-tor, au eit'jae wuh kim-shah favour t' wuh sa-te'kru. 'ra nam-tor ish-veh?' ya'akash wuh sa-te'kru. 'ik i lau vuzh veh weht mev fi' t'nash-veh yut.' 'du lau vuzh rehkuh, ' kilko-tor wuh sa-te'kru, 'tonk'peh tor ri glenonau ik i dungi spare ish-veh ha'kiv.' yi wuh ask'ersu seshau si' ish-veh mev heh lighted ish-veh na' wuh pla-kur ta'hal, heh u' ak u' wuh zamu wreaths t' vuzh had she-tor, wuh manikin vesh' tra' k' wuh pi' cudgel svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor: 'ra tor t'nash-veh s'haile a'fic?' 'kwul ne' tor terra ik riyeht judge tra', heh ish-veh constable, heh spare ri wuh sa-te'kru vi has skasau me ni has-bosh.' yi wuh manikin tevan-tor fi' au spo' igen-wesh, darting nash yut heh ik yut, heh whosoever vesh' ni mau u' estuhl k' ish-veh cudgel tevan-tor tor terra, heh did ri venture tor stir va'ashiv. Wuh sa-te'kru vesh' terrified; au threw himself fi' wuh ask'ersu's mercy, heh goh tor nam-tor kal-tor tor ha-tor na' ek', mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh kingdom na' ish-veh sha', heh ish-veh ko-fu tor ko-telsu. Wuh raven tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh ko-te'kru vi had wuh pi' ko-fu, fam dvun nuh' nu'ri tor sahr-tor sa'awek. Veh gad wuh kan vesh' maut troublesome, heh wuh ko-mekh kupi ri hizhuk ish-veh, tor ra she would. She grew impatient, heh seeing wuh ravens hashan pauk wuh castle, she tu'ash wuh krani, heh leralmin-tor: 'i istaya du vesh' wuh raven heh would hash-tor maf, yi i dang ma wuh pi' sochya.' scarcely vesh' wuh zhit s' ish-veh ru'lut, lu wuh kan svi' ish-veh kar vesh' da-tor vi' wuh raven, heh flew maf s' ish-veh k'fai wuh tu'ash krani. Wuh kushel nem-tor its hash tor wuh gu'gelik lapan heh hafau tra' na' wuh akarshif, heh meanwhile wuh mekhlar kupi zhu-tor nothing t' ish-veh kan. Wu po' nash, wuh sasu vesh' tor ish-veh yut k'fai wuh lapan lu au puzhu-tor wuh raven calling, heh au zahal-tor wuh ralash t' wuh spes. U' au drew be', wuh raven leralmin-tor, 'i am k' keshtan wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, tonk'peh am i' ne' wuh spell t' ein enchantment; du mokuhlek, however, eku me elik.' 'ra am i tor tor?' au ya'akash. She kilko-tor, 'hal-tor weh-irak vi' wuh lapan abi' du sarlah tor wuh kelek, wherein ha-tor wuh hinek kosu; she dungi nufai du yem-tukh heh mon, tonk'peh du bolau ri nem-tor t' either; kuv du tor, du dungi tevan vi' wuh glu yuk, heh dungi ri nam-tor kup tor gol'nev me. Svi' wuh bah-ker za' wuh kelek nam-tor wuh suk mazhiv-kur-tuh, heh fi' ik du bolau lamok heh glantau na' me. I dungau yetur tra' svi' t'nash-veh carriage na' dahkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh aru na' rehkuh successive gad; wuh wuh'rak gad ish-veh dungi nam-tor drawn k' kehkuh wan-kur, wuh dahr k' kehkuh chestnut, heh wuh kim-shah k' kehkuh nesh-kur jarel; tonk'peh kuv du vravshau tor potau kum'i heh i talal du sleeping, i dungau ri nam-tor eku elik.' wuh sasu ugau tor tor ek' ik she istau, tonk'peh wuh raven leralmin-tor, 'alas! I fai-tor kauk i' ik du dungi nem-tor vel s' wuh kosu heh nam-tor unable tor korsau me.' wuh sasu assured ish-veh va'ashiv ik au would fi' rai khrosahp esta wuh vel tor yokul il mon. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh kelek heh went svi'udish, wuh hinek kosu ragel-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'ri donku-tor sasu! Uf zungor du nam-tor! Sarlah svi' heh shom heh kal-tor me mazhiv-kur-tor du vel tor yokul heh mon.' 'rai, ' kilko-tor wuh sasu, 'i dungi neither yokul ri mon.' tonk'peh she would ri trasha ish-veh sa'awek, heh urged ish-veh taran, 'kuv du dungi ri yokul sovek-vel, k'puu du lau nem-tor wuh draught t' wine; veh mon tum-tor na' nothing, ' heh na' kim-shah au kal-tor himself tor nam-tor persuaded, heh drank. U' ish-veh drew na' wuh kru'minaakh wadan, au went s'udish vi' wuh bah-ker heh mounted wuh mazhiv-kur-tuh tor await wuh raven. Suddenly wuh olaya t' zung sarlah abru' ish-veh, heh unable tor tehnau ish-veh, au ti ne' na' wuh pi' du', fully satalau, however, tor potau kum'i; tonk'peh svi' wuh'ashiv minute ish-veh bezhun a'ing t' ish-veh sha' accord, heh au tevan-tor vi' such wuh glu yuk, ik ek' wuh ralash svi' wuh panu would ri ma awakened ish-veh. Na' dahkuh o'wak-vel wuh raven sarlah driving bi', drawn k' ish-veh kehkuh wan-kur jarel; tonk'peh kauk fa' she pulau wuh gla-tor, she leralmin-tor tor herself, sighing, 'i fai-tor au has tevan-tor asleep.' lu she svi-tor wuh bah-ker, tra' she afer-tor ish-veh u' she had ptha, lying fi' wuh mazhiv-kur-tuh, sahris asleep. She prah si' t' ish-veh carriage heh went tor ish-veh; she puvutau ish-veh heh hutau ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ek' svi' vain, au fam dvun fator sleeping. Wuh thurai gad na' aru, wuh hinek kosu sarlah tor ish-veh va'ashiv k' yem-tukh heh mon if au palikauk klee'fah. Na' kim-shah, overcome k' ish-veh persistent entreaties ik au would nem-tor vel, au abertau wuh makh heh drank va'ashiv. Na' dahkuh o'wak-vel au went vi' wuh bah-ker heh fi' tor wuh mazhiv-kur-tuh tor glantau na' wuh raven. Au had ri vesh' tra' wu fa' au began tor olau ni zungor ik ish-veh sikrus seemed hardly kup tor nenikaya ish-veh, heh au kupi ri lamok abruvenik sovek longer; ni va'ashiv au ti ne' heh tevan-tor sahris asleep. U' wuh raven drove bi' ish-veh kehkuh chestnut jarel, she leralmin-tor sorrowfully tor herself, 'i fai-tor au has tevan-tor asleep.' she went u' fa' tor glazhau na' ish-veh, tonk'peh au yuk-tor, heh ish-veh vesh' impossible tor awaken ish-veh. Wuh zahalik gad wuh hinek kosu leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'ra nam-tor nash? Du nam-tor ri eating il drinking sovek-vel, tor du aitlun tor stau yourself?' au kilko-tor, 'i lau ri heh dungi ri either yokul il mon.' tonk'peh she shitau ne' wuh dish t' yem-tukh heh wuh makh t' wine svi' khom t' ish-veh, heh lu au smelt wuh wine, au vesh' unable tor tehnau wuh temptation, heh nem-tor wuh glu draught. Lu wuh wadan sarlah pauk va'ashiv au went u' tsuri fi' tor wuh mazhiv-kur-tuh svi' wuh bah-ker tor await wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, tonk'peh au olau kauk weht overcome k' weariness do fi' wuh dahkuh previous gad, heh throwing himself ne', au yuk-tor spo' wuh lap-fek. Na' dahkuh o'wak-vel wuh raven kupi nam-tor gla-tor approaching, heh nash wak ish-veh coachman heh kanok-vei pa' ish-veh, u' muhl u' ish-veh jarel, vesh' nesh-kur. She vesh' sadder do ek'wak u' she drove bi', heh leralmin-tor mournfully, 'i fai-tor au has tevan-tor asleep, heh dungi ri nam-tor kup tor eku me elik.' she afer-tor ish-veh sleeping heavily, heh ek' ish-veh urgam tor awaken ish-veh vesh' t' rai avail. Yi she shitau be' ish-veh wuh loaf, heh ein kahm, heh wuh mashek t' wine, t' such wuh ves, ik however mau au nem-tor t' au, au would worla tor'ovau lehkuh. Po' ik she drew wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov, fi' if ish-veh ahm vesh' thes-na', ska' ish-veh ozh, heh shitau ish-veh fi-tor veh t' ish-veh. T'forti, she laid wuh nuhm be' ish-veh, svi' if, po' giving ish-veh particulars t' wuh yem-tukh heh mon she had losrak na' ish-veh, she shahtau k' wuh zahalik zhit: 'gla-tor nash-veh ik u' wu u' du hafau la' du dungi worla nam-tor kup tor eku me elik; kuv, however, du fam dvun istaya tor tor ni, sarlah tor wuh pi-maat-kur castle t' stromberg; nash nam-tor muhl k'svi ish-veh tepul tor accomplish.' she yi fun-tor tor ish-veh carriage heh drove tor wuh pi-maat-kur castle t' stromberg. Lu wuh sasu awoke heh afer-tor ik au had vesh' sleeping, au vesh' grieved na' khaf-spol, heh leralmin-tor, 'she has rai vet vesh' la' heh driven maf va'ashiv, heh ish-veh nam-tor i' nuh' tab-ma na' me tor korsau ish-veh.' yi ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' wuh vel if vesh' lying be' ish-veh; au telv-tor wuh nuhm, heh fai-tor s' ish-veh ek' ik had pavesh-tor. Au she-tor abru rik' vohtaya, nayik tor palikaya fi' ish-veh yut heh tor pulau wuh castle t' stromberg, tonk'peh au had rai idea svi' if kharat au ought tor hal-tor. Au travelled pa' wuh akarshif svi' psthan t' ish-veh heh sarlah na' kim-shah tor wuh gu'gelik laptra, k'fai'ei au went fi' walking na' leh-keh gad heh fam dvun kupi ri talal wuh yut si'. Wuh'wak weht wuh mu-yor sarlah fi', heh worn si' au ti ne' ne' wuh bush heh tevan-tor asleep. Va'ashiv wuh thurai gad au pursued ish-veh yut k'fai wuh laptra, heh ik khru, thinking tor shom va'ashiv, au ti ne' u' fa', tonk'peh au puzhu-tor such wuh howling heh wailing ik au afer-tor ish-veh impossible tor yuk. Au bek-tor till ish-veh vesh' darker heh sutra had palikau tor ta'hal abru ish-veh kelek, heh yi seeing wuh pi' glimmer ahead t' ish-veh, au went na' ish-veh. Au afer-tor ik wuh ta'hal sarlah s' wuh kelek if glazhau smaller do ish-veh really vesh', s' wuh contrast t' its pidek k' ik t' wuh immense masuk'veh vi lam-tor svi' khom t' ish-veh. Au nahp tor himself, 'kuv wuh masuk'veh gla-tor me going svi', t'nash-veh ha'kiv dungi ri nam-tor don mau.' however, po' wuh du' au summoned abru courage heh went fa'rak. Lu wuh masuk'veh gla-tor ish-veh, au puvutau si', 'ish-veh nam-tor kunli na' ik du ma sarlah, na' i ma ri had sovek-vel tor yokul na' wuh akarshif. I mokuhlek ma du i' na' t'nash-veh mu'yor-yem.' 'i would rather du kal-tor ik sa'awek, ' leralmin-tor wuh sasu, 'na' i ri tor willingly mazhiv-kur-tor myself abru tor nam-tor yokul; kuv du nam-tor wanting yem-tukh i ma hiyet tor satisfy ish-veh avon.' 'kuv ik nam-tor ni, ' kilko-tor wuh masuk'veh, 'i dungi trasha du svi' sochya; i goh nahp t' eating du fai'ei i had nothing else.' ni au went indoors teretuhr heh hayal-tor ne', heh wuh sasu katau si' wuh kap, kahm, heh wine, if hi au had yokul heh mon-tor t' au, vesh' fam dvun unconsumed. Wuh masuk'veh vesh' sanoi k' wuh rom cheer, heh ate heh drank tor ish-veh khaf-spol's content. Lu au had shahtau ish-veh mu'yor-yem wuh sasu ya'akash ish-veh kuv au kupi kharik ish-veh tor wuh castle t' stromberg. Wuh masuk'veh leralmin-tor, 'i dungi glazhau fi' t'nash-veh besan; fi' ish-veh nam-tor pu'ulidau ek' wuh kahr, pi'kahr, heh kelek.' ni au zaprah ish-veh besan, heh glazhau na' wuh castle, tonk'peh kupi ri talal ish-veh. 'worla kashek, ' au leralmin-tor, 'i ma larger besan upstairs svi' wuh cupboard, etek dungi glazhau fi' eifa, ' tonk'peh au pstha svi' vain, na' wuh castle vesh' ri pu'ulidau kauk fi' aifa. Wuh sasu i' nahp au dang spo' tor fator ish-veh halovaya, tonk'peh wuh masuk'veh eit'jae ish-veh tor hafau na' wuh gad il dahkuh longer abi' wuh fun t' ish-veh sa-kai, vi vesh' maf svi' psthan t' provisions. Lu wuh sa-kai sarlah ha-kel, au ya'akash ish-veh pa' wuh castle t' stromberg, heh au var-tor au au would glazhau fi' ish-veh sha' besan u' ak u' au had yokul heh appeased ish-veh avon. Accordingly, lu au had shahtau ish-veh mu'yor-yem, au ek' went abru teretuhr tor ish-veh tvi-shal heh glazhau k'fai ish-veh besan, tonk'peh wuh castle vesh' ri tor nam-tor afer-tor. Yi au zaprah vath older besan, heh au went fi' looking na' wuh castle abi' na' kim-shah au afer-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wehk thousand miles maf. 'uf dungau i nam-tor kup tor prah tra'?' ya'akash wuh sasu. 'i ma dahkuh wadan tor spare, ' leralmin-tor wuh masuk'veh, 'heh i dungi lesh du vi' wuh neighbourhood t' wuh castle; i bolau yi fun tor glazhau po' wuh kan vi nam-tor svi' etwel tun.' wuh masuk'veh, thereupon, lesh wuh sasu tor k'svi pa' wuh hundred leagues t' wuh castle, wilat au losrak ish-veh, taran, 'du dungi nam-tor kup tor lates wuh hafayat t' wuh yut yourself.' wuh sasu halovau fi' gad heh mu-yor till au pulau wuh pi-maat-kur castle t' stromberg. Au afer-tor ish-veh situated, however, fi' wuh makh suk'kunel, heh looking abru s' wuh ash'ya gla-tor ish-veh wuh enchanted maiden yetur pauk ish-veh castle heh yi hal-tor svi'udish. Au vesh' overjoyed tor gla-tor ish-veh, heh longed tor prah tor wuh fik t' wuh suk'kunel, tonk'peh wuh vla vesh' ni slippery ik kanok wak au attempted tor qots'noi au tevan-tor pla' va'ashiv. Lu gla-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' impossible tor pulau ish-veh, au vesh' greatly grieved, heh leralmin-tor tor himself, 'i dungi hafau la' heh bek-tor na' ish-veh, ' ni au torvau himself wuh pi' hut, heh tra' au hayal-tor heh glantau na' wuh bosh tevun, heh kanok gad gla-tor ish-veh wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu driving pauk ish-veh castle, tonk'peh fam dvun vesh' unable tor prah nearer tor ish-veh. Looking si' s' ish-veh hut veh gad gla-tor ish-veh rehkuh robbers fighting heh au shoret au, 'oekon nam-tor k' du.' au pehkau lu au puzhu-tor wuh vutau, tonk'peh looking pauk heh seeing kling, au went fi' va'ashiv k' ish-veh fighting, if i' became weht furious. 'oekon nam-tor k' du, ' au maf-tor va'ashiv, heh va'ashiv au svizh-tor heh glazhau pa', tonk'peh seeing kling went pla' tor ish-veh fighting. Wuh wuh wak au puvutau si', 'oekon nam-tor k' du, ' heh yi thinking au dang spo' tor fai-tor wuh aishan t' dispute svi' wuh rehkuh sasu, au went si' heh ya'akash au po au vesh' fighting ni angrily k' veh wuh'ashiv. Veh t' au leralmin-tor ik au had afer-tor wuh terpau, heh ik au had tonk'peh tor kwul ish-veh tehnat sovek svep k'fai'ei au istau tor be' dvun, heh ish-veh iyi flew tu'ash. Wuh'ashiv var-tor ish-veh ik au had afer-tor wuh tor-sai if rendered its wearer invisible; heh wuh wuh had kum-tor wuh jarel if would lesh its rider abru' sovek obstacle, heh kauk abru wuh makh suk'kunel. Au had vesh' unable tor klopau whether au would potau teretuhr heh ma wuh vel svi' tsuri, il whether au would dahshauk. Fi' khaf-spol nash, wuh sasu leralmin-tor, 'i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du vel svi' di'kizh na' eifa rehkuh vel; ri donku, na' ik i ma ri prah, tonk'peh vel ik nam-tor t' irak weht tala. I bolau wuh'rak, however, skan-tor whether ek' du ma var-tor me pa' ish-veh rehkuh vel nam-tor yeht.' wuh robbers, therefore, tor ish-veh prah fi' wuh jarel, heh handed ish-veh wuh terpau heh wuh tor-sai, heh lu au had shitau nash pauk ish-veh au vesh' rai longer visible. Yi au tevan-tor fi-tor au k' wuh terpau heh kuhsh-tor au veh po' wuh'ashiv, maf-tor, 'tra', du idle vagabonds, du ma prah ra du nazh; nam-tor du satisfied i'!' po' nash au fau-tor abru wuh makh suk'kunel. Lu au pulau wuh temep t' wuh castle, au afer-tor ish-veh a'ing, tonk'peh au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh salur k' ish-veh terpau, heh ish-veh flew eik tu'ash na' wuh'wak heh au be' dvun-tor k'fai. Au mounted wuh ash-tor heh svi-tor wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh maiden vesh' sitting, k' wuh pi-maat-kur goblet bosh t' wine svi' khom t' ish-veh. She kupi ri gla-tor ish-veh na' au fam dvun sai-vel-tor ish-veh tor-sai. Au nem-tor wuh mokov if she had putan-tor ish-veh ska' ish-veh ozh, heh threw ish-veh vi' wuh goblet, ni ik ish-veh rang u' ish-veh estuhl wuh lanet. 'ik nam-tor t'nash-veh sha' mokov, ' she sporiben, 'heh kuv ik nam-tor ni wuh sasu bolau isha nam-tor la' vi nam-tor coming tor eku me elik.' she sought na' ish-veh pa' wuh castle, tonk'peh kupi talal ish-veh nowhere. Meanwhile au had hal-tor s'udish va'ashiv heh mounted ish-veh jarel heh lehm-tor ska' wuh tor-sai. Lu therefore sarlah ish-veh tor wuh castle temep gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh, heh maf-tor aloud na' mak. Yi au dismounted heh nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar; heh she shok-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'i' du ma indeed eku me elik, heh fa-gad etek dungi u'thet etwel kal'i'farr.' wuh pi-maat-kur kushel tra' vesh' wuh sasu vi had rehkuh sa-fu, wuh youngest t' ik vesh' puvutau dummling, [*] heh vesh' despised, mocked, heh sneered na' fi' kanok occasion. [*] simpleton ish-veh pavesh-tor ik wuh eldest aitlu tor hal-tor vi' wuh laptra tor hew lapan, heh fa' au went ish-veh ko-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh vaksurik slor cake heh wuh mashek t' wine svi' zek ik au lau ri dash s' avon il mag. Lu au svi-tor wuh laptra au ragel-tor wuh pi' zhai-kur-haired hinek sasu vi bade ish-veh rom gad, heh leralmin-tor: 'tor mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh krus t' cake s' ish-veh abru'lik, heh kal-tor me ma wuh draught t' ish-veh wine; i am ni k'avon heh thirsty.' tonk'peh wuh clever sa-fu kilko-tor: 'kuv i mazhiv-kur-tor du t'nash-veh cake heh wine, i dungau ma rim na' myself; nam-tor ska' k' du, ' heh au losrak wuh pi' sasu standing heh went fi'. Tonk'peh lu au began tor hew ne' wuh lap, ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' au tor wuh riyeht shad-kisheya, heh wuh la'ash tresahk ish-veh svi' wuh kar, ni ik au had tor hal-tor ha-kel heh ma ish-veh bound abru. Heh nash vesh' wuh pi' zhai-kur sasu's doing. Po' nash wuh dahr sa-fu went vi' wuh laptra, heh ish-veh ko-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh, spo' wuh eldest, wuh cake heh wuh mashek t' wine. Wuh pi' hinek zhai-kur sasu ragel-tor ish-veh likewise, heh ya'akash ish-veh na' wuh krus t' cake heh wuh mon t' wine. Tonk'peh wuh dahr sa-fu, nuh', leralmin-tor sensibly hiyet: 'ra i mazhiv-kur-tor du dungi nam-tor taken maf s' myself; nam-tor ska'!' heh au losrak wuh pi' sasu standing heh went fi'. Ish-veh taflaya, however, vesh' ri vohtau; lu au had tor wuh zamu salur na' wuh lap au kwul-tor himself svi' wuh mal, ni ik au had tor nam-tor lesh ha-kel. Yi dummling leralmin-tor: 'sa-mekh, tor ti'amah heh tresahk lapan.' wuh sa-mekh kilko-tor: 'ish-veh sa-kai ma dash-tor themselves k' ish-veh, trasha ish-veh sa'awek, du ri tor ken-tor sovek-vel pa' ish-veh.' tonk'peh dummling eit'jae ni wu ik na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor: 'aishan hal-tor yi, du dungi prah wiser k' hurting yourself.' ish-veh ko-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh cake tor k' masu heh leipau svi' wuh cinders, heh k' ish-veh wuh mashek t' sfith naliveh. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh laptra wuh pi' hinek zhai-kur sasu ragel-tor ish-veh likewise, heh na'shaya ish-veh, leralmin-tor: 'mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh krus t' ish-veh cake heh wuh mon si' t' ish-veh mashek; i am ni k'avon heh thirsty.' dummling kilko-tor: 'i ma goh cinder-cake heh sfith naliveh; kuv ik sanoi du, etek dungi hayal-tor ne' heh yokul.' ni au hayal-tor ne', heh lu dummling seshau si' ish-veh cinder-cake, ish-veh vesh' wuh tok-ti slor cake, heh wuh sfith naliveh had shetau rom wine. Ni au ate heh drank, heh po' ik wuh pi' sasu leralmin-tor: 'opi' du ma wuh rom khaf-spol, heh nam-tor willing tor dahsaya ra du ma, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du rom kunli. Tra' lam-tor wuh hinek lap, tresahk ish-veh ne', heh du dungi talal vel na' wuh gir.' yi wuh pi' sasu nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh. Dummling went heh tresahk ne' wuh lap, heh lu ish-veh tevan-tor tra' vesh' wuh kushel sitting svi' wuh gir k' kan t' pure pi-maat-tukh. Au abertau ish-veh abru, heh taking ish-veh k' ish-veh, went tor wuh ha-shal wilat au nahp au would stay wuh mu-yor. I' wuh kasu had rehkuh daughters, vi gla-tor wuh kushel heh vesh' curious tor fai-tor ra such wuh wonderful kushel lau nam-tor, heh would ma tishau ki' veh t' its pi-maat-kur kan. Wuh eldest nahp: 'i dungau ak talal wuh opportunity t' pulling si' wuh kan, ' heh u' ak u' dummling had hal-tor si' she seized wuh kushel k' wuh rala, tonk'peh ish-veh ozh heh el'ru hafau sticking sahris tor ish-veh. Wuh dahr sarlah ak afterwards, thinking goh t' uf she lau prah wuh kan na' herself, tonk'peh she had scarcely estuhl ish-veh ko-kai do she vesh' meskarau sahris. Na' kim-shah wuh wuh isha sarlah k' wuh spo' intent, heh wuh vath shei si': 'potau maf; na' goodness' sake potau maf!' tonk'peh she did ri ken-tor po she vesh' tor potau maf. 'wuh vath nam-tor tra', ' she nahp, 'i lau u' muhl nam-tor tra' nuh', ' heh sahr-tor tor au; tonk'peh u' ak u' she had estuhl ish-veh ko-kai, she hafau sticking sahris tor ish-veh. Ni au had tor spend wuh mu-yor k' wuh kushel. Wuh thurai asal dummling nem-tor wuh kushel ne' ish-veh kar heh eku si', rik' troubling himself pa' wuh rehkuh ko-kan vi vesh' hanging fi' tor ish-veh. Au vesh' obliged tor sahr-tor po' ish-veh continually, i' losrak, i' gas'rak, wherever ish-veh mal nem-tor ish-veh. Svi' wuh svitan t' wuh vunai wuh parson ragel-tor au, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh procession au leralmin-tor: 'na' mesh, du rom-na'-nothing ko-kan, po nam-tor du sahran mes' wuh vunai po' nash nu'ri sasu? Nam-tor ik seemly?' na' wuh ka wak au seized wuh youngest k' wuh el'ru svi' zek tor seshaya ish-veh maf, tonk'peh u' ak u' au estuhl ish-veh au likewise terpau sahris, heh vesh' himself obliged tor sahr-tor za'. Fa' wu wuh sexton sarlah k' heh gla-tor ish-veh trensu, wuh parson, sahran za' rehkuh ko-kan. Au vesh' astonished na' nash heh puvutau si': 'tonk'peh! Ish-veh reverence, whither maf ni sahris? Ri tor yen-tor ik etek ma wuh christening nash-gad!' heh sahran po' ish-veh au nem-tor ish-veh k' wuh sleeve, tonk'peh vesh' isha meskarau sahris tor ish-veh. Whilst wuh kaukuh vesh' sahr-tor thus veh za' wuh vath, dahkuh labourers sarlah k' ish-veh hoes s' wuh vunai; wuh parson shoret au heh eit'jae ik au would eku ish-veh heh wuh sexton elik. Tonk'peh au had scarcely estuhl wuh sexton lu au vesh' meskarau sahris, heh i' tra' vesh' stehkuh t' au sahran za' dummling heh wuh kushel. Ak afterwards sarlah ish-veh tor wuh kahr, wilat wuh sa-te'kru khau vi had wuh ko-fu vi vesh' ni serious ik kling kupi tor ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Ni au had shitau forth wuh decree ik whosoever dang nam-tor kup tor tor ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut dang marry ish-veh. Lu dummling puzhu-tor nash, au went k' ish-veh kushel heh ek' ish-veh ranau fa' wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, heh u' ak u' gla-tor ish-veh wuh stehkuh sutra sahran fi' heh fi', veh za' wuh vath, she began tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut ved loudly, heh u' kuv she would worla pehkaya. Thereupon dummling ya'akash ki' ish-veh na' ish-veh ko-telsu; tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru did ri spo' wuh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav, heh tor ek' manner t' tobeg-tor heh leralmin-tor au bolau wuh'rak torvau wuh sasu vi kupi mon wuh cellarful t' wine. Dummling nahp t' wuh pi' zhai-kur sasu, vi kupi certainly gol'nev ish-veh; ni au went vi' wuh laptra, heh svi' wuh ka shi wilat au had felled wuh lap, gla-tor ish-veh wuh sasu sitting, vi had wuh maut sorrowful limuk. Dummling ya'akash ish-veh ra au vesh' taking tor khaf-spol ni sorely, heh au kilko-tor: 'i ma such wuh lo'uk mag heh fam yehat quench ish-veh; samu masu i fam yehat lamok, wuh subok t' wine i ma aishan emptied, tonk'peh ik tor me nam-tor spo' wuh eku fi' wuh fal kov!' 'tra', i mokuhlek gol'nev du, ' leralmin-tor dummling, 'aishan sarlah k' me heh du dungau nam-tor satisfied.' au pufulag-tor ish-veh vi' wuh sa-te'kru's cellar, heh wuh sasu keh'sei abru' wuh masuk' subok, heh drank heh drank till ish-veh loins dash-tor, heh fa' wuh gad vesh' si' au had emptied ek' wuh subok. Yi dummling ya'akash wuh'wak weht na' ish-veh bride, tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru vesh' smertau ik such wuh watosh katravahsu, ik kanok-veh puvutau dummling, dang nem-tor maf ish-veh ko-fu, heh au tor wuh uzh nosh; au bolau wuh'rak talal wuh sasu vi kupi yokul wuh bosh suk'kunel t' kap. Dummling did ri nah-tor wu, tonk'peh went zehik vi' wuh laptra, wilat svi' wuh ka shi tra' hayal-tor wuh sasu vi vesh' tying abru ish-veh ak'shem k' wuh zhel, heh tor wuh awful limuk, heh taran: 'i ma yokul wuh bosh ovenful t' padukau, tonk'peh ra rom nam-tor ik lu veh has such wuh avon u' i? T'nash-veh skaun-sa'haf hafau herbosh, heh i bolau tie myself abru kuv i am ri tor tev-tor t' avon.' na' nash dummling vesh' glad, heh leralmin-tor: 'prah abru heh sarlah k' me; du dungau yokul yourself bosh.' au pufulag-tor ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru's palace wilat ek' wuh flour svi' wuh bosh kingdom vesh' tershau, heh s' ish-veh au aisha wuh masuk' suk'kunel t' kap tor nam-tor leipau. Wuh sasu s' wuh laptra lam-tor fa' ish-veh, began tor yokul, heh k' wuh shaht t' veh gad wuh bosh suk'kunel had vanished. Yi dummling na' wuh wuh wak ya'akash na' ish-veh bride; tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru va'ashiv sought wuh yut si', heh ordered wuh hali if kupi mashalo-thalv fi' solektra heh fi' masu. 'u' ak u' sarlah du masu-halovaun pla' svi' ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor au, 'du dungau ma t'nash-veh ko-fu na' ko-telsu.' dummling went zehik vi' wuh laptra, heh tra' hayal-tor wuh pi' zhai-kur sasu tor ik au had putan-tor ish-veh cake. Lu au puzhu-tor ra dummling aitlu, au leralmin-tor: 'opi' du ma putan-tor me tor yokul heh tor mon, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh hali; heh i tor ek' nash fai'ei du wuh'wak vesh' ves tor me.' yi au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh hali if kupi mashalo-thalv fi' solektra heh masu, heh lu wuh sa-te'kru gla-tor ik, au kupi rai longer prevent ish-veh s' having ish-veh ko-fu. Wuh wedding vesh' u'thet, heh po' wuh sa-te'kru's tevakh, dummling inherited ish-veh kingdom heh ha-tor na' wuh akarshif contentedly k' ish-veh ko-telsu. Wuh masu t' ha'kiv wu fa' du il i vesh' pukeshta, tra' reigned, svi' wuh shasol wuh lo'uk yut ska', wuh sa-te'kru vi had rehkuh sa-fu. Nash sa-te'kru wuh'wak tevan-tor maut has-bosh--ni has-bosh ik kling nahp au kupi ha-tor. Ish-veh sa-fu vesh' maut mau grieved na' ish-veh sa-mekh's has-mar; heh u' au vesh' walking teretuhr maut mournfully svi' wuh bah-ker t' wuh palace, wuh pi' hinek sasu ragel-tor au heh ya'akash ra vesh' wuh tukh. Au var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' maut has-bosh, heh ik au vesh' kwes nothing kupi korsau ish-veh. 'i fai-tor ra would, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi' hinek sasu; 'ish-veh nam-tor wuh masu t' ha'kiv. Kuv au kupi ma wuh draught t' ish-veh au would nam-tor muhl va'ashiv; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor maut lerash tor prah.' yi wuh eldest sa-fu leralmin-tor, 'i dungi ak talal ish-veh': heh au went tor wuh has-bosh sa-te'kru, heh eit'jae ik au lau hal-tor svi' psthan t' wuh masu t' ha'kiv, u' ish-veh vesh' wuh goh vel ik kupi korsau ish-veh. 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. 'i had rather tev-tor do shi du svi' such lo'uk tehvar u' du bolau ragel-tor k' svi' ish-veh halovaya.' tonk'peh au eit'jae ni lerash ik wuh sa-te'kru kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor; heh wuh prince nahp tor himself, 'kuv i katau t'nash-veh sa-mekh nash masu, au dungi tor me lad heir tor ish-veh kingdom.' yi au eku si': heh lu au had hal-tor fi' ish-veh yut ein wak sarlah ish-veh tor wuh glu ku-li, overhung k' kov heh lapan; heh u' au glazhau pa', au gla-tor standing abru' ish-veh fi' veh t' wuh kov wuh pi' watosh kobsu, k' wuh sugarloaf taik heh wuh ug'yon-kur tor-sai; heh wuh kobsu puvutau tor ish-veh heh leralmin-tor, 'prince, whither ni sahris?' 'ra nam-tor ik tor thee, du watosh imp?' leralmin-tor wuh prince haughtily, heh fau-tor fi'. Tonk'peh wuh kobsu vesh' enraged na' ish-veh kloshai, heh laid wuh pu'a spell t' has-bosh-kunli fi-tor ish-veh; ni ik u' au fau-tor fi' wuh suk'kunel be' dvun became narrower heh narrower, heh na' kim-shah wuh yut vesh' ni straitened ik au kupi ri hal-tor tor ash fa'rak: heh lu au nahp ki' da-tor ish-veh jarel pauk heh hal-tor pla' wuh yut sarlah ish-veh, au puzhu-tor wuh ral abru'teruklar-ru'lut ringing pauk ish-veh, heh afer-tor ik wuh yut vesh' a'ing za' ish-veh, ni ik au vesh' ikap-tor svi' ek' pauk. Au thurai ar'kada tor prah ska' ish-veh jarel heh tor ish-veh yut fi' ash'ya, tonk'peh va'ashiv wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut rang svi' ish-veh kaluk, heh au afer-tor himself unable tor dvun wuh ash, heh thus au vesh' punekwitau tor abide spellbound. Meantime wuh hinek sa-te'kru vesh' svizh-tor fi' svi' kanok-gadik rok t' ish-veh sa-fu's fun, till na' kim-shah wuh dahr sa-fu leralmin-tor, 'sa-mekh, i dungi hal-tor svi' psthan t' wuh masu t' ha'kiv.' na' au nahp tor himself, 't'nash-veh sa-kai nam-tor surely tevik, heh wuh kingdom dungi tevan tor me kuv i talal wuh masu.' wuh sa-te'kru vesh' palikauk maut unwilling tor kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, tonk'peh na' kim-shah yielded tor ish-veh istaya. Ni au eku si' heh zahal-tor wuh ka fau-yut if ish-veh sa-kai had ovsoh, heh ragel-tor k' wuh ka mnv, vi pehkau ish-veh na' wuh ka gla-tor svi' wuh suk'kunel, taran, u' fa', 'prince, prince, whither ni sahris?' 'kashek ish-veh sha' tek'ik, busybody!' leralmin-tor wuh prince scornfully, heh fau-tor fi'. Tonk'peh wuh kobsu shitau wuh ka spell fi-tor ish-veh u' au shitau fi' ish-veh tela'at sa-kai, heh au, nuh', vesh' na' kim-shah obliged tor nem-tor abru ish-veh abode svi' wuh khaf-spol t' wuh suk'kunel. Thus ish-veh nam-tor k' yaut silly sutra, vi nah-tor themselves abru' kanok-veh else, heh nam-tor nuh' yaut tor ya'akash il nem-tor na'shikh. Lu wuh dahr prince had thus vesh' hal-tor wuh akarshif, wuh youngest sa-fu leralmin-tor au would hal-tor heh psthan na' wuh masu t' ha'kiv, heh trusted au dang ak nam-tor kup tor tor ish-veh sa-mekh muhl va'ashiv. Ni au eku si', heh wuh kobsu ragel-tor ish-veh nuh' na' wuh ka gla-tor svi' wuh ku-li, among wuh suk'kunel, heh leralmin-tor, 'prince, whither ni sahris?' heh wuh prince leralmin-tor, 'i am going svi' psthan t' wuh masu t' ha'kiv, fai'ei t'nash-veh sa-mekh nam-tor has-bosh, heh spo' tor tev-tor: mokuhlek du gol'nev me? Pray nam-tor ves, heh mamuk me kuv du mokuhlek!' 'tor du fai-tor wilat ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor afer-tor?' ya'akash wuh kobsu. 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh prince, 'i tor ri. Pray var-tor me kuv du fai-tor.' 'yi u' du ma spoken tor me kindly, heh nam-tor kau-bosh hiyet tor seek na' na'shikh, i dungi var-tor du uf heh wilat tor hal-tor. Wuh masu du seek sikar s' wuh muhl svi' wuh enchanted castle; heh, ik du lau nam-tor kup tor pulau ish-veh svi' ek'manek, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh shek-tukh wand heh dahkuh pi' loaves t' kap; kwul wuh shek-tukh svep t' wuh castle rehkuh wak k' wuh wand, heh ish-veh dungi tu'ash: dahkuh k'avon lions dungi nam-tor lying ne' svi'udish gaping na' ish-veh shi-kar-tor, tonk'peh kuv du lehm au wuh kap au dungi kal-tor du be' dvun; yi hasten fi' tor wuh muhl, heh nem-tor ein t' wuh masu t' ha'kiv fa' wuh wak-vel kwul-tor leh-dah; na' kuv du tarry longer wuh svep dungi ikap-tor fi-tor du na' ek'wak.' yi wuh prince itaren ish-veh pi' t'hy'la k' wuh ug'yon-kur tor-sai na' ish-veh friendly mamuk, heh nem-tor wuh wand heh wuh kap, heh went travelling fi' heh fi', abru' masutra heh abru' solektra, till sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh halovaya's shaht, heh afer-tor kanok-vei tor nam-tor u' wuh kobsu had var-tor ish-veh. Wuh svep flew tu'ash na' wuh wuh shad-kisheya t' wuh wand, heh lu wuh lions vesh' quieted au went fi' k'fai wuh castle heh sarlah na' wu-vath tor wuh vaksurik tvur. Pa' ish-veh au gla-tor several knights sitting svi' wuh trance; yi au seshau ska' ish-veh mokov heh shitau au fi' ish-veh sha' ozh. Svi' wuh'ashiv tvi-shal gla-tor ish-veh fi' wuh pasu wuh shek heh wuh loaf t' kap, if au isha nem-tor. Further fi' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh vaksurik nu'ri t'sai hayal-tor fi-tor wuh ku-san; heh she welcomed ish-veh joyfully, heh leralmin-tor, kuv au would eku ish-veh elik s' wuh spell ik bound ish-veh, wuh kingdom dang nam-tor ish-veh, kuv au would sarlah pla' svi' wuh tevun heh marry ish-veh. Yi she var-tor ish-veh ik wuh muhl ik meskarau wuh masu t' ha'kiv vesh' svi' wuh palace bah-ker; heh bade ish-veh tor haste, heh bes-tor ra au aitlu fa' wuh wak-vel kwul-tor leh-dah. Au lates-tor fi'; heh u' au lates-tor k'fai vaksurik bah-ker sarlah ish-veh tor wuh delightful shady gla-tor svi' if lam-tor wuh ku-san; heh au nahp tor himself, u' au olau zungor, ik au would shom himself na' wuh du', heh gaze fi' wuh lovely scenes pa' ish-veh. Ni au laid himself ne', heh yuk tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh unawares, ni ik au did ri wake abru till wuh wak-vel vesh' striking wuh yonuk tor leh-dah. Yi au sprang s' wuh ku-san dreadfully koltha, sahr-tor tor wuh muhl, boshau wuh cup ik vesh' standing k' ish-veh bosh t' masu, heh hastened tor prah maf svi' wak. Aishan u' au vesh' going s' wuh shek-tukh svep ish-veh kwul-tor leh-dah, heh wuh svep tevan-tor ni sahris fi-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh snapped ska' wuh krus t' ish-veh timut. Lu au afer-tor himself safe, au vesh' overjoyed tor nah-tor ik au had prah wuh masu t' ha'kiv; heh u' au vesh' going fi' ish-veh yut homewards, au be' dvun-tor k' wuh pi' kobsu, vi, lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh shek heh wuh loaf, leralmin-tor, 'du ma tor wuh thol prize; k' wuh shek du mokuhlek na' wuh salur slay bosh ya'akash'er, heh wuh kap dungi worla vravshau du.' yi wuh prince nahp tor himself, 'i fam yehat hal-tor ha-kel tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh rik' t'nash-veh sa-kai'; ni au leralmin-tor, 't'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, fam yehat du var-tor me wilat t'nash-veh dahkuh sa-kai nam-tor, vi eku si' svi' psthan t' wuh masu t' ha'kiv fa' me, heh worla sarlah pla'?' 'i ma ikap-tor au abru k' wuh sem-rik svi' dahkuh suk'kunel, ' leralmin-tor wuh kobsu, 'fai'ei au vesh' yaut heh has-bosh-behaved, heh scorned tor ya'akash na'shikh.' wuh prince eit'jae ni lerash na' ish-veh sa-kai, ik wuh kobsu na' kim-shah eku au elik, hi unwillingly, taran, 'beware t' au, na' au ma rasahkos khaf-spol.' ish-veh sa-kai, however, vesh' greatly rejoiced tor gla-tor au, heh var-tor au ek' ik had pavesh-tor tor ish-veh; uf au had afer-tor wuh masu t' ha'kiv, heh had taken wuh cup bosh t' ish-veh; heh uf au had eku wuh vaksurik princess elik s' wuh spell ik bound ish-veh; heh uf she had engaged tor bek-tor wuh bosh tevun, heh yi tor marry ish-veh, heh tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh kingdom. Yi au ek' rehkuh fau-tor fi' teretuhr, heh fi' ish-veh yut ha-kel sarlah tor wuh shasol ik vesh' laid thinoi k' t'naehm heh wuh dreadful mair-yem-penak, ni ik ish-veh vesh' ptha ek' bolau tev-tor na' aitlun. Tonk'peh wuh prince mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sa-te'kru t' wuh solektra wuh kap, heh ek' ish-veh kingdom ate t' ish-veh. Heh au lent wuh sa-te'kru wuh wonderful shek, heh au slew wuh nemut's ya'akash'er k' ish-veh; heh thus wuh kingdom vesh' wuh'wak weht svi' sochya heh plenty. Svi' wuh ka manner au befriended dahkuh vath shasol k'fai'ei au be' dvun-tor fi' ish-veh yut. Lu sarlah au tor wuh masutra, au prah vi' wuh hali heh du' ish-veh halan wuh dahkuh eldest leralmin-tor tor themselves, 'etwel sa-kai has prah wuh masu if etek kupi ri talal, therefore etwel sa-mekh dungi forsake etek heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh kingdom, if nam-tor etwel gas'rak'; ni au vesh' bosh t' envy heh revenge, heh sep-wafikh teretuhr uf au kupi ruin ish-veh. Yi au bek-tor till au vesh' sahris asleep, heh mukau wuh masu t' ha'kiv s' wuh cup, heh nem-tor ish-veh na' themselves, giving ish-veh sfith(-) masutra-masu instead. Lu sarlah au tor ish-veh halovaya's shaht, wuh youngest sa-fu katau ish-veh cup tor wuh has-bosh sa-te'kru, ik au lau mon heh nam-tor hakau. Scarcely, however, had au zahv-tor wuh sfith(-) masutra-masu lu au became weh-rasahkos kauk do au vesh' fa'; heh yi fi' wuh tela'at sa-fu sarlah svi', heh tenah wuh youngest na' ra au had ovsoh; heh leralmin-tor ik au aitlu tor gisam ish-veh sa-mekh, tonk'peh ik au had afer-tor wuh masu t' ha'kiv, heh had katau ish-veh k' au. Au rai sooner began tor mon t' ra au katau ish-veh, do au olau ish-veh has-mar trasha ish-veh, heh vesh' u' karik heh muhl u' svi' ish-veh younger gad. Yi au went tor ish-veh sa-kai, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'muhl, sa-kai, du afer-tor wuh masu t' ha'kiv, did du? Du ma had wuh trouble heh etek dungau ma wuh reward. Pray, k' ek' ish-veh cleverness, po did ri du khartau tor potau ish-veh bezhun tu'ash? Thurai tevun veh t' etek dungi nem-tor maf ish-veh vaksurik princess, kuv du ri tor nem-tor tun. Du had weh-rom leralmin nothing pa' nash tor etwel sa-mekh, na' au tor ri dva-tor wuh zhit du leralmin; heh kuv du var-tor var, du dungau pak-tor ish-veh ha'kiv vi' wuh bargain: tonk'peh nam'uh hizhuk, heh etek dungi kal-tor du ska'.' wuh hinek sa-te'kru vesh' fam dvun maut reshnek k' ish-veh youngest sa-fu, heh nahp ik au really tvai ki' taken maf ish-veh ha'kiv; ni au puvutau ish-veh kelek teretuhr, heh ya'akash ra dang nam-tor ovsoh, heh ek' sep-wafikh ik au ought tor nam-tor tostau. Wuh prince fai-tor nothing t' ra vesh' going fi', till veh gad, lu wuh sa-te'kru's chief huntsmen went wuh-hunting k' ish-veh, heh au vesh' sa'awek svi' wuh lapan teretuhr, wuh huntsman glazhau ni sorrowful ik wuh prince leralmin-tor, 't'nash-veh t'hy'la, ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' du?' 'i fam yehat heh dare ri var-tor du, ' leralmin-tor au. Tonk'peh wuh prince eit'jae maut lerash, heh leralmin-tor, 'goh var-tor me ra ish-veh nam-tor, heh ri tor nah-tor i dungau nam-tor reshnek, na' i dungi forgive du.' 'alas!' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman; 'wuh sa-te'kru has ordered me tor pohshau du.' wuh prince palikau na' nash, heh leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor me ha-tor, heh i dungi rubah sai-vel k' du; du dungau nem-tor t'nash-veh royal tor-pal tor gluvaya tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh tor du mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh shabby veh.' 'k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman; 'i am sure i dungau nam-tor glad tor korsau du, na' i kupi ri ma pohshaya du.' yi au nem-tor wuh prince's tor-pal, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shabby veh, heh went maf k'fai wuh lapan. Ein wak po', rehkuh grand embassies sarlah tor wuh hinek sa-te'kru's kelek, k' don-ka mazhiv-kur t' pi-maat-tukh heh taluhk kov na' ish-veh youngest sa-fu; i' ek' aifa vesh' satau s' wuh rehkuh sa-te'kru tor ik au had lent ish-veh shek heh loaf t' kap, svi' zek tor rid au t' ish-veh nemut heh yem-tor ish-veh sutra. Nash estuhl wuh hinek sa-te'kru's khaf-spol, heh au nahp ish-veh sa-fu lau fam dvun nam-tor guiltless, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh kelek, 'o ik t'nash-veh sa-fu vesh' fam dvun alive! Uf ish-veh grieves me ik i had ish-veh pustau!' 'au nam-tor fam dvun alive, ' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman; 'heh i am glad ik i had pity fi' ish-veh, tonk'peh kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor svi' sochya, heh katau ha-kel ish-veh royal tor-pal.' na' nash wuh sa-te'kru vesh' overwhelmed k' mak, heh tor ish-veh fainu throughout ek' ish-veh kingdom, ik kuv ish-veh sa-fu would sarlah pla' tor ish-veh kelek au would forgive ish-veh. Meanwhile wuh princess vesh' eagerly waiting till ish-veh deliverer dang sarlah pla'; heh had wuh fau-yut tor leading abru tor ish-veh palace ek' t' shining pi-maat-tukh; heh var-tor ish-veh courtiers ik whoever sarlah fi' horseback, heh fau-tor zehik abru tor wuh temep fi-tor ish-veh, vesh' ish-veh yeht lover; heh ik au bolau kal-tor ish-veh svi': tonk'peh whoever fau-tor fi' veh vla t' ish-veh, au bolau nam-tor sure vesh' ri wuh gas'rak veh; heh ik au bolau satau ish-veh maf na' wuh'wak. Wuh wak ak sarlah, lu wuh eldest sa-kai nahp ik au would tor haste tor hal-tor tor wuh princess, heh leralmin ik au vesh' wuh veh vi had eku ish-veh elik, heh ik au dang ma ish-veh na' ish-veh ko-telsu, heh wuh kingdom k' ish-veh. U' sarlah ish-veh fa' wuh palace heh gla-tor wuh pi-maat-kur fau-yut, au pehkau tor glazhau na' ish-veh, heh au nahp tor himself, 'ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity tor fau fi-tor nash vaksurik fau-yut'; ni au da-tor aside heh fau-tor fi' wuh gas'rak-el'ru vla t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh temep, wuh klashau, vi had gla-tor wuh fau-yut au nem-tor, leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, au kupi ri nam-tor ra au leralmin-tor au vesh', heh bolau hal-tor pa' ish-veh business. Wuh dahr prince eku si' ak afterwards fi' wuh ka skrol; heh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh pi-maat-kur fau-yut, heh ish-veh jarel had eku veh ash'ya fi-tor ish-veh, au pehkau tor glazhau na' ish-veh, heh nahp ish-veh maut vaksurik, heh leralmin-tor tor himself, 'ra wuh pity ish-veh nam-tor ik sovek-vel dang tread la'!' yi au nuh' da-tor aside heh fau-tor fi' wuh losrak vla t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh temep wuh klashau leralmin-tor au vesh' ri wuh yeht prince, heh ik au nuh' bolau hal-tor maf pa' ish-veh business; heh maf au went. I' lu wuh bosh tevun vesh' sarlah pauk, wuh wuh sa-kai losrak wuh laptra svi' if au had lain ip-sut na' pthak t' ish-veh sa-mekh's reshan, heh eku si' svi' psthan t' ish-veh betrothed bride. Ni au halovau fi', thinking t' ish-veh ek' wuh yut, heh fau-tor ni sahris ik au did ri kauk gla-tor ra wuh fau-yut vesh' tor t', tonk'peh went k' ish-veh jarel zehik abru' ish-veh; heh u' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh temep ish-veh flew tu'ash, heh wuh princess welcomed ish-veh k' mak, heh leralmin-tor au vesh' ish-veh deliverer, heh dang i' nam-tor ish-veh sa-telsu heh s'haile t' wuh kingdom. Lu wuh wuh'rak mak na' ish-veh latva vesh' abru', wuh princess var-tor ish-veh she had puzhu-tor t' ish-veh sa-mekh having forgiven ish-veh, heh t' ish-veh istaya tor ma ish-veh ha-kel va'ashiv: ni, fa' ish-veh wedding k' wuh princess, au went tor yaret ish-veh sa-mekh, taking ish-veh k' ish-veh. Yi au var-tor ish-veh kanok-vei; uf ish-veh sa-kai had kravau heh robbed ish-veh, heh wi ik au had borne ek' eifa wrongs na' wuh ashaya t' ish-veh sa-mekh. Heh wuh hinek sa-te'kru vesh' maut reshnek, heh aitlu tor taflau ish-veh wicked sa-fu; tonk'peh au tor ish-veh stron, heh prah vi' wuh hali heh masu-halovau maf abru' wuh eik masutra, heh wilat au went tor kling fai-tor heh kling tun-tor. Heh i' wuh hinek sa-te'kru hoknau teretuhr ish-veh kelek, heh ya'akash ek' ish-veh kingdom tor sarlah heh u'thet wuh wedding t' ish-veh sa-fu heh wuh princess. Heh nu'ri heh hinek, thol heh squire, gentle heh velik, sarlah na' wuh'wak fi' wuh summons; heh among wuh shom sarlah wuh friendly kobsu, k' wuh sugarloaf taik, heh wuh uzh ug'yon-kur tor-sai. Heh wuh wedding vesh' meskarau, heh wuh merry kus-vakh sahr-tor. Heh ek' wuh rom sutra au tam-tor heh au uralau, heh gadzhai heh frolick'd i mokuhlek't var-tor uf wu. Wuh leh-dah huntsmen tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu vi had wuh bride ik au ashau maut mau. Heh lu au vesh' sitting be' ish-veh heh maut kunli, ro'fori sarlah ik ish-veh sa-mekh ti has-bosh unto tevakh, heh aitlu tor gla-tor ish-veh wuh'wak va'ashiv fa' ish-veh shaht. Yi au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh k'diwa: 'i bolau i' hal-tor heh trasha du, i mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh mokov u' wuh remembrance t' me. Lu i am sa-te'kru, i dungi fun heh zaprah du.' ni au fau-tor maf, heh lu au pulau ish-veh sa-mekh, wuh latter vesh' dangerously has-bosh, heh be' ish-veh tevakh. Au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'tal-kam sa-fu, i istau tor gla-tor du wuh'wak va'ashiv fa' t'nash-veh shaht, ugaya me tor marry u' i istaya, ' heh au ahmau wuh ac'ruth sa-te'kru's ko-fu vi vesh' tor nam-tor ish-veh ko-telsu. Wuh sa-fu vesh' svi' such trouble ik au did ri nah-tor ra au vesh' doing, heh leralmin-tor: 'ha, tal-kam sa-mekh, ish-veh dungi dungau nam-tor ovsoh, ' heh thereupon wuh sa-te'kru ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun, heh tev-tor. Lu therefore wuh sa-fu had vesh' afsakau sa-te'kru, heh wuh wak t' mourning vesh' abru', au vesh' punekwitau tor potau wuh ugaya if au had putan-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, heh aisha wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu tor nam-tor ya'akash svi' kal'i'farr, heh she vesh' ugau tor ish-veh. Ish-veh wuh'rak betrothed puzhu-tor t' nash, heh fretted ni mau pa' ish-veh faithfulness ik she nearly tev-tor. Yi ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'dearest kan, po nam-tor du ni maf? Du dungau ma whatsoever du dungi.' she nahp na' wuh moment heh leralmin-tor: 'tal-kam sa-mekh, i istaya na' leh-wun ko-kan exactly spo' myself svi' limuk, khlop, heh suk'es.' wuh sa-mekh leralmin-tor: 'kuv ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat, ish-veh aitlun dungau nam-tor fulfilled, ' heh au aisha wuh psthan tor nam-tor tor svi' ish-veh bosh kingdom, abi' leh-wun nu'ri maidens vesh' afer-tor vi exactly resembled ish-veh ko-fu svi' limuk, khlop, heh suk'es. Lu sarlah au tor wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, she had leh-dah saikhut t' huntsmen's sai-vel tor, ek' kahkwa, heh wuh leh-wun maidens had tor shitau fi' wuh huntsmen's sai-vel, heh she herself shitau fi' wuh twelfth saikhut. Thereupon she nem-tor ish-veh trasha t' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh fau-tor maf k' au, heh fau-tor tor wuh kelek t' ish-veh former betrothed, ik she ashau ni dearly. Yi she ya'akash kuv au required sovek huntsmen, heh kuv au would nem-tor ek' t' au vi' ish-veh dvin. Wuh sa-te'kru glazhau na' ish-veh heh did ri fai-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh u' au vesh' such handsome katravahsu, au leralmin-tor: 'ha, ' heh ik au would willingly nem-tor au, heh i' au vesh' wuh sa-te'kru's leh-dah huntsmen. Wuh sa-te'kru, however, had wuh lion if vesh' wuh wondrous aushfa, na' au fai-tor ek' ip-sut heh tsat vel. Sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun ish-veh khru au leralmin-tor tor wuh sa-te'kru: 'du nah-tor du ma leh-dah huntsmen?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru, 'au nam-tor leh-dah huntsmen.' wuh lion fator: 'du nam-tor mistaken, au nam-tor leh-dah ko-kan.' wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: 'ik fam yehat nam-tor yeht! Uf dungi du skan-tor ik tor me?' 'oh, aishan kal-tor ein peas nam-tor strewn svi' wuh ante-tvi-shal, ' kilko-tor wuh lion, 'heh yi du dungi ak gla-tor. Sasu ma wuh pesik ash, heh lu au lates abru' peas rim t' au stir, tonk'peh ko-kan halan heh skip, heh zaseshau ish-veh ash'ya, heh wuh peas padukau pa'.' wuh sa-te'kru vesh' muhl sanoi k' wuh counsel, heh aisha wuh peas tor nam-tor strewn. Tra' vesh', however, wuh dvinsu t' wuh sa-te'kru's vi favoured wuh huntsmen, heh lu au puzhu-tor ik au vesh' going tor nam-tor shitau tor nash nisan au went tor au heh ashiv-tor kanok-vei, heh leralmin-tor: 'wuh lion aitlu tor tor wuh sa-te'kru dva-tor ik du nam-tor ko-kan.' yi wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu itaren ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh maidens: 'gluvaya ein karik'es, heh ash firmly fi' wuh peas.' ni thurai asal lu wuh sa-te'kru had wuh leh-dah huntsmen puvutau fa' ish-veh, heh sarlah au vi' wuh ante-tvi-shal wilat wuh peas vesh' lying, au ash-tor ni firmly fi' au, heh had such wuh karik, sure lates, ik ri veh t' wuh peas either padukau il stirred. Yi au went maf va'ashiv, heh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor tor wuh lion: 'du ma ti tor me, au lates aishan spo' sasu.' wuh lion leralmin-tor: 'au ma vesh' informed ik au vesh' going tor nam-tor shitau tor wuh nisan, heh ma assumed ein karik'es. Aishan kal-tor leh-dah spinning-halek nam-tor katau vi' wuh ante-tvi-shal, heh au dungi hal-tor tor au heh nam-tor sanoi k' au, heh ik nam-tor ra rai sasu would tor.' wuh sa-te'kru tishau wuh na'shikh, heh had wuh spinning-halek shitau svi' wuh ante-tvi-shal. Tonk'peh wuh dvinsu, vi vesh' muhl sashitau tor wuh huntsmen, went tor au, heh disclosed wuh ar'tu. Ni lu au vesh' sa'awek wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu leralmin-tor tor ish-veh leh-wun ko-kan: 'gluvaya ein constraint, heh ri tor glazhau pauk na' wuh spinning-halek.' heh thurai asal lu wuh sa-te'kru had ish-veh leh-dah huntsmen summoned, au went k'fai wuh ante-tvi-shal, heh worla wuh'wak glazhau na' wuh spinning-halek. Yi wuh sa-te'kru va'ashiv leralmin-tor tor wuh lion: 'du ma tehs-tor me, au nam-tor sasu, na' au ma ri glazhau na' wuh spinning-halek.' wuh lion kilko-tor: 'au ma restrained themselves.' wuh sa-te'kru, however, would rai longer dva-tor wuh lion. Wuh leh-dah huntsmen kwon-hau-ov zahal-tor wuh sa-te'kru tor wuh a'vesh', heh ish-veh liking na' au continually increased. I' sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun ik wuh'wak lu au vesh' si' hunting, ro'fori sarlah ik wuh sa-te'kru's bride vesh' approaching. Lu wuh yeht bride puzhu-tor ik, ish-veh dash-tor ish-veh ni mau ik ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' siyah pushau, heh she tevan-tor fainting tor wuh solektra. Wuh sa-te'kru nahp vel had pavesh-tor tor ish-veh tal-kam huntsman, sahr-tor abru tor ish-veh, aitlu tor gol'nev ish-veh, heh drew ish-veh glove ska'. Yi gla-tor ish-veh wuh mokov if au had putan-tor tor ish-veh wuh'rak bride, heh lu au glazhau svi' ish-veh limuk au recognized ish-veh. Yi ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' ni estuhl ik au shok-tor ish-veh, heh lu she tu'ash ish-veh bezhun au leralmin-tor: 'du nam-tor t'nash-veh, heh i am ish-veh, heh kling svi' wuh panu mokuhlek rubitau ik.' au satau wuh skladasu tor wuh vath bride, heh entreated ish-veh tor fun tor ish-veh sha' kingdom, na' au had wuh ko-telsu already, heh ein-veh vi had aishan afer-tor wuh hinek tal-muv did ri require wuh uzh veh. Thereupon wuh wedding vesh' u'thet, heh wuh lion vesh' va'ashiv taken vi' favour, fai'ei, po' ek', au had var-tor wuh yeht'es. Wuh sa-te'kru t' wuh pi-maat-kur suk'kunel tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh merchant vi had goh veh kan, wuh sa-fu, ik vesh' maut nu'ri, heh barely kup tor sahr-tor sa'awek. Au had dahkuh richly laden ships yi tor wuh halan fi-tor wuh masutra, svi' if au had fihal-tor ek' ish-veh don-tak, svi' wuh rok t' tor lo'uk nazh-tor, lu wuh ro'fori sarlah ik fi' vesh' pakik. Thus s' hasu wuh don-ka sasu au became ek' na' wuh'wak ni maut ri donku-tor ik nothing vesh' losrak tor ish-veh tonk'peh veh pi' besau t' solektra; heh tra' au k'ashiv went svi' wuh khru tor nem-tor ish-veh lates, heh ease ish-veh kashek t' wuh pi' t' ish-veh trouble. Veh gad, u' au vesh' roaming bi' svi' wuh khav-kur orenau, thinking k' rai lo'uk comfort fi' ra au had vesh' heh ra au i' vesh', heh vesh' spo' tor nam-tor, ek' fi' wuh sudden tra' lam-tor fa' ish-veh wuh pi', rough-looking, nesh-kur kobsu. 'prithee, t'hy'la, po ni sorrowful?' leralmin-tor au tor wuh merchant; 'ra nam-tor ish-veh du nem-tor ni deeply tor khaf-spol?' 'kuv du would tor me sovek rom i would willingly var-tor du, ' leralmin-tor wuh merchant. 'vi fai-tor tonk'peh i lau?' leralmin-tor wuh pi' sasu: 'var-tor me ra ails du, heh sos'eh du dungi talal i lau nam-tor t' ein nam-tor-tor.' yi wuh merchant var-tor ish-veh uf ek' ish-veh don-tak vesh' hal-tor tor wuh lanet t' wuh masutra, heh uf au had nothing losrak tonk'peh ik pi' besau t' solektra. 'oh, trouble ri yourself pa' ik, ' leralmin-tor wuh kobsu; 'goh undertake tor katau me la', leh-dah tevun hence, whatever ragel-tor du wuh'rak fi' ish-veh going ha-kel, heh i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du u' mau u' du sanoi.' wuh merchant nahp nash vesh' rai lo'uk vel tor ya'akash; ik ish-veh would danik kesik nam-tor ish-veh dog il ish-veh aushfa, il vel t' ik wihfelau, tonk'peh forgot ish-veh pi' sa-kan heinel; ni au sep-wafikh tor wuh bargain, heh signed heh fen-tor wuh tel-tor tor tor ra vesh' ya'akash t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh u' au drew be' ha-kel, ish-veh pi' sa-kan vesh' ni glad tor gla-tor ish-veh ik au crept za' ish-veh, heh laid sahris meskaraya t' ish-veh mal, heh glazhau abru svi' ish-veh limuk heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. Yi wuh sa-mekh palikau, trembling k' pthak heh horror, heh gla-tor ra ish-veh vesh' ik au had bound himself tor tor; tonk'peh u' rai pi-maat-tukh vesh' sarlah, au tor himself hagik k' thinking ik ish-veh vesh' goh wuh kha'wal ik wuh kobsu vesh' mavaun ish-veh, heh ik, na' sovek tav, lu wuh donku sarlah, au dang gla-tor wuh bearer, heh would ri nem-tor ish-veh svi'. Pa' wuh tevun-krus afterwards au went upstairs vi' wuh lumber-tvi-shal tor glazhau na' ein hinek shek-tukh, ik au lau makau ish-veh heh ashenau wuh pi' donku; heh tra', instead t' ish-veh shek-tukh, gla-tor ish-veh wuh suk tuh t' pi-maat-tukh lying fi' wuh lan-tol. Na' wuh glan t' nash au vesh' overjoyed, heh forgetting ek' pa' ish-veh sa-fu, went vi' trade va'ashiv, heh became wuh richer merchant do fa'. Meantime pi' heinel grew abru, heh u' wuh shaht t' wuh leh-dah tevun drew be' wuh merchant began tor vutau tor kashek ish-veh tel-tor, heh became maut maf heh thoughtful; ni ik tun heh sorrow vesh' written fi-tor ish-veh limuk. Wuh sa-kan veh gad ya'akash ra vesh' wuh tukh, tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh would ri var-tor na' ein wak; na' kim-shah, however, au leralmin-tor ik au had, rik' fai-tor ish-veh, makau ish-veh na' pi-maat-tukh tor wuh pi', watosh-looking, nesh-kur kobsu, heh ik wuh leh-dah tevun vesh' coming pauk lu au bolau potau ish-veh zhit. Yi heinel leralmin-tor, 'sa-mekh, mazhiv-kur-tor yourself maut pi' trouble pa' ik; i dungau nam-tor nuh' mau na' wuh pi' sasu.' lu wuh wak sarlah, wuh sa-mekh heh sa-fu went si' teretuhr tor wuh shi sep-wafikh fi-tor: heh wuh sa-fu drew wuh da-kuv fi' wuh solektra, heh eku himself heh ish-veh sa-mekh svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh. Wuh pi' nesh-kur kobsu ak sarlah, heh lates-tor pauk heh pauk pa' wuh da-kuv, tonk'peh kupi ri talal sovek yut tor prah vi' ish-veh, heh au either kupi ri, il dared ri, spen-tor abru' ish-veh. Na' kim-shah wuh sa-kan leralmin-tor tor ish-veh. 'ma du sovek-vel tor leralmin tor etek, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, il ra tor du aitlun?' i' heinel had afer-tor wuh t'hy'la svi' wuh rom pu'a, ik vesh' tishau t' ish-veh, heh had var-tor ish-veh ra tor tor; na' nash pu'a fai-tor ra rom kunli vesh' svi' mahr-kel na' ish-veh. 'ma du katau me ra du leralmin-tor du would?' leralmin-tor wuh kobsu tor wuh merchant. Wuh hinek sasu meskarau ish-veh lahv, tonk'peh heinel leralmin-tor va'ashiv, 'ra tor du aitlun la'?' wuh kobsu leralmin-tor, 'sarlah nash-veh tor variben k' ish-veh sa-mekh, ri k' du.' 'du ma kravau heh taken svi' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-fu; 'pray mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru ish-veh tel-tor na' wuh'wak.' 'rom heh softly, ' leralmin-tor wuh pi' hinek sasu; 'gas'rak nam-tor gas'rak; i ma vlitau t'nash-veh donku, heh ish-veh sa-mekh has had ish-veh, heh spent ish-veh; ni nam-tor ni rom u' tor kal-tor me ma ra i vlitau ish-veh na'.' 'du bolau ma t'nash-veh consent tor ik wuh'rak, ' leralmin-tor heinel, 'ni sanoi tor ash svi' la', heh kal-tor etek variben ish-veh abru'.' wuh hinek sasu wa'limatau, heh gluvau ish-veh zud, u' kuv au dang ma vesh' maut glad tor prah vi' wuh da-kuv kuv au kupi. Yi na' kim-shah, po' wuh wu variben, sarlah au tor zhil. Heinel sep-wafikh ik ish-veh sa-mekh bolau mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru, heh ik ni irak wuh kobsu dang ma ish-veh yut: tonk'peh, fi' wuh vath el'ru, wuh pu'a had var-tor heinel ra fortune vesh' svi' mahr-kel na' ish-veh, kuv au zahal-tor ish-veh sha' rivak; heh au did ri dvel-tor tor nam-tor putan-tor abru tor ish-veh hump-backed t'hy'la, vi seemed ni anxious na' ish-veh apc'koik. Ni, tor tor wuh wihfelau t' drawn puk t' wuh tukh, ish-veh vesh' settled ik heinel dang nam-tor shitau vi' wuh tu'ash masu-hali, ik ti fi' wuh masutra-gef lerash k'; ik wuh sa-mekh dang kwitaya ish-veh ska' k' ish-veh sha' el'ru, heh ik au dang thus nam-tor eku adrift, heh losrak tor wuh rasahkos il rom kunli t' salan heh igen-va. Yi au nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh eku himself svi' wuh masu-hali, tonk'peh fa' ish-veh prah irak ska' wuh pral kwul-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh tevan-tor k' veh vla neik svi' wuh masu, ni wuh merchant nahp ik ri donku-tor heinel vesh' pakik, heh went ha-kel maut sorrowful, du' wuh kobsu went ish-veh yut, thinking ik na' sovek tav au had had ish-veh revenge. Wuh masu-hali, however, did ri ne'hal-tor, na' wuh rom pu'a nem-tor tun t' ish-veh t'hy'la, heh ak ashenau wuh masu-hali abru va'ashiv, heh ish-veh went safely fi'. Wuh nu'ri sasu hayal-tor safe k'svi, till na' wu-vath ish-veh sahr-tor ashore fi-tor wuh ri-fainu solektra. U' au spen-tor fi-tor wuh gef gla-tor ish-veh fa' ish-veh wuh vaksurik castle tonk'peh herbosh heh dreary k'svi, na' ish-veh vesh' enchanted.
