'la', ' leralmin-tor au tor himself, 'bolau i talal wuh prize wuh rom pu'a var-tor me t'.' ni au wuh'wak weht pstha wuh bosh palace k'fai, till na' kim-shah au afer-tor wuh wan-kur oluhk, lying coiled abru fi' wuh an'kar svi' veh t' wuh tvi-shal. I' wuh wan-kur oluhk vesh' wuh enchanted princess; heh she vesh' maut glad tor gla-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'nam-tor du na' kim-shah sarlah tor eku me elik? Leh-dah wu tevun ma i bek-tor la' na' wuh pu'a tor katau du hither u' she ugau, na' du sa'awek mokuhlek korsau me. Nash mu-yor leh-dah sasu dungi sarlah: ish-veh limuk dungi nam-tor nesh-kur, heh au dungi nam-tor sai-vel-tor svi' naf-elakh fo-wein. Au dungi ya'akash ra du tor la', tonk'peh mazhiv-kur-tor rai kilko-srashiv; heh kal-tor au tor ra au dungi--kuhsh-tor, wonil-zehl, k'hy, prick, il torment du--lesh ek'; goh stariben ri wuh zhit, heh na' leh-dah o'wak-vel au bolau hal-tor maf. Wuh dahr mu-yor leh-dah vath dungi sarlah: heh wuh wuh mu-yor dah-leh-kehkuh, vi dungi kauk tresahk ska' ish-veh patam; tonk'peh na' wuh twelfth wadan t' ik mu-yor ish-veh tepul nam-tor hal-tor, heh i dungau nam-tor elik, heh dungi sarlah heh katau du wuh masu t' ha'kiv, heh dungi pu-tor du k' ish-veh, heh katau du pla' tor ha'kiv heh muhl'es.' heh ek' sarlah tor be' dvun u' she had leralmin-tor; heinel spitau ek', heh stariben ri wuh zhit; heh wuh wuh mu-yor wuh princess sarlah, heh tevan-tor fi' ish-veh talu heh shok-tor ish-veh. Mak heh gladness thorau forth throughout wuh castle, wuh wedding vesh' u'thet, heh au vesh' crowned sa-te'kru t' wuh pi-maat-kur suk'kunel. Au ha-tor teretuhr maut kunling, heh wuh ko-te'kru had wuh sa-fu. Heh thus ohkuh tevun had be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh patam, lu wuh sa-te'kru nahp t' ish-veh sa-mekh; heh au began tor wu tor gla-tor ish-veh wuh'wak va'ashiv. Tonk'peh wuh ko-te'kru vesh' tehnat ish-veh going, heh leralmin-tor, 'i fai-tor muhl ik misfortunes dungi sarlah fi-tor etek kuv du hal-tor.' however, au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rai shom till she sep-wafikh. Na' ish-veh going maf she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh wishing-mokov, heh leralmin-tor, 'nem-tor nash mokov, heh shitau ish-veh fi' ish-veh ozh; whatever du istaya ish-veh dungi katau du; goh ugaya worla tor tor nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh tor katau me hence tor ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek.' yi au leralmin-tor au would tor ra she ya'akash, heh shitau wuh mokov fi' ish-veh ozh, heh istau himself be' wuh kahr wilat ish-veh sa-mekh ha-tor. Heinel afer-tor himself na' wuh temep svi' wuh moment; tonk'peh wuh klashau would ri kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor svi', fai'ei au vesh' ni strangely clad. Ni au went abru tor wuh neighbouring kunel, wilat wuh shepherd dwelt, heh yahv-tor ish-veh hinek pelal, heh thus be' dvun-tor ri-fainu vi' wuh kahr. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh sa-mekh's kelek, au leralmin-tor au vesh' ish-veh sa-fu; tonk'peh wuh merchant would ri dva-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor au had had tonk'peh veh sa-fu, ish-veh ri donku-tor heinel, vi au fai-tor vesh' wu opi' tevik: heh u' au vesh' goh sai-vel-tor spo' wuh ri donku-tor shepherd, au would ri kauk mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sovek-vel tor yokul. Wuh sa-te'kru, however, fam dvun vowed ik au vesh' ish-veh sa-fu, heh leralmin-tor, 'nam-tor tra' rai ulidar k' if du would fai-tor me kuv i am really ish-veh sa-fu?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, 'etwel heinel had wuh ulidar spo' wuh raspberry fi' ish-veh gas'rak kar.' yi au gluvau au wuh ulidar, heh au fai-tor ik ra au had leralmin-tor vesh' yeht. Au thurai var-tor au uf au vesh' sa-te'kru t' wuh pi-maat-kur suk'kunel, heh vesh' telik tor wuh princess, heh had wuh sa-fu stehkuh tevun hinek. Tonk'peh wuh merchant leralmin-tor, 'ik mokuhlek worla nam-tor yeht; au bolau nam-tor wuh tok-ti sa-te'kru truly vi halovau pa' svi' wuh shepherd's pelal!' na' nash wuh sa-fu vesh' smertau; heh forgetting ish-veh zhit, da-tor ish-veh mokov, heh istau na' ish-veh ko-te'kru heh sa-fu. Svi' wuh instant au lam-tor fa' ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh ko-te'kru wept, heh leralmin-tor au had pushau ish-veh zhit, heh rasahkos kunli would zahal-tor. Au did ek' au kupi tor soothe ish-veh, heh she na' kim-shah seemed tor nam-tor appeased; tonk'peh she vesh' ri ni svi' yeht'es, heh vesh' goh thinking uf she dang taflau ish-veh. Veh gad au nem-tor ish-veh tor lates k' ish-veh s' wuh kahr, heh gluvau ish-veh wuh gla-tor wilat wuh masu-hali vesh' eku adrift fi-tor wuh eik mashau. Yi au hayal-tor himself ne', heh leralmin-tor, 'i am maut mau zungor; hayal-tor k' me, i dungi shom t'nash-veh patam svi' ish-veh lap, heh yuk wuh du'.' u' ak u' au had tevan-tor asleep, however, she drew wuh mokov s' ish-veh ozh, heh crept softly maf, heh istau herself heh ish-veh sa-fu na' ha-kel svi' ish-veh kingdom. Heh lu au awoke au afer-tor himself sa'awek, heh gla-tor ik wuh mokov vesh' hal-tor s' ish-veh ozh. 'i mokuhlek worla hal-tor pla' tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh's kelek, ' leralmin-tor au; 'au would leralmin i am wuh sorcerer: i dungi halovaya forth vi' wuh panu, till sarlah nash-veh va'ashiv tor t'nash-veh kingdom.' ni taran au eku si' heh travelled till sarlah ish-veh tor wuh kunel, wilat rehkuh masuk'veh vesh' thresh-tor ish-veh sa-mekh's goods; heh u' gla-tor au ish-veh be' dvun au lit'dhae heh leralmin-tor, 'pi' sasu ma nasik wits; au dungau krus wuh goods svi' etek.' i' tra' vesh' wuh shek ik tresahk ska' wuh nemut's patam whenever wuh wearer mazhiv-kur-tor wuh zhit, 'patam ska'!'; wuh tor-sai ik tor wuh owner invisible, il mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sovek shid au sanoi; heh wuh shif t' kluf ik lesh wuh wearer wherever au istau. Heinel leralmin-tor au bolau wuh'rak kal-tor ish-veh ar'kadan aifa wonderful vel, yi au lau fai-tor uf tor eku wuh tala fi-tor au. Yi au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh tor-sai, heh au istau himself wuh hash-tor, heh svi' wuh moment au vesh' wuh hash-tor. 'wuh tor-sai nam-tor maut muhl, ' leralmin-tor au: 'i' mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh shek.' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor au; 'ri vita du undertake ri tor leralmin, "patam ska'!" na' kuv du tor etek nam-tor ek' tevik sasu.' ni au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh, charging ish-veh tor ar'kadan ish-veh fi' wuh lap. Au thurai ya'akash na' wuh kluf isha; heh wuh moment au had ek' rehkuh svi' ish-veh tepul, au istau himself na' wuh pi-maat-kur suk'kunel; heh tra' au vesh' na' wuh'wak. Ni wuh masuk'veh vesh' losrak za' k' rai goods tor thresh il quarrel pa'. U' heinel sarlah be' ish-veh castle au puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' merry ralash-tanaf; heh wuh sutra pa' var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh ko-te'kru vesh' pa' tor marry wuh'ashiv sa-telsu. Yi au threw ish-veh tor-sai pa' ish-veh, heh be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh castle tvur, heh shitau himself k' wuh vla t' wuh ko-te'kru, wilat kling gla-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh lu sovek-vel tor yokul vesh' shitau fi-tor ish-veh math, au nem-tor ish-veh maf heh ate ish-veh himself; heh lu wuh makh t' wine vesh' handed tor ish-veh, au nem-tor ish-veh heh drank ish-veh; heh thus, hi au potau fi' giving ish-veh kahm heh mon, ish-veh math heh cup vesh' kwon-hau-ov herbosh. Fi-tor nash, pthak heh remorse sarlah abru' ish-veh, heh she went vi' ish-veh tvi-shal sa'awek, heh hayal-tor tra' weeping; heh au zahal-tor ish-veh tra'. 'alas!' leralmin-tor she tor herself, 'vesh' i ri wuh'wak eku elik? Po yi tor nash enchantment fam dvun seem tor bind me?' 'riyeht heh fickle veh!' leralmin-tor au. 'veh indeed sarlah vi eku thee elik, heh au nam-tor i' be' thee va'ashiv; tonk'peh uf ma du nam-tor-tor ish-veh? Ought au tor ma had such skasaya s' thee?' yi au went si' heh satau maf wuh apc'koik, heh leralmin-tor wuh wedding vesh' na' wuh shaht, na' ik au vesh' sarlah pla' tor wuh kingdom. Tonk'peh wuh princes, peers, heh lo'uk sasu mocked na' ish-veh. However, au would svi-tor vi' rai parley k' au, tonk'peh goh ya'akash au kuv au would hal-tor svi' sochya il ri. Yi au da-tor fi-tor ish-veh heh ar'kada tor seize ish-veh; tonk'peh au drew ish-veh shek. 'patam ska'!' maf-tor au; heh k' wuh zhit wuh traitors' patam tevan-tor fa' ish-veh, heh heinel vesh' wuh'wak weht sa-te'kru t' wuh pi-maat-kur suk'kunel. Hassu knowall tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh ri donku-tor peasant puvutau crabb, vi drove k' dahkuh oxen wuh tus t' lapan tor wuh kahr, heh makau ish-veh tor wuh hassu na' dahkuh talers. Lu wuh donku vesh' hasu tum-tor si' tor ish-veh, ish-veh ni pavesh-tor ik wuh hassu vesh' sitting na' pasu, heh lu wuh peasant gla-tor uf muhl au ate heh drank, ish-veh khaf-spol aitlu ra gla-tor ish-veh, heh would willingly ma vesh' wuh hassu nuh'. Ni au hafau standing wuh du', heh na' wu-vath inquired kuv au nuh' kupi ri nam-tor wuh hassu. 'oh, ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh hassu, 'ik nam-tor ak khartau.' 'ra bolau i tor?' ya'akash wuh peasant. 'svi' wuh wuh'rak shi mahr-tor yourself wuh wuh b c dunap t' wuh ves if has wuh cock fi' wuh frontispiece; svi' wuh dahr, da-tor ish-veh hal heh ish-veh dahkuh oxen vi' donku, heh prah yourself ein sai-vel, heh whatsoever else pertains tor haseret; thirdly, ma wuh glat kras-tor na' yourself k' wuh zhit: "i am hassu knowall, " heh ma ik nailed abru abru' ish-veh kelek-svep.' wuh peasant did kanok-vei ik au had vesh' var-tor tor tor. Lu au had doctored sutra awhile, tonk'peh ri wu, wuh don-ka heh lo'uk s'haile had ein donku stolen. Yi au vesh' var-tor pa' hassu knowall vi ha-tor svi' such heh such wuh pi'kahr, heh bolau fai-tor ra had shetau t' wuh donku. Ni wuh s'haile had wuh jarel harnessed tor ish-veh carriage, drove si' tor wuh pi'kahr, heh ya'akash crabb kuv au vesh' hassu knowall. Ha, au vesh', au leralmin-tor. Yi au vesh' tor hal-tor k' ish-veh heh katau pla' wuh stolen donku. 'oh, ha, tonk'peh grete, t'nash-veh ko-telsu, bolau hal-tor nuh'.' wuh s'haile vesh' willing, heh kal-tor fi' t' au ma wuh ku-san svi' wuh carriage, heh au ek' drove maf teretuhr. Lu sarlah au tor wuh nobleman's castle, wuh pasu vesh' sak-tor, heh crabb vesh' var-tor tor hayal-tor ne' heh yokul. 'ha, tonk'peh t'nash-veh ko-telsu, grete, nuh', ' leralmin-tor au, heh au hayal-tor himself k' ish-veh na' wuh pasu. Heh lu wuh wuh'rak dvinsu sarlah k' wuh dish t' delicate panavau, wuh peasant nudged ish-veh ko-telsu, heh leralmin-tor: 'grete, ik vesh' wuh wuh'rak, ' meaning ik vesh' wuh dvinsu vi katau wuh wuh'rak dish. Wuh dvinsu, however, nahp au intended k' ik tor leralmin: 'ik nam-tor wuh wuh'rak pi'tak, ' heh u' au actually vesh' ni, au vesh' terrified, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh comrade s'udish: 'wuh hassu fai-tor ek': etek dungau panavau has-bosh, au leralmin-tor i vesh' wuh wuh'rak.' wuh dahr did ri aitlun tor hal-tor svi' na' ek', tonk'peh vesh' punekwitau. Ni lu au went svi' k' ish-veh dish, wuh peasant nudged ish-veh ko-telsu, heh leralmin-tor: 'grete, ik nam-tor wuh dahr.' nash dvinsu vesh' kaing alarmed, heh au prah si' u' sahris u' au kupi. Wuh wuh panavau rai weh-rom, na' wuh peasant va'ashiv leralmin-tor: 'grete, ik nam-tor wuh wuh.' wuh fourth had tor lesh svi' wuh dish ik vesh' wein-tor, heh wuh s'haile var-tor wuh hassu ik au vesh' tor gluvaya ish-veh renkup'es, heh guess ra vesh' ne'rak wuh wein. Actually, tra' vesh' crabs. Wuh hassu glazhau na' wuh dish, had rai idea ra tor leralmin, heh maf-tor: 'ah, ri donku-tor crabb.' lu wuh s'haile puzhu-tor ik, au maf-tor: 'tra'! Au fai-tor ish-veh; au bolau isha fai-tor vi has wuh donku!' fi' nash wuh dvinsu glazhau terribly uneasy, heh tor wuh glat tor wuh hassu ik au istau ish-veh tor ash s'udish na' wuh moment. Lu therefore au went si', ek' kehkuh t' au confessed tor ish-veh ik au had stolen wuh donku, heh leralmin-tor ik au would willingly restore ish-veh heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh ras hau-ov vi' wuh bargain, kuv au would ri denounce au, na' kuv au did au would nam-tor geldau. Au pufulag-tor ish-veh tor wuh gla-tor wilat wuh donku vesh' ip-sut. K' nash wuh hassu vesh' satisfied, heh fun-tor tor wuh tvur, hayal-tor ne' tor wuh pasu, heh leralmin-tor: 't'nash-veh s'haile, i' dungi i psthan svi' t'nash-veh dunap wilat wuh pi-maat-tukh nam-tor ipik.' wuh fifth dvinsu, however, crept vi' wuh stove tor zhu-tor kuv wuh hassu fai-tor fam dvun weht. Tonk'peh wuh hassu hayal-tor fam dvun heh tu'ash ish-veh wuh b c dunap, da-tor wuh thalv pla'rak heh fa'rak, heh glazhau na' wuh cock. U' au kupi ri talal ish-veh iyi au leralmin-tor: 'i fai-tor du nam-tor tra', ni du had weh-rom sasarlah!' yi wuh katravahsu svi' wuh stove nahp ik wuh hassu tvai ish-veh, heh bosh t' vash, sprang si', maf-tor: 'ik sasu fai-tor kanok-vei!' yi hassu knowall gluvau wuh s'haile wilat wuh donku vesh', tonk'peh did ri leralmin vi had stolen ish-veh, heh poprah s' fi' vla mau donku svi' reward, heh became wuh renowned sasu. Wuh stehkuh ravens tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh sasu vi had stehkuh sa-fu, heh kim-shah t' ek' veh ko-fu. Hi wuh pi' ko-kan vesh' maut takov, she vesh' ni kobat heh pi' ik au nahp she kupi ri ha-tor; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor she dang na' wuh'wak nam-tor christened. Ni wuh sa-mekh satau veh t' ish-veh sa-fu svi' haste tor wuh sikar tor prah ein masu, tonk'peh wuh vath shehkuh sahr-tor k' ish-veh. Tik aitlu tor nam-tor wuh'rak na' bestan wuh masu, heh ni au vesh' svi' such wuh brax ik ek' kal-tor ish-veh pitchers tevan vi' wuh muhl, heh au lam-tor maut foolishly looking na' veh wuh'ashiv, heh did ri fai-tor ra tor tor, na' rim dared hal-tor ha-kel. Svi' wuh meantime wuh sa-mekh vesh' uneasy, heh kupi ri var-tor ra tor wuh nu'ri sasu stay ni wu. 'surely, ' leralmin-tor au, 'wuh bosh stehkuh bolau ma yen-tor themselves abru' ein zhagra t' mavau'; heh lu au had bek-tor fam dvun longer heh au wi did ri sarlah, au flew vi' wuh reshan heh istau au ek' da-tor vi' ravens. Scarcely had au spoken aifa zhit lu au puzhu-tor wuh croaking abru' ish-veh patam, heh glazhau abru heh gla-tor stehkuh ravens u' nesh-kur u' kastik-kov hashan pauk heh pauk. Sorry u' au vesh' tor gla-tor ish-veh istaya ni fulfilled, au did ri fai-tor uf ra vesh' ovsoh kupi nam-tor undone, heh comforted himself u' muhl u' au kupi na' wuh pak t' ish-veh stehkuh sa-fu k' ish-veh tal-kam pi' ko-fu, vi ak became stronger heh kanok gad weht vaksurik. Na' wuh akarshif she did ri fai-tor ik she had ek'wak had sovek sa-kai; na' ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh nem-tor tun ri tor stariben t' au fa' ish-veh: tonk'peh veh gad k' pavesh she puzhu-tor wuh sutra pa' ish-veh stariben t' au. 'ha, ' leralmin-tor au, 'she nam-tor vaksurik indeed, tonk'peh fam dvun 'tis wuh pity ik ish-veh sa-kai dang ma vesh' pakik na' ish-veh sake.' yi she vesh' mau grieved, heh went tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh, heh ya'akash kuv she had sovek sa-kai, heh ra had shetau t' au. Ni au dared rai longer ip-sut wuh yeht'es s' ish-veh, tonk'peh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh dungi t' sha-ka-ri, heh ik ish-veh keshtan vesh' goh wuh innocent aishan t' ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh pi' ko-kan pula'tusa sadly pa' ish-veh kanok gad, heh nahp herself bound tor tor ek' she kupi tor katau ish-veh sa-kai pla'; heh she had neither shom il ease, till na' wu-vath veh gad she vazgau maf, heh eku si' vi' wuh eik panu tor talal ish-veh sa-kai, wherever au lau nam-tor, heh elik au, whatever ish-veh lau kodona ish-veh. She nem-tor nothing k' ish-veh tonk'peh wuh pi' mokov if ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh had putan-tor ish-veh, wuh loaf t' kap svi' nuf she dang nam-tor k'avon, wuh pi' pitcher t' masu svi' nuf she dang nam-tor thirsty, heh wuh pi' stool tor shom fi-tor lu she dang nam-tor weary. Thus she went fi' heh fi', heh halovau till sarlah ish-veh tor wuh panu's shaht; yi sarlah ish-veh tor wuh yel, tonk'peh wuh yel glazhau mau nuh' fal heh yonalik; ni she sahr-tor maf sahris tor wuh aikum, tonk'peh wuh aikum vesh' samu heh chilly, heh leralmin-tor, 'i fnish-tor kahm heh khaf nash yut!' ni she nem-tor herself maf svi' wuh brax heh sarlah tor wuh yel, heh wuh yel vesh' friendly heh ves tor ish-veh, heh tik yel hayal-tor fi-tor ish-veh sha' pi' stool; tonk'peh wuh asal yel she-tor abru heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh pi' krus t' lapan, heh leralmin-tor, 'kuv du ma ri nash pi' krus t' lapan, du fam yehat unlock wuh castle ik lam-tor fi' wuh makh-suk'kunel, heh tra' ish-veh sa-kai ha-tor.' wuh pi' ko-kan nem-tor wuh krus t' lapan, padukau ish-veh abru svi' wuh pi' sai, heh went fi' va'ashiv abi' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh makh-suk'kunel, heh afer-tor wuh svep ikap-tor. Yi she olau na' wuh pi' krus t' lapan; tonk'peh lu she unwrapped wuh sai ish-veh vesh' ri tra', heh gla-tor ish-veh she had pakik wuh mazhiv-kur t' wuh rom yel. Ra vesh' tor nam-tor ovsoh? She aitlu tor korsau ish-veh sa-kai, heh had rai tal-muv t' wuh castle t' wuh makh-suk'kunel; ni nash faithful pi' ko-kai nem-tor wuh lipau s' ish-veh abru'lik heh tresahk ska' ish-veh wuhr-ozh, ik vesh' aishan wuh suk'es t' wuh krus t' lapan she had pakik, heh shitau ish-veh svi' wuh svep heh tu'ash ish-veh. U' she went svi', wuh pi' kobsu sarlah abru tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'ra nam-tor du seeking na'?' 'i seek na' t'nash-veh sa-kai, wuh stehkuh ravens, ' kilko-tor she. Yi wuh kobsu leralmin-tor, 't'nash-veh trensu nam-tor ri na' ha-kel; tonk'peh kuv du dungi bek-tor till sarlah au, pray ash svi'.' i' wuh pi' kobsu vesh' getting ish-veh aru-yem pok, heh au katau ish-veh yem-tukh fi-tor stehkuh pi' math, heh ish-veh mon svi' stehkuh pi' bezhun-zaneshu, heh eku au fi-tor wuh pasu, heh s' tik pi' math ish-veh ko-kai ate wuh pi' krus, heh s' tik pi' makh she drank wuh pi' eku; tonk'peh she kal-tor wuh mokov ik she had katau k' ish-veh tevan vi' wuh kim-shah makh. Fi' wuh sudden she puzhu-tor wuh fluttering heh croaking svi' wuh sov, heh wuh kobsu leralmin-tor, 'la' sarlah t'nash-veh trensu.' lu sarlah au svi', au aitlu tor yokul heh mon, heh glazhau na' ish-veh pi' math heh bezhun-zaneshu. Yi leralmin-tor veh po' wuh vath, 'vi has yokul s' t'nash-veh pi' math? Heh vi has vesh' drinking s' t'nash-veh pi' makh?' 'caw! Caw! Muhl i ween mortal bru-lar ma nash yut vesh'.' lu wuh seventh sarlah tor wuh lanet t' ish-veh makh, heh afer-tor tra' wuh mokov, au glazhau na' ish-veh, heh fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sa-mekh's heh ko-mekh's, heh leralmin-tor, 'o ik etwel pi' ko-kai would tonk'peh sarlah! Yi etek dang nam-tor elik.' lu wuh pi' ko-kan puzhu-tor nash (na' she lam-tor za' wuh svep ek' wuh wak heh shroi), she sahr-tor fa'rak, heh svi' wuh instant ek' wuh ravens nem-tor ish-veh gas'rak shid va'ashiv; heh ek' teraya-martaya heh shok-tor tik vath, heh went merrily ha-kel. Wuh wedding t' mrs fox wuh'rak var tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh hinek fox k' naukuh harr, vi pudva-tor ik ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' ri faithful tor ish-veh, heh istau tor shitau ish-veh tor wuh nisan. Au sakadau himself si' ne' wuh wu-ku-san, did ri dvun wuh sikrus, heh behaved u' kuv au vesh' kov tevik. Mrs fox went abru tor ish-veh tvi-shal, ikap-tor herself svi', heh ish-veh maid, din-tor aushfa, hayal-tor k' wuh yon, heh did wuh fasan. Lu ish-veh became fainu ik wuh hinek fox vesh' tevik, suitors presented themselves. Wuh maid puzhu-tor ein-veh standing na' wuh kelek-svep, knocking. She went heh tu'ash ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh nu'ri fox, vi leralmin-tor: 'ra lau du nam-tor pa', din-tor aushfa? Tor du yuk il tor du wake?' she kilko-tor: 'i am ri sleeping, i am waking, would du fai-tor ra i am tor? I am boiling lamekh naliveh k' butter, dungi du nam-tor t'nash-veh be'hai'la na' mu'yor-yem?' 'rai, nemaiyo, din-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh fox, 'ra nam-tor mrs fox doing?' wuh maid kilko-tor: 'she nam-tor sitting svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, moaning svi' ish-veh gloom, weeping ish-veh pi' bezhun ved yon-kur, fai'ei hinek mr fox nam-tor tevik.' 'tor aishan var-tor ish-veh, din-tor, ik wuh nu'ri fox nam-tor la', vi would spo' tor woo ish-veh.' 'certainly, nu'ri osu.' wuh aushfa hal-tor abru wuh kaiden halan, pash, wuh svep she knocks na' sayumak, sayumak, sayumak, 'mistress fox, nam-tor du svi'udish?' 'oh, ha, t'nash-veh pi' aushfa, ' she maf-tor. 'wuh wooer au lam-tor na' wuh svep si' tra'.' 'ra tor au glazhau spo', t'nash-veh tal-kam?' 'has au naukuh u' vaksurik harr u' wuh tab-ma mr fox?' 'oh, rai, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa, 'au has goh veh.' 'yi i dungi ri ma ish-veh.' din-tor aushfa went downstairs heh satau wuh wooer maf. Ak afterwards tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv knock, heh wuh'ashiv fox vesh' na' wuh svep vi istau tor woo mrs fox. Au had dahkuh harr, tonk'peh au did ri panavau weh-rom do wuh wuh'rak. Po' nash fam dvun weht sarlah, tik k' veh harr weht do wuh vath, tonk'peh au vesh' ek' da-tor maf, abi' na' kim-shah veh sarlah vi had naukuh harr, spo' hinek mr fox. Lu wuh kir'an puzhu-tor ik, she leralmin-tor joyfully tor wuh aushfa: 'i' tu'ash wuh temep heh svep ek' eik, heh lesh hinek mr fox s'udish.' tonk'peh aishan u' wuh wedding vesh' going tor nam-tor solemnized, hinek mr fox stirred ne' wuh wu-ku-san, heh cudgelled ek' wuh rabble, heh drove au heh mrs fox s' wuh kelek. Dahr var lu hinek mr fox vesh' tevik, wuh wolf sarlah u' wuh suitor, heh knocked na' wuh svep, heh wuh aushfa vi vesh' dvinsu tor mrs fox, tu'ash ish-veh na' ish-veh. Wuh wolf puna-shau ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 'rom gad, mrs aushfa t' kehrewit, uf sarlah ish-veh ik sa'awek du hayal-tor? Ra nam-tor du tor rom?' wuh aushfa kilko-tor: 'svi' thas i'm breaking kap ni slor, dungi du nam-tor t'nash-veh be'hai'la, heh yokul?' 'rai, nemaiyo, mrs aushfa, ' kilko-tor wuh wolf. 'nam-tor mrs fox ri na' ha-kel?' wuh aushfa leralmin-tor: 'she hayal-tor upstairs svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, bewailing ish-veh sorrowful doom, bewailing ish-veh trouble ni sival, na' hinek mr fox nam-tor rai weht.' wuh wolf kilko-tor: 'kuv she's svi' aitlun t' wuh sa-telsu i', yi dungi ish-veh sanoi ish-veh tor ash ne'?' wuh aushfa sahr-tor sahris abru wuh stair, heh kal-tor ish-veh harr hash-tor la' heh tra', abi' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh parlour svep. K' ish-veh kaukuh pi-maat-tukh mokov na' wuh svep she knocks: 'nam-tor du k'svi, rom mistress fox? Kuv du're svi' aitlun t' wuh sa-telsu i', yi dungi ish-veh sanoi du tor ash ne'? Mrs fox ya'akash: 'has wuh gentleman yon-kur stockings fi', heh has au wuh sfekau ru'lut?' 'rai, ' kilko-tor wuh aushfa. 'yi au skil-tor't tor na' me.' lu wuh wolf vesh' hal-tor, sarlah wuh dog, wuh stag, wuh hare, wuh lesh, wuh lion, heh ek' wuh beasts t' wuh laptra, veh po' wuh vath. Tonk'peh veh t' wuh rom qualities if hinek mr fox had ma, vesh' kwon-hau-ov lacking, heh wuh aushfa had continually tor satau wuh suitors maf. Na' wu-vath sarlah wuh nu'ri fox. Yi mrs fox leralmin-tor: 'has wuh gentleman yon-kur stockings fi', heh has wuh pi' sfekau ru'lut?' 'ha, ' leralmin-tor wuh aushfa, 'au has.' 'yi kal-tor ish-veh sarlah upstairs, ' leralmin-tor mrs fox, heh ordered wuh dvinsu tor dator wuh wedding gadzhak. 'fnashtaya me wuh tvi-shal u' sok'i u' du mokuhlek, abru k' wuh krani, fling si' t'nash-veh hinek sasu! Na' wehk wuh tok-ti thelik aushfa au katau, wi t' ish-veh ko-telsu au worla nahp, tonk'peh ate abru kanok veh au kum-tor.' yi wuh wedding vesh' solemnized k' nu'ri mr fox, heh tra' vesh' mau rejoicing heh taman; heh kuv au ma ri losrak ska', au nam-tor taman fam dvun. Wuh yarmok u' wuh merry nu'ri huntsman vesh' wuh'wak going brax bi' k'fai wuh lapan, tra' sarlah abru wuh pi' hinek kosu, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'rom gad, rom gad; du seem merry hiyet, tonk'peh i am k'avon heh thirsty; tor pray mazhiv-kur-tor me vel tor yokul.' wuh huntsman nem-tor pity fi' ish-veh, heh shitau ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh abru'lik heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ra au had. Yi au aitlu tor hal-tor ish-veh yut; tonk'peh she nem-tor meskaraya t' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'shroi, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, tor ra i am going tor var-tor du; i dungi reward du na' ish-veh kindness; hal-tor ish-veh yut, heh po' wuh pi' wak du dungi sarlah tor wuh lap wilat du dungi gla-tor naukuh kushel sitting fi' wuh tor-sai. Pohshau vi' wuh midst t' au, heh veh dungi tevan ne' tevik: wuh tor-sai dungi tevan nuh'; nem-tor ish-veh, ish-veh nam-tor wuh wishing-tor-sai, heh lu du sai-vel-tor ish-veh du dungi talal yourself na' sovek shi wilat du lau istaya tor nam-tor. Tresahk tu'ash wuh tevik kushel, nem-tor si' its khaf-spol heh potau ish-veh, heh du dungi talal wuh krus t' pi-maat-tukh ne' ish-veh trak kanok asal lu du shen. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh kushel's khaf-spol ik dungi katau du nash rom kunli.' wuh huntsman itaren ish-veh, heh nahp tor himself, 'kuv ek' nash tor pavesh-tor, ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh tok-ti vel na' me.' lu au had hal-tor wuh hundred ash-tor il ni, au puzhu-tor wuh screaming heh chirping svi' wuh khlup abru' ish-veh, heh glazhau abru heh gla-tor wuh treit t' kushel pulling wuh tor-sai k' ish-veh dun heh ash'ya; screaming, fighting, heh tugging na' tik vath u' kuv tik istau ki' ish-veh himself. 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman, 'nash nam-tor wonderful; nash pavesh-tor aishan u' wuh hinek kosu leralmin-tor'; yi au pohshaya vi' wuh midst t' au ni ik ish-veh kan flew ek' pa'. Ska' went wuh treit chattering maf; tonk'peh veh tevan-tor ne' tevik, heh wuh tor-sai k' ish-veh. Yi wuh huntsman did u' wuh hinek kosu var-tor ish-veh, tresahk tu'ash wuh kushel, nem-tor si' wuh khaf-spol, heh lesh wuh tor-sai ha-kel k' ish-veh. Wuh thurai asal lu au awoke au abertau abru ish-veh trak, heh tra' ti wuh krus t' pi-maat-tukh glittering ne'rak; wuh ka pavesh-tor thurai gad, heh indeed kanok gad lu au arose. Au heaped abru wuh lo'uk deal t' pi-maat-tukh, heh na' kim-shah nahp tor himself, 't' ra nam-tor-tor nam-tor nash pi-maat-tukh tor me whilst i am na' ha-kel? I dungi hal-tor si' vi' wuh panu heh glazhau pa' me.' yi au nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh t'hylara, heh geldau ish-veh sa'haf heh kes-wun pa' ish-veh talu, heh went ish-veh yut. Ish-veh ni pavesh-tor ik ish-veh fau-yut veh gad pufulag-tor k'fai wuh bali lapan, na' wuh shaht t' if vesh' wuh suk castle svi' wuh yar-kur ne-yartra, heh na' veh t' wuh krani lam-tor wuh hinek kosu k' wuh maut vaksurik nu'ri t'sai k' ish-veh vla looking pa' au. I' wuh hinek kosu vesh' wuh witch, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, 'tra' nam-tor wuh nu'ri sasu coming s' wuh lapan vi lesh wuh wonderful prize; etek bolau prah ish-veh maf s' ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam kan, na' ish-veh nam-tor weht nunau na' etek do na' ish-veh. Au has wuh kushel's khaf-spol ik katau wuh krus t' pi-maat-tukh ne' ish-veh trak kanok asal.' meantime wuh huntsman sarlah nearer heh glazhau na' wuh t'sai, heh leralmin-tor tor himself, 'i ma vesh' travelling ni wu ik i dang spo' tor hal-tor vi' nash castle heh shom myself, na' i ma donku hiyet tor vlitau na' sovek-vel i aitlun'; tonk'peh wuh yeht utvau vesh', ik au aitlu tor gla-tor weht t' wuh vaksurik t'sai. Yi au went vi' wuh kelek, heh vesh' welcomed kindly; heh ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' au vesh' ni mau svi' ashaya ik au nahp t' nothing else tonk'peh looking na' wuh t'sai's bezhun, heh doing kanok-vei ik she istau. Yi wuh hinek kosu leralmin-tor, 'i' nam-tor wuh wak na' getting wuh kushel's khaf-spol.' ni wuh t'sai vazgau ish-veh maf, heh au worla afer-tor sovek weht pi-maat-tukh ne' ish-veh trak, na' ish-veh ti i' ne' wuh nu'ri t'sai's, heh wuh hinek kosu nem-tor ish-veh maf kanok asal; tonk'peh au vesh' ni mau svi' ashaya ik au worla din-tor ish-veh prize. 'muhl, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek witch, 'etek ma prah wuh kushel's khaf-spol, tonk'peh ri wuh wishing-tor-sai wi, heh ik etek bolau isha prah.' 'kal-tor etek trasha ish-veh ik, ' leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai; 'au has already pakik ish-veh don-tak.' yi wuh witch vesh' maut reshnek, heh leralmin-tor, 'such wuh tor-sai nam-tor wuh maut ritsuri heh wonderful vel, heh i bolau heh dungi ma ish-veh.' ni she did u' wuh hinek kosu var-tor ish-veh, heh eku herself na' wuh krani, heh glazhau pa' wuh shasol heh seemed maut sorrowful; yi wuh huntsman leralmin-tor, 'ra tor du ni maf?' 'alas! Tal-kam osu, ' leralmin-tor she, 'yonder ti wuh zasuhl kov wilat ek' wuh ost'syn lerash-khush tor'ovau, heh i aitlun ni mau tor hal-tor tra', ik whenever i nah-tor t' ish-veh i fam yehat gol'nev hasu sorrowful, na' vi mokuhlek pulau ish-veh? Goh wuh kushel heh wuh hash-tor--sasu fam yehat.' 'kuv ik's ek' ish-veh tushat, ' leralmin-tor wuh huntsman, 'i'll nem-tor du tra' k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol'; ni au drew ish-veh ne' ish-veh tor-sai, heh wuh moment au istau tor nam-tor fi' wuh zasuhl suk'kunel au vesh' fi' tra'. Wuh lerash-khush glittered ni fi' ek' vla ik au vesh' delighted k' wuh glan heh abrashau wuh finest. Tonk'peh wuh hinek witch tor wuh glu yuk sarlah fi-tor ish-veh, heh au leralmin-tor tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, 'kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne' heh shom ourselves wuh pi', i am ni zungor ik i fam yehat lamok sovek longer.' ni au hayal-tor ne', heh au laid ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh lap heh tevan-tor asleep; heh whilst au vesh' sleeping fi' she nem-tor wuh tor-sai s' ish-veh tipan, geldau ish-veh fi' ish-veh sha', abrashau wuh lerash-khush, heh istau herself ha-kel va'ashiv. Lu au awoke heh afer-tor ik ish-veh t'sai had tricked ish-veh, heh losrak ish-veh sa'awek fi' wuh kwai kov, au leralmin-tor, 'alas! Ra roguery tra' nam-tor svi' wuh panu!' heh tra' au hayal-tor svi' lo'uk tushat heh pthak, ri fai-tor ra tor tor. I' nash kov belonged tor kei masuk'veh vi ha-tor fi-tor ish-veh; heh u' gla-tor ish-veh rehkuh t' au striding pa', au nahp tor himself, 'i mokuhlek goh korsau myself k' feigning tor nam-tor asleep'; ni au laid himself ne' u' kuv au vesh' svi' wuh ralash yuk. Lu wuh masuk'veh sarlah abru tor ish-veh, wuh wuh'rak kwitau ish-veh k' ish-veh ash'ya, heh leralmin-tor, 'ra worm nam-tor nash ik ti la' tcha-tor abru?' 'tread fi-tor ish-veh heh stau ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh dahr. 'ish-veh's ri don wuh trouble, ' leralmin-tor wuh wuh; 'kal-tor ish-veh ha-tor, au'll hal-tor climbing higher abru wuh suk'kunel, heh ein wan dungi sarlah rolling heh lesh ish-veh maf.' heh au be' dvun-tor fi'. Tonk'peh wuh huntsman had puzhu-tor ek' au leralmin-tor; heh u' ak u' au vesh' hal-tor, au sasu-tor tor wuh fik t' wuh suk'kunel, heh lu au had hayal-tor tra' wuh pen wak wuh wan sarlah rolling pa' ish-veh, heh kum-tor ish-veh svi' wuh whirlwind heh spitau ish-veh bi' na' ein wak, till ish-veh settled svi' wuh bah-ker, heh au tevan-tor ved kogavik tor wuh solektra svi' wuh yar-kur heh cabbages. Yi au glazhau pa' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'i istaya i had vel tor yokul, kuv ri i dungau nam-tor weh-rasahkos ska' do fa'; na' la' gla-tor nash-veh neither savas il savas, il sovek ves t' savas, nothing tonk'peh sazh.' na' kim-shah au nahp tor himself, 'i mokuhlek yokul yarmok, ish-veh dungi uzhau heh karik-tor me.' ni au picked si' wuh tok-ti patam heh ate t' ish-veh; tonk'peh scarcely had au vitem-tor dahkuh zeshaya lu au olau himself ved rubai, heh gla-tor k' horror ik au vesh' da-tor vi' wuh ass. However, au fam dvun olau maut k'avon, heh wuh yarmok zahv-tor maut nice; ni au ate fi' till sarlah ish-veh tor wuh'ashiv ves t' yarmok, heh scarcely had au zahv-tor ish-veh lu au olau wuh'ashiv rubah sarlah abru' ish-veh, heh ak gla-tor ik au vesh' kunli hiyet tor ma afer-tor ish-veh hinek shid va'ashiv. Yi au laid himself ne' heh yuk-tor ska' wuh pi' t' ish-veh weariness; heh lu au awoke wuh thurai asal au shau ska' wuh patam fi' t' wuh rom heh wuh rasahkos yarmok, heh nahp tor himself, 'nash dungi gol'nev me tor t'nash-veh fortune va'ashiv, heh enable me tor vlitau ska' ein sular-ves na' ish-veh treachery.' ni au went maf tor ar'kadan heh talal wuh castle t' ish-veh t'hylara; heh po' wandering pa' wuh zamu gad au luckily afer-tor ish-veh. Yi au kurau ish-veh limuk ek' abru' khav-kur, ni ik kauk ish-veh ko-mekh would ri ma fainu ish-veh, heh went vi' wuh castle heh ya'akash na' wuh lodging; 'i am ni zungor, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ik i mokuhlek hal-tor rai weh-irak.' 'countryman, ' leralmin-tor wuh witch, 'vi nam-tor du? Heh ra nam-tor ish-veh business?' 'i am, ' leralmin-tor au, 'wuh skladasu satau k' wuh sa-te'kru tor talal wuh finest yarmok ik tor'ovau ne' wuh yel. I ma vesh' kunli hiyet tor talal ish-veh, heh ma katau ish-veh k' me; tonk'peh wuh falek t' wuh yel scorches ni ik ish-veh palikau tor wither, heh i ri tor fai-tor ik i mokuhlek lesh ish-veh weh-irak.' lu wuh witch heh wuh nu'ri t'sai puzhu-tor t' ish-veh vaksurik yarmok, au longed tor zahvan ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'tal-kam countryman, kal-tor etek aishan zahvan ish-veh.' 'tor nam-tor sure, ' kilko-tor au; 'i ma dahkuh patam t' ish-veh k' me, heh dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du veh'; ni au tu'ash ish-veh sa'haf heh mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh rasahkos. Yi wuh witch herself nem-tor ish-veh vi' wuh af'tum sai-vel-tor; heh lu ish-veh vesh' pok she kupi ri bek-tor till ish-veh vesh' lesh abru, tonk'peh nem-tor wuh zamu mor iyi heh shitau au svi' ish-veh ru'lut, heh scarcely vesh' au vitem-tor lu she pakik ish-veh sha' shid heh sahr-tor braying ne' vi' wuh kelek svi' wuh shid t' wuh ass. I' wuh dvinsu-maid sarlah vi' wuh af'tum, heh seeing wuh yarmok pok, vesh' going tor lesh ish-veh abru; tonk'peh fi' wuh yut she nuh' olau wuh istaya tor zahvan ish-veh u' wuh hinek kosu had ovsoh, heh ate ein mor; ni she isha vesh' da-tor vi' wuh ass heh sahr-tor po' wuh vath, letting wuh dish k' wuh yarmok tevan fi' wuh solektra. Wuh skladasu hayal-tor ek' nash wak k' wuh vaksurik nu'ri t'sai, heh u' kling sarlah k' wuh yarmok heh she longed tor zahvan ish-veh, she leralmin-tor, 'i ri tor fai-tor wilat wuh yarmok mokuhlek nam-tor.' yi au nahp vel bolau ma pavesh-tor, heh leralmin-tor, 'i dungi hal-tor vi' wuh af'tum heh gla-tor.' heh u' au went gla-tor ish-veh dahkuh asses svi' wuh kelek sahran pa', heh wuh yarmok lying fi' wuh solektra. 'ek' gas'rak!' leralmin-tor au; 'eifa dahkuh ma had ish-veh thresh.' yi au nem-tor abru wuh shom t' wuh mor, laid au fi' wuh dish heh katau au tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, taran, 'i katau du wuh dish myself ik du lau ri bek-tor sovek longer.' ni she ate t' ish-veh, heh spo' wuh vath sahr-tor ska' vi' wuh kelek braying maf. Yi wuh huntsman pu-tor ish-veh limuk heh went vi' wuh kelek ik au lau fai-tor ish-veh. 'i' du dungau nam-tor vlitau na' ish-veh roguery, ' leralmin-tor au; heh tied au ek' rehkuh tor wuh man-elakh heh nem-tor au bi' k' ish-veh till au sarlah tor wuh mill heh knocked na' wuh krani. 'ra's wuh tukh?' leralmin-tor wuh miller. 'i ma rehkuh tiresome beasts la', ' leralmin-tor wuh vath; 'kuv du dungi nem-tor au, mazhiv-kur-tor au yem-tukh heh tvi-shal, heh skasau au u' i var-tor du, i dungi vlitau du whatever du ya'akash.' 'k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ' leralmin-tor wuh miller; 'tonk'peh uf dungau i skasau au?' yi wuh huntsman leralmin-tor, 'mazhiv-kur-tor wuh hinek veh zhel rehkuh wak wuh gad heh hay wuh'wak; mazhiv-kur-tor wuh thurai (vi vesh' wuh dvinsu-maid) zhel wuh'wak wuh gad heh hay rehkuh wak; heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh youngest (vi vesh' wuh vaksurik t'sai) hay rehkuh wak wuh gad heh rai zhel': na' au kupi ri talal ish-veh svi' ish-veh khaf-spol ki' ish-veh beaten. Po' nash au went pla' tor wuh castle, wilat au afer-tor kanok-vei au aitlu. Ein gad po', wuh miller sarlah tor ish-veh heh var-tor ish-veh ik wuh hinek ass vesh' tevik; 'wuh vath dahkuh, ' leralmin-tor au, 'nam-tor alive heh yokul, tonk'peh nam-tor ni sorrowful ik au fam yehat kim-shah wu.' yi wuh huntsman pitied au, heh var-tor wuh miller tor yetur au pla' tor ish-veh, heh lu sarlah au, au mazhiv-kur-tor au ein t' wuh rom yarmok tor yokul. Heh wuh vaksurik nu'ri t'sai tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef fa' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, 'o dearest huntsman! Forgive me ek' wuh has-bosh i ma ovsoh du; t'nash-veh ko-mekh punekwitau me tor ish-veh, ish-veh vesh' tehnat t'nash-veh dungi, na' i kwon-hau-ov ashau du maut mau. Ish-veh wishing-tor-sai geldau abru svi' wuh tsorayek, heh u' na' wuh kushel's khaf-spol, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh du nuh'.' tonk'peh au leralmin-tor, 'potau ish-veh, ish-veh dungi nam-tor aishan wuh ka vel, na' i tvai tor tor du t'nash-veh ko-telsu.' ni au vesh' telik, heh ha-tor teretuhr maut kunling till au tev-tor. Wuh var t' wuh youth vi went forth tor oren-tor ra pthak vesh' wuh ac'ruth sa-mekh had dahkuh sa-fu, wuh tela'at t' vi vesh' klon heh sensible, heh kupi tor kanok-vei, tonk'peh wuh younger vesh' stupid heh kupi neither oren-tor il ken-tor sovek-vel, heh lu sutra gla-tor ish-veh au leralmin-tor: 'tra''s wuh katravahsu vi dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sa-mekh ein trouble!' lu sovek-vel had tor nam-tor ovsoh, ish-veh vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh tela'at vi vesh' punekwitau tor tor ish-veh; tonk'peh kuv ish-veh sa-mekh bade ish-veh zaprah sovek-vel lu ish-veh vesh' tab-ma, il svi' wuh mu-yor-wak, heh wuh yut pufulag-tor k'fai wuh churchyard, il sovek vath dismal shi, au kilko-tor: 'oh, rai sa-mekh, i'll ri hal-tor tra', ish-veh tor me ak'shem-hutau!' na' au vesh' kwes. Il lu var vesh' var-tor k' wuh yon na' mu-yor if tor wuh kahm creep, wuh listeners sometimes leralmin-tor: 'oh, ish-veh tor etek ak'shem-hutau!' wuh younger hayal-tor svi' wuh teruk heh shroi k' wuh shom t' au, heh kupi ri glenonau ra au kupi tvai. 'au nam-tor kwon-hau-ov taran: "ish-veh tor me ak'shem-hutau, ish-veh tor me ak'shem-hutau!" ish-veh tor ri tor me ak'shem-hutau, ' nahp au. 'ik, nuh', bolau nam-tor wuh tanaf t' if i ken-tor nothing!' i' sarlah ish-veh tor be' dvun ik ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh veh gad: 'hearken tor me, du katravahsu svi' wuh teruk tra', du nam-tor growing ha-vol heh karik, heh du nuh' bolau oren-tor vel k' if du mokuhlek pinkau ish-veh kap. Glazhau uf ish-veh sa-kai ar'kada, tonk'peh du ri tor kauk pinkau ish-veh alem.' 'muhl, sa-mekh, ' au kilko-tor, 'i am ved willing tor oren-tor vel--indeed, kuv ish-veh kupi tonk'peh nam-tor khartau, i dang spo' tor oren-tor uf tor ak'shem-hutau. I ri tor ken-tor ik na' ek' wi.' wuh tela'at sa-kai abru'teruklar-ru'lut lu au puzhu-tor ik, heh nahp tor himself: 'goodness, ra wuh blockhead ik sa-kai t' t'nash-veh nam-tor! Au dungi worla nam-tor rom na' sovek-vel u' wu u' au ha-tor! Au vi aitlu tor nam-tor wuh el'urokesor bolau vulaya himself betimes.' wuh sa-mekh spes-tevan, heh kilko-tor ish-veh: 'du dungau ak oren-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor tor ak'shem-hutau, tonk'peh du dungi ri pinkau ish-veh kap k' ik.' ak po' nash wuh sexton sarlah tor wuh kelek fi' wuh yaret, heh wuh sa-mekh bewailed ish-veh trouble, heh var-tor ish-veh uf ish-veh younger sa-fu vesh' ni pla'rak svi' kanok respect ik au fai-tor nothing heh oren-tor nothing. 'aishan nah-tor, ' leralmin-tor au, 'lu i ya'akash ish-veh uf au vesh' going tor pinkau ish-veh kap, au actually aitlu tor oren-tor tor ak'shem-hutau.' 'kuv ik nam-tor ek', ' kilko-tor wuh sexton, 'au mokuhlek oren-tor ik k' me. Satau ish-veh tor me, heh i dungi ak polish ish-veh.' wuh sa-mekh vesh' glad tor tor ish-veh, na' au nahp: 'ish-veh dungi ranau wuh sa-kan wuh pi'.' wuh sexton therefore nem-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh kelek, heh au had tor mokov wuh church kus-vakh. Po' wuh gad il dahkuh, wuh sexton awoke ish-veh na' midnight, heh bade ish-veh arise heh hal-tor abru vi' wuh church kispek heh mokov wuh kus-vakh. 'du dungau ak oren-tor ra shuddering nam-tor, ' nahp au, heh secretly went tra' fa' ish-veh; heh lu wuh sa-kan vesh' na' wuh fik t' wuh kispek heh da-tor pauk, heh vesh' aishan going tor nem-tor meskaraya t' wuh kus-vakh man-elakh, gla-tor ish-veh wuh wan-kur khlop standing fi' wuh kaiden mesyutik wuh sounding razh. 'vi nam-tor tra'?' maf-tor au, tonk'peh wuh khlop tor rai kilko, heh did ri dvun il stir. 'mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kilko-srashiv, ' maf-tor wuh sa-kan, 'il nem-tor yourself ska', du ma rai business la' na' mu-yor.' wuh sexton, however, hafau standing motionless ik wuh sa-kan lau nah-tor au vesh' wuh tam'a. Wuh sa-kan maf-tor wuh dahr wak: 'ra tor du aitlun la'?--stariben kuv du nam-tor wuh trau katravahsu, il i dungi lehm du ne' wuh ash-tor!' wuh sexton nahp: 'au mokuhlek't tvai tor nam-tor u' rasahkos u' ish-veh zhit, ' uttered rai ralash heh lam-tor u' kuv au vesh' tor t' kov. Yi wuh sa-kan puvutau tor ish-veh na' wuh wuh wak, heh u' ik vesh' isha tor rai lof, au sahr-tor tehnat ish-veh heh kwitau wuh tam'a ne' wuh kaiden, ni ik ish-veh tevan-tor ne' wuh lehkuh ash-tor heh hafau lying tra' svi' wuh teruk. Thereupon au rang wuh kus-vakh, went ha-kel, heh rik' taran wuh zhit went tor sar-tak, heh tevan-tor asleep. Wuh sexton's ko-telsu bek-tor wuh akarshif na' ish-veh sa-telsu, tonk'peh au did ri sarlah pla'. Na' wu-vath she became uneasy, heh wakened wuh sa-kan, heh ya'akash: 'tor du fai-tor wilat t'nash-veh sa-telsu nam-tor? Au sasu-tor abru wuh kispek fa' du did.' 'rai, i ri tor fai-tor, ' kilko-tor wuh sa-kan, 'tonk'peh ein-veh vesh' standing k' wuh sounding razh fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh ash-tor, heh u' au would neither mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kilko-srashiv il hal-tor maf, i nem-tor ish-veh na' wuh scoundrel, heh threw ish-veh downstairs. Aishan hal-tor tra' heh du dungi gla-tor kuv ish-veh vesh' au. I dang nam-tor sorry kuv ish-veh vesh'.' wuh kosu sahr-tor maf heh afer-tor ish-veh sa-telsu, vi vesh' lying moaning svi' wuh teruk, heh had pushau ish-veh mal. She lesh ish-veh ne', heh yi k' ral shei she hastened tor wuh sa-kan's sa-mekh, 'ish-veh sa-kan, ' maf-tor she, 'has vesh' wuh aishan t' wuh lo'uk misfortune! Au has lehm-tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu ne' wuh ash-tor ni ik au shau ish-veh mal. Nem-tor wuh rom-na'-nothing katravahsu s' etwel kelek.' wuh sa-mekh vesh' terrified, heh sahr-tor thither heh scolded wuh sa-kan. 'ra wicked tricks nam-tor aifa?' leralmin-tor au. 'wuh e'shua bolau ma shitau au vi' ish-veh patam.' 'sa-mekh, ' au kilko-tor, 'tor shroi tor me. I am ved innocent. Au vesh' standing tra' k' mu-yor spo' veh intent fi' doing ek'rasah. I did ri fai-tor vi ish-veh vesh', heh i entreated ish-veh rehkuh wak either tor stariben il tor hal-tor maf.' 'ah, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-mekh, 'i ma nothing tonk'peh unhappiness k' du. Hal-tor s' t'nash-veh glan. Dungi gla-tor nash-veh du rai weht.' 'ha, sa-mekh, gas'rak willingly, bek-tor goh abi' ish-veh nam-tor gad. Yi dungi i hal-tor forth heh oren-tor uf tor ak'shem-hutau, heh yi i dungau, na' sovek tav, ken-tor veh tanaf if dungi nenikaya me.' 'oren-tor ra du dungi, ' stariben wuh sa-mekh, 'ish-veh nam-tor ek' wuh ka tor me. La' nam-tor kau-leh talers na' du. Nem-tor aifa heh hal-tor vi' wuh eik panu, heh var-tor kling s' whence du sarlah, heh vi nam-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, na' i ma utvau tor nam-tor kafusik t' du.' 'ha, sa-mekh, ish-veh dungau nam-tor u' du dungi. Kuv du aitlun nothing weht do ik, i mokuhlek easily potau ish-veh svi' kashek.' lu wuh gad dawned, therefore, wuh sa-kan shitau ish-veh kau-leh talers vi' ish-veh abru'lik, heh went forth fi' wuh lo'uk yut, heh continually leralmin-tor tor himself: 'kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau! Kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau!' yi wuh sasu betau vi puzhu-tor nash conversation if wuh youth vesh' holding k' himself, heh lu au had lates-tor wuh pi' weh-irak tor wilat au kupi gla-tor wuh geld-stau-nentu, wuh sasu leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'glazhau, tra' nam-tor wuh lap wilat stehkuh sasu ma telik wuh ropemaker's ko-fu, heh nam-tor i' learning uf tor hash-tor. Hayal-tor ne' ne'rak ish-veh, heh bek-tor till mu-yor sarlah, heh du dungi ak oren-tor uf tor ak'shem-hutau.' 'kuv ik nam-tor ek' ik nam-tor aitlu, ' kilko-tor wuh youth, 'ish-veh nam-tor easily ovsoh; tonk'peh kuv i oren-tor uf tor ak'shem-hutau u' sahris u' ik, du dungau ma t'nash-veh kau-leh talers. Aishan sarlah pla' tor me lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal.' yi wuh youth went tor wuh geld-stau-nentu, hayal-tor ne' ne'rak ish-veh, heh bek-tor till khru sarlah. Heh u' au vesh' samu, au lighted himself wuh yon, tonk'peh na' midnight wuh salan blew ni sharply ik svi' spite t' ish-veh yon, au kupi ri prah lamekh. Heh u' wuh salan knocked wuh geldau sasu tehnat tik vath, heh au dvun-tor pla'rak heh fa'rak, au nahp tor himself: 'kuv du shiver ne' k' wuh yon, uf eifa abru abru' bolau le-sumaya heh dash!' heh u' au olau pity na' au, au ashenau wuh pu'uth, heh sasu-tor abru, unbound veh t' au po' wuh vath, heh katau ne' ek' stehkuh. Yi au stoked wuh yon, blew ish-veh, heh eku au ek' pauk ish-veh tor lamekh themselves. Tonk'peh au hayal-tor tra' heh did ri stir, heh wuh yon kum-tor ish-veh sai-vel. Ni au leralmin-tor: 'nem-tor tun, il i dungi geldau du abru va'ashiv.' wuh tevik sasu, however, did ri zhu-tor, tonk'peh vesh' ved ralash-fam, heh kal-tor ish-veh a'cit hal-tor fi' yontau. Na' nash au grew reshnek, heh leralmin-tor: 'kuv du dungi ri nem-tor tun, i fam yehat gol'nev du, i dungi ri nam-tor yontau k' du, ' heh au geldau au abru va'ashiv tik svi' ish-veh da-tor. Yi au hayal-tor ne' k' ish-veh yon heh tevan-tor asleep, heh wuh thurai asal wuh sasu sarlah tor ish-veh heh aitlu ki' wuh kau-leh talers, heh leralmin-tor: 'muhl tor du fai-tor uf tor ak'shem-hutau?' 'rai, ' kilko-tor au, 'uf dang i fai-tor? Eifa katravahsu abru tra' did ri tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut, heh vesh' ni stupid ik au kal-tor wuh zamu hinek a'cit if au had fi' ish-veh ak'shem prah yontau.' yi wuh sasu gla-tor ik au would ri prah wuh kau-leh talers ik gad, heh went maf taran: 'such wuh youth has worla sarlah t'nash-veh yut fa'.' wuh youth likewise went ish-veh yut, heh wuh'wak weht began tor mutter tor himself: 'ah, kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau! Ah, kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau!' wuh waggoner vi vesh' striding za' ish-veh puzhu-tor nash heh ya'akash: 'vi nam-tor du?' 'i ri tor fai-tor, ' kilko-tor wuh youth. Yi wuh waggoner ya'akash: 's' whence tor sarlah du?' 'i fai-tor ri.' 'vi nam-tor ish-veh sa-mekh?' 'ik i lau ri var-tor du.' 'ra nam-tor ish-veh ik du nam-tor kwon-hau-ov muttering svi' ish-veh zud?' 'ah, ' kilko-tor wuh youth, 'i tor ni istaya i kupi ak'shem-hutau, tonk'peh kling mokuhlek saven-tor me uf.' 'hiyet t' ish-veh duhik chatter, ' leralmin-tor wuh waggoner. 'sarlah, hal-tor k' me, dungi gla-tor nash-veh pa' wuh shi na' du.' wuh youth went k' wuh waggoner, heh svi' wuh khru au lasha na' wuh ha-shal wilat au istau tor be' dvun wuh mu-yor. Yi na' wuh entrance t' wuh parlour wuh youth va'ashiv leralmin-tor ved loudly: 'kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau! Kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau!' wuh kasu vi puzhu-tor nash, abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh leralmin-tor: 'kuv ik nam-tor ish-veh aitlun, tra' ought tor nam-tor wuh rom opportunity na' du la'.' 'ah, nam'uh ralash-fam, ' leralmin-tor wuh hostess, 'ni wehk prying persons ma already pakik ish-veh ha-tor, ish-veh would nam-tor wuh pity heh wuh mesh kuv such vaksurik bezhun u' aifa dang worla gla-tor wuh gad-ha'khlup va'ashiv.' tonk'peh wuh youth leralmin-tor: 'however rihagik ish-veh lau nam-tor, i dungi oren-tor ish-veh. Na' nash lof indeed ma i halovau forth.' au kal-tor wuh kasu ma rai shom, abi' wuh latter var-tor ish-veh, ik ri irak s' thence lam-tor wuh haunted castle wilat sovek-veh kupi maut easily oren-tor ra shuddering vesh', kuv au would tonk'peh glantau svi' ish-veh na' rehkuh mu-yor. Wuh sa-te'kru had ugau ik au vi would venture dang ma ish-veh ko-fu tor ko-telsu, heh she vesh' wuh danik vaksurik maiden wuh yel min-tor fi'. Likewise svi' wuh castle ti lo'uk treasures, if vesh' klashau k' ek'rasah tam'a, heh aifa treasures would yi nam-tor el-tor, heh would tor wuh ri donku-tor sasu don-ka hiyet. Already wehk sasu had hal-tor vi' wuh castle, tonk'peh u' wi rim had sasarlah va'ashiv. Yi wuh youth went thurai asal tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh leralmin-tor: 'kuv ish-veh nam-tor kal-tor, i dungi willingly glantau rehkuh mu-yor svi' wuh haunted castle.' wuh sa-te'kru glazhau na' ish-veh, heh u' wuh youth sanoi ish-veh, au leralmin-tor: 'du lau ya'akash na' rehkuh vel tor nem-tor vi' wuh castle k' du, tonk'peh au bolau nam-tor vel rik' ha'kiv.' yi au kilko-tor: 'yi i ya'akash na' wuh yon, wuh turning da-skrimek, heh wuh tresahk-tor-dohn k' wuh lipau.' wuh sa-te'kru had aifa vel lesh vi' wuh castle na' ish-veh du' wuh gad. Lu mu-yor vesh' bestan be', wuh youth went abru heh tor himself wuh ugelik yon svi' veh t' wuh tvi-shal, shitau wuh tresahk-tor-dohn heh lipau be' ish-veh, heh hayal-tor himself k' wuh turning-da-skrimek. 'ah, kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau!' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh i dungau ri oren-tor ish-veh la' either.' na' midnight au vesh' pa' tor poke ish-veh yon, heh u' au vesh' blowing ish-veh, vel maf-tor suddenly s' veh teruk: 'au, miau! Uf samu etek nam-tor!' 'du duhsu!' maf-tor au, 'ra nam-tor du maf-tor pa'? Kuv du nam-tor samu, sarlah heh nem-tor wuh ku-san k' wuh yon heh lamekh yourselves.' heh lu au had leralmin-tor ik, dahkuh lo'uk nesh-kur aushfa sarlah k' veh tremendous leap heh hayal-tor ne' fi' tik vla t' ish-veh, heh glazhau savagely na' ish-veh k' ish-veh yonalik bezhun. Po' wuh pen wak, lu au had warmed themselves, au leralmin-tor: 'comrade, dungau etek ma wuh zhagra t' nop?' 'po ri?' au kilko-tor, 'tonk'peh aishan gluvaya me ish-veh paws.' yi au sakadau si' ish-veh spahk. 'oh, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ra wu felu du ma! Bek-tor, i bolau wuh'rak tresahk au na' du.' thereupon au seized au k' wuh drahk, shitau au fi' wuh tresahk-tor-dohn heh screwed ish-veh ash'ya sahris. 'i ma glazhau na' ish-veh ozh, ' leralmin-tor au, 'heh t'nash-veh fancy na' nop-mavaun has hal-tor, ' heh au kwul-tor au tevik heh threw au si' vi' wuh masu. Tonk'peh lu au had tor maf k' aifa dahkuh, heh vesh' pa' tor hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv k' ish-veh yon, si' s' kanok razh heh teruk sarlah nesh-kur aushfa heh nesh-kur dogs k' yon-kur-fal naf-elakh, heh weht heh weht t' au sarlah abi' au kupi rai longer dvun, heh au saul-tor horribly, heh prah fi' ish-veh yon, seshau ish-veh tor krus, heh ar'kada tor shitau ish-veh si'. Au glantau au na' wuh du' quietly, tonk'peh na' kim-shah lu au vesh' going nuh' irak, au seized ish-veh tresahk-tor-lipau, heh maf-tor: 'maf k' du, vermin, ' heh began tor tresahk au ne'. Ein t' au sahr-tor maf, wuh vath au pustau, heh threw si' vi' wuh aluk-muzh. Lu sarlah ish-veh pla' au fanned wuh kilyon t' ish-veh yon va'ashiv heh warmed himself. Heh u' au thus hayal-tor, ish-veh bezhun would potau tu'ash rai longer, heh au olau wuh aitlun tor yuk. Yi au glazhau pauk heh gla-tor wuh lo'uk sar-tak svi' wuh teruk. 'ik nam-tor wuh maut vel na' me, ' leralmin-tor au, heh prah vi' ish-veh. Lu au vesh' aishan going tor ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun, however, wuh sar-tak began tor dvun t' its sha' accord, heh went abru' wuh bosh t' wuh castle. 'ik's gas'rak, ' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh hal-tor faster.' yi wuh sar-tak padukau fi' u' kuv shehkuh jarel vesh' harnessed tor ish-veh, abru heh ne', abru' thresholds heh kaiden, tonk'peh suddenly spen-tor, spen-tor, ish-veh da-tor abru' upside ne', heh ti fi' ish-veh spo' wuh suk'kunel. Tonk'peh au threw quilts heh trak abru svi' wuh sov, prah si' heh leralmin-tor: 'i' sovek-veh vi tishau, lau yetur, ' heh ti ne' k' ish-veh yon, heh yuk-tor till ish-veh vesh' gad. Svi' wuh asal wuh sa-te'kru sarlah, heh lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh lying tra' fi' wuh solektra, au nahp wuh ek'rasah tam'a had pustau ish-veh heh au vesh' tevik. Yi leralmin-tor au: 'po' ek' ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity, --na' ni handsome wuh sasu.' wuh youth puzhu-tor ish-veh, prah abru, heh leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh has ri sarlah tor ik wi.' yi wuh sa-te'kru vesh' astonished, tonk'peh maut glad, heh ya'akash uf au had panavau. 'maut muhl indeed, ' kilko-tor au; 'veh mu-yor nam-tor vesht, wuh dahkuh vath dungi be' dvun likewise.' yi au went tor wuh innkeeper, vi tu'ash ish-veh bezhun maut eik, heh leralmin-tor: 'i worla gishu tor gla-tor du alive va'ashiv! Ma du oren-tor uf tor ak'shem-hutau wi?' 'rai, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ish-veh nam-tor ek' svi' vain. Kuv ein-veh would tonk'peh var-tor me!' wuh dahr mu-yor au va'ashiv went abru vi' wuh hinek castle, hayal-tor ne' k' wuh yon, heh wuh'wak weht began ish-veh hinek song: 'kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau!' lu midnight sarlah, wuh uproar heh ralash t' tumbling pa' vesh' puzhu-tor; na' wuh'rak ish-veh vesh' neik, tonk'peh ish-veh grew louder heh louder. Yi ish-veh vesh' hizhuk na' wuh du', heh na' wu-vath k' wuh ral shei, ulef wuh sasu sarlah ne' wuh vuzh-mev heh tevan-tor fa' ish-veh. 'hullo!' maf-tor au, 'wuh'ashiv ulef belongs tor nash. Nash nam-tor ri hiyet!' yi wuh uproar began va'ashiv, tra' vesh' wuh roaring heh howling, heh wuh vath ulef tevan-tor ne' likewise. 'bek-tor, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i dungi aishan stoke abru wuh yon wuh pi' na' du.' lu au had ovsoh ik heh glazhau pauk va'ashiv, wuh dahkuh krus vesh' terau, heh wuh hideous sasu vesh' sitting svi' ish-veh shi. 'ik nam-tor rai krus t' etwel bargain, ' leralmin-tor wuh youth, 'wuh wu-ku-san nam-tor t'nash-veh.' wuh sasu aitlu tor kwitaya ish-veh maf; wuh youth, however, would ri kal-tor ik, tonk'peh kwit ish-veh ska' k' ek' ish-veh karik'es, heh hayal-tor himself va'ashiv svi' ish-veh sha' shi. Yi fam dvun weht sasu tevan-tor ne', veh po' wuh vath; au katau naukuh tevik sasu's mal heh dahkuh grat, heh eku au abru heh mavau na' naukuh-pins k' au. Wuh youth isha aitlu tor mavau heh leralmin-tor: 'shroi du, mokuhlek i hau du?' 'ha, kuv du ma sovek donku.' 'donku hiyet, ' kilko-tor au, 'tonk'peh ish-veh rin'k'n nam-tor ri ved pauk.' yi au nem-tor wuh grat heh shitau au svi' wuh da-skrimek heh da-tor au till au vesh' pauk. 'tra', i' au dungi padukau weh-rom!' leralmin-tor au. 'hurrah! I' etek'll ma mihrsh!' au mavau k' au heh pakik ein t' ish-veh donku, tonk'peh lu ish-veh kwul-tor leh-dah, kanok-vei vanished s' ish-veh glan. Au ti ne' heh quietly tevan-tor asleep. Thurai asal wuh sa-te'kru sarlah tor inquire po' ish-veh. 'uf has ish-veh panavau k' du nash wak?' ya'akash au. 'i ma vesh' mavaun na' naukuh-pins, ' au kilko-tor, 'heh ma pakik wuh couple t' farthings.' 'ma du ri ak'shem-hutau yi?' 'ra?' leralmin-tor au, 'i ma had wuh wonderful wak! Kuv i did tonk'peh fai-tor ra ish-veh vesh' tor ak'shem-hutau!' wuh wuh mu-yor au hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv fi' ish-veh wu-ku-san heh leralmin-tor ved sadly: 'kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau.' lu ish-veh grew tab-ma, shehkuh ha-vol sasu sarlah svi' heh katau wuh tevikeh-natuhn. Yi au leralmin-tor: 'ha, ha, ik nam-tor certainly t'nash-veh pi' krei, vi tev-tor goh wuh zamu gad ago, ' heh au beckoned k' ish-veh ozh, heh maf-tor: 'sarlah, pi' krei, sarlah.' au shitau wuh tevikeh-natuhn fi' wuh solektra, tonk'peh au went tor ish-veh heh nem-tor wuh lid ska', heh wuh tevik sasu ti therein. Au olau ish-veh limuk, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' samu u' le-suma. 'bek-tor, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i dungi lamekh du wuh pi', ' heh went tor wuh yon heh warmed ish-veh el'ru heh laid ish-veh fi' wuh tevik sasu's limuk, tonk'peh au hafau samu. Yi au nem-tor ish-veh si', heh hayal-tor ne' k' wuh yon heh laid ish-veh fi' ish-veh thasek heh tetau ish-veh kar ik wuh khaf lau da-kuvau va'ashiv. U' nash isha did rai rom, au nahp tor himself: 'lu dahkuh sutra ti svi' sar-tak teretuhr, au lamekh tik vath, ' heh lesh ish-veh tor wuh sar-tak, wein-tor ish-veh abru' heh ti ne' k' ish-veh. Po' wuh pen wak wuh tevik sasu became lamekh nuh', heh began tor dvun. Yi leralmin-tor wuh youth, 'gla-tor, pi' krei, ma i ri warmed du?' wuh tevik sasu, however, prah abru heh maf-tor: 'i' dungi i strangle du.' 'ra!' leralmin-tor au, 'nam-tor ik wuh yut du itaren me? Du dungau na' wuh'wak hal-tor vi' ish-veh tevikeh-natuhn va'ashiv, ' heh au nem-tor ish-veh abru, threw ish-veh vi' ish-veh, heh ikap-tor wuh lid. Yi sarlah wuh shehkuh sasu heh lesh ish-veh maf va'ashiv. 'i fam yehat khartau tor ak'shem-hutau, ' leralmin-tor au. 'i dungau worla oren-tor ish-veh la' u' wu u' i ha-tor.' yi wuh sasu svi-tor vi vesh' taller do ek' vath, heh glazhau terrible. Au vesh' hinek, however, heh had wuh wu wan-kur hisahk. 'du wretch, ' maf-tor au, 'du dungau ak oren-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor tor ak'shem-hutau, na' du dungau tev-tor.' 'ri ni sahris, ' kilko-tor wuh youth. 'kuv i am tor tev-tor, i dungau ma ki' wuh leralmin svi' ish-veh.' 'i dungi ak seize du, ' leralmin-tor wuh shaka. 'softly, softly, ri tor variben ni suk'. I am u' karik u' du nam-tor, heh sos'eh kauk stronger.' 'etek dungau gla-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu. 'kuv du nam-tor stronger, i dungi kal-tor du hal-tor--sarlah, etek dungi ar'kadan.' yi au pufulag-tor ish-veh k' gu'gelik tvur tor wuh zhuksu's zhuk-fasek, nem-tor wuh la'ash, heh k' veh salur kwul-tor wuh mah-vihpan vi' wuh solektra. 'i mokuhlek tor weh-rom do ik, ' leralmin-tor wuh youth, heh went tor wuh vath mah-vihpan. Wuh hinek sasu shitau himself be' heh aitlu tor glazhau fi', heh ish-veh wan-kur hisahk geldau ne'. Yi wuh youth seized wuh la'ash, thresh wuh mah-vihpan k' veh salur, heh svi' ish-veh kum-tor wuh hinek sasu's hisahk. 'i' i ma du, ' leralmin-tor wuh youth. 'i' ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh da-tor tor tev-tor.' yi au seized wuh shek-tukh mofek heh kuhsh-tor wuh hinek sasu till au nau heh entreated ish-veh tor pehkaya, lu au would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh lo'uk don-tak. Wuh youth drew si' wuh la'ash heh kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor. Wuh hinek sasu pufulag-tor ish-veh pla' vi' wuh castle, heh svi' wuh cellar gluvau ish-veh rehkuh tuf bosh t' pi-maat-tukh. 't' aifa, ' leralmin-tor au, 'veh krus nam-tor na' wuh ri donku-tor, wuh vath na' wuh sa-te'kru, wuh wuh ish-veh.' svi' wuh meantime ish-veh kwul-tor leh-dah, heh wuh tam'a sasaudau, ni ik wuh youth lam-tor svi' mu'khlup'es. 'i dungau fam dvun nam-tor kup tor talal t'nash-veh yut si', ' leralmin-tor au, heh olau pa', afer-tor wuh yut vi' wuh tvi-shal, heh yuk-tor tra' k' ish-veh yon. Thurai asal wuh sa-te'kru sarlah heh leralmin-tor: 'i' du bolau ma oren-tor ra shuddering nam-tor?' 'rai, ' au kilko-tor; 'ra mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor? T'nash-veh tevik krei vesh' la', heh wuh bearded sasu sarlah heh gluvau me wuh lo'uk deal t' donku ne' ne', tonk'peh kling var-tor me ra ish-veh vesh' tor ak'shem-hutau.' 'yi, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru, 'du ma korsau wuh castle, heh dungau marry t'nash-veh ko-fu.' 'ik nam-tor ek' maut muhl, ' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh fam dvun i ri tor fai-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor tor ak'shem-hutau!' yi wuh pi-maat-tukh vesh' katau abru heh wuh wedding u'thet; tonk'peh howsoever mau wuh nu'ri sa-te'kru ashau ish-veh ko-telsu, heh however kunli au vesh', au fam dvun leralmin-tor kwon-hau-ov: 'kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau--kuv i kupi tonk'peh ak'shem-hutau.' heh nash na' kim-shah resha ish-veh. Ish-veh waiting-maid leralmin-tor: 'i dungi talal wuh bohrau na' ish-veh; au dungau ak oren-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor tor ak'shem-hutau.' she went si' tor wuh pilash if yumau k'fai wuh bah-ker, heh had wuh bosh bucketful t' gudgeons katau tor ish-veh. Na' mu-yor lu wuh nu'ri sa-te'kru vesh' sleeping, ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' tor bes-tor wuh sai-vel ska' ish-veh heh herbosh wuh mashuk bosh t' samu masu k' wuh gudgeons svi' ish-veh abru' ish-veh, ni ik wuh pi' aluk would sprawl pa' ish-veh. Yi au woke abru heh maf-tor: 'oh, ra tor me ak'shem-hutau ni?--ra tor me ak'shem-hutau ni, tal-kam ko-telsu? Ah! I' i fai-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor tor ak'shem-hutau!' sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk wuh lo'uk sa-te'kru t' wuh solektra irak maf svi' wuh she'rak had wuh ko-fu vi vesh' maut vaksurik, tonk'peh ni yaut, heh haughty, heh conceited, ik rim t' wuh princes vi sarlah tor ya'akash ish-veh svi' kal'i'farr vesh' rom hiyet na' ish-veh, heh she goh tor torvukh t' au. Wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh sa-te'kru meskarau wuh lo'uk gadzhak, heh ya'akash thither ek' ish-veh suitors; heh au ek' hayal-tor svi' wuh zehl, ranged fupa s' ish-veh lan--sa-te'kru, heh princes, heh dukes, heh earls, heh tum-tor, heh barons, heh knights. Yi wuh princess sarlah svi', heh u' she be' dvun-tor k' au she had vel spiteful tor leralmin tor kanok veh. Wuh wuh'rak vesh' nuh' thelik: 'au's u' pauk u' wuh matuhlek, ' leralmin-tor she. Wuh thurai vesh' nuh' ha-vol: 'ra wuh maypole!' leralmin-tor she. Wuh thurai vesh' nuh' pen: 'ra wuh dumpling!' leralmin-tor she. Wuh fourth vesh' nuh' spoh, heh she puvutau ish-veh 'wallface.' wuh fifth vesh' nuh' yon-kur, ni she puvutau ish-veh 'coxcomb.' wuh sixth vesh' ri zehik hiyet; ni she leralmin-tor au vesh' spo' wuh yar-kur terpau, ik had vesh' laid tor pseth abru' wuh leipausu's fasek. Heh thus she had ein kha'wal tor treshaya fi-tor kanok veh: tonk'peh she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor weht do ek' na' wuh rom sa-te'kru vi vesh' tra'. 'glazhau na' ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor she; 'ish-veh hisahk nam-tor spo' wuh hinek mop; au dungau nam-tor puvutau grisly-hisahk.' ni wuh sa-te'kru prah wuh re'hei t' grisly-hisahk. Tonk'peh wuh hinek sa-te'kru vesh' maut reshnek lu gla-tor ish-veh uf ish-veh ko-fu behaved, heh uf she has-bosh-skasau ek' ish-veh be'hai'la; heh au vowed ik, willing il unwilling, she dang marry wuh wuh'rak sasu, nam-tor au prince il beggar, ik sarlah tor wuh svep. Dahkuh gad po' tra' sarlah k' wuh travelling fiddler, vi began tor mavau ne' wuh krani heh eit'jae alms; heh lu wuh sa-te'kru puzhu-tor ish-veh, au leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor ish-veh sarlah svi'.' ni au katau svi' wuh kitork-looking katravahsu; heh lu au had uralau fa' wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh princess, au eit'jae wuh boon. Yi wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'du ma uralau ni muhl, ik i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du t'nash-veh ko-fu na' ish-veh ko-telsu.' wuh princess eit'jae heh prayed; tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'i ma sworn tor mazhiv-kur-tor du tor wuh wuh'rak comer, heh i dungi potau t'nash-veh zhit.' ni zhit heh bezhun-masu vesh' t' rai avail; wuh parson vesh' satau na', heh she vesh' telik tor wuh fiddler. Lu nash vesh' abru' wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'i' prah pok tor hal-tor--du bolau ri stay la'--du bolau haolvaya fi' k' ish-veh sa-telsu.' yi wuh fiddler went ish-veh yut, heh nem-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh, heh au ak sarlah tor wuh lo'uk lapan. 'pray, ' leralmin-tor she, 't'vi nam-tor nash lapan?' 'ish-veh belongs tor sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk, ' kilko-tor au; 'hadst thou taken ish-veh, ek' had vesh' thine.' 'ah! Unlucky wretch ik i am!' spes-tevan she; 'would ik i had telik sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk!' thurai sarlah au tor ein tok-ti ne-yartra. 't'vi nam-tor aifa vaksurik yar-kur ne-yartra?' leralmin-tor she. 'au belong tor sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk, hadst thou taken ish-veh, au had ek' vesh' thine.' 'ah! Unlucky wretch ik i am!' leralmin-tor she; 'would ik i had telik sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk!' yi sarlah au tor wuh lo'uk kahr. 't'vi nam-tor nash thol kahr?' leralmin-tor she. 'ish-veh t' sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk; hadst thou taken ish-veh, ish-veh had ek' vesh' thine.' 'ah! Wretch ik i am!' spes-tevan she; 'po did i ri marry sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk?' 'ik nam-tor rai business t' t'nash-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh fiddler: 'po dang du istaya na' wuh'ashiv sa-telsu? Am ri i rom hiyet na' du?' na' kim-shah sarlah au tor wuh pi' cottage. 'ra wuh paltry shi!' leralmin-tor she; 'tor ik tor ik pi' kitork razh belong?' yi wuh fiddler leralmin-tor, 'ik nam-tor ish-veh heh t'nash-veh kelek, wilat etek nam-tor tor ha-tor.' 'wilat nam-tor ish-veh dvinsu?' maf-tor she. 'ra tor etek aitlun k' dvinsu?' leralmin-tor au; 'du bolau tor na' yourself whatever nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh. I' tor wuh yon, heh shitau fi' masu heh fas-tor t'nash-veh mu'yor-yem, na' i am maut zungor.' tonk'peh wuh princess fai-tor nothing t' tor yon heh fasan, heh wuh fiddler vesh' punekwitau tor gol'nev ish-veh. Lu au had yokul wuh maut scanty yem au went tor sar-tak; tonk'peh wuh fiddler puvutau ish-veh abru maut lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal tor sok'i wuh kelek. Thus au ha-tor na' dahkuh gad: heh lu au had yokul abru ek' tra' vesh' svi' wuh cottage, wuh sasu leralmin-tor, 'ko-telsu, etek mokuhlek't hal-tor fi' thus, spending donku heh earning nothing. Du bolau oren-tor tor pris-tor ki'haf.' yi au went si' heh tresahk willows, heh katau au ha-kel, heh she began tor pris-tor; tonk'peh ish-veh tor ish-veh ozh maut sival. 'gla-tor nash-veh nash ar'kadan skil-tor't tor, ' leralmin-tor au: 'ar'kadan heh padan; sos'eh du dungi tor ik weh-rom.' ni she hayal-tor ne' heh ar'kada tor padan; tonk'peh wuh og-elakh tresahk ish-veh sival ozh till wuh khaf sahr-tor. 'gla-tor i', ' leralmin-tor wuh fiddler, 'du nam-tor rom na' nothing; du mokuhlek tor rai ar'kadan: ra wuh bargain i ma prah! However, i'll ar'kadan heh eku abru wuh trade svi' sunil heh sunil, heh du dungau lamok svi' wuh mahr-kel heh makau au.' 'alas!' spes-tevan she, 'kuv sovek t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh's kelek dang be' dvun k' heh gla-tor me standing svi' wuh mahr-kel, uf au dungi abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' me!' tonk'peh ish-veh sa-telsu did ri palutunau ik, heh leralmin-tor she bolau ar'kadan, kuv she did ri istaya tor tev-tor t' avon. Palikauk wuh trade went muhl; na' wehk sutra, seeing such wuh vaksurik kosu, went tor mahr-tor ish-veh wares, heh vlitau ish-veh donku rik' thinking t' taking maf wuh goods. Au ha-tor fi' nash u' wu u' ish-veh palesh-tor; heh yi ish-veh sa-telsu bought wuh sluk lot t' ware, heh she hayal-tor herself ne' k' ish-veh svi' wuh teruk t' wuh mahr-kel; tonk'peh wuh drunken ask'ersu ak sarlah k', heh fau-tor ish-veh jarel tehnat ish-veh stall, heh shau ek' ish-veh goods vi' wuh thousand krus. Yi she began tor maf, heh fai-tor ri ra tor tor. 'ah! Ra dungi shetau t' me?' leralmin-tor she; 'ra dungi t'nash-veh sa-telsu leralmin?' ni she sahr-tor ha-kel heh var-tor ish-veh ek'. 'vi would ma nahp du would ma vesh' ni silly, ' leralmin-tor au, 'u' tor shitau wuh earthenware stall svi' wuh teruk t' wuh mahr-kel, wilat kanok-veh be' dvun-tor? Tonk'peh kal-tor etek ma rai weht maf-tor; gla-tor nash-veh du nam-tor ri nunau na' nash wihfelau t' ar'kadan, ni i ma vesh' tor wuh sa-te'kru's palace, heh ya'akash kuv au did ri aitlun wuh af'tum-maid; heh au leralmin au dungi nem-tor du, heh tra' du dungi ma plenty tor yokul.' thus wuh princess became wuh af'tum-maid, heh gol-tor wuh fas-tor tor tor ek' wuh dirtiest ar'kadan; tonk'peh she vesh' kal-tor tor lesh ha-kel ein t' wuh kahm ik vesh' losrak, heh fi' nash au ha-tor. She had ri vesh' tra' wu fa' she puzhu-tor ik wuh sa-te'kru's eldest sa-fu vesh' be' dvun-tor k', going tor nam-tor telik; heh she went tor veh t' wuh krani heh glazhau si'. Kanok-vei vesh' pok, heh ek' wuh pomp heh ugel'es t' wuh kelek vesh' tra'. Yi she bitterly grieved na' wuh pride heh folly if had katau ish-veh ni neik. Heh wuh dvinsu mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ein t' wuh don-ka kahm, if she shitau vi' ish-veh ki'haf tor nem-tor ha-kel. Ek' fi' wuh sudden, u' she vesh' going si', svi' sarlah wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu svi' pi-maat-kur sai-vel; heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh vaksurik kosu na' wuh svep, au nem-tor ish-veh k' wuh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor she dang nam-tor ish-veh tersu svi' wuh tam; tonk'peh she trembled na' pthak, na' gla-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk, vi vesh' tor torvukh t' ish-veh. However, au potau sahris meskaraya, heh pufulag-tor ish-veh svi'; heh wuh wein t' wuh ki'haf sarlah ska', ni ik wuh kahm svi' ish-veh tevan-tor pa'. Yi kanok-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh jeered na' ish-veh; heh she vesh' ni abashed, ik she istau herself wuh thousand ash'ya glu svi' wuh terra. She sprang tor wuh svep tor sahr-tor maf; tonk'peh fi' wuh ash-tor sa-te'kru grisly-hisahk overtook ish-veh, heh katau ish-veh pla' heh leralmin-tor, 'pthak me ri! I am wuh fiddler vi has ha-tor k' du svi' wuh hut. I katau du tra' fai'ei i really ashau du. I am isha wuh ask'ersu ik overset ish-veh stall. I ma ovsoh ek' nash goh tor bohrau du t' ish-veh silly pride, heh tor gluvaya du wuh folly t' ish-veh has-bosh-skasaya t' me. I' ek' nam-tor abru': du ma oren-tor kau, heh ish-veh nam-tor wak tor meskaraya etwel kal'i'farr gadzhak.' yi wuh chamberlains sarlah heh katau ish-veh wuh danik vaksurik pelal; heh ish-veh sa-mekh heh ish-veh bosh kelek vesh' tra' already, heh welcomed ish-veh ha-kel fi' ish-veh kal'i'farr. Mak vesh' svi' kanok limuk heh kanok khaf-spol. Wuh gadzhak vesh' grand; au tam-tor heh sang; ek' vesh' merry; heh i goh istaya ik du heh i had vesh' t' wuh party. Shek-tukh hans tra' vesh' wuh'wak fi-tor wuh wak wuh sa-te'kru vi had wuh lo'uk laptra be' ish-veh palace, bosh t' ek' ves t' kwai animals. Veh gad au satau si' wuh huntsman tor pohshau ish-veh wuh roe, tonk'peh au did ri sarlah pla'. 'sos'eh ein kisheya has befallen ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru, heh wuh thurai gad au satau si' dahkuh weht huntsmen vi vesh' tor psthan na' ish-veh, tonk'peh au nuh' stayed maf. Yi fi' wuh wuh gad, au satau na' ek' ish-veh huntsmen, heh leralmin-tor: 'scour wuh bosh laptra k'fai, heh ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru abi' du ma afer-tor ek' rehkuh.' tonk'peh t' aifa isha, rim sarlah ha-kel va'ashiv, rim vesh' gla-tor va'ashiv. S' ik wak forth, kling would sovek longer venture vi' wuh laptra, heh ish-veh ti tra' svi' glu stillness heh awek'es, heh nothing vesh' gla-tor t' ish-veh, tonk'peh sometimes wuh eagle il wuh hawk hashan abru' ish-veh. Nash palesh-tor na' wehk tevun, lu wuh ri-fainu huntsman tor'pra himself tor wuh sa-te'kru u' seeking wuh situation, heh nufau tor hal-tor vi' wuh tehvar-bosh laptra. Wuh sa-te'kru, however, would ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh consent, heh leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh nam-tor ri safe svi' tra'; i pthak ish-veh would panavau k' du rai weh-rom do k' wuh vath, heh du would worla sasarlah va'ashiv.' wuh huntsman kilko-tor: 's'haile, i dungi venture ish-veh na' t'nash-veh sha' risk, t' pthak i fai-tor nothing.' wuh huntsman therefore betook himself k' ish-veh dog tor wuh laptra. Ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' wuh dog tevan-tor svi' k' ein zhagra fi' wuh yut, heh aitlu tor pursue ish-veh; tonk'peh hardly had wuh dog sahr-tor dahkuh ash-tor lu ish-veh lam-tor fa' wuh glu patra, kupi hal-tor rai weh-irak, heh wuh sai-fam kar sakadau itself s' wuh masu, seized ish-veh, heh drew ish-veh ne'. Lu wuh huntsman gla-tor ik, au went pla' heh zaprah rehkuh sasu tor sarlah k' mashuk heh bale si' wuh masu. Lu au kupi gla-tor tor wuh lanet tra' ti wuh kwai sasu t'vi ak'shem vesh' khav-kur spo' zhar-tor shek-tukh, heh t'vi isachya geldau abru' ish-veh limuk ne' tor ish-veh mal-nef. Au bound ish-veh k' elakh, heh pufulag-tor ish-veh maf tor wuh castle. Tra' vesh' lo'uk astonishment abru' wuh kwai sasu; wuh sa-te'kru, however, had ish-veh shitau svi' wuh shek-tukh kraisek svi' ish-veh courtyard, heh forbade wuh svep tor nam-tor tu'ash fi' kusut t' tevakh, heh wuh ko-te'kru herself vesh' tor nem-tor wuh tal-muv vi' ish-veh keeping. Heh s' nash wak forth kanok-veh kupi va'ashiv hal-tor vi' wuh laptra k' ek'manek. Wuh sa-te'kru had wuh sa-fu t' ohkuh tevun, vi vesh' wuh'wak mavaun svi' wuh courtyard, heh du' au vesh' mavaun, ish-veh pi-maat-kur rin'k'n tevan-tor vi' wuh kraisek. Wuh sa-kan sahr-tor thither heh leralmin-tor: 'mazhiv-kur-tor me t'nash-veh rin'k'n si'.' 'ri till du ma tu'ash wuh svep na' me, ' kilko-tor wuh sasu. 'rai, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-kan, 'i dungi ri tor ik; wuh sa-te'kru has zadik ish-veh, ' heh sahr-tor maf. Wuh thurai gad au va'ashiv went heh ya'akash na' ish-veh rin'k'n; wuh kwai sasu leralmin-tor: 'tu'ash t'nash-veh svep, ' tonk'peh wuh sa-kan would ri. Fi' wuh wuh gad wuh sa-te'kru had ridden si' hunting, heh wuh sa-kan went wuh'wak weht heh leralmin-tor: 'i fam yehat tu'ash wuh svep kauk kuv i istau, na' i ma ri wuh tal-muv.' yi wuh kwai sasu leralmin-tor: 'ish-veh ti ne' ish-veh ko-mekh's trak, du mokuhlek prah ish-veh tra'.' wuh sa-kan, vi aitlu ki' ish-veh rin'k'n pla', vishizhau ek' nahp tor wuh salan, heh katau wuh tal-muv. Wuh svep tu'ash k' rihag'es, heh wuh sa-kan k'hy ish-veh ozh. Lu ish-veh vesh' tu'ash wuh kwai sasu ash-tor si', mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh pi-maat-kur rin'k'n, heh hurried maf. Wuh sa-kan had shetau kwes; au puvutau heh maf-tor po' ish-veh: 'oh, kwai sasu, ri tor hal-tor maf, il i dungau nam-tor beaten!' wuh kwai sasu da-tor pla', nem-tor ish-veh abru, eku ish-veh fi' ish-veh tipan, heh went k' hasty ash-tor vi' wuh laptra. Lu wuh sa-te'kru sarlah ha-kel, au glantau wuh herbosh kraisek, heh ya'akash wuh ko-te'kru uf ik had pavesh-tor. She fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh, heh sought wuh tal-muv, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' hal-tor. She puvutau wuh sa-kan, tonk'peh kling kilko-tor. Wuh sa-te'kru satau si' sutra tor seek na' ish-veh svi' wuh vunai, tonk'peh au did ri talal ish-veh. Yi au kupi easily guess ra had pavesh-tor, heh mau tushat reigned svi' wuh royal kelek. Lu wuh kwai sasu had wuh'wak weht pulau wuh gu'gelik laptra, au nem-tor wuh sa-kan ne' s' ish-veh tipan, heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: 'du dungi worla gla-tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh va'ashiv, tonk'peh i dungi potau du k' me, na' du ma eku me elik, heh i ma utan'es fi' du. Kuv du tor ek' i nufai du, du dungau panavau muhl. T' treasure heh pi-maat-tukh ma i hiyet, heh weht do sovek-veh svi' wuh panu.' au tor wuh sar-tak t' yekuhl na' wuh sa-kan fi' if au yuk-tor, heh wuh thurai asal wuh sasu nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh muhl, heh leralmin-tor: 'behold, wuh pi-maat-tukh muhl nam-tor u' ugelik heh pa'shik u' khush, du dungau hayal-tor be' ish-veh, heh nem-tor tun ik nothing tevan-tor vi' ish-veh, il ish-veh dungi nam-tor flau. I dungi sarlah kanok khru tor gla-tor kuv du ma obeyed t'nash-veh zek.' wuh sa-kan shitau himself k' wuh rihk t' wuh muhl, heh k'ashiv gla-tor wuh pi-maat-kur aluk il wuh pi-maat-kur oluhk gluvaya itself therein, heh nem-tor tun ik nothing tevan-tor svi'. U' au vesh' thus sitting, ish-veh ozh dash-tor ish-veh ni violently ik au involuntarily shitau ish-veh svi' wuh masu. Au drew ish-veh sahris si' va'ashiv, tonk'peh gla-tor ik ish-veh vesh' ved gilded, heh whatsoever kusut-tor au nem-tor tor pu-tor wuh pi-maat-tukh ska' va'ashiv, ek' vesh' tor rai lof. Svi' wuh khru shek-tukh hans sarlah pla', glazhau na' wuh sa-kan, heh leralmin-tor: 'ra has pavesh-tor tor wuh muhl?' 'nothing nothing, ' au kilko-tor, heh meskarau ish-veh ozh za' ish-veh pla', ik wuh sasu lau ri gla-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh au leralmin-tor: 'du ma spis-tor ish-veh ozh vi' wuh masu, nash wak ish-veh lau be' dvun, tonk'peh nem-tor tun du ri tor va'ashiv kal-tor sovek-vel hal-tor svi'.' k' gad-keshtan wuh sa-kan vesh' already sitting k' wuh muhl heh watching ish-veh. Ish-veh ozh dash-tor ish-veh va'ashiv heh au be' dvun-tor ish-veh abru' ish-veh patam, heh yi unhappily wuh isachya tevan-tor ne' vi' wuh muhl. Au nem-tor ish-veh sahris si', tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' already ved gilded. Shek-tukh hans sarlah, heh already fai-tor ra had pavesh-tor. 'du ma kal-tor wuh isachya tevan vi' wuh muhl, ' leralmin-tor au. 'i dungi kal-tor du tor glantau k' ish-veh wuh'wak weht, tonk'peh kuv nash pavesh-tor na' wuh wuh wak yi wuh muhl nam-tor flau heh du mokuhlek rai longer hafau k' me.' fi' wuh wuh gad, wuh sa-kan hayal-tor k' wuh muhl, heh did ri stir ish-veh ozh, however mau ish-veh dash-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh wak vesh' wu tor ish-veh, heh au glazhau na' wuh haulan t' ish-veh limuk fi' wuh skonn t' wuh masu. Heh u' au fam dvun keh'sei ne' weht heh weht du' au vesh' doing ni, heh trying tor glazhau zehik vi' wuh bezhun, ish-veh wu isachya tevan-tor ne' s' ish-veh tipan vi' wuh masu. Au ashenau himself abru sahris, tonk'peh wuh bosh t' wuh isachya t' ish-veh patam vesh' already pi-maat-kur heh min-tor spo' wuh yel. Du mokuhlek glenonau uf terrified wuh ri donku-tor sa-kan vesh'! Au nem-tor ish-veh abru'lik-handkerchief heh tied ish-veh pauk ish-veh patam, svi' zek ik wuh sasu lau ri gla-tor ish-veh. Lu sarlah ish-veh au already fai-tor kanok-vei, heh leralmin-tor: 'nem-tor wuh handkerchief ska'.' yi wuh pi-maat-kur isachya salash forth, heh kal-tor wuh sa-kan tobeg himself u' au lau, ish-veh vesh' t' rai nam-tor-tor. 'du ma ri lam-tor wuh trial heh mokuhlek stay la' rai longer. Hal-tor forth vi' wuh panu, tra' du dungi oren-tor ra poverty nam-tor. Tonk'peh u' du ma ri wuh rasahkos khaf-spol, heh u' i tvai muhl k' du, tra' nam-tor veh vel i dungi vahl du; kuv du tevan vi' sovek rihag'es, sarlah tor wuh laptra heh maf: "shek-tukh hans, " heh yi dungi-sarlah nash-veh heh gol'nev du. T'nash-veh tepul nam-tor lo'uk, weht tor du nah-tor, heh i ma pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh svi' mau-yan.' yi wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu losrak wuh laptra, heh lates-tor k' beaten heh unbeaten yut ek'wak onwards abi' na' wu-vath au pulau wuh lo'uk kahr. Tra' au glazhau na' ar'kadan, tonk'peh kupi talal rim, heh au oren-tor nothing k' if au kupi gol'nev himself. Na' wu-vath au went tor wuh palace, heh ya'akash kuv au would nem-tor ish-veh svi'. Wuh sutra pa' kelek did mokov fai-tor ra nam-tor-tor au kupi tor t' ish-veh, tonk'peh au tishau ish-veh, heh var-tor ish-veh tor stay. Na' wu-vath wuh fas-tor nem-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh dvin, heh leralmin-tor au lau lesh lapan heh masu, heh dref wuh cinders teretuhr. Wuh'wak lu ish-veh ni pavesh-tor ik kling else vesh' na' el'ru, wuh fas-tor ordered ish-veh tor lesh wuh yem-tukh tor wuh royal pasu, tonk'peh u' au did ri spo' tor kal-tor ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya nam-tor gla-tor, au potau ish-veh pi' taik fi'. Such wuh vel u' ik had worla wi sarlah ne' wuh sa-te'kru's beglanau, heh au leralmin-tor: 'lu sarlah du tor wuh royal pasu du bolau nem-tor ish-veh taik ska'.' au kilko-tor: 'ah, s'haile, i fam yehat; i ma wuh rasahkos sival shi fi' t'nash-veh patam.' yi wuh sa-te'kru had wuh fas-tor puvutau fa' ish-veh heh scolded ish-veh, heh ya'akash uf au kupi nem-tor such wuh sa-kan u' ik vi' ish-veh dvin; heh ik au vesh' tor satau ish-veh maf na' wuh'wak. Wuh fas-tor, however, had pity fi' ish-veh, heh di'kizh-tor ish-veh na' wuh bahsu's sa-kan. Heh i' wuh sa-kan had tor kastik heh masu wuh bah-ker, hoe heh hil-tor, heh lesh wuh salan heh rasahkos igen-va. Wuh'wak svi' belaar lu au vesh' working sa'awek svi' wuh bah-ker, wuh gad vesh' ni lamekh au nem-tor ish-veh pi' taik ska' ik wuh sov lau samuyau ish-veh. U' wuh yel min-tor fi' ish-veh isachya ish-veh glittered heh kahai ni ik wuh ha'zehl tevan-tor vi' wuh shi'yuk t' wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, heh abru she sprang tor gla-tor ra ik kupi nam-tor. Yi gla-tor ish-veh wuh sa-kan, heh maf-tor tor ish-veh: 'sa-kan, katau me wuh wreath t' svai.' au shitau ish-veh taik fi' k' ek' haste, heh hoknau kwai vunai-svai heh bound au teretuhr. Lu au vesh' ascending wuh kaiden k' au, wuh bahsu ragel-tor ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: 'uf mokuhlek du nem-tor wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu wuh garland t' such tsuri svai? Hal-tor sahris, heh prah wuh'ashiv, heh seek si' wuh prettiest heh ritsuri.' 'oh, rai, ' kilko-tor wuh sa-kan, 'wuh kwai ones ma weht scent, heh dungi sanoi ish-veh weh-rom.' lu au prah vi' wuh tvi-shal, wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu leralmin-tor: 'nem-tor ish-veh taik ska', ish-veh nam-tor ri seemly tor potau ish-veh fi' svi' t'nash-veh la'es.' au va'ashiv leralmin-tor: 'i lau ri, i ma wuh sival patam.' she, however, kum-tor na' ish-veh taik heh seshau ish-veh ska', heh yi ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya padukau ne' fi' ish-veh tipan, heh ish-veh vesh' splendid tor behold. Au aitlu tor sahr-tor si', tonk'peh she meskarau ish-veh k' wuh kar, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh handful t' ducats. K' aifa au trashu, tonk'peh au tun-tor nothing na' wuh pi-maat-tukh krus. Au nem-tor au tor wuh bahsu, heh leralmin-tor: 'i la' au tor ish-veh kanu, au mokuhlek mavau k' au.' wuh zahalik gad wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu va'ashiv puvutau tor ish-veh ik au vesh' tor katau ish-veh wuh wreath t' vunai-svai, heh yi au went svi' k' ish-veh, she instantly snatched na' ish-veh taik, heh aitlu tor nem-tor ish-veh maf s' ish-veh, tonk'peh au meskarau ish-veh sahris k' fi' el'ru. She va'ashiv mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh handful t' ducats, tonk'peh au would ri potau au, heh mazhiv-kur-tor au tor wuh bahsu na' playthings na' ish-veh kanu. Fi' wuh wuh gad vel went aishan wuh ka; she kupi ri prah ish-veh taik maf s' ish-veh, heh au would ri ma ish-veh donku. Ri wu afterwards, wuh shasol vesh' overrun k' t'naehm. Wuh sa-te'kru hoknau teretuhr ish-veh sutra, heh did ri fai-tor whether il ri au kupi nufai sovek opposition tor wuh nemut, vi vesh' superior svi' karik'es heh had wuh mighty ya'akash'er. Yi leralmin-tor wuh bahsu's sa-kan: 'i am grown abru, heh dungi hal-tor tor wuh t'naehm isha, goh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh jarel.' wuh vath abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh leralmin-tor: 'seek veh na' yourself lu etek nam-tor hal-tor, etek dungi trasha veh za' etek svi' wuh tihet na' du.' lu au had hal-tor forth, au went vi' wuh tihet, heh pufulag-tor wuh jarel si'; ish-veh vesh' lame t' veh ash'ya, heh limped hobblety jib, hobblety jib; nevertheless au mounted ish-veh, heh fau-tor maf tor wuh gu'gelik laptra. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh outskirts, au puvutau 'shek-tukh hans' rehkuh wak ni loudly ik ish-veh echoed k'fai wuh lap. Thereupon wuh kwai sasu saudau iyi, heh leralmin-tor: 'ra tor du aitlun?' 'i aitlun wuh karik steed, na' i am going tor wuh t'naehm.'
