'ik du dungau ma, heh fam dvun weht do du ya'akash na'.' yi wuh kwai sasu went pla' vi' wuh laptra, heh ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' wuh tihet-sa-kan sasarlah t' ish-veh, vi pufulag-tor wuh jarel ik snorted k' its han-sharular, heh kupi hardly nam-tor restrained, heh za' au zahal-tor wuh lo'uk vus t' warriors entirely putanovau svi' shek-tukh, heh ish-veh shek kahai svi' wuh yel. Wuh youth tor abru' ish-veh rehkuh-legged jarel tor wuh tihet-sa-kan, mounted wuh vath, heh fau-tor na' wuh patam t' wuh ask'ersu. Lu au prah be' wuh battlefield wuh lo'uk krus t' wuh sa-te'kru's sasu had already tevan-tor, heh pi' vesh' wanting tor tor wuh shom mazhiv-kur-tor yut. Yi wuh youth ausahr-tor thither k' ish-veh shek-tukh ask'ersu, shau spo' wuh suk'masutra-eshu'a abru' wuh nemut, heh kuhsh-tor ne' ek' vi opposed ish-veh. Au began tor sasahr-tor, tonk'peh wuh youth pursued, heh worla pehkau, abi' tra' vesh' ri wuh single sasu losrak. Instead t' returning tor wuh sa-te'kru, however, au conducted ish-veh vus k' byways pla' tor wuh laptra, heh puvutau forth shek-tukh hans. 'ra tor du aitlun?' ya'akash wuh kwai sasu. 'nem-tor pla' ish-veh jarel heh ish-veh vus, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me t'nash-veh rehkuh-legged jarel va'ashiv.' ek' ik au ya'akash vesh' ovsoh, heh ak au vesh' riding fi' ish-veh rehkuh-legged jarel. Lu wuh sa-te'kru fun-tor tor ish-veh palace, ish-veh ko-fu went tor ragel-tor ish-veh, heh istau ish-veh mak t' ish-veh skil. 'i am ri wuh veh vi lesh maf wuh skil, ' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh wuh flekh kenelsu vi sarlah tor t'nash-veh assistance k' ish-veh ask'ersu.' wuh ko-fu aitlu tor zhu-tor vi wuh flekh kenelsu vesh', tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru did ri fai-tor, heh leralmin-tor: 'au zahal-tor wuh nemut, heh i did ri gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv.' she inquired t' wuh bahsu wilat ish-veh sa-kan vesh', tonk'peh au abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh leralmin-tor: 'au has aishan sarlah ha-kel fi' ish-veh rehkuh-legged jarel, heh wuh vath ma vesh' mocking ish-veh, heh maf-tor: "la' sarlah etwel hobblety jib pla' va'ashiv!" au ya'akash, nuh': "ne' ra labah ma du vesh' lying sleeping ek' wuh wak?" ni au leralmin-tor: "i did wuh buhfik t' ek', heh ish-veh would ma hal-tor badly rik' me." heh yi au vesh' fam dvun weht ridiculed.' wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor tor ish-veh ko-fu: 'i dungi afsakau wuh lo'uk gadzhak ik dungau kim-shah na' rehkuh gad, heh du dungau lehm wuh pi-maat-kur savas. Sos'eh wuh ri-fainu sasu dungi gluvaya himself.' lu wuh gadzhak vesh' tor'pra, wuh youth went si' tor wuh laptra, heh puvutau shek-tukh hans. 'ra tor du aitlun?' ya'akash au. 'ik i lau kum wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu's pi-maat-kur savas.' 'ish-veh nam-tor u' safe u' kuv du had ish-veh already, ' leralmin-tor shek-tukh hans. 'du dungau likewise ma wuh saikhut t' yon-kur fo-wein na' wuh occasion, heh fau fi' wuh spirited chestnut-jarel.' lu wuh gad sarlah, wuh youth ausahr-tor tor wuh gla-tor, nem-tor ish-veh shi svi' wuh knights, heh vesh' recognized k' kling. Wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu sarlah fa'rak, heh threw wuh pi-maat-kur savas tor wuh knights, tonk'peh rim t' au kum-tor ish-veh tonk'peh au, goh u' ak u' au had ish-veh au ausahr-tor maf. Fi' wuh dahr gad shek-tukh hans putanovau ish-veh u' wuh wan-kur kenelsu, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh wan-kur jarel. Va'ashiv au vesh' wuh goh veh vi kum-tor wuh savas, heh au did ri svizh-tor wuh instant, tonk'peh ausahr-tor ska' k' ish-veh. Wuh sa-te'kru grew reshnek, heh leralmin-tor: 'ik nam-tor ri kal-tor; au bolau saudau fa' me heh var-tor ish-veh ahm.' au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh zek ik kuv wuh kenelsu vi kum-tor wuh savas, dang hal-tor maf va'ashiv au dang pursue ish-veh, heh kuv au would ri sarlah pla' willingly, au vesh' tor tresahk ish-veh ne' heh stab ish-veh. Fi' wuh wuh gad, au poprah s' shek-tukh hans wuh saikhut t' nesh-kur fo-wein heh wuh nesh-kur jarel, heh va'ashiv au kum-tor wuh savas. Tonk'peh lu au vesh' riding ska' k' ish-veh, wuh sa-te'kru's attendants pursued ish-veh, heh veh t' au prah ni be' ish-veh ik au wounded wuh youth's mal k' wuh sfek t' ish-veh shek. Wuh youth nevertheless stron-tor s' au, tonk'peh ish-veh jarel leapt ni violently ik wuh helmet tevan-tor s' wuh youth's patam, heh au kupi gla-tor ik au had pi-maat-kur isachya. Au fau-tor pla' heh tor'pra nash tor wuh sa-te'kru. Wuh zahalik gad wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu ya'akash wuh bahsu pa' ish-veh sa-kan. 'au nam-tor na' ar'kadan svi' wuh bah-ker; wuh queer creature has vesh' na' wuh gad-muf nuh', heh goh sarlah ha-kel za-gad khru; au has likewise shown t'nash-veh kanu rehkuh pi-maat-kur savas if au has skil-tor.' wuh sa-te'kru had ish-veh summoned vi' ish-veh la'es, heh sarlah ish-veh heh va'ashiv had ish-veh pi' taik fi' ish-veh patam. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu went abru tor ish-veh heh nem-tor ish-veh ska', heh yi ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya tevan-tor ne' abru' ish-veh tipan, heh au vesh' ni handsome ik ek' vesh' putaurau. 'nam-tor du wuh kenelsu vi sarlah kanok gad tor wuh gad-muf, kwon-hau-ov svi' natya colours, heh vi kum-tor wuh rehkuh pi-maat-kur savas?' ya'akash wuh sa-te'kru. 'ha, ' kilko-tor au, 'heh la' wuh savas nam-tor, ' heh au nem-tor au s' ish-veh abru'lik, heh fun-tor au tor wuh sa-te'kru. 'kuv du aitlun further skan, du lau gla-tor wuh skek if ish-veh sutra mazhiv-kur-tor me lu au zahal-tor me. Tonk'peh i am likewise wuh kenelsu vi gol-tor du tor ish-veh skil abru' ish-veh nemut.' 'kuv du mokuhlek perform such deeds u' ik, du nam-tor rai bahsu's sa-kan; var-tor me, vi nam-tor ish-veh sa-mekh?' 't'nash-veh sa-mekh nam-tor wuh mighty sa-te'kru, heh pi-maat-tukh ma i svi' plenty u' lo'uk u' i require.' 'i muhl gla-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru, 'ik i owe t'nash-veh itaren tor du; mokuhlek i tor sovek-vel tor sanoi du?' 'ha, ' kilko-tor au, 'ik indeed du mokuhlek. Mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh ko-fu tor ko-telsu.' wuh maiden abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh leralmin-tor: 'au tor ri lamok mau fi' hali-kal, tonk'peh i ma already gla-tor k' ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya ik au vesh' rai bahsu's sa-kan, ' heh yi she went heh shok-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh sarlah tor wuh wedding, heh vesh' svi' lo'uk delight, na' au had putan-tor abru ek' rok t' ek'wak seeing ish-veh tal-kam sa-fu va'ashiv. Heh u' au vesh' sitting na' wuh kal'i'farr-gadzhak, wuh ralash-tanaf suddenly pehkau, wuh svep tu'ash, heh wuh stately sa-te'kru sarlah svi' k' wuh lo'uk retinue. Au went abru tor wuh youth, nartau ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: 'i am shek-tukh hans, heh vesh' k' enchantment wuh kwai sasu, tonk'peh du ma eku me elik; ek' wuh treasures if i ma, dungau nam-tor ish-veh veltra.' aushfa-wadi tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh sa-te'kru, t'vi ko-te'kru had isachya t' wuh purest pi-maat-tukh, heh vesh' ni vaksurik ik ish-veh match vesh' ri tor nam-tor ragel-tor k' fi' wuh bosh limuk t' wuh terra. Tonk'peh nash vaksurik ko-te'kru tevan-tor has-bosh, heh lu she olau ik ish-veh shaht drew be' she puvutau wuh sa-te'kru tor ish-veh heh leralmin-tor, 'ugaya me ik du dungi worla marry va'ashiv, vita du ragel-tor k' wuh ko-telsu vi nam-tor u' vaksurik u' i am, heh vi has pi-maat-kur isachya spo' t'nash-veh.' yi lu wuh sa-te'kru svi' ish-veh tushat ugau ek' she ya'akash, she ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun heh tev-tor. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru vesh' ri tor nam-tor comforted, heh na' wuh akarshif worla nahp t' taking wuh'ashiv ko-telsu. Na' kim-shah, however, ish-veh kau-bosh sasu leralmin-tor, 'nash dungi ri tor; wuh sa-te'kru bolau marry va'ashiv, ik etek lau ma wuh ko-te'kru.' ni skladasu vesh' satau irak heh eik, tor seek na' wuh bride u' vaksurik u' wuh tab-ma ko-te'kru. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai princess svi' wuh panu ni vaksurik; heh kuv tra' had vesh', fam dvun tra' vesh' ri veh tor nam-tor afer-tor vi had pi-maat-kur isachya. Ni wuh skladasu sarlah ha-kel, heh had had ek' ish-veh trouble na' nothing. I' wuh sa-te'kru had wuh ko-fu, vi vesh' aishan u' vaksurik u' ish-veh ko-mekh, heh had wuh ka pi-maat-kur isachya. Heh lu she vesh' grown abru, wuh sa-te'kru glazhau na' ish-veh heh gla-tor ik she vesh' aishan spo' nash tab-ma ko-te'kru: yi au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh courtiers, 'sos ri marry t'nash-veh ko-fu? She nam-tor wuh maut glakuv t' t'nash-veh tevik ko-telsu: vita i ma ish-veh, i dungau ri talal sovek bride fi-tor wuh bosh terra, heh du leralmin tra' bolau nam-tor wuh ko-te'kru.' lu wuh courtiers puzhu-tor nash au vesh' kolaya, heh leralmin-tor, 'sha-ka-ri zadau ik wuh sa-mekh dang marry ish-veh ko-fu! S' ni lo'uk wuh sin rai rom mokuhlek sarlah.' heh ish-veh ko-fu vesh' isha kolaya, tonk'peh rok-tor wuh sa-te'kru would ak mazhiv-kur-tor abru such nahp; ni she leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'fa' i marry sovek-veh i bolau ma rehkuh sai-vel: veh bolau nam-tor t' pi-maat-tukh, spo' wuh yel; wuh'ashiv bolau nam-tor t' shining haul-tukh, spo' wuh aikum; heh wuh wuh bolau nam-tor dazzling u' wuh yel: isha nash, i aitlun wuh tvi-kovtra t' wuh thousand natya ves t' ausachya shitau teretuhr, tor if kanok beast svi' wuh kingdom bolau mazhiv-kur-tor wuh krus t' ish-veh wadi.' heh thus she nahp au would nah-tor t' wuh tukh rai weht. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru tor wuh danik skilful workmen svi' ish-veh kingdom pris-tor wuh rehkuh sai-vel: veh pi-maat-kur, spo' wuh yel; wuh'ashiv silvery, spo' wuh aikum; heh wuh wuh sparkling, spo' wuh yel: heh ish-veh shi'ka'ree vesh' var-tor tor shi'kar si' ek' wuh beasts svi' ish-veh kingdom, heh tor nem-tor wuh finest ausachya s' ish-veh wadi: heh thus wuh tvi-kovtra t' wuh thousand furs vesh' tor. Lu ek' vesh' pok, wuh sa-te'kru satau au tor ish-veh; tonk'peh she prah abru svi' wuh mu-yor lu ek' vesh' asleep, heh nem-tor rehkuh t' ish-veh trinkets, wuh pi-maat-kur mokov, wuh pi-maat-kur necklace, heh wuh pi-maat-kur brooch, heh sa'haf-tor wuh rehkuh sai-vel--t' wuh yel, wuh aikum, heh wuh yel--abru svi' wuh nutshell, heh wrapped herself abru svi' wuh tvi-kovtra tor t' ek' wihfelau t' ausachya, heh besmeared ish-veh limuk heh el'ru k' soot. Yi she threw herself fi-tor sha-ka-ri na' gol'nev svi' ish-veh bolaya, heh went maf, heh halovau fi' wuh bosh mu-yor, till na' kim-shah sarlah ish-veh tor wuh suk lapan. U' she vesh' maut zungor, she hayal-tor herself ne' svi' wuh hollow t' wuh lap heh ak tevan-tor asleep: heh tra' she yuk-tor fi' till ish-veh vesh' midday. I' u' wuh sa-te'kru tor ik wuh lapan belonged vesh' hunting svi' ish-veh, ish-veh dogs sarlah tor wuh lap, heh began tor snuff pa', heh sahr-tor pauk heh pauk, heh kas-wadi. 'glazhau nasik!' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru tor wuh huntsmen, 'heh gla-tor ra wihfelau t' zhagra ti tra'.' heh wuh huntsmen went abru tor wuh lap, heh lu au sarlah pla' va'ashiv leralmin-tor, 'svi' wuh hollow lap tra' ti wuh danik wonderful beast, such u' etek worla gla-tor fa'; its wadi seems tor nam-tor t' wuh thousand ves t' ausachya, tonk'peh tra' ish-veh ti sahris asleep.' 'gla-tor, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru, 'kuv du mokuhlek kum ish-veh alive, heh etek dungi nem-tor ish-veh k' etek.' ni wuh huntsmen nem-tor ish-veh abru, heh wuh maiden awoke heh vesh' greatly koltha, heh leralmin-tor, 'i am wuh ri donku-tor kan ik has neither sa-mekh il ko-mekh losrak; ma pity fi' me heh nem-tor me k' du.' yi au leralmin-tor, 'ha, din-tor aushfa-wadi, du dungi tor na' wuh af'tum; du mokuhlek fnashtaya abru wuh vitush, heh tor vel t' ik wihfelau.' ni au shitau ish-veh vi' wuh coach, heh nem-tor ish-veh ha-kel tor wuh sa-te'kru's palace. Yi au gluvau ish-veh wuh pi' teruk ne' wuh staircase, wilat rai ta'hal t' gad ek'wak peeped svi', heh leralmin-tor, 'aushfa-wadi, du lau ti heh yuk tra'.' heh she vesh' satau vi' wuh af'tum, heh tor tor zaprah lapan heh masu, tor salur wuh yon, pluck wuh poultry, pick wuh bar-got, sift wuh vitush, heh tor ek' wuh kitork ar'kadan. Thus aushfa-wadi ha-tor na' wuh akarshif maut sorrowfully. 'ah! Takov princess!' nahp she, 'ra dungi i' shetau t' thee?' tonk'peh ish-veh pavesh-tor veh gad ik wuh gadzhak vesh' tor nam-tor meskarau svi' wuh sa-te'kru's castle, ni she leralmin-tor tor wuh fas-tor, 'sos hal-tor abru wuh pi' du' heh gla-tor ra nam-tor going fi'? I dungi nem-tor tun heh lamok za' wuh svep.' heh wuh fas-tor leralmin-tor, 'ha, du lau hal-tor, tonk'peh nam-tor pla' va'ashiv svi' ulef wuh wadan's wak, tor dref si' wuh vitush.' yi she nem-tor ish-veh pi' ha'gelek, heh went vi' ish-veh thif'etek, heh nem-tor ska' wuh ausachya wadi, heh pu-tor wuh soot s' ska' ish-veh limuk heh el'ru, ni ik ish-veh vaksur min-tor forth spo' wuh yel s' za' wuh wan. She thurai tu'ash ish-veh nutshell, heh katau s' ish-veh wuh sai-vel ik min-tor spo' wuh yel, heh ni went tor wuh gadzhak. Kanok-veh tor yut na' ish-veh, na' kling fai-tor ish-veh, heh au nahp she kupi nam-tor rai lehkuh tor wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru sarlah abru tor ish-veh, heh meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru heh tam-tor k' ish-veh; heh au nahp svi' ish-veh khaf-spol, 'i worla gla-tor sovek veh ulef ni vaksurik.' lu wuh tam vesh' na' wuh shaht she curtsied; heh lu wuh sa-te'kru glazhau pauk na' ish-veh, she vesh' hal-tor, kling fai-tor wither. Wuh klashau ik lam-tor na' wuh castle temep vesh' puvutau svi': tonk'peh au had gla-tor kling. Wuh yeht'es vesh', ik she had sahr-tor vi' ish-veh pi' thif'etek, seshau ska' ish-veh sai-vel, blackened ish-veh limuk heh el'ru, shitau fi' wuh ausachya-wadi tor-sai, heh vesh' aushfa-wadi va'ashiv. Lu she went vi' wuh af'tum tor ish-veh ar'kadan, heh began tor dref wuh vitush, wuh fas-tor leralmin-tor, 'kal-tor ik sa'awek till wuh asal, heh falek wuh sa-te'kru's shur; i dang spo' tor sahr-tor abru i' heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh peep: tonk'peh nem-tor tun du ri tor kal-tor wuh isachya tevan vi' ish-veh, il du dungi sahr-tor wuh pavesh t' worla eating va'ashiv.' u' ak u' wuh fas-tor went maf, aushfa-wadi falek-tor wuh sa-te'kru's shur, heh toasted wuh shihvek t' kap wuh'rak, u' nicely u' ek'wak she kupi; heh lu ish-veh vesh' pok, she went heh glazhau svi' wuh thif'etek na' ish-veh pi' pi-maat-kur mokov, heh shitau ish-veh vi' wuh dish svi' if wuh shur vesh'. Lu wuh tam vesh' abru', wuh sa-te'kru ordered ish-veh shur tor nam-tor katau svi'; heh ish-veh sanoi ish-veh ni muhl, ik au nahp au had worla zahv-tor sovek ni rom fa'. Na' wuh lanet gla-tor ish-veh wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov lying; heh u' au kupi ri tor si' uf ish-veh had prah tra', au ordered wuh fas-tor tor nam-tor satau na'. Wuh fas-tor vesh' koltha lu au puzhu-tor wuh zek, heh leralmin-tor tor aushfa-wadi, 'du bolau ma kal-tor wuh isachya tevan vi' wuh shur; kuv ish-veh nam-tor ni, du dungi ma wuh rom beating.' yi au went fa' wuh sa-te'kru, heh au ya'akash ish-veh vi had pufas-tor wuh shur. 'i did, ' kilko-tor wuh fas-tor. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'ik nam-tor ri yeht; ish-veh vesh' weh-rom ovsoh do du kupi tor ish-veh.' yi au kilko-tor, 'tor var-tor wuh yeht'es i did ri fas-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh aushfa-wadi did.' 'yi kal-tor aushfa-wadi sarlah abru, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru: heh lu sarlah ish-veh au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, 'vi nam-tor du?' 'i am wuh ri donku-tor kan, ' leralmin-tor she, 'ik has pakik fi' sa-mekh heh ko-mekh.' 'uf sarlah du svi' t'nash-veh palace?' ya'akash au. 'i am rom na' nothing, ' leralmin-tor she, 'tonk'peh tor nam-tor scullion-ko-kan, heh ki' kluf heh ash'el lehm-tor na' t'nash-veh patam.' 'tonk'peh uf did du prah wuh mokov ik vesh' svi' wuh shur?' ya'akash wuh sa-te'kru. Yi she would ri sha' ik she fai-tor sovek-vel pa' wuh mokov; ni wuh sa-te'kru satau ish-veh maf va'ashiv pa' ish-veh business. Po' wuh wak tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv gadzhak, heh aushfa-wadi ya'akash wuh fas-tor tor kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor abru heh gla-tor ish-veh u' fa'. 'ha, ' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh sarlah va'ashiv svi' ulef wuh wadan, heh fas-tor wuh sa-te'kru wuh shur ik au tishau ni mau.' yi she sahr-tor tor ish-veh pi' thif'etek, pu-tor herself sahris, heh nem-tor ish-veh sai-vel si' if vesh' silvery u' wuh aikum, heh shitau ish-veh fi'; heh lu she went svi', looking spo' wuh sa-te'kru's ko-fu, wuh sa-te'kru went abru tor ish-veh, heh rejoiced na' seeing ish-veh va'ashiv, heh lu wuh tam began au tam-tor k' ish-veh. Po' wuh tam vesh' na' wuh shaht she khartau tor trel si', ni slyly ik wuh sa-te'kru did ri gla-tor wilat she vesh' hal-tor; tonk'peh she sprang vi' ish-veh pi' thif'etek, heh tor herself vi' aushfa-wadi va'ashiv, heh went vi' wuh af'tum tor fas-tor wuh shur. Whilst wuh fas-tor vesh' abru' kaiden, she prah wuh pi-maat-kur necklace heh eku-tor ish-veh vi' wuh shur; yi ish-veh vesh' katau tor wuh sa-te'kru, vi ate ish-veh, heh ish-veh sanoi ish-veh u' muhl u' fa'; ni au satau na' wuh fas-tor, vi vesh' va'ashiv punekwitau tor var-tor ish-veh ik aushfa-wadi had pufas-tor ish-veh. Aushfa-wadi vesh' katau va'ashiv fa' wuh sa-te'kru, tonk'peh she fam dvun var-tor ish-veh ik she vesh' goh nunau ki' kluf heh ash'el lehm-tor na' ish-veh patam. Tonk'peh lu wuh sa-te'kru had ordered wuh gadzhak tor nam-tor prah pok na' wuh wuh wak, ish-veh pavesh-tor aishan wuh ka u' fa'. 'du bolau nam-tor wuh witch, aushfa-wadi, ' leralmin-tor wuh fas-tor; 'na' du kwon-hau-ov shitau vel vi' ish-veh shur, ni ik ish-veh sanoi wuh sa-te'kru weh-rom do t'nash-veh.' however, au kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor abru u' fa'. Yi she shitau fi' ish-veh sai-vel if sparkled spo' wuh yel, heh went vi' wuh rin'k'n-tvi-shal svi' ish-veh; heh wuh sa-te'kru tam-tor k' ish-veh va'ashiv, heh nahp she had worla glazhau ni vaksurik u' she did yi. Ni whilst au vesh' taman k' ish-veh, au shitau wuh pi-maat-tukh mokov fi' ish-veh ozh rik' ish-veh seeing ish-veh, heh ordered ik wuh tam dang nam-tor potau abru wuh akarshif. Lu ish-veh vesh' na' wuh shaht, au would ma meskarau ish-veh sahris k' wuh el'ru, tonk'peh she trel-tor maf, heh sprang ni sahris k'fai wuh patreitan ik au pakik glan t' ish-veh: heh she sahr-tor u' sahris u' she kupi vi' ish-veh pi' thif'etek ne' wuh kaiden. Tonk'peh nash wak she potau maf nuh' wu, heh stayed mesakh wuh ulef-wadan; ni she had ri wak tor nem-tor ska' ish-veh tok-ti sai-vel, heh threw ish-veh ausachya tvi-kovtra abru' ish-veh, heh svi' ish-veh haste did ri blacken herself ek' abru' k' soot, tonk'peh losrak veh t' ish-veh ozh wan-kur. Yi she sahr-tor vi' wuh af'tum, heh pufas-tor wuh sa-te'kru's shur; heh u' ak u' wuh fas-tor vesh' hal-tor, she shitau wuh pi-maat-kur brooch vi' wuh dish. Lu wuh sa-te'kru prah tor wuh lanet, au ordered aushfa-wadi tor nam-tor puvutau wuh'wak weht, heh ak gla-tor wuh wan-kur ozh, heh wuh mokov ik au had shitau fi' ish-veh whilst au vesh' taman: ni au seized ish-veh el'ru, heh potau sahris meskaraya t' ish-veh, heh lu she aitlu tor thal herself heh sikar maf, wuh ausachya tor-sai tevan-tor ska' wuh pi' fi' veh vla, heh wuh starry sai-vel sparkled ne'rak ish-veh. Yi au prah meskaraya t' wuh ausachya heh tore ish-veh ska', heh ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya heh vaksurik shid vesh' gla-tor, heh she kupi rai longer ip-sut herself: ni she pu-tor wuh soot heh vitush s' ish-veh limuk, heh gluvau herself tor nam-tor wuh danik vaksurik princess fi-tor wuh limuk t' wuh terra. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, 'du nam-tor t'nash-veh k'diwa bride, heh etek dungi worla weht nam-tor parted s' tik vath.' heh wuh wedding gadzhak vesh' meskarau, heh wuh merry gad ish-veh vesh', u' ek'wak vesh' puzhu-tor t' il gla-tor svi' ik shasol, il indeed svi' sovek vath. Izh-wan-kur heh she-tor-yon-kur tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh ri donku-tor kir'an vi ha-tor svi' wuh lonely cottage. Svi' khom t' wuh cottage vesh' wuh bah-ker wherein lam-tor dahkuh she-tor-lap, veh t' if spitau wan-kur heh wuh vath yon-kur roses. She had dahkuh kanu vi vesh' spo' wuh dahkuh she-tor-lap, heh veh vesh' puvutau izh-wan-kur, heh wuh vath she-tor-yon-kur. Au vesh' u' rom heh kunli, u' toranik heh cheerful u' ek'wak dahkuh kanu svi' wuh panu vesh', goh izh-wan-kur vesh' weht hizhuk heh gentle do she-tor-yon-kur. She-tor-yon-kur tishau weh-rom tor sahr-tor pa' svi' wuh ne-yartra heh vunai seeking svai heh catching mathra; tonk'peh izh-wan-kur hayal-tor na' ha-kel k' ish-veh ko-mekh, heh gol-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh housework, il telv-tor tor ish-veh lu tra' vesh' nothing tor tor. Wuh dahkuh kanu vesh' ni tishau t' veh wuh'ashiv ik au kwon-hau-ov meskarau tik vath k' wuh el'ru lu au went si' teretuhr, heh lu izh-wan-kur leralmin-tor: 'etek dungi ri trasha tik vath, ' she-tor-yon-kur kilko-tor: 'worla ni wu u' etek ha-tor, ' heh ish-veh ko-mekh would hau: 'ra veh has she bolau thresh k' wuh vath.' au k'ashiv sahr-tor pa' wuh laptra sa'awek heh hoknau yon-kur nei-savas, heh rai beasts did au sovek klau, tonk'peh sarlah beyik au trustfully. Wuh pi' hare would yokul wuh cabbage-mor s' ish-veh el'ru, wuh roe grazed k' ish-veh vla, wuh stag leapt merrily k' au, heh wuh kushel hayal-tor fam dvun fi-tor wuh boughs, heh sang whatever au fai-tor. Rai mishap overtook au; kuv au had stayed nuh' tab-ma svi' wuh laptra, heh mu-yor sarlah fi', au laid themselves ne' be' veh wuh'ashiv fi-tor wuh yekuhl, heh yuk-tor abi' asal sarlah, heh ish-veh ko-mekh fai-tor nash heh did ri worry fi' ish-veh khrosahp. Wuh'wak lu au had spent wuh mu-yor svi' wuh lapan heh wuh gad-keshtan had kastorilau au, gla-tor au wuh vaksurik kan svi' wuh shining wan-kur sai-vel sitting be' ish-veh sar-tak. Au prah abru heh glazhau ved kindly na' au, tonk'peh leralmin-tor nothing heh went vi' wuh laptra. Heh lu au glazhau pauk au afer-tor ik au had vesh' sleeping ved beyik wuh precipice, heh would certainly ma tevan-tor vi' ish-veh svi' wuh mu'khlup'es kuv au had hal-tor goh wuh zamu sahr-tor further. Heh ish-veh ko-mekh var-tor au ik ish-veh bolau ma vesh' wuh ha'su vi paluntunau rom kanu. Izh-wan-kur heh she-tor-yon-kur potau ish-veh ko-mekh's pi' cottage ni pu ik ish-veh vesh' wuh sanosh tor glazhau svi'udish ish-veh. Svi' wuh belaar she-tor-yon-kur nem-tor tun t' wuh kelek, heh kanok asal laid wuh wreath t' svai k' ish-veh ko-mekh's sar-tak fa' she awoke, svi' if vesh' wuh she-tor s' tik lap. Svi' wuh karil izh-wan-kur lit wuh yon heh geldau wuh kettle fi' wuh hob. Wuh kettle vesh' t' dvesh-tukh heh min-tor spo' pi-maat-tukh, ni brightly vesh' ish-veh polished. Svi' wuh khru, lu wuh snowflakes tevan-tor, wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor: 'hal-tor, izh-wan-kur, heh terk wuh svep, ' heh yi au hayal-tor pauk wuh hearth, heh wuh ko-mekh nem-tor ish-veh spectacles heh telv-tor aloud s' wuh suk dunap, heh wuh dahkuh ko-kan shroi u' au hayal-tor heh pada-tor. Heh beyik au ti wuh lamb fi-tor wuh lan-tol, heh za' au fi-tor wuh perch hayal-tor wuh wan-kur dove k' its patam ipik ne'rak its rala. Veh khru, u' au vesh' thus sitting comfortably teretuhr, ein-veh knocked na' wuh svep u' kuv au istau tor nam-tor kal-tor svi'. Wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor: 'sahris, she-tor-yon-kur, tu'ash wuh svep, ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh traveller vi nam-tor seeking rau-nol.' she-tor-yon-kur went heh kwitau pla' wuh terk, thinking ik ish-veh vesh' wuh ri donku-tor sasu, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri; ish-veh vesh' wuh lesh ik sakadau ish-veh sax'ksei, nesh-kur patam k'svi wuh svep. She-tor-yon-kur shei heh sprang pla', wuh lamb bleated, wuh dove nuv-tor, heh izh-wan-kur ip-sut herself za' ish-veh ko-mekh's sar-tak. Tonk'peh wuh lesh began tor stariben heh leralmin-tor: 'ri tor nam-tor kwes, i dungi tor du rai klau! I am ulef-le-sumalik, heh goh aitlun tor lamekh myself wuh pi' be' du.' 'ri donku-tor lesh, ' leralmin-tor wuh ko-mekh, 'ti ne' k' wuh yon, goh nem-tor tun ik du ri tor yontau ish-veh tor-pal.' yi she maf-tor: 'izh-wan-kur, she-tor-yon-kur, sarlah si', wuh lesh dungi tor du rai klau, au tvai muhl.' ni au fi' sarlah si', heh k'-heh-k' wuh lamb heh dove sarlah nearer, heh vesh' ri kwes t' ish-veh. Wuh lesh leralmin-tor: 'la', kanu, knock wuh izh s' t'nash-veh tor-pal wuh pi''; ni au katau wuh fnash-vel heh swept wuh lesh's ip-sut sok'i; heh au sakadau himself k' wuh yon heh growled contentedly heh comfortably. Ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' au grew ved na' ha-kel, heh mavau tricks k' ish-veh om'toi be'hai'la. Au seshau ish-veh isachya k' ish-veh el'ru, shitau ish-veh ash'ya fi-tor ish-veh pla' heh padukau ish-veh pa', il au nem-tor wuh hazel-dvelek heh kuhsh-tor ish-veh, heh lu au growled au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. Tonk'peh wuh lesh nem-tor ish-veh ek' svi' rom krus, goh lu au vesh' nuh' rough au puvutau si': 'trasha me alive, kanu, izh-wan-kur, she-tor-yon-kur, dungi du kuhsh-tor ish-veh wooer tevik?' lu ish-veh vesh' sar-tak-wak, heh wuh vath went tor sar-tak, wuh ko-mekh leralmin-tor tor wuh lesh: 'du mokuhlek ti tra' k' wuh hearth, heh yi du dungi nam-tor safe s' wuh samu heh wuh rasahkos igen-va.' u' ak u' gad dawned wuh dahkuh kanu kal-tor ish-veh si', heh au sahr-tor mes' wuh izh vi' wuh laptra. Henceforth wuh lesh sarlah kanok khru na' wuh ka wak, laid himself ne' k' wuh hearth, heh kal-tor wuh kanu amuse themselves k' ish-veh u' mau u' au tishau; heh au prah ni nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh ik wuh svep vesh' worla terau abi' ish-veh nesh-kur t'hy'la had lasha. Lu sikar had sarlah heh ek' s'udish vesh' yar-kur, wuh lesh leralmin-tor veh asal tor izh-wan-kur: 'i' i bolau hal-tor maf, heh fam yehat sarlah pla' na' wuh bosh belaar.' 'wilat nam-tor du going, yi, tal-kam lesh?' ya'akash izh-wan-kur. 'i bolau hal-tor vi' wuh laptra heh klashausu t'nash-veh treasures s' wuh wicked dwarfs. Svi' wuh karil, lu wuh terra nam-tor le-sumalik lerash, au nam-tor obliged tor stay ne' heh fam yehat ar'kadan ish-veh yut k'fai; tonk'peh i', lu wuh yel has thawed heh warmed wuh terra, au shaya k'fai ish-veh, heh sasarlah tor ihv-tor heh vazgau; heh ra wuh'wak prah vi' ish-veh el'ru, heh svi' ish-veh tauk, tor ri easily gla-tor gad-ha'khlup va'ashiv.' izh-wan-kur vesh' ved sorry na' ish-veh trashan, heh u' she unbolted wuh svep na' ish-veh, heh wuh lesh vesh' hurrying si', au kum-tor tehnat wuh terk heh wuh krus t' ish-veh hairy tor-pal vesh' torn ska', heh ish-veh seemed tor izh-wan-kur u' kuv she had gla-tor pi-maat-tukh shining k'fai ish-veh, tonk'peh she vesh' ri sure pa' ish-veh. Wuh lesh sahr-tor maf sahris, heh vesh' ak s' glan za' wuh lap. Wuh pen wak afterwards wuh ko-mekh satau ish-veh kanu vi' wuh laptra tor prah yon-lapan. Tra' au afer-tor wuh suk' lap if ti felled fi' wuh solektra, heh beyik wuh lap-fek vel vesh' jumping pla'rak heh fa'rak svi' wuh yar, tonk'peh au kupi ri tor si' ra ish-veh vesh'. Lu sarlah au nearer gla-tor au wuh kobsu k' wuh hinek withered limuk heh wuh izh-wan-kur hisahk wuh ker wu. Wuh shaht t' wuh hisahk vesh' kum-tor svi' wuh treshaya t' wuh lap, heh wuh pi' katravahsu vesh' jumping pa' spo' wuh dog tied tor wuh man-elakh, heh did ri fai-tor ra tor tor. Au glared na' wuh ko-kan k' ish-veh yonalik yon-kur bezhun heh maf-tor: 'po tor du lamok tra'? Mokuhlek du ri sarlah la' heh gol'nev me?' 'ra nam-tor du abru tor, pi' sasu?' ya'akash she-tor-yon-kur. 'du stupid, prying kushel!' kilko-tor wuh kobsu: 'i vesh' going tor thresh wuh lap tor prah wuh pi' lapan na' fasan. Wuh pi' zeshau t' yem-tukh ik etek sutra prah nam-tor iyi yontau abru k' ras lap-fek; etek ri tor vitem-tor ni mau u' du dirik, greedy sular. I had aishan driven wuh shihvek safely svi', heh kanok-vei vesh' going u' i istau; tonk'peh wuh cursed shihvek vesh' nuh' mos heh suddenly sprang si', heh wuh lap a'ing ni sahris ik i kupi ri seshaya si' t'nash-veh vaksurik wan-kur hisahk; ni i' ish-veh nam-tor wufik heh i fam yehat prah maf, heh wuh silly, sleek, thas-limuk-tor vel abru'teruklar-ru'lut! Ugh! Uf odious du nam-tor!' wuh kanu ar'kada maut lerash, tonk'peh au kupi ri seshaya wuh hisahk si', ish-veh vesh' kum-tor nuh' sahris. 'i dungi sahr-tor heh zaprah ein-veh, ' leralmin-tor she-tor-yon-kur. 'du senseless kushel!' snarled wuh kobsu; 'po dang du zaprah ein-veh? Du nam-tor already dahkuh nuh' wehk na' me; mokuhlek du ri nah-tor t' vel weh-rom?' 'ri tor nam-tor impatient, ' leralmin-tor izh-wan-kur, 'i dungi gol'nev du, ' heh she seshau ish-veh scissors s' ish-veh abru'lik, heh tresahk ska' wuh shaht t' wuh hisahk. U' ak u' wuh kobsu olau himself elik au laid meskaraya t' wuh sa'haf if ti svi' wuh gir t' wuh lap, heh if vesh' bosh t' pi-maat-tukh, heh abertau ish-veh abru, grumbling tor himself: 'uncouth sutra, tor tresahk ska' wuh krus t' t'nash-veh tok-ti hisahk. Rasahkos kunli tor du!' heh yi au swung wuh sa'haf fi-tor ish-veh pla', heh went ska' rik' kauk wuh'wak looking na' wuh kanu. Ein wak afterwards izh-wan-kur heh she-tor-yon-kur went tor kum wuh dish t' aluk. U' sarlah au be' wuh brook gla-tor au vel spo' wuh suk grasshopper jumping na' wuh masu, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' going tor leap svi'. Au sahr-tor tor ish-veh heh afer-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh kobsu. 'wilat nam-tor du going?' leralmin-tor she-tor-yon-kur; 'du surely ri tor aitlun tor hal-tor vi' wuh masu?' 'i am ri such wuh duhsu!' maf-tor wuh kobsu; 'ri tor gla-tor du ik wuh accursed aluk aitlu tor seshaya me svi'?' wuh pi' sasu had vesh' sitting tra' fishing, heh unluckily wuh salan had tangled abru ish-veh hisahk k' wuh fishing-zehl; wuh moment later wuh suk' aluk tor wuh zeshaya heh wuh kobat creature had ri karik'es tor seshaya ish-veh si'; wuh aluk potau wuh upper el'ru heh seshau wuh kobsu na' ish-veh. Au meskarau fi' tor ek' wuh reeds heh rushes, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' t' pi' rom, na' au vesh' punekwitau tor zahal-tor wuh dvun t' wuh aluk, heh vesh' svi' akali tehvar t' hasu zaseshau vi' wuh masu. Wuh ko-kan sarlah aishan svi' wak; au meskarau ish-veh sahris heh ar'kada tor elik ish-veh hisahk s' wuh zehl, tonk'peh ek' svi' vain, hisahk heh zehl vesh' entangled sahris teretuhr. Tra' vesh' nothing tor tor tonk'peh tor katau si' wuh scissors heh tresahk wuh hisahk, whereby wuh pi' krus t' ish-veh vesh' pakik. Lu wuh kobsu gla-tor ik au shei si': 'nam-tor ik civil, du toadstool, tor disfigure wuh sasu's limuk? Vesh' ish-veh ri hiyet tor clip ska' wuh shaht t' t'nash-veh hisahk? I' du ma tresahk ska' wuh buhfik krus t' ish-veh. I fam yehat kal-tor myself nam-tor gla-tor k' t'nash-veh sutra. I istaya du had vesh' tor tor sahr-tor wuh lad ska' ish-veh ash'el!' yi au nem-tor si' wuh sa'haf t' pearls if ti svi' wuh rushes, heh rik' wuh'ashiv zhit au zaseshau ish-veh maf heh sasaudau za' wuh kov. Ish-veh pavesh-tor ik ak afterwards wuh ko-mekh satau wuh dahkuh kanu tor wuh kahr tor mahr-tor og-lum heh og-elakh, heh laces heh ribbons. Wuh fau-yut pufulag-tor au mes' wuh heath fi-tor if masuk' krus t' kov ti strewn pa'. Tra' au pubeglanau wuh suk kushel hovering svi' wuh sov, hashan slowly pauk heh pauk abru' au; ish-veh sank weh-neik heh weh-neik, heh na' kim-shah settled be' wuh kov ri irak maf. Iyi au puzhu-tor wuh ral, piteous maf. Au sahr-tor abru heh gla-tor k' horror ik wuh eagle had seized ish-veh hinek acquaintance wuh kobsu, heh vesh' going tor lesh ish-veh ska'. Wuh kanu, bosh t' pity, na' wuh'wak nem-tor wufik meskaraya t' wuh pi' sasu, heh seshau tehnat wuh eagle ni wu ik na' kim-shah au kal-tor ish-veh booty hal-tor. U' ak u' wuh kobsu had recovered s' ish-veh wuh'rak kolthak au maf-tor k' ish-veh shrill spes: 'kupi du ri ma ovsoh ish-veh weht carefully! Du zaseshau na' t'nash-veh khav-kur tor-pal ni ik ish-veh nam-tor ek' torn heh bosh t' razh, du om'toi creatures!' yi au nem-tor abru wuh sa'haf bosh t' taluhk kov, heh trel-tor maf va'ashiv ne' wuh kov vi' ish-veh razh. Wuh ko-kan, vi k' nash wak vesh' nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh ingratitude, went fi' ish-veh yut heh did ish-veh business svi' kahr. U' au tuhsau wuh heath va'ashiv fi' ish-veh yut ha-kel au ak'wikmun wuh kobsu, vi had emptied si' ish-veh sa'haf t' taluhk kov svi' wuh sok'i gla-tor, heh had ri nahp ik sovek-veh would sarlah tra' ni tab-ma. Wuh khru yel min-tor fi-tor wuh maut-ugelik kov; au glittered heh sparkled k' ek' colours ni beautifully ik wuh kanu lam-tor fam dvun heh nantau na' au. 'po tor du lamok gaping tra'?' maf-tor wuh kobsu, heh ish-veh ashen-zhai-kur limuk became khaf-tukh-yon-kur k' reshan. Au vesh' fam dvun cursing lu wuh ral growling vesh' puzhu-tor, heh wuh nesh-kur lesh sarlah sahr-tor na' au si' t' wuh laptra. Wuh kobsu sprang abru svi' wuh kolthak, tonk'peh au kupi ri pulau ish-veh tauk, na' wuh lesh vesh' already ikap-tor. Yi svi' wuh dread t' ish-veh khaf-spol au maf-tor: 'tal-kam mr lesh, spare me, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du ek' t'nash-veh treasures; glazhau, wuh vaksurik ek'zer lying tra'! Vahl me t'nash-veh ha'kiv; ra tor du aitlun k' such wuh slender pi' katravahsu u' i? Du would ri olau me svi' ish-veh zud. Sarlah, nem-tor aifa dahkuh wicked ko-kan, au nam-tor sival morsels na' du, thelik u' nu'ri quails; na' mercy's sake yokul au!' wuh lesh nem-tor rai heed t' ish-veh zhit, tonk'peh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh wicked creature wuh single salur k' ish-veh paw, heh au did ri dvun va'ashiv. Wuh ko-kan had sahr-tor maf, tonk'peh wuh lesh puvutau tor au: 'izh-wan-kur heh she-tor-yon-kur, ri tor nam-tor kwes; bek-tor, dungi-sarlah nash-veh k' du.' yi au recognized ish-veh spes heh bek-tor, heh lu sarlah ish-veh abru tor au suddenly ish-veh bearskin tevan-tor ska', heh au lam-tor tra' wuh handsome sasu, clothed ek' svi' pi-maat-tukh. 'i am wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu, ' au leralmin-tor, 'heh i vesh' bewitched k' ik wicked kobsu, vi had stolen t'nash-veh treasures; i ma had tor sahr-tor pa' wuh laptra u' wuh savage lesh abi' i vesh' el-tor k' ish-veh tevakh. I' au has prah ish-veh muhl-nazh-tor taflaya. Izh-wan-kur vesh' telik tor ish-veh, heh she-tor-yon-kur tor ish-veh sa-kai, heh au dahsau svi' au wuh lo'uk treasure if wuh kobsu had hoknau teretuhr svi' ish-veh tauk. Wuh hinek ko-mekh ha-tor peacefully heh kunling k' ish-veh kanu na' wehk tevun. She nem-tor wuh dahkuh she-tor-lap k' ish-veh, heh au lam-tor fa' ish-veh krani, heh kanok tevun spitau wuh danik vaksurik roses, wan-kur heh yon-kur.
